āryamañjuśriye kumārabhūtāya namaḥ 
uttamajano hi prāyaśo guruṃ śraddhādevatāṃ cābhyarcyakarmasu pravartata ityayamapyahamuttamajananayamanuvartī madhyāntavibhāgasūtrabhāṣyaṃ cikīrṣustatpraṇeturvaktuś ca pūjāṃ kṛtvā tadarthavibhāgāya prayukta iti pratipādayannāha  śāstrasyā'sya praṇetāram ityādi 
evaṃ kṛtvā ko guṇaḥ prāpyate  guṇavato hitakāriṇaś ca pūjayatāmeṣāṃ puṇyamupacīyate 
puṇya upacite samārambhād vighnavināyakairanupahatānalpena prayāsena samāpayantīti 
athavā praṇetṛpraṇeyapravacanāt sūtrapraṇetṛvaktṛvṛttīṣu gauravotpādanārthamāha śāstrasyā'sya praṇetāram iti sarvam 
tatra praṇetṛvacanāt sūtre gauravam utpadyate 
yasyā'sya kārikāśāstrasyāryamaitreyaḥ praṇetā 
sa caikajātipratibandhāt sarvabodhisattvābhijñādhāraṇīpratisaṃvit samādhīndriyakṣāntivimokṣaiḥ paramaṃ pāraṃ gataḥ sarvāsu bodhisattvabhūmiṣu  niḥśeṣam api prahīṇāvaraṇaḥ 
vaktṛsamādānadvāreṇa vṛttau gauravam utpadyate 
vaktā punar atrācāryā'sangaḥ tasmācchrutvācāryambhadantavasubandhuḥ tad bhāṣyam akarot 
tayor uttaram aprajñāvator abhrānti prativedhadhāraṇopadeśasāmarthyād atra sūtrārtho'bhrāntam upadiṣṭa iti vṛttau gauravam utpadyate 
evaṃ ye pudgalaṃ pramāṇīkurvanti teṣāṃ sūtravṛttyo gauravotpattiḥ 
ye ca dharmānusāriṇas teṣāṃ sūtravṛttyoḥ śubhārthā'vabodhaḥ 
jāte ca niścaye iyaṃ praṇeturvaktuś ca pratītyā prabhāvanā na tu tarkāgamamātreṇa prabhāvaneti praṇetṛvaktṛgauravotpattiḥ 
idam idānīṃ vaktavyaṃ  kīdṛśaṃ śāstrarūpaṃ 
śāstraṃ kim iti cet nāmapadavyañjanakāyaprabhāsā vijñaptayaḥ śāstraṃ 
atha vā lokottarajñānaprāpakaśabdaviśeṣaprabhāsā vijñaptayaḥ śāstraṃ 
kathaṃ vijñaptayaḥ praṇīyanta ucyante vā 
praṇetṛvijñaptiprabhatvat prajñaptīnāṃ nātra doṣaḥ 
śiṣyadhārmiko hi śīlasamādhiprajñāviśeṣotpādāt kāyavānmanasāṃbhārānutpatīkarmaṇo nivartate sambhārotpattikarmāṇi ca pravartate 
atha vā śāstralakṣaṇasya śāsanācchāstraṃ 
svalakṣaṇaṃ yad upadeśo bhāsamānasarva kleśaprahāṇāya nirantaradīrghavividhatīvraduḥkhabhītyāś ca durgater bhavāc ca santrāyate 
tasmāt kleśaripuśāsanād bhavadurgatisantārāc ca śāstralakṣaṇaṃ 
etac ca dvayam api sarvasmin mahāyāne sarvasmiṃś ca tad vyākhyāne vidyate nānyatreti 
ata etac chāstraṃ 
āha ca  yacchāsti ca kleśaripūn aśeṣān santrāyate durgatito bhavāc ca 
tacchāsanā  guṇāc ca śāstraṃ etad dvayaṃ cānyamateṣu nāsti 
asyeti 
kriyānadvāreṇa saptavastusangrahasya kleśajñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇaprāpakasya madhyāntavibhāgakārikāśāstrasya hṛdi sthitatvād asyeti pratyakṣopadeśaḥ 
praṇetārm iti kartāraṃ 
yadyapy ayaṃ dhātuḥ prāpaṇārthas tathāpi praśabdasaṃyogāt viśeṣārthako draṣṭavyaḥ 
uktaṃ hi   upasargeṇa dhātvartho balād anyaḥ pratīyate 
gangāsalilamādhuryaṃ sāgareṇa yathāmbhasā 
sugatātmajam iti 
suṣṭhu gataḥ savāsana kleśāvaraṇāj jñeyāvaraṇāc cāpratiṣṭhitaṃ virvāṇam iti sugataḥ 
sa ca sarvavāsanāvaraṇaprahīṇaḥ sarvathā sarvadharmāvabodhasvarūpaḥ sarvavibhūtyāśrayabhūtaṇiratnavad acintyaprabhāvavigrahaḥ sarvasattvānāmanābhogena sarvārtha raṇasamartho nirvikalpakajñānaviśeṣātmakaḥ sugataḥ taj janitatvān nirvikalpasya jñānasya 
tasmāt tasmin vā jātaḥ sugatātmajaḥ 
athavā sugatātmanā jāta iti sugatātmajaḥ 
yathoktaṃ sūtrāntare jāto bhavati tathāgatavaṃśe tadātmakavstu pratilābhād iti 
evaṃ sati bodhisattvasya daśamyāṃ bhūmau pratiṣṭhitasya sarvākāraṃ jñeyaṃ vastu karatalastham ivāmalakaṃ tattvaṃśukāvacchāditalocanasyevābhāsamāyāti 
bhagavataḥ punar apanītalocanāvaraṇasyevetyayaṃ viśeṣaḥ 
atra hi sugatātmajasya śāstrapraṇetur avabodhasampat pradarśitā lābhasatkāranirapekṣasya śāstrapraṇetṛtvena karuṇāsampat prajñāsampacca 
vaktāram iti vyākhyānasya kartāraṃ 
abhyarhyeti sambadhyate 
sugatātmajamityapītyapare 
sa punar āryā'sangaḥ 
tasya hīdaṃ śāstram abhivyaktaṃ ākhyātaṃ cāryamaitreyādhiṣṭhānāt dharmasantānena 
ceti samuccaye pādapūraṇe'dhikavacane vā 
anyān api buddhabodhisattvānarcayitvā na kevalaṃ praṇetāraṃ vaktārañceti 
kebhyo vaktāraṃ 
asmad ādibhya iti 
vayam ādir yeṣāṃ te'samadādayas tebhyo'smadādibhyaḥ 
anenātmana upadeśasyāmṛṣātvaṃ vyajyate 
abhyarhyeti abhyarcya 
abhitaḥ purataḥ sākṣād iva sthitaṃ 
arhitvā arcayitvā kāyavānmanobhiḥ 
śāstrasya praṇetāraṃ vaktāraṃ cābhyarcya kiṃ kariṣyasītyāha  yatīṣye'rthavivecane 
iti 
yatnamārapsye arthavivecane arthavivareṇe pṛthagbhāvakaraṇe vā 
iyaṃ ca nimittārthā saptamī 
arthavivecananimittam ityarthaḥ 
  arthaḥ punar atra śāstraśarīram iti 
ete saptārthā hyasmin śāstra upadiśyanta iti vacanāt 
kim artham idaṃ śāstraṃ praṇītaṃ 
buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ samyag nirvikalpajñānotpādanārthaṃ 
dharmanairātmyadeśanatayā nirvikalpajñānotpādāt tadabhyāsāc ca niḥśeṣasavāsana kleśajñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇam avāpyate 
ayaṃ punardharmanairātbhyasyavirodhavādo yat sarvadharmarahitatā dharmanairātmyam
antarvyāpārapuruṣarahitatā ca dharmanairātmyam ityatas tat pratiṣedhena tathābhūtanairātmyapratipādanārthaṃ śāstrārambhaḥ 
lakṣaṇāvaraṇādiṣv apratipannavipratipannānāṃ samyag avabodhotpādanād apratipattivipratipattyapanayanārtham ity anye 
atha vā pañcākārajñeyaṃ lokadhātusattvadharmavineyopāyadhātvātmake pratyekam anantaprabhedatvād durvijñeyam iti bodhisattvānāṃ yaścittasankocas tad apanayanārtham āha  lakṣaṇaṃ hyāvṛtis tattvaṃ 
iti 
tatrāditaḥ śāstraśarīraṃ vyavasthāpyata iti 
tatreti śāstrasyārthavivecane śāstre  vā 
ādita iti prathamata iti 
śāstraṃ vivaraṇaṃ 
taccharīraṃ saṃkṣepaḥ piṇḍārtho vāśrayārthena vā śarīraṃ 
yathā hi bāhyādhyātmikāyatanāśrayaḥ kāyaḥ śarīram ity ucyate evaṃ yānarthān niścitya śāstraṃ pravartate te'rthās tasya śarīraṃ 
te ca saptyārthā lakṣaṇādayaḥ 
vyavasthāpyata iti prajñāpyate ākhyāyata ityarthaḥ 
nanu śāstrāvabhodhenaiva taccharīraṃ vijñāsyata iti nirarthakam ādau tad vyavasthāpanaṃ 
na nirarthakaṃ śiṣyā'nugrahārthatvāt 
gatārtho hi śiṣyaḥ sukhaṃ vistaram ucyamānaṃ pratipādyate 
dṛṣṭā bhūmir niḥśankam aśvavāhaneneva nānyathā 
ityete saptārthā hyasmin śāstra upadiśyante 
itiḥ śāstraśarīrasamāptyarthaḥ 
eta iti ye lakṣaṇādaya uddiṣṭāḥ 
sapteti saṃkhyāparyantādhigamārtham upādānaṃ 
arthyanta ityarthā adhigamyanta iti yāvat 
asmin śāstra iti madhyāntavibhāgasaṃjñake 
upadiśyanta ityākhyāyante viniściyante vā 
yad uta iti tathā'rthapratipādananipātaḥ 
lakṣaṇam iti 
lakṣyante'neneti lakṣaṇaṃ 
tac ca dvividhaṃ sankleśalakṣaṇaṃ vyavadānalakṣaṇāñca 
tatra sankleśalakṣaṇaṃ navavidhaṃ 
abhūtaparikalpo'sti ityārabhya yāvat saptadhā'bhūtakalpanāt iti 
śeṣeṇārdhena vyavadānalakṣaṇam ākhyātaṃ 
yadi lakṣyante'neneti laksaṇam ityevaṃ sati lakṣaṇasya sankleśavyavadānabhedo bhaved iti naitad evaṃ 
svabhāva eva hi bhāvānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ 
tad yathā pṛthivīdhātuḥ kharalakṣaṇo na ca kharatvāt pṛthivīdhātuḥ pṛthagastīti 
atha vā lakṣyate tad iti lakṣaṇaṃ 
evaṃ hi sankleśo vyavadānañca sankleśavyavadānātmatvena lakṣyata iti lakṣaṇaṃ 
atha vā dvayoḥ sankleśavyavadānayor lakṣaṇaṃ dvividhaṃ svalakṣaṇañca sāmānyalakṣaṇañca 
āvaraṇam iti 
āvṛṇoti kuśalān dharmānāvriyante'nena kuśaladharmā utpattivibandhāt ityāvaraṇaṃ 
tat punas tripañcāśat prakāraṃ 
tattvam iti 
tadevedaṃ tat tasya bhāvas tattvam aviparyāsa ityarthaḥ 
tac ca daśa prakāraṃ 
  vipakṣaprahāṇārthaḥ pakṣaḥ pratipakṣaḥ 
sa sārgaḥ 
tadabhyāso bhāvanā 
avasthā tasyaiva santānenotpattiviśeṣaḥ 
sā punar ekānnaviṃśatiprakārā gotrāvasthādikā 
phalasya lābhaḥ phalaprāptiḥ 
tat punaḥ pañcadaśaprakāraṃ vipākaphalādi 
yānānuttartham iti 
gamyate'neneti yānaṃ 
yānac ca tadānuttaryañceti yānānuttaryaṃ 
tat punastrividhaṃ pratipattyānuttaryādi 
saptamo'rtha iti niyamārtham anukramārthañcāha 
etāvanta evārthā nirdiśyante nāto'nya iti 
anukramaḥ punar ayaṃ lokottarajñānānukūlyārthaḥ 
tathā hi bodhisattvenādhimukticaryābhūmisthitena śīlapratiṣṭhitena prathamaṃ sankleśavyavadānakuśalena bhavitavyaṃ 
tataḥ kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ yasya yad āvaraṇaṃ tasya taj jñeyaṃ 
tasyāprahāṇād vimukter asambhavād avijñānañca prahātuṃ na śakyate doṣadarśanāt 
tatas tadāvaraṇād yenālambanena cittaṃ vimucyate tatttvaṃ veditavyaṃ 
tatastenālambhanenatadāvaraṇasya yena prayogena kṣayo bhavati sā pratipakṣabhāvanā jñeyā
tatas tasyāṃ pratipakṣabhāvāyāṃ vipakṣahānyā pratipakṣavṛddhyā cā'vasthā jñeyā gotrāvasthādikā 
tato lokottaradharmābhimukhīkaraṇaṃ phalāni srota apatti phalādīni veditavyāni 
sarvam apyetat srottaratvācchrāvakādibhiḥ sādhāraṇaṃ bodhisattvānāṃ 
yathoktaṃ sūtre  sa pravrajitaḥ śrāvakaśikṣācāragocarasamudācāram api śikṣate pratyekabuddhaśikṣācāragocarasamudācāram api śikṣate bodhisattvaśikṣācāragocarasamudācāram api śikṣate 
bodhisattvānāṃ tvānuttaryam asādhāraṇaṃ 
saptamo'rtha ānuttaryaṃ 
anyastvāha 
sankleśavyavadānalakṣaṇe kauśalotpādanārtham ādau laksaṇaṃ 
tatra yaḥ sankleśas tadāvaraṇaṃ 
yad vyavadānaṃ tat tattvaṃ 
āvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ ca tattvādhigamād bhavatītyata āvaraṇatattvaṃ 
tat prahāṇopāyapradarśanārthaṃ tataḥ saparivāraḥ pratipakṣo mārgaḥ 
tasya mārgasyādimadhyānteṣu mṛdumadhyādhimātraprabhedapradarśanārthaṃ tatrāvasthā 
avasthānurūpaṃ phalamāvahatīti tad anantaraṃ phalaṃ 
etac ca sarvaṃ bodhisattvasya śrāvakādisādhāraṇam ity asādhāraṇamahāyānanayaprakāśanārthaṃ yānānuttaryam iti 
apare punar āhuḥ 
sadasal lakṣaṇajñāpanārthaṃ prathamato lakṣaṇam ākhyātaṃ 
lakṣaṇaṃ jñātvāvaraṇaṃ prahātavyaṃ tattvaṃ ca sākṣāt kartavyam iti tad anantaram āvaraṇatattvaṃ 
  tayoś ca prahāṇasākṣātkaraṇayor ayam upāya iti pratipakṣabhāvanā 
tasyāś ca tāratamyam avasthāviśeṣaḥ 
tat kṛtañca prahāṇaṃ phalaṃ 
tad anantaraṃ yānānuttaryam iti prakāśanārtham ayam anukrama iti 
anyacca sattvasya sadasad dharmasaṃmohāpavādasamāropaprahāṇārthaṃ lakṣaṇanirdeśaḥ 
prahīṇasaṃmohasyāvaraṇakauśalārtham āvaraṇaṃ 
tenāvṛtaṃ tattvam iti tattvakauśalārthaṃ tad anantaraṃ tattvaṃ 
tattvapratividdhabhāvanayāvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ bhavatīti tattvānantaraṃ pratipakṣabhāvanā 
tat prabhedakauśalārtham avasthā 
avasthayāṃ phalaṃ prabhāvitavyam ityavasthānantaraṃ phalaṃ tat kauśalotpādanārthaṃ 
sarvam etan mahāyānamāgamyeti yānānuttaryam ante nirdiṣṭaṃ 
 tatra lakṣaṇam ārabhyāha  abhūtaparikalpo'sti dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate 
śūnyatā vidyate tv atra tasyām api sa vidyate 
iti 
tatreti lakṣaṇāvaraṇādisaptārtheṣu nirdiṣṭeṣu lakṣaṇam adhikṛtyoddiśyāha  abhūtaparikalpo'sti iti 
yathoddiśas tathā nirdeśa iti kṛtvā 
lakṣaṇañca prāg uddiṣṭamatastasyaiva śeṣebhyo nirdeśaḥ prāgārabhyate 
kecit virundhanti sarvadharmāḥ sarvathā niḥsvabhāvāḥ śaśaviśāṇavad ityataḥ sarvāpavādapratiṣedhārthamāha  abhūtaparikalpo'stīti 
svabhāvata iti vākyaśeṣaḥ 
nanv evaṃ sūtravirodhaḥ  sarvadharmāḥ śūnyā iti śāstre vacanāt 
nāsti virodhaḥ yasmāt  dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate 
abhūtaparikalpo hi grāhyagrāhakasvarūparahitaḥ śūnya ucyate na tu sarvathā niḥsvabhāvaḥ 
ato na sūtravirodhaḥ 
yadyevaṃ dvayaṃ śaśaviṣāṇavat sarvathā nāsti 
abhūtaparikalpaś ca paramārthataḥ svabhāvato'styevaṃ śūnyatā'bhāvaprasangaḥ 
naitad evaṃ yasmāt   śūnyatā vidyate tvatra iyam eva hi śūnyatā yā grāhagrāhakarahitatā'bhūtaparikalpasyeti na śūnyatāyā nāstitvaṃ bhavati 
yadyadvayā śūnyatā sā cābhūtaparikalpe'sti kasmād vayamamuktāḥ 
vidyamānā ca kasmān na gṛhyata iti saṃśayāpanayanārthaṃ  tasyām api sa vidyate 
ityāha 
yasmācchūnyatāyām apyabhūtaparikalpo vidyate tasmād bhavanto na muktāḥ 
ata eva ca samalatvān na prasannābdhātavad gṛhyate 
atha vā cittacaittebhyo'nyatra rūpādayo dravyatvena santīti yad darśanaṃ tat pratiṣedhārtham āha  abhūtaparikalpo'sti dravyataḥ 
nāsti rūpaṃ tad vyatiriktaṃ dravyata iti 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  yasmāt  dvayaṃtatra na vidyate 
na hy abhūtaparikalpaḥ kasyacid grāhako nāpi kenacit gṛhyate 
kiṃ tarhi grāhyagrāhakatvaṃ bhāvamātram eva 
yato vijñānād bahī rūpādayo na gṛhyante 
svapnāadivad vijñānaṃ rūpādyābhāsam utapdyate 
na ca yad yasya kāraṇaṃ tad abhāve tasyotpattir yujyate 
tasmān nirālambanam eva svapnādāviva 
anyatrāpi svabījaparipākād arthābhāsaṃ vijñānam utpadyate ity avaseyaṃ 
grāhyābhāve grāhakasyābhāvād grāhye'sati grāhako bhavituṃ na yujyate 
tasmān na rūpam abhūtaparikalpāt pṛthag asti 
yadi tarhi grāhyabhāvastena viśuddhyālambanābhāvān mokṣābhāvaḥ 
naitad evaṃ yasmāt  śūnyatā vidyate tvatra tu śabdo yasmād arthaḥ 
śūnyatā hi vuśuddhyālambanā 
sā ca grāhyagrāhakarahitatā 'bhūtapraikalpe'stīti na mokṣābhāvaḥ 
yady abhūtaparikalpe'sti sā vidyamānā kimarthaṃ na gṛhyate 
abhūtaparikalpāvṛtatvān na gṛhyata ākāśanairmalyavat na tu asattvād iti pratipādayann āha  tasyām api sa vidyata iti 
atha vā sarvāpavādapratiṣedhārtham āha   abhūtaparikalpo'sti iti 
na sarvam asat nāpi sadātmakaṃ vijñānapariṇāmāatmanā'stīti kṛtvā 
ye tu manyante yathaiva rūpādayaḥ prakhyāyante tathiavābhūtaparikalpāt svabhāvataḥ pṛthag vidyanta iti tān pratyāha abhūtasamāropapratiṣedhārthaṃ  dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate 
iti 
abhūtaparikalpamātraṃ vidyata ityabhiprāyaḥ 
kenacit dvayor abhāvo vo vnadhyāputravat cheda rūpo gṛhyate 
anyair antarvyāpārapuruṣarahitatā dharmāṇāṃ śūnyate'tyucyate 
ataḥ śūnyatāpavādapratiṣedhārthaṃ bhūtanairātmyakhyāpanārthañcāha  śūnyatā vidyate tvatra iti 
yadyabhūtaparikalpe śūnyatāstyevaṃ sati sarvaprāṇinām aprayatnena mokṣaprasangaḥ 
nāsyetad yasmāt  tasyām api sa vidyate 
na hyaviśodhitāyāṃ śūnyatāyāṃ mokṣo'sti sankliṣṭā ca mahatā yatnena viśodhyata iti nāsty ayatnena mokṣaḥ 
atha vā lakṣaṇaṃ sankleśavyavadānābhidhānād anyan nāstītyataḥ sankleśavyavadānalakṣaṇapradarśanārthamāha  abhūtaparikalpo'sti iti vistaraḥ 
abhūtaparikalpasvabhāvaḥ saṃkleśo bhrāntilakṣaṇatvāt 
katham etaj jñātavyaṃ bhrāntilakṣaṇam iti  yena  dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate svātmanyavidhyamānena grāhyagrāhakākāreṇa pratyānād bhrāntisvarūpeṇa jñayate
edāniṃ vyavadānasvarūpapradarṣana arthamāḥ  śūnyatā vidyate tvatra iti
śūnyatāsvabhāvo hi vyavadānaṃ dvayābhāvasvabhāvatvāt 
atra ca śūnyatāprabhāvitatvāt mārganirodhayor api grahaṇamṃ veditavyaṃ 
sankleśapakṣād eva vyavadānapakṣo mārgayitavyo na punaḥ pṛthaktvam asyāstīti pradarśanārtham āha atreti 
yadi dvayaṃ nāsti kathaṃ tasyāṃ vidyamānāyāṃ loko bhrānta ityāha  tasyām api sa vidyate iti 
grāhyagrāhakavikalpo hastyādyākāraśūnyamāyāyām iva hastyākārādayaḥ 
abhūtam asmin dvayaṃ parikalpyate'nena vetyabhūtaparikalpaḥ 
abhūtavacanena ca yathā'yaṃ parikalpyate grāhyagrāhakatvena tathā nāstīti pradarśayati 
parikalpavacanena tvartho yathā parikalpyate tathārtho na vidhyate iti pradarṣayati
evam asya grāhyagrāhakavinirmuktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ paridīpitaṃ bhavati 
kaḥ punar asau  atītānāgatavartamānā hetuphalabhūtās traidhātukā anādikālikā nirvāṇaparyavasānāḥ saṃsārānurūpāścittacaittā aviśeṣeṇābhūtaparikalpaḥ 
viśeṣeṇa  tu grāhyagrāhakavikalpaḥ 
tatra grāhyavikalpo'rthasattvapratibhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ 
grāhakavikalpa ātmavijñaptipratibhāsaṃ 
dvayaṃ grāhyaṃ grāhakañceti 
tatra grāhyaṃ rūpādi 
grāhakaṃ cakṣūr vijñānādi 
grāhyagrāhakabhāvena virahitatā viviktatā hyabhūtaparikalpasya śanyatā 
na tv abhūtaparikalpo'pyabhāvaḥ yathā śūnyā rajjuḥ sarpasvabhāvenātat svabhāvatvāt sarvakālaṃ śūnyā na tu rajju svabhāvena tathehāpi 
tasyām api sa vidyata iti abhūtaparikalpaḥ 
evaṃ hy āgantukāvaraṇopakliṣṭatvāt tad agrahaṇam uktam abdhātvādivad iti 
evaṃ yad yatra nāsti tat tena śūnyam iti yathābhūtaṃ samanupaśyatīti 
kiṃ kutra nāsti  abhūtaparikalpe dvayaṃ 
ato'bhūtaparikalpaṃ dvayena śūnyaṃ paśyati 
yat punar atrā'vaśiṣṭaṃ tat sat 
kiṃ punar ihāvaśiṣṭaṃ  abhūtaparikalpaḥ śūnyatā ca 
tad ubhayam ihāstītyanādhyāropānapavādena paśyan yathābhūtaṃ prajānāti 
tatrābhūtaparikalpe'dvayadarśanād anadhyāropaḥ 
abhūtaparikalpasya śūnyatāścāstitvadarśanād anapavādaḥ 
aviparītaṃ śūnyatālakṣaṇam udbhāvitaṃ bhavati 
yac chūnyaṃ tasya sad bhāvāt yena śūnyaṃ tasya tatrābhāvāt 
sarvabhāve sarvābhāve vā nāviparītaṃ śūnyatālakṣaṇaṃ 
śūnyatāyā evābhāvaprasangāt 
na śūnyasaṃjñā'satyāṃ śūunyatāyāṃ yujyate 
dharmatāyā hi bhāvāyāt tattvād anityatvādivat 
dvayam astīti śūnyatābhāvaḥ 
yadi śaśaviṣāṇakalpanena dvayaṃ kathaṃ tenābhūtaparikalpasya śūnyatāsambhavaḥ  anyena hy anyasya śūunyatā dṛṣṭā yathā bhikṣubhir vihārasya 
naitad evaṃ 
yathā rajjur māyā vā svātmany avidyamānena sarpākāreṇa puruṣādinā prabhāsate 
tatra kasyacid grāhanirvartanārthaṃ sarpapuruṣādibhiś ca śūnyety ucyate 
evam abhūtaparikalpo'pi svātmany avidyamānena grāhyagrāhakākāreṇa prakhyāyamāno bālānāṃ tad grāhābhiniveśaty ājanārthaṃ dvayena śūnyam ity ucyate 
  na śūnyaṃ nā'pi cā'śūnyaṃ iti 
kim artham asau śloka ārabdha iti  sarvasya saṃskṛtasyāsaṃskṛtasya ca dvayarahitatājñāpanārthaṃ 
evaṃ ca hyekāntapratikṣepeṇa sarvam idaṃ na śūnyaṃ nāśūnyam iti prajñāpāramitāpāṭhābhiprāyatāviṣkṛtā bhavati 
anyathā pūrvāparaviruddham etat syāt 
kiñca madhyamāpratipat prakāśanārthaṃ 
anyathaikāntikaśūnyataivāśanyānto vā syāt 
apavādasamāropapratiṣedhopasaṃhārārthaṃ vā'syārambhaḥ 
hetupratyayapratibaddhātmalābhād abhūtaparikalpaḥ saṃskṛtaṃ 
śūnyatā punas tan nirapekṣatvād asaṃskṛtaṃ 
vidhīyate prajñāpāramitādimadhye paṭhyate 
sattvād abhūtaparikalpasya na saṃskṛtaṃ śūnyam abhūtaparikalpātmatvena 
asatvād dvayasya 
grāhyagrāhakātmanā śūnyaṃ 
śūnyātāyās tu sarvam abhūtaparikalpe tad dharmateti kṛtvā 
śūnyatāyām apy abhūtaparikalpo dharmirūpeṇa vidyate 
evam asaṃskṛtam api dharmatārūpeṇa na śūnyaṃ 
abhāvasaṃjñakena dvayena svarūpaśūnyaṃ 
sā ca madhyamā pratipad iti ratnakūṭādimadhye'stīti kāśyapāyam eko'ntaḥ 
nāstītyayaṃ dvitīyo'ntaḥ 
yadetayor dvayor antayor madhyamiyam ucyate kāśyapa madhyamā pratipad dharmāṇāṃ bhūtapratyavekṣeti sā madhyamā pratipadevam anulomitā 
sarvam iti saṃskṛtam asaṃskṛtañca 
naikāntena śūnyam ity abhūtaparikalpasya tac chūnyatāyāś ca  sadbhāvāt 
nāpyekāntenāśūnyaṃ dvayasyābhāvāt 
sarvanāstitvaṃ sarvāstitvaṃ vā'nta eva syāt 
na madhyamā pratipad 
 evam abhūtaparikalpasya sal lakṣaṇam asallakṣaṇañca khyāpayitveti 
idaṃ sattvena lakṣyata iti sattvam eva sallakṣaṇaṃ 
abhūtaparikalpo vidyata ity anenābhūtaparikalpasya sattvaṃ pradarśayatīty arthaḥ 
evam asattvena lakṣyata iti asatvam evāsal lakṣaṇāt 
tat punar yad grāhyagrāhakabhāvenāsattvaṃ 
yasmād abhūtaparikalpe dvayaṃ nāsti tasmād abhūtaparikalpo'pi dvayātmanā nāstīty uktaṃ bhavati 
svalakṣaṇaṃ khyāpayatīti 
ko viśeṣo'sti sallakṣaṇasvalakṣaṇayoḥ  sallakṣaṇaṃ hi sāmānyaṃ 
svalakṣaṇam tu viśeṣaḥ 
yadi svalakṣaṇam anākhyātamatra kiṃ syāt  śarīram abhūtaparikalpasya noktaṃ syāt 
atas tac charīrapratipādanārtham ucyate  arthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsaṃ prajāyate 
vijñānaṃ nāsti cā'syārthas tadabhāvāt tadapyasat 
iti 
atha vā grāhyagrāhakarahitatā'bhūtaparikalpamātrate'ty ucciṣṭaṃ 
tasyām abhūtaparikalpamātratāyām indriyaviṣayavijñānaṃ yathā vyavasthitaṃ na jñāyata 
abhūtaparikalpapratibhāsabhedena tad vyavasthitajñāpanārtham abhūtaparikalpasya svalakṣaṇaṃ khyāpayati  arthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsaṃ 
iti vistaraḥ 
  atha vā 'bhūtaparikalpo'stītyanena tat sattvamātraṃ jñāyate na tu tat svabhāvaḥ 
dvayābhāve'pi yad grāhyagrāhakābhiniveśakāraṇaṃ na vijñāyate dvayaṃ ca nāstīti yataḥ pratīyate tad api noktam ityatas tat pratipādanārtham āha  arthasattvātmavijñapti pratibhāsaṃ iti vistaraḥ 
tatra vijñānasvabhāvo'bhūtaparikalpaḥ 
tac ca vijñānaṃ sasamprayogam abhipretaṃ 
pradhānena tu vijñānaṃ gṛhītaṃ 
sa eva grāhyagrāhakābhiniveśo'rthasattvādipratibhāsanibandhanaḥ 
nāsti cāsyārthas tadabhāvāt tad apyasat 
iti 
dvayābhāvakāraṇaṃ 
tatrārthasattvapratibhāsamālayavijñānaṃ sasamprayogaṃ 
tac ca vipākatvād avyākṛtam eva 
ātmapratibhāsaṃ kliṣṭaṃ manaḥ sasaṃprayogaṃ 
tac ca nivṛtāvyākṛtaṃ kleśasaṃprayuktatvād uktaṃ 
vijñaptipratibhāsaṃ kuśalākuśalāvyākṛtaṃ sasamprayigañcakṣur vijñānādi ṣaṭkaṃ 
tadetānyarthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsānyaṣṭau vijñānāni sasamprayogāṇi samudayasatyasangṛhītāt sahakāripratyayāpekṣād ālayavijñānāt yathāsaṃbhavaṃ pañcagatiṣu prabhavanti 
kaścit kuśalā'kuśalaavyākṛtadharmavāsanāpariṇāmaviśeṣo'styālayavijñānasya yadādhipatyena parasparabhinnābhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ prajāyate 
katham asatyarthādau vijñānaṃ tadābhāsam utpadyate  na hi puruṣe'sati sthāṇuḥ puruṣābhāso bhavatīti 
naiṣa doṣaḥ 
arthādyābhāsaṃ hi vijñānaṃ bālā vijñānāt pṛthag arthāstitvenā'bhiniviśante taimirikasya keśoṇḍukādivat 
tasmāt tadabhiniveśatyājanārtham ucyate  vijñānam evedam arthādyābhāsam utpadyate taimirikāṇām iva keśoṇḍukādyābhāsaṃ vināpyarthasattvādineti 
evaṃ cāṣṭavijñānavastukaḥ paratantro'bhūtaparikalpa ity uktaṃ bhavati 
rūpādabhāveneti rūpaśabdagandharasaspraṣṭavya dharmasvarūpeṇa pratibhāsaṃ tadākāreṇotpannatvāt 
sattvapratibhāsaṃ yat pañcendriyatvena svaparasantānayoḥ 
pratibhāsa ity adhikṛtaṃ 
adhikasaktisthānatvāt pañcasv indriyeṣu sattvākhyā 
tais teṣu vā sajjata iti sattvaḥ 
tadākārotpattitām upādāya vijñānaṃ tadābhāsam iti 
ātmapratibhāsaṃ kliṣṭaṃ manaḥ ātmamohādisamprayogād iti kliṣṭasya manasa ātmamohenātmadṛṣṭyā ātmatṛṣṇāyā'smimānena ca nityaṃ samprayuktatvāt  teṣāñcātmālambanatvādy uktam ātmapratibhāsatvaṃ kliṣṭasya manasaḥ 
vijñaptipratibhāsaṃ ṣaḍ vijñānānīti 
viṣamagrāhakarūpeṇa prakhyānāt tadākārotpattitām upādāya vijñaptipratibhāsaṃ 
nāsti cāsyārtha iti catuṣṭayasyākārasyeti 
arthasattvapratibhāsasyānākāratvāt ātmavijñaptipratibhāsasya ca vitathapratibhāsatvād iti arthasattvapratibhāsasyānākāratvāt ātmavijñaptipratibhāsasya ca vitathapratibhāsatvād iti arthasattvapratibhāsayor grāhyarūpeṇa prakhyānād vitathapratibhāsatvāsambhavād anākāratvam evārthābhāve kāraṇaṃ 
na tv anyayor grāhakarūpeṇa prakhyānād anākāraḥ 
vitathapratibhāsatvem evārthābhāve kāraṇam uktaṃ 
ākāro hyālambanasyānityādirūpeṇa grahaṇaprakāraḥ 
sa cānayor nāsti grāhyarūpeṇa prakhyānāt 
ato'nākāratvād agrāhakatvād ityarthaḥ 
ālambanasamvedanaṃ vākāraḥ 
tac ca tayor nāstīty upalabdhyabhāvād anākāraḥ 
yadyubhayam apy anākāraṃ parasparabhinnasvarūpac ca rūpādivac cakṣurādivac ca evaṃ sati lokaśāstraprasiddhebhyo rūpādibhyaścakṣurādibhyaś ca vijñānasya ko'sāvātmātiśayo yatas tān nirākritya tair abhinnarūpaṃ vijñānaṃ gṛhyate tad avyatiriktasyārthasyāsambhavāt  etad evaṃ vyavasthāpyate  yasmād bhinnarthasvarūpamasannapicittāsantānapratiniyamena svabījāt pratyekātmagrahītaṃ bhinnārthādipratibhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ prasūyate 
tathāhi pretā apaḥ pūyapurīṣamūtrādipūrṇā dhṛtadaṇḍapāṇibhir ubhayataḥ purusaiḥ saṃrakṣyamāṇāḥ paśyanti manuṣYādayaḥ punaḥ svacchaśītalodakaparipūrṇā nirvibandhā ity upalabhante 
yoginaścāśubhamanasikārādy abhyastā nirantaraṃ pṛthivīṃ kankālapūrṇāṃ paśyanti 
tathā pṛthivyādi kṛtsneṣu sarvaṃ pṛthivayādibhir vyāptaṃ paśyati 
na cārthapratibuddhātmalābhasyaarthamantareṇaarthasvarūpād vā bhinnākārasya vijñānāsya prasūtir yuktā 
tasmāt tad arthamantareṇa sarvam arthasattvādinirbhāsaṃ vijñānam eva prasūyata iti niścīyate 
grāhyābhāve dvayor ātmavijñaptipratibhāsayor grāhakākāreṇa prakhyānāt vitathapratibhāsatvaṃ 
atha vā yathā vijñānenārthaḥ parikalpyate tathārthasyābhāvo vyāghrādiśrutyādiṣv iva vitathālambanatvād vitathapratibhāsatā 
tathā hi vijñaptir api vijñapty antaraparikalpitenātmanā śūnyeti siddhāntaḥ 
ataścārthasattvavijñānasyevātmavijñaptipratibhāsasyāpyarthābhāvaḥ 
arthābhāvāt tad vijñānam asat 
vijānātīti vijñānaṃ grāhyābhāve vijānanāpy ayuktaṃ 
tasmād arthābhāvād vijñātṛtvena vijñānam asad na  tv arthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsatayā 
tad asattve hi sarvathā'bhāvaprasangaḥ 
tad avyatirekeṇa vijñānasvabhāvānirdeśāt 
tad bhinnasvabhāve sati tad vijñānaṃ kathaṃ yujyeta kathaṃ parasparaṃ bhinnaṃ bhavet  
 evaṃgrāhyagrāhakābhāvāt tat pratibhāsavijñānasadbhāvāc ca yat pūrvaṃ pratijñātaṃ  abhūtaparikalpo'sti dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate 
iti tat prasiddham iti pradarśayann āha  abhūtaparikalpatvaṃ siddham asya bhavatyataḥ 
abhūtaparikalpatvañca teṣāñcaturṇāṃ vijñānānāṃ siddhaṃ 
ata ity anantaroktād hetorarthābhāvāt tad apy asad iti punar apy abhūtaparikalpāstitvaprasādhanārthaṃ dvayābhāvaprasādhanārthañcāha  na tathā sarvathā'bhāvāt ityādi 
atha vā ata iti vakṣyamāṇādvetoḥ 
tameva pradarṣayannāh na tathā sarvathā'bhāvāt iti
na tathā'stitvān na ca sarvathā nāstitvāt tad grāhyagrāhakapratibhāsam utpadyate 
tatra catuḥprakāre'py anākāratvād vitathākāratvāc ca yathāsambhavaṃ grāhakatvābhāvaḥ 
vijñaptyantaraparikalpitena cātmanā sarvasya śūnyatvād grāhyatvābhāvaḥ 
na ca sarvathā'bhāvo bhrāntimātrasyotpādād ityātmatvenābhāvo na tu yadākāreṇa pratibhāsate tena bhrāntir ucyare māyāvat 
mātra śabdas tadadhikavyavacchedārthaḥ 
etad uktaṃ bhavati  bhrāntivijñānasya sadbhāvān na sarvathā'bhāva iti 
kimartha punas tasya bhrāntivijñānasyā'bhāva eva neṣyate grāhyagrāhakābhāvavat  na hi kenacit tasyāstitvaṃ kalpayituṃ śakyate sarvāvijñānaviṣayātikrāntatvād ity abhipretam iti cet 
yasmāt  tat kṣayān muktir iṣyate 
ato'syābhāva eva neṣyate 
kiṃ tarhi sankleśavyavadānapakṣasāmarthāt tad astitvam anumīyate 
  anyatheti yadi tasya sarvathābhāva eveṣyate na bandho na mokṣa iti 
bhrāntimātre'py asati sankleśābhāvād bandho'pi nāsti 
pūrvaṃ baddho mucyata iti kṛtvā muktir api na syāt 
atha vā kathaṃ na yathā prakhyāti tathā bhāveneṣyate sarvathā vā'bhāva iti parābhiprāyavyudāsārtham āha  tat kṣayān muktir iṣyate 
tasmiṃścāparikṣīṇe bandha ityarthād uktaṃ bhavati 
anyathā hi na bandho na mokṣa iti sankleśavyavadānāpavādadoṣaḥ syāt 
yathā grāhyagrāhakatvena bhrāntir udbhāsitā'pi yadi tathā syāt paramārthata evaṃ sati nityaḥ sankleśaḥ syāt 
tathā ca nirvāṇābhāvaḥ 
evaṃ ca bhrāntimātrasyāpy abhāve sankleśābhāvo nityañca vyavadānaṃ prasajyeta 
evaṃ cobhayathāpi mokṣārthināṃ vyartho yatnaḥ syāt 
ato'vaśyam abhūtaparikalpabhāvo'bhyupagantavyo dvayābhāvaś ca 
 sangrahalakṣaṇaṃ khyāpayatīti sangraha eva lakṣaṇaṃ 
atha vā yena sangraho lakṣyate tat sangrahalakṣaṇaṃ 
tac ca kim artham uktaṃ  atra hi grāhyagrāhakarahitam abhūtaparikalpamātramevāstīty ayuktaṃ 
sūtrāntareṣu punas trayaḥ svabhāvāḥ paṭhyante 
ataḥ sūtrāntarair avirodhapradarśanārthaṃ teṣām iha sangraha ucyate 
ata eva vṛttikāra āha  abhūtaparikalpamātre satīti vistareṇa  kalpitaḥ paratantraś ca pariniṣpanna eva ca 
arthād abhūtakalpāc ca dvayābhāvāc ca deśitaḥ 
iti 
grāhyaṃ grāhakaṃ ca svabhāvaśūnyatvād abhūtam apy astitvena parikalpyata iti  parikalpita ucyate 
sa punar dravyato'sannapi vyavahārato'stīti svabhāva ucyate 
paratantraḥ paravaśaḥ hetupratyayapratibaddhajanmakatvāt 
āha ca  akalpitaḥ pratyayaco'nabhilāpyaś ca sarvathā 
paratantrasvabhāvo hi śuddhalaukikagocaraḥ 
yā'bhūtaparikalpasya dvayarahitatā sa pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvaḥ tasyā'saṃskṛtatvāt nirvikāratvena pariniṣpannatvāt 
āha ca  kalpitena svabhāvena tasya yā'tyantaśūnyatā 
svabhāvaḥ pariniṣpanno 'vikalpajñānagocaraḥ 
arthād ityarthādhipatyād uktaṃ 
evam abhūtaparikalpād dvayābhāvācceti vaktavyaṃ 
arthaḥ parikalpitaḥ svabhāva ityartho'tra rūpādayaścakṣurādaya ātmā vijñaptayaś ca 
sa ca kalpitena svabhāvenābhūtaparikalpe nāstīty asan parikalpitaḥ svabhāva ucyate 
āha ca  akalpito vikalpo hi vikalpāntarakalpitaḥ 
svabhāvo nāstyasau tasya vikalpāntarakalpitaḥ 
abhūtaparikalpaḥ paratantraḥ svabhāva iti 
parair hetupratyayais tantryate janyate na tu svayambhavatīti paratantraḥ 
grāhyagrāhakābhāvaḥ pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāva iti 
nirvikārapariniṣpattyā'viparītapariniṣpattyā ca parniṣpannatvāt pariniṣpanna ucyate 
atra hy abhūtaparikalpasya dvayarahitatā grāhyagrāhakābhāva uktaḥ 
na tu dvayasyābhāvamātraṃ 
evañcābhūtaparikalpa eva hetupratyapāratantryāt paratantraḥ 
sa eva grāhyagrāhakarūpeṇa svātmany avidyamānena prakhyānāt parikalpitaḥ 
sa eva grāhyagrāhakarahitatvāt pariniṣpannaḥ 
evam abhūtaparikalpe trayaḥ svabhāvāḥ sangrahītāḥ 
etenā'bhūtaparikalpam anūdya parijñeyaṃ parijñāya prahātavyaṃ parijñāya sākṣāt kartavyañca vastu sandarśitaṃ bhavati 
  aparijñātāsal lakṣaṇo hy abhūtaparikalpaḥ kleśakarmajanmasankleśāya sampravartate 
ato'sallakṣaṇaparijñānārtham upāyaṃ pradarśayann āha  upalabdhiṃ samāśritya iti vistaraḥ 
abhūtaparikalpe tad upalakṣaṇam abhūtaparikalpo veti 
grāhyagrāhakayor asattvam evā'sallakṣaṇaṃ 
tatrānupraveśas tad avabodhaḥ 
tasyopāyo yatas tad asallakṣaṇam anupraviśati 
sa punar dharmadhātoḥ sarvatragārthapratibodhaprayoganiśraya viśeṣaḥ kuśalo dvividhaḥ 
tad upalakṣyā'yaṃ śloka uktaḥ 
vijñaptimātropalabdhiṃ niśrityā'rthā'nupalabdhir jāyata iti 
idaṃ vijñaptimātram ālambanārtharahitaṃ svabījaparipākād rūpādyābhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ pravartate na tu rūpādiko'rtho'stītyevaṃ grāhakopalabdhiṃ niśritya grāhyānupalabdhiṃ praviśati 
evaṃ hy anena vicārayitavyaṃ  utpadyamānam anutpannaṃ vā vijñānaṃ viṣayamālambeta 
tatrotpadyamānaṃ viṣayaṃ nālambate utpadyamānasyāsattvāt 
notpannam api viṣayapratibhāsātmanotpannatvāt 
na ca viṣayapratibhāsātmanotpattim uktvā vijñānasyānyā kriyā'sti yāṃ kriyāṃ kurvat vijñānaṃ viṣayam ālambana ity ucyate 
yadi vālambanasya vartamāna eva vijñāne vyāpāro notpadyamāne evam ālambanapratyayo na vijṇyānotpādakaḥ 
tat parikalpanaṃ nirarthakaṃ 
vartamānālambanagrahaṇe kṣaṇabhedadoṣo bhavati 
na cātmātiśayabhāve pūrvavad vijñānenālambanagrahaṇaṃ yujyate 
athālambanagrahaṇakāle tasyātmātiśaya iṣyate evam apy ātmātiśayasyānyata eva darśanād anyadevotpannam ālambanaṃ gṛhṇātīti prasajyate 
anyo manyate  nirudhyamāno'rtha evotpadyamānasya vijñānasyālambanapratyayaḥ 
sa ca svākārapratibhāsa jñānakāraṇatvena śeṣebhyaḥ pratyayebhyo viśiṣyata  iti 
tenāpi rūpādiparamāṇavastat samūho vālambanatvena parikalpyate 
ubhayathāpi cālambanābhāvaḥ 
sarvam eva hi vijñānaṃ ghaṭapaṭādipratibhāsam utpadyate na tu paramāṇupratibhāsaṃ 
na cā'rthākārasyā'nyanirbhāsasya vijñānasyānyad ālambanaṃ 
cakṣurādīnām apy ālambanatvaprasanga iti 
yo'pi manyate samuditāḥ paramāṇava ālambanaṃ na pratyekaṃ tasyāpy ayam aparihāraḥ 
samuditā api hi te pratyekam evālambanatveneṣYante na tat samudāyena 
tatra paramāṇūnāṃ pratyekapratibhāsaṃ jñānaṃ notpadyate nāpi tat samudāyapratibhāsaṃ 
tasmān na paramāṇūnām ālambanatvaṃ sambhavati 
nāpi paramāṇusamūha ālambanaṃ prajñaptisataḥ kāraṇatvāsambhavāt 
vijñānakāraṇaṃ hi samanantarādipratyayavad ālambanapratyayo'pīṣyate 
tasmān na nirudhyamāno'pyālambanaṃ 
atha ca niruddha ālambanaṃ evaṃ satyātītānāgataṃ viṣayaḥ syāt 
svapnādau tu vijñānam anālambanam iti siddhaṃ 
nā'nālambanaṃ svapnādivijñānaṃ nimittālambanatvād iti kecit 
nimittaṃ punar arthapratibimbaṃ viprayuktasaṃskārasvabhāvaṃ 
na hi svapnādāvasatyarthe tannimittaṃ yujyate mukhādyabhāve tat pratibimbavat 
utpadyamānam utpannaṃ vālambanaṃ vijñānanimittam abhāvān nirodhāc ceti pūrvam uktaṃ 
vijñānameva arthapratibhāsatvād arthapratibimbaṃ 
ato na viprayuktasaṃskārātmakaṃ nimittaṃ yujyate 
avaśyaṃ cārthākāraṃ vijñānam abhyupagantavyaṃ 
anākāre hi tasmin grāhyagrāhakaniyama eva na syāt 
anyastvapratighaṃ rūpameva svapne yogināṃ cāśubhādāvālambanaṃ manyate 
tasyāpi varṇasaṃsthānādyātmakatvād apratighatvaṃ manomātraviṣayatvañca virudhyate 
na cāvijñaptimātrād anyad apratighaṃ rūpaṃ śāstre varṇyate 
tasmāt kalpanāmātram eva 
aparastv anubhūtārtham eva svapne vijñānaviṣayatvenecchati jātyandhena svapne nīlādirūpāgrahaṇāt 
na jātyandhaḥ svapne rūpaṃ na gṛhṇāti 
avyutpannasanketatvāt tu nāmato na jānāty ato nānyasyācaṣṭe 
yadi cānubhūtasyaiva svapne darśanam evaṃ jātyandhasyāpi rūpadarśanaṃ kiṃ neṣyate  tenāpi pūrvajanmasu rūpam upalabdham eva 
na ca  vartamānajanmany upalabdham eva svapne pratibhāsate 
na hy atītānāgatavartamānānubhave suptasya jāgrataś ca kaścid viśeṣo'sti 
tasmāt parikalpamātram evaitad anubhūtārthaviṣayaṃ svapne vijñānam iti 
 atītasya cābhāvān nirviṣayaṃ vijñānam eva svapne'rthābhāsam utpadyata iti niścayaḥ 
evaṃ vijñaptimātratvenopalambhād arthā'nupalabdhir bhāvyeti 
ya arthā'nupalabdhiṃ niścitya vijṇaptimātrasyāpyanupalabdhirjāyata iti
yatha na vijṇyanād bahiḥ parikalpitaṃ grāhyamastīti vijñaptimātratābalena manogrāhyābhāvaṃ praviśati tathā grāhyabhāvabalena vijñaptimātrasyāpy abhāvaṃ pratipadyate 
na grāhyābhāve grāhakatvaṃ yujyate 
grāhyam apekṣya tad grāhakasya vyavasthāpanāt 
evam asallakṣaṇaṃ grāhyagrāhakayoḥ parikalpitarūpayoḥ praviśati nābhūtaparikalpasyeti darśanaṃ bhavati 
kim arthaṃ punaḥ prathamata eva vijñaptimātrasyaivābhāvaṃ na vibhāvayati  grāhyapratibaddhatvāddhi grāhakasyopalabhyārthābhāve sukhaṃ praveśaḥ syād ālambanasvabhāvavināśāt 
anyathā bhāvāpavādam eva kuryāt 
grāhyagrāhakayoḥ parasparanirapekṣatvāt 
imāñca grāhyagrāhakavikalpātītāṃ jñānabhūmiṃ saṃbhāreṣu nirantaraṃ pravartamānaḥ prathamakalpāsaṃkhyeyaparisamāptau praviṣati 
tathā hi vijñaptimātram idaṃ niśritya rūpānupalambhānukūlo lokottaramārge prathama uṣmagatākhyaḥ saparivāraḥ samādhirāmukhī bhavati 
tasyānantaraṃ mūrdhākhyaḥ 
tasyānantaram aśeṣagrāhyānupalambhād grāhakānupalabhānukūlaḥ kṣāntyākhyaḥ samādhiḥ 
tasyānantaram arthānupalabdhiṃ niśritya vijñaptimātrasyāpy anupalabdhiṃ bhāvayan laukikāgryadharmākhyaḥ prajñādisahitaḥ saparivāraḥ samādhir āmukhībhavati 
tad anantaraṃ darśanamārgaḥ 
tatraiva ca sarvatragadharmadhātvadhigamāt prathamāṃ bhūmiṃ praviśatīti 
ayaṃ ca tattvamanaskāro nāvimuktimanaskāro'pramāṇādivat 
 upalabdhir upalabdhitvenā'siddhā 
abhūtārthapratibhāsatayā tūpalabdhir ityucyate'nupalabdhisvabhāvā'pi satī 
  upalabdher anupalabdhisvabhāvatvam iti pradarśayann āha  upalabdhes tataḥ siddhā nopalabdhisvabhāvatā 
iti 
atha vā yat pūrvaṃ pratijñātam abhūtaparikalpe dvayaṃ nāstīti tad anenākāreṇa pratyātmavedyatvāt siddham iti pradarśayann āha  upalabdhes tataḥ siddhā nopalabhisvabhāvatā 
iti 
tata iti  upalabhyārthābhāve upālabdhyabhāvāt 
upalabdhir iti bhāvakartṛkaraṇānām anyatamat parikalpyate 
etat tritayam apy abhāvān na yujyate 
upalabdhes tataḥ siddhā nopalabdhisvabhāvatā 
ata eva vṛttikāra āha  upalabhyārthābhāva upalabdhyayogād iti 
tasmāc ca samatā jñeyā nopalambhopalambhayoḥ 
yasmād upalabdhir anupalabdhisvabhāvā tasmāt samatā tulyatā jñeyā 
arthānupalambhasya vijñaptimātratopalambhasya cāsattvād aviśeṣataḥ 
upalabdhyanupalabdhiśabdayoḥ parasparaviruddhatvāpanaya nārthamāha  abhūtārthapratibhāsatayā tūpalabdhir ity ucyate 
na tu tayā kiñcid upalabhyte'rthābhāvād iti 
ataḥ paramārthato 'nupalabdhisvabhāvā'pi satīti nāsti virodhaḥ 
apara āha  yaś ca bālānām asatyārthe'rthopalambho yaścāryāṇām arthānupalambhas tayor dvayos tulyalakṣaṇatvāt samatā jñeyā sarpabhrānty anupalabdhivat 
ata eva bravīti  abhūtārthapratibhāsatayā tūpalabdhir ity ucyate'nupalabdhisvabhāvā'pi satīti sarpabhrānty anupalabdhivyapadeśavad iti 
anyaḥ punar āha  yaś ca bālānāṃ grāhakopalambho yaścāryāṇām arthābhāvād grāhakānupalambhas tayor dvayor upalambhānupalambhayor ubahyato'pi samatā jñeyā grāhye'sati grāhakābhāvāviśeṣāt 
ata evāha  abhūtārthapratibhāsatayeti vistaraḥ 
kecitu manyante samāropā'pavādapratipakṣeṇāha  tasmāc ca samtā jñeyā nopalambhopalambhayoḥ 
iti 
arthābhāvād upalabdher upalabdhisvarūpatvenā'bhāvāt svarūpeṇa tad abhāva ucyate 
upalambha upalabdhisvabhāvo nāpanīyate nāpyanupalabdhisvabhāvaḥ prakṣipyate 
kiṃ tarhi samam etad ubhayaṃ nirvikalpatayā 
tasmānnopalambhopalambhayoḥ samāropāpavādanirapekṣeṇa pratyātmasamatā jñeyeti 
āha ca  nāpaneyam ataḥ kiñcit prakṣeptavyaṃ na kiñcana 
draṣṭavyaṃ bhūtato bhūtaṃ bhūtadarśī vimucyate 
  yadyevaṃ kathaṃ vijñaptir upalabdhir ity ucyate 
abhūtārthapratibhāsatayā loke śāstre ca tathā pratītatvād anupalabdhisvabhāvā'pi satīti 
prabhedalakṣaṇaṃ khyāpayati kāmarūpārūpyadhātvātmakamabhūtaparikalpasya prabhedo nānāprakāratā 
prabheda eva lakṣaṇamiti prabhedalakṣaṇam anena prabhedenā'bhūtaparikalpasya lakṣaṇāt 
prabhedalakṣaṇañca kimarthaṃ khyāpyate abhūtaparikalpamātre kāmarūpadhātvorayogāt 
yo'yaṃ dhātubhāvena vipakṣapratipakṣabhedādāryapudgalādibhedaḥ sa na prāpnotīti mahān śāsanopaplavaḥ prasajyata ityāśankyudāsārthaṃ prabhedalakṣaṇamākhyātam 
atha vā yatra vitarkavicāraustastatraivā'bhūtaparikalpo'sti na tvanyatreti yo manyate tadapanayanārthaṃ prabhedalakṣaṇamucyate 
abhūtaparikalpastu cittacaittāstridhātukāḥ 
na tu yatraiva vitarkavicārāviti 
yathā rūpaṃ bhūtāni bhautikañca evamabhūtaparikalpo'pi cittaṃ caittāś ca na kevalaṃ cittameva 
te ca tridhātukasvabhāvāḥ 
kāmarūpākhyāvacarabhedena tridhātukaḥ 
tatra ye tasmād abhūtaparikalpānnarakādyākārā viṃśatiprakārāḥ pravartante sa kāmadhātuḥ 
ye saptadaśaprakārā brāhkamāyikādyākārāste rūpadhātuḥ 
ya ākāśānantyāyatanādyākārāścatuḥprakārāste ārūpyadhātuḥ 
anyaḥ punarāha  aprahīṇakāmarāgā avibhūtārūpyasaṃjñāś ca kāmāvacaraḥ kāmadhātuḥ 
prahīṇakāmarāgā avibhūtārūpyasaṃjñāś ca rūpāvacaro rūpadhātuḥ 
prahīṇakāmarūparāgā vibhūtā rūpyasaṃjñāścārūpyāvacara ārūpyadhātuḥ 
kāmarāgānuśayitāḥ kāmadhātuḥ 
rūparāgānuśayitā rūpadhātuḥ 
ārūpyarāgānuśayitā ārūpyadhāturityanye 
  satatacikṣepakakścaitasikaduḥkhaprakārāḥ kāmadhātuḥ 
samāhitā vigatacaitasikaduḥkhaprakārā rūpadhātuḥ 
samāhitāḥ prahīṇamukhaduḥkhaprakārā ārūpadhāturityapare 
aprahīṇagandharasatadvijñānābnhāsāḥ kāmadhātuḥ 
prahīṇagandharasatadvijñānābhāsā rūpadhātuḥ 
prahīṇapañcadaśadhātvābhāsā ārūpyadhāturityapare 
teṣu sarveṣu vyākhyāneṣu katame ta ityavaśyaṃ pūrvavyākhyānoktā eva vaktavyā iti sākānkṣāṇyevaitāni vyākhyānāni 
abhūtaparikalpādhikāre punarabhūtaparikalpagrahaṇamanupalabdhyantaritatvād iti 
paryāyalakṣaṇañceti 
cittacaittānāṃ prabhedaṃ khyāpayitvā'bhūtaparikalpasya paryāyalakṣaṇaṃ khyāpayati 
kathaṃ kṛtvā  abhūparikalpyavastunaḥ svabhāvaviśeṣaparikalpanayā cittacaittānāṃ pravṛttatvāt 
arthasvarūpaviśeṣadṛṣṭiścittacaittā abhūtaparikalpaśceti paryāyāntarbhūtāḥ 
tatrārthamātre dṛṣṭir vijñānam iti 
mātraśabdo viśeṣanirāsārthaḥ 
tenāgṛhītaviśeṣā vastusvarūpamātropalabdhir ityarthaḥ 
arthaviśeṣe dṛṣṭiścaitasā vedanādaya iti 
tena tena viśeṣarūpeṇa tatrātipravṛtteḥ 
tatrāhlādakaparitāpakatvaviśeṣo yas tasya bhāvasya yat saumanasyādisthānaṃ tad grahaṇaṃ vedanā 
strīpuruṣādivyavahāralakṣaṇo yo'rthaviśeṣas tad grahaṇaṃ saṃjñā 
evam anye'pi yathāyogaṃ yojyāḥ 
evaṃ caiṣāmāśrayālambanakāladravyasamatābhiḥ samprayuktatvaṃ na tvākārasamatayāpi vijñānāviśeṣaprasangāt 
cittaviśeṣā eva caitasā ihābhipretā iti kecijjānanti 
tedeva vijñānaṃ tādṛśasvarūpādinā vicitrapratibhāsam utpadyate mayūracandrikavat 
katham ekaṃ vicitrañca  naikaṃ hi lakṣaṇaṃ loke vicitram iṣyate 
mā bhūd ekam anekasvabhāvam iti syād eṣa  doṣo yadi dharmasvabhāvaḥ syāt 
bhrāntimātre tu naiṣa doṣaḥ 
kva tathā sarvathā bhāvāt iti vacanāt 
naitad evaṃ sūtravacanavirodhāt 
yā vedanā yā saṃjñā yac cittaṃ yad vijñānañca saṃsṛṣṭvā amī dharmā na visaṃsṛṣṭā iti 
saṃsargaś ca nāma satāṃ yugapac ca bhavatīti 
yo hi dharmasvabhāvam apariniṣpannam icchati tasyaitat sūtram asminnarthe'jñāpakam iti 
 abhūtaparikalpamātre'nyasya cābhāve hetuphalaprabhedaṃ na vijñāyata iti tat pratipādanārthaṃ pravṛttilakṣaṇañca khyāpayati 
anena hetuphalabhāvenā'bhūtaparikalpa iti lakṣaṇaṃ 
pravṛttir eva lakṣaṇaṃ pravṛttilakṣaṇaṃ 
pravṛttiḥ punar divdhā  kṣaṇaparamparāpravṛttir yadādipatyena pratyutpanna upabhogasankleśaḥ janmāntarapravṛttiś ca yadādhipatyenāyatyāṃ kleśakarmajanmasankleśaḥ 
iha kṣaṇaparamparāpravṛttiḥ pravṛttilakṣaṇam uktaṃ 
janmāntarapravṛttiṃ sankleśalakṣaṇatvena khyāpayiṣyati 
ekaṃ pratyayavijñānaṃ iti vistaraḥ 
tatraikam ityālayavijñānaṃ śeṣāṇāṃ saptānāṃ vijñānānāṃ hetupratyayabhāvena hetur iti pratyayavijñānaṃ 
dvitīyam aupabhogikaṃ 
iti 
vijñānam ity anuvartate 
tat phalam iti vākyaśeṣaḥ 
tat punaḥ saptavidhaṃ pravṛttivijñānam upabhogaprayojakatvād aupabhogikaṃ 
upabhogaparicchedaprerakās tatra caitasāḥ 
iti 
tatra vijñāne ye caitasās te'pi tat phalam iti sambandhaḥ 
vijñānatvād ekayogakṣematvāc ca 
ālayavijñānam anyeṣāṃ vijñānānāṃ pratyayatvāt pratyayavijñānam iti 
ālīyante sarve sāsravā dharmās tatra phalabhāvena tac ca teṣu hetubhāvenetyālayaḥ 
  sattvabhājanalokavijñāanāt tannirbhāsatayā vijñānaṃ 
tac caikāntavipākatvād avyākṛtaṃ 
sarveṣāṃ sāsravāṇāṃ dharmāṇāṃ bījam anubadhnāti anyeṣāñca pravṛttivijñānānāṃ hetupratyayo bhavatīti pratyayavijñānaṃ 
tat pratyayaṃ pravṛttijñānamoupabhogikam iti 
tasmād ālayavijñānāt pratyetīti tat pratyayam utpadyata ityarthaḥ 
katham utpadyate  pravṛttivijñānaṃ hy ālayavijñānāt pravartamānam anutpannasya taj jātīyasya pravṛttivijñānasyotpādakaṃ bījam ālayavijñāne paripuṣṇāti 
tasmāt paripuṣṭabījāt pariṇāmaviśeṣaprāptāt punas taj jātīyaṃ pravṛttivijñānam utpadyata ityevaṃ tat pratyayaṃ pravṛttivijñānaṃ bhavati 
nanv ālayavijñānam apy aupabhogikaṃ pravṛttivijñānañca pratyayavijñānaṃ prasajyate aduḥkhāsukhavedanopabhogāśrayatvāt ālayavijñāne ca vāsanābhāvanāt 
na pratyayabhāvavyatirekeṇānyā vāsanābhāvanā'sti 
yathoktam abhidharmasūtragāthāyāṃ  sarvadharmā hi ālīnā vijñāne teṣu tat tathā 
anyonyaṃ phalabhāvena hetubhāvena sarvadā 
iti 
na prasajyate tad vedanāyā durupalakṣYatvāt 
na tadaupabhogikatvena lakṣyate pravṛttivijñānavat 
prakarṣagataṃ vā jñeyaṃ sūryavat 
tathā hy upabhogatrividhavedanāśrayatvaṃ pravṛttivijñānasyaiva na tvālayavijñānasyeti 
hetupratyayaścātra vivakṣito na pratyayamātraṃ 
tathā hi kuśalākuśaladharmādhipatyād ālayavijñānaṃ vipākaniṣyandaphalavāsanāṃ parigṛhṇāti 
avyākṛtadharmādhipatyāc ca niṣyandaphalavāsanām eveti 
ata ālayavijñānaṃ niravaśeṣāṇāṃ sāsravadharmāṇāṃ hetupratyayaḥ 
pravṛttivijñānaṃ tu ālayavijñānasyādhipatipratyaya iti nāsti pravṛttivijñānasya pratyayatvaprasangaḥ 
upabhogo vedaneti 
triprakārāpy upabhukṣyata ity upabhogaḥ anubhūyata ity arthaḥ 
bhavarasasārasarūpā vedanā 
tasmā bālās tat saṃvedanārthaṃ viṣayam abhiniviśante 
na kevalaṃ vedanā arthopalabdhir apy upabhoga ityanye 
tac ca na upabhogo vedaneti bhāṣyavirodhāt 
arthopalabdhiś ca na vijñānād anyeti na tasyāścaitasatvaṃ prayujyate 
veditaparicchedaḥ saṃjñā sukhādiviśeṣodgrahaṇātmakatvāt 
upabhoge saṃjñāyāñ ca prerakāḥ saṃskārā vijñānasya cetanāmanaskārādayaḥ 
  atha vā 
upabhogo vedaneti yathāsvamālambanānubhāvāt sukhādivedanīyakarmānubhavanāc ca 
evaṃ viṣayakarmaṇor upabhuktir vedanety upabhogaḥ 
viṣayacihnaṃ vyavahāranimittaṃ paricchinnaṃ karotīti paricchedaḥ saṃjñā 
vijñānāntarālambana ābhogaḥ saṃskārāḥ 
tataścetanādyādhipatyād vijñānam ālambanānantaraṃ bhajate 
ādiśabdena chandhādayo gṛhyante 
uktaṃ yato yādṛśo yad arthā ca pravṛttir iti 
 tatra chādanād avidyayā yathābhūtadarśanāvabandhanāt 
ropaṇāt saṃskārair vijñāne karmavāsanāyāḥ pratiṣṭhāpanāt 
nayanād vijñānenopapattisthānasaṃprāpaṇāt 
samparigrahaṇān nāmarūpeṇātmabhāvasya 
pūraṇāt ṣaḍāyatanena 
triparicchedāt sparśena 
upabhogād vedanayā 
karṣaṇāt tṛṣṇayā karmākṣiptasya punar bhavasya 
nibandhanād upādānair vijñānasyotpatyanukūleṣu kāmādiṣu 
ābhimukhyād bhavena kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ puarnbhave vipākadānāyābhimukhīkaraṇāt 
duḥKhanā jantyā jarāmaraṇena ca parikliśyate jagat 
sankleśalakṣaṇañca khyāpayatīti kleśakarmajanmasankleśā yathā pravartamānā jagataḥ parikleśāya bhavanti tat sankleśalakṣaṇaṃ 
tathācā'satyapyātmaninabhūtaparikalpamātrāt saṃsāraḥ prajāyate iti pradarśanāthaṃ khyāpyate 
chādanādropaṇāc caiva nayanāt samparigrahāt 
iti vistaraḥ 
so'yaṃ pravṛttipakṣamadhi dvādaśāngaḥ pratītyasamutpādo darśitaḥ 
tatra chādanāt 
kliśyate jagad ityantavacanaṃ sarveṇa sambadhyate 
kena chādanāt kathaṃ vā chādanāt kliśyata iti  ata āha  avidyayā yathābhūtadarśanavibandhād iti 
avidyayā hy adarśanātmakatvād bhūtadarśanaviṣaye pracchādite bhūtadarśanaṃ notpadyate'to bhūtadarśanotpattivibandhanād avidyā bhūtadarśanavibandhaḥ 
bhūtadarśanaṃ punaḥ prādhānyena lokottaraprajñā tat pṛṣṭhodbhavatvāt tat pṛṣṭhalābhāt tad avagamāc ca tat prayoga iti śrutacintābhāvanāmayī bhūtadarśanam ity ucyate 
bhūtadarśanavibandhād avidyā saṃskārāṇāṃ pratyaya ityevaṃ chādanād avidyayā kliśyate jagad iti 
  ropaṇāt kliśyate jagad iti sambadhyate 
kena ropaṇāt kva kasya vetyata āha saṃskārair vijñāne karmavāsanāyā iti 
tatra saṃskārā yat kāyikaṃ karma vācikaṃ mānasaṃ ca puṇyāpuṇyāniñjyasvarūpaṃ tat punar bhavam abhisaṃskarotīti saṃskāraḥ 
apraṇihitaṃ rohayatītyarthaḥ 
tadeva ca saṃskāraśabdenocyate na tu sarvaṃ 
taccābidyādhipatyāt punar bhavam ākṣeptuṃ samarthaṃ bhavati na sattāmātreṇetyavidyāpratyayāḥ saṃskārā ity ucyate 
tathāhi tāny anutpannavidyasya punarbhavaṃ saṃskurvanti notpannavidyasya 
na cādhipatyamātreṇaivāvidyā saṃskārāṇāṃ pratyaya ucyate sāmānyena sā samutthānapratyayopi 
avidhyā hi samprayuktvādhyathā sarvakleṣānāṃ sāmānyena samutyānapratyayastayā tatsamuttyā nāṃ cetanānām api 
api saṃskārāṇāṃ bhavabhogabhedaprārthanānvayānāṃ samutthāne tat sahabhūtā'vidyā sāmānyapratyayaḥ 
āniñjyānām api tad bhūminiḥsaranadṛṣṭisamutthānānāṃ tat sahabhūtā'vidyā sāmānyapratyaya iti saṃskārāṇāṃ pratyaya uktaḥ 
vijñāna iti atrālayavijñānam abhipretaṃ na tu pravṛttivijñānaṃ 
vyuparatapravṛttivijñānasyotpattisthānanayanā'sambhavāt kuśalakliṣṭayoś ca samavadhānābhāvāt saṃskārais tatra karmavāsanāyāḥ pratiṣṭhāpanābhāvāt 
karmavāsanāyā iti 
kā punar iyaṃ karmavāsanā nāma  anāgatasya janmano bījaṃ hetubhāvaḥ 
tad yathā brīhiphalaṃ bhūmibhasmapurīṣādipratyayaviśeṣam apekṣya pariṇamad ankurotpattau hetubhūtaṃ bījam iti 
pratiṣṭhāpanād iti ropaṇam eva paryāyāntareṇācaṣṭe 
pratiṣṭhāpanaṃ punaratra vijñānasantāne tat prathamatas tad bījasyāpy āyanaṃ 
nahi kasyacit sāsravasya dharmasyānāsravasyevāpūrvaṃ bījam ādhīyate 
evaṃ saṃskārair vijñāne punarbhāvabījādhānāj jagat kliśyate 
nayanāj jagat kliśyata iti 
kena nayanāt kva kasya veti na vijñāyata ityāha vijñānenotpatti sthānasaṃpreṣaṇād iti 
karmaparibhāvitena vijñānena santānavṛttyā cyutisthānād upapattisthāne punar bhavabījabhūtāyā vāsanāyāḥ prāpaṇaṃ nayanaṃ 
tathā ca sati na pratisandhivijñānaṃ saṃskārapratyayaṃ pūrvakālabhavavijñānam eva  saṃskārapratyayam iti pradarśitaṃ bhavati 
nahi vinaṣṭāt kāraṇāt kāryotpattir yujyate 
ārūpyasamāpatīlābhino hi yatraiva cyavante tatraivotpadyanta iti katham ārūpyeṣūpapattisthānaprāpaṇam iti tad yathāyogaṃ veditavyaṃ nāmarūpavat 
samparigrahāj jagat kliśyata iti 
kena samparigrahāt kasya vetyata āha  nāmarūpeṇātmabhāvasyeti 
nāmarūpaṃ hi pañcaskandhāḥ 
te ca pratisaṇdhim upādāya kalalārbudapeśīghanapraśākhāvasthā anutpannaṣaḍāyatanā vijñānapratyayaṃ nāmarūpam iti 
tad bhāvitaviśeṣeṇa hy anatareṣu nikāyasabhāgeṣu tad viśiṣṭatvaṃ sidhyati 
tasmiṃścotpanne manuṣyatiryagādinikāyasabhāgabedād ātmabhāvo bhidyata iti nāmarūpeṇātmabhāvaḥ parigṛhīta ity ucyate 
atha vā''maraṇāt sarvam evātmabhāvaṃ parigṛhṇāti tat prathamataḥ sarvasya hetubhāvena vyavasthānād iti 
atha vā'bhinne'pi nāmarūpeṇāti tat prathamataḥ sarvasya hetubhāvena vyavasthānād iti 
atha vā'bhinne'pi nāmarūpeṇātmabhāvo yathā parigṛhyeta tat pṛthaktvena darśayati yathā sarvaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ pañcabhiḥ skandhaiḥ sangṛhītam iti 
aupapādukānāṃ tu vijñānapratyayaṃ ṣaḍāyatanam evetyato vijñānapratyayaṃ nāmarūpaṃ yathāsambhavaṃ veditavyaṃ 
pūraṇāt kliśyata iti 
kena pūraṇāt kasya veti 
ṣaḍāyatanena 
nāmarūpasangṛhītaṃ śarīraṃ 
nāmarūpāvasthāyāṃ hi śarīram aparipūrṇam ucyate cakṣurādy āyatanābhāvāt 
asti ca tasyām avasthāyāṃ kāyāyatanaṃ manāayatanañca tad apy aparipūrṇam eva āśritāśrayaparipūryabhāvāt 
ṣaḍāyatanāvasthāyāṃ punaścakṣurādyabhinirvṛtta āśritaḥ paripūrṇo bhavati 
kāyāyatanaṃ ca paripūrṇaṃ bhavati taccakṣūr ādyāśritānāṃ paripūrṇatvāt 
kathaṃ tac cakṣurādi āśritaṃ  tat pratibaddhavṛttitvāt 
manāayatanam api ṣaḍvijñānasangṛhītaṃ tadānīṃ niravaśeṣāśrayaparipūritāt paripūrṇaṃ bhavati 
angapratyangaparipūritāś ca ṣaḍāyatanāvasthāyām eva 
āśrayaparipūraṇāt ṣaḍāyatanena kliśyate jagad iti veditavyaṃ 
triparicchedāj jagat kliśyata iti sambadhyate 
trayāṇāṃ hīndriyaviṣayavijñānasannipāte indriyasya sukhādivedanotpattyanukūlo yastriprakāro vikāras tat paricchedaḥ sparśaḥ 
ata evāyam indriyavikārasādṛśyaṃ spṛśati tadākāratayeti sparśa ucyate 
  atha vā ṣaḍāyatanapratyayaḥ sparśa indriyasya sukhādivedanānukūlaṃ trividhaṃ vikāraṃ prasūte 
upabhogād vedanayeti 
vedanā hi tṛṣṇayopabhujyate āsvādyata ity arthaḥ 
puṇyādikarmopabhogād vā vedanopabhogaḥ 
atha vopabhogo'tra vedanāyā anubhavaḥ 
sukhādiṣucānubhūyamāneṣu tatra sukhādiparipoṣaṇād anurāgapratighamohaiḥ kliśyate jagat 
karṣaṇād iti 
karṣaṇāt kena kasya veti na vijñāyata ity ata āha tṛṣṇayā karmākṣiptasya punar bhavasyeti 
saṃskārair vijñāne bījaparipoṣaṇenākṣiptasya punar bhavasyodaka kalpayā tṛṣṇayā sarvagatiṣv aviśeṣeṇātmabhāvābhilāṣayā yadārdrīkṛtaḥ puar bhava utpattāv upayunkte utpattiṃ cāvasthāpayati tat karṣaṇaṃ 
nibandhanāt 
kena nibandhanāt kva kasya veti praśnāvakāśe svayam evāha upādānair vijñānasyopapattyanukūleṣu kāmādiṣv iti 
chandarāgalakṣaṇaiścaturbhir upādānair karmākṣiptaṃ vijñānam utpattyanukūleṣu kāmadṛṣṭiśīlavratātmavādeṣu nibadhnāti avasthāpayati ca vijñānaṃ hi cchandarāgavaśāt tatra vartate 
ābhimukhyādity atrāpi parapraśnāvakāśe svayamevaha bhavena kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ punar bhava vipākadānāyābhimukhīkaraṇād iti 
yathānibandhanaṃ vijñānasya pūrvakṛtaṃ karma paunarbhavikaṃ vāsanāvasthaṃ vipākaphalaṃ prati vṛttilambhanād bhavaḥ sadbhūta ākṣiptabhavaś ca nirvṛttaye'bhimukhībhavati evaṃ bhavenābhimukhīkaraṇāj jagat kliśyate 
duḥkhitāj jātyā jarāmaraṇena ca 
kiṃ  kliśyate jagad iti 
evaṃ bhavāt punarbhavābhinirvṛttau satyāmādita eva garbhādhāne śukraśoṇite vijñānasammūrcchanāt kliśyate 
tathā māturāmāśayapakvāśayayor antarāle parivartanāt kliśyate 
tathā ca mātubhojanacaryayoḥ sankaṭaghunoraparityāgād api kliśyate 
tathā sambhādhe  nāśucinā mārgeṇa nirgacchati 
kliśyate jagaj jātaṃ punar jarayā khālityapālityādilakṣaṇayā maraṇena ca nāmarūpabhedalakṣaṇena priyābhyāṃ yauvanajīvitābhyāṃ bhraśyamānaṃ 
kliśyate jagad iti 
gacchatīti jagat 
sabhāgāvakāśāt kṣaṇāvakāśaṃ  gacchatīty arthaḥ 
kliśYata iti jātijarāvyādhimaraṇādibhis traidhātuke kṣaṇaparamparayā''javañjavībhāvena ca pīḍyata ityarthaḥ 
kliśyata iti na vyavadāyata ity apare 
evam ayaṃ sankleśalakṣaṇo dvādaśāngaḥ pratītyasamutpādaśchādanādyekādaśabhir arthair vyavadānavipakṣaḥ 
avidyādy utpattikramaḥ pūrvapūrvasyottarottarāvāhanāt 
 tredhā sankleśaḥ  kleśasaṃkleśaḥ karmasankleśaḥ janmasankleśaśca 
tatra kleśasankleśo'vidyātṛṣṇopādānāni 
karmasankleśaḥ saṃskārā bhavaś ca 
janmasaṃkleśaḥ śeṣāṇyangāni 
dvedhā saṃkleśaḥ  hetusaṃkleśaḥ phalasaṃkleśaś ca 
tatra hetusaṃkleśaḥ kleśakarmasvabhāvair angaiḥ 
phalasaṃkleśaś ca śeṣaiḥ 
saptadhā saṃkleśaḥ saptavidho hetuḥ viparyāsahetuḥ ākṣepahetuḥ upanayahetuḥ parigrahahetuḥ upabhogahetuḥ ākarṣaṇahetuḥ udvegahetuś ca  
tatra viparyāsahetur avidyā 
ākṣepahetuḥ saṃskārāḥ 
upanayahetur vijñānaṃ 
parigrahahetur nāmarūpaṣaḍāyatane 
upabhogahetuḥ sparśavedane 
ākarṣaṇahetus tṛṣṇopādānabhavāḥ 
udvegahetur jātijarāmaraṇe 
sacaścaiṣa saṃkleśo'bhūtaparikalpāt pravartata iti 
katividhaḥ punar anena dvādaśāngena na pratītyasamutpādena samāsataḥ saṃkleśaḥ pradarśita ityata evedam ucyate so'yaṃ dvādaśāngaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ  tredhā dvedhā ca saṃkleśaḥ saptadhā iti 
ca śabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ parivartārthaś ca 
kleśa eva saṃkleśa iti kleśasaṃkleśaḥ 
evaṃ karmajanmasaṃkleśau 
kleśo hi pravartamānaḥ svaparātmanor vyābādhakatvāt saṃkleśaḥ 
yathoktaṃ sūtre'pi  rakto rāgaparīta ātmavyābādhāyāpi cetayate paravyābādhāyā'pi cetayate 
ubhayavyābādāyāpi cetayate 
evaṃ dveṣo mohaścāpi veditavya iti 
karmajanmasaṃkleśayoścotpādakatvāt saṃkleśaḥ 
tathā hi kleśādhipatyena karma janmākṣipati dṛṣṭasatyasya satyapi karmaṇi punar bhavākṣepābhāvāt kleśasamudācāreṇa punar bhavabījasya bhavīkaraṇāt kliṣṭacittasya ca punarbhavapratisandhibandhāj janma sankleśenaiva hetunā 
tato'rhataḥ pratisandhibandhābhāvaḥ kliṣṭacittābhāvāt 
karma ca śubhāśubhaṃ tadātve kāyacittayor āyāsanimittatvād āyatyāñca vipākadānāt sankleśaḥ 
janmā'pi sarvopadravāspadatvāt sankleśa iti 
tredhā sankleśaḥ 
hetordvidhā bhedāt 
kleśasankleśo vidyātṛṣṇopādānānīti tritayam api kleśātmakatvāt 
karmasankleśaḥ saṃskārā bhavaśceti  dvayam api karmātmakatvāt 
ayantu viśeṣaḥ  svarūpāvasthaṃ karma saṃskārāḥ bījāvasthaṃ bhava iti 
janmasaṃkleśaḥ śeṣāṇyangānīti vijñānanāmarūpaṣaḍāyatanasparśavedanājātijarāmaraṇāni eṣāṃ janmasangṛhītatvāt 
dvedhā saṃkleśo hetuphalābhyāṃ prabhidyate 
hetusaṃkleśaḥ kleśakarmasvabhāvair angaiḥ 
phalasaṃkleśaś ca śeṣair angair iti 
tatra hetusaṃkleśatvaṃ karmakleśānāṃ vijñānādivedanāparyantaṃ jātyātmakaṃ jarāmaraṇādīnavajanma sampādayitum abhipravṛttatvāt 
phalasaṃkleśaś ca śeṣair vijñānādibhiḥ karmakleśaphalatvāt 
punaḥ sa eva pratītyasamutpādaḥ saptadhā saṃkleśa iti viparyāsākṣepopanayaparigrahopabhogākarṣaṇodvegahetutvāt saptavidho hetuḥ 
tatra viparyāsahetur avidyeti 
avidyāgato hi tattvasammohād anityādīn nityādirūpeṇa viparyasyatīti 
ākṣepahetuḥ saṃskārā iti vijñāne caturangātmajanmabījasya pratiṣṭhāpanāt 
upanayahetur vijñānam itīha cyutasyopapattiviṣaYa upanayanāt 
parigrahahetur nāmarūpaṣaḍāyatana ity upanītasya nāmarūpaṣaḍāyatanābhyāṃ nikāyasabhāgaparigrahāt 
pūrvaṃ nāmarūpeṇaiva parigraha ukto jarāyujādikāṃ yonim abhipretya idānīm upapādukam adhikṛtya ṣaḍāyatanenā'pi parigraha uktaḥ 
atha vā nāmarūpeṇa tat prathamata ātmabhāvamātrasya sangraho vivakṣitaḥ 
iha tv aparipūrṇasya paripūrṇasya ceti nāsti virodhaḥ 
upabhogahetuḥ sparśavedana iti 
sakāraṇenānubhavena kuśalākuśalakarmavipākasyopabhogāt 
ākarṣaṇahetus tṛṣṇopādānabhavā iti 
sa upabhuktakarmavipāko bālas tasyāṃ tasyāṃ vedanāyāṃ tṛṣyati 
vivṛddhatṛṣṇaś ca tat saṃyogatṛṣṇayā kāmādīn upādatte 
tad upādānāc cāsya pūrvabhūtaṃ paunarbhavikaṃ karma vāsanāvasthaṃ pariṇataṃ yathākṣiptavipākadānayā pravṛttiṃ labdhvā bhavo bhavati 
sa ca tṛṣṇopādānabhavaḥ saṃskārākṣiptaḥ punar bhavābhinirvṛttaya ākṛṣyate abhimukhīkriyata iti tṛṣṇopādānabhavā ākarṣaṇahetuḥ 
atha vā tṛṣṇāvaśena cchandarāgānurūpānyatarakarmavāsanābhimukhāt tṛṣṇopādānabhavā ākarṣaṇahetuḥ 
udvegahetur jātijarāmaraṇe ityevamatra jarmākarṣaṇāt tasmiṃstasmin sattvanikāye jātijarāmaraṇaduḥkham anyacca śokaparidevaduḥkhadaurmanasyopāyāsaduḥkham anantaprabhedam anubhavatīti 
  tatra tridhā sankleśā'bhidhānena kleśakarmaṇo janmanaḥ sādhāraṇāsādhāraṇahetutvaṃ darśitaṃ 
kleśo hi janmānkurasya sādhāraṇakāraṇaṃ bhūmyādivat 
karmatvasādhāraṇakāraṇaṃ ankurasyeva bījaṃ tad bhedena janambhedād iti 
atha vā nātra pūrvāntāparāntamadhyāntāni trīṇi kāṇḍāni kiṃ tarhi karmakleśaphalānīti pradarśayati
dvividhābhidhānena hetuphalamātram evedaṃ nātrānyaḥ sankliśyate kārako vedako veti pradarśayati 
atha vā'tra karmakleśamātram eva hetuḥ 
tayor bhāvābhāvāj janmabhāvābhāvadarśanāt 
atas tat phalam eva janma 
tasmānnātra hetuḥ phalaṃ vā sarvatra pañcaskandhikāvastheti pradarśayati 
saptadhāhetunirdeśena punar dvividhaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ pradarśitaḥ ākṣepalakṣaṇo'bhinirvṛttilakṣaṇaśceti 
tatrākṣepalakṣaṇaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ saptyabhir angair nirdiṣṭaḥ yenākṣīpyate yathākṣipyate yaccākṣipyate tat pradarśanāt 
abhinirvṛttilakṣaṇaḥ pañcabhir angaiḥ tasyākṣiptasya yenābhinirvṛttir yathābhinirvṛttir yā cābhinirvṛttiḥ tasyāñca ya ādīnava iti 
kenākṣīpyate  avidyāpratyayaiḥ saṃskāraiḥ yathā tattvaṃ mugdhvā viparītaṃ saṃjānāti kuśalākuśalāniñjyān saṃskārānabhisaṃskāroti 
katham ākṣipyate taiḥ saṃskāraiḥ  vijñāne bījapoṣaṇād utpattibhavyatāyām avasthāpanāt 
kim ākṣipyate  paunarbhavikaṃ nāmarūpaṃ ṣaḍāyatanaṃ sparśo vedanā ca yathāyogaṃ 
tadevam ākṣiptaṃ kenābhinirvartyate  yathoktakrameṇa pūrvākṣiptādihotpannāṃ vedanāṃ pratītya yā tṛṣṇotpannā tat pratyayenopādānena 
kathaṃ tenābhinirvartyate  tasya vijñāne vāsanāvasthasya karmaṇas tena bhavīkaraṇāt 
bahuvidhā hi vijñāne karmavāsanā vartate vicitrasaṃskāraparibhāvitatvāt 
upādānaviśeṣaparigraheṇa yenātra punar bhavatvaṃ vartate so'tra bhava ucyate 
kā punaḥ sa'bhinivruttiḥ  yā tasyākṣiptasya nāmarūpādiksyāyatyāṃ jātiḥ 
tasyaṃ punaḥ satyāṃ ka ādīnavaḥ  jarāmaraṇaṃ priyayauvanajīvitabhraṃśādīti 
atra tūpanayahetur nirarthaṃ iti cet na nirarthakaḥ 
vicchinnamaraṇād bhavopapattibhavapravṛttyadhigamanirākaraṇārthaṃ 
sarve caite sankleśā abhūtaparikalpāt pravartanta iti cittacaittāśrayatvāt sankleśasya 
uktaṃ hi tat  abhūtaparikalpaśca cittacaittās tridhātukāḥ 
iti 
  abhūtaparikalpapiṇḍārthaḥ piṇḍārthaḥ punar abhūtaparikalpasya navavidhaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ paridīpitaṃ bhavati 
sallakṣaṇaṃ asallākṣaṇaṃ svalakṣaṇaṃ sangrahalakṣaṇaṃ asallakṣaṇā'nupraveśopāyalakṣaṇaṃ prabhedalakṣaṇaṃ paryāyalakṣaṇaṃ pravṛttilakṣaṇaṃ saṃkleśalakṣaṇañca 
piṇḍārthaḥ punar abhūtaparikalpasyeti vistareṇārthanirdeśaḥ sukhāvabodhārthaṃ piṇḍārthanirdeśo'vismaraṇārthañca 
tato'trārthadvayam uktaṃ 
sallakṣaṇaṃ  abhūtaparikalpo'sti iti 
asallakṣaṇaṃ  dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate 
iti 
svalakṣaṇaṃ  arthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsaṃ prajāyate vijñānaṃ 
iti 
sangrahalakṣaṇaṃ  kalpitaḥ paratantraś ca pariniṣpanna eva ca 
iti 
asallakṣaṇānupraveśopāyalakṣaṇaṃ  upalabdhiṃ samāśritya nopalabdhiḥ prajāyate 
ityādi 
prabhedalakṣaṇaṃ  abhūtaparikalpaś ca cittacaittās tridhātukāḥ 
iti 
paryāyalakṣaṇaṃ  tarthārthadṛṣṭir vijñānaṃ tad viśeṣe tu caitasāḥ 
iti 
pravṛttilakṣaṇaṃ  ekaṃ pratyayavijñānaṃ dvitīyaṃ aupabhogikaṃ 
iti 
saṃkleśalakṣaṇaṃ  chādanād ropaṇāc caiva nayanāt samparigrahāt ityādi 
 evam abhūtaparikalpaṃ navaprakāraṃ khyāpayitvā yathā śūnyatā vijñeyā tan nirdeśatīti ko'trābhisambandhaḥ  dvayam anena pratijñātam abhūtaparikalpaḥ śūnyatā ca 
  saṃkleśapūrvakaṃ ca vyavadānaṃ 
dharmāvabodhāśrayañca dharmatāvadhāraṇam ityato'bhūtaparikalpanirdeśānantaraṃ yathā śūnyatā vijñeyā tathā nirdiśati  lakṣaṇañcā'tha paryāya iti vistaraḥ 
tatra lakṣaṇaṃ hi bhāvābhāvapratiṣedhātmatā sarvatra śūnyathāprabhedavyāpakatvāt 
nāmāntaraṃ paryāyaḥ 
paryāyānuguṇaṃ paryāyapravṛttinimittaṃ paryāyārthaḥ 
ākāśavad abhinnalakṣaṇatvān nirvikalpatve'py āgantukopakleśasaṃyogaviyogāvasthābhedād bhedaḥ 
anyaś ca pudgaladharmasamāropabhedād bhedaḥ ṣoḍaśavidhaḥ 
sādhanaṃ śūnyatāprabhedapradarśane yuktiḥ 
kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ yadebhiḥ prakāraiḥ śūnyatā vijñātavyā  viśuddhyālambanatvād viśuddhyarthibhir lakṣaṇato vijñeyā 
sūtrāntareṣu paryāyanirdeśeṣv asammohārthaṃ paryāyārthaḥ 
paryāyārthā'vabodhārthācchūnyatāyā viśuddhyālambanatvena niścitatvāt paryāyārthaḥ 
saṃkleśe nirākṛte sā viśuddheti tat saṃkleśaprahāṇāya yatnotpādanārthaṃ bhedataḥ 
bheda sādhanāvabodhād vikārābhāve saty api bhedaṃ sukhaṃ pratipadyata iti bhedasādhanato'pi vijñeyeti 
 pṛthaktve sati dharmād anyā dharmateti na yujyate anityatāduḥkhatāvat 
ekatve sati viśuddhyālambanaṃ jñānaṃ na syāt sāmānyalakṣaṇañca 
etena tattvā'nyatvavinirmuktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ paridīpitaṃ bhavati 
kathaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ vijñeyam iti lakṣaṇaṃ hi prāg uddiṣṭam ityatas tadeva prathamataḥ pṛṣṭaṃ  dvayā'bhāvo hy abhāvasya bhāvaḥ śūnyasya lakṣaṇaṃ 
  iti vijñeyaṃ 
dvayasya grāhyasya grāhakasya cā'bhūtaparikalpe'bhūtaparikalpena vā parikalpitātmakatvād vasturūpeṇā'bhāvaḥ 
tasya ca dvayābhāvasya yo bhāva etac chūnyatāyā lakṣaṇaṃ 
kārikānuguṇyāc cātra bhāvapratyayaluptanirdeśo draṣṭavyaḥ 
abhāvasya bhāva iti kim etat  abhāvasyātmatvam astitvaṃ 
anyathā dvayabhāvasyāstitvam eva syāt 
tad bhāvasya bhāvato'vidyamānatvāt 
ata evāha  ity abhāvasvabhāvalakṣaṇatvaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ paridīpitaṃ bhavati na bhāvarūpalakṣaṇam iti 
bhāvapratiṣedhavācakatvād abhāvaśabdasya bhāvaśabdābhāve'pyeṣo'rthovagamyata iti bhāvaśabdo'trādhikaḥ nādhikaḥ dvayābhāvaḥ śūnyatālakṣaṇam itīyati nirdiśyamāne dvayābhāvasya svātantryam evātra gamyate śaśaviṣāṇābhāvavat na duḥkhatādivad dharmatārūpatā 
tasmādevam ucyate dvayābhāvaḥ śūnyatā 
tasya cā'bhāvasyā'bhūtaparikalpe bhāvaḥ śūnyate'ty ucyate 
abhāvasya bhāvalakṣaṇaparigṛhītatvād dharmatārūpatā pradarśitā 
atha vā dvayābhāvaḥ śūnyatety abhāvaśabdasya sāmānyavācitān na vijñāyate katamo'trābhāvo'bhipreta ity atyantā'bhāvapradarśanārtham ucyate  abhūtaparikalpe dvayābhāvasya bhāva iti 
na hi prāg abhāvapradhvaṃsābhāvau svopadānād anyatrākhyātuṃ yujyete 
anyonyābhāvasvya caikāśratvaṃ na yujyate ubhayāśritatvāt 
tasmād bhāvasyābhāvalakṣaṇopādānād grāhyagrāhakayor atyantābhāva eva śūnyatetyetaj jñāpitaṃ bhavati 
yady abhāvātmikā śūnyatā kathaṃ paramārtha ucyate  paramajñānaviṣayatvād anityatāvat na tu vastutvāt 
api cābhāvasvabhāvo naiṣaḥ 
yasmādyaśvā'sau tad abhāvasvabhāvaḥ sa  na bhāvo nā'pi cā'bhāvaḥ 
kathaṃ na bhāvaḥ  yasmād dvayasyā'bhāvaḥ 
bhāvatve hi na dvayabhāvasyātyantābhāvaḥ syāt nā'bhūtaparikalpadharmatā 
kathaṃ nābhāvaḥ  yasmād dvayābhāvasya bhāvaḥ 
nahi dvayābhāvo dvayābhāvasvarūpeṇābhāvaḥ 
so'bhāvaśced dvayasyāstitvaṃ syān na ca syād abhūtaparikalpasya dharmatā yathā nityaduḥkhatā 
sattvasya viparyāsatvena samāropitasya nityasukhabhāvābhāvasvarūpatvān na bhāvo nāpy abhāva ity ucyate 
yadi punar abhūtaparikalpasya śūnyatā dharmatāsti kim asau tasmād anyo vaktavya utānanya ity ato bravīti  etac ca śūnyatāyā lakṣaṇam iti 
abhāvasya svarūpam eva 
  athavā bhāva evābhāvapratiṣedhātmakaḥ 
tasmād abhūtaparikalpāt  na pṛthaktvaikalakṣaṇaṃ 
pṛthaktve sati dharmād anyā dharmateti na yujyate 
kaḥ punar ayogaḥ  dharmād vibhinnalakṣaṇatvād dharmatā dharmāntaram eva bhavati tad anyadharmavat 
na ca dharmāntaraṃ dharmāntarasya dharmatā bhavitum arhati tatra punar dharmāntaram anveṣṭavyam ity anavasthāprasangāt 
anityatāduḥkhatāvad iti 
yathā'nityatā'nityebhyo nānyā duḥkhatā ca duḥkhād eva śūnyatā'pi na śūnyād anyeti 
ekatve sati viśuddhyālambanaṃ na syāt sāmānyalakṣaṇañceti 
viśuddhyate'neneti viśuddhir mārgaḥ dharmasvalakṣaṇād ananyatvān mārgālambanaṃ na syāt dharmasvalakṣaṇavat 
tasmāc ca na sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ yujyate 
svalakṣaṇād ananyatvāt 
tasyāpi dharmasvarūpavat parasparato bheda iti sāmānyatā hīyate 
atha vā svalakṣaṇasya tasmād anyatvād bhāvasvarūpavad bhedābhāvaḥ 
tataś ca sāmānyalakṣaṇasyāpy abhāvaḥ bhedāpekṣatvāt sāmānyalakṣaṇasya 
atha vā viśuddhyartham ālambanaṃ viśuddhyālambanaṃ na bhāvasvalakṣaṇam ālambyamānaṃ viśuddhim āvahati sarvasattvaviśuddhiprasangāt 
yadyanyānanyatvenāvaktavyā kathaṃ nirgranthavādo nā'lambito bhavati  yo hi bhāvasya satastattvānyatvena vyākaroti tena nirgranthavād ālambyate 
śūnyatā tu na bhāva iti nāstyayaṃ doṣaḥ 
etena śūnyatā sallakṣanā'bhāvasvarūpalakṣaṇā'dvayalakṣaṇā tattvānyatva vinirmuktalakṣaṇā ca paridīpitā 
uktaṃ śūnyatālakṣaṇaṃ 
 paryāya idānīm ucyate  tathatā bhūtakoṭiścā'nimittaṃ paramārthatā 
dharmadhātuś ca paryāyāḥ śūnyatāyāḥ samāsataḥ 
iti 
paryāyo nāmaikasyārthasya bhinnaśabdaiḥ pratyāyanaṃ paryāyārthābhidhānam iti paryāya ucyate 
tānyabhidhānāni sūtrāntareṣu śūnyataiva nirdiśyante 
etac ca paryāyapañcakaṃ yathāpradhānaṃ gāthāyām uktam evam anye'pi paryāyā ihānuktāḥ pravacanād upadhāryāḥ 
  tad yathā  advayatā avikalpadhātuḥ dharmatā anabhilapyatā anirodhaḥ asaṃskṛtaṃ nirvāṇādi 
 kathaṃ paryāyārtho vijñeya ityetad darśayati 
naite śabdā gauṇāḥ kiṃ tarhi anvarthā iti  ananyathā'viparyāsatan nirodhāryagocaraiḥ 
hetutvāccāryadharmāṇāṃ paryāyārtho yathākramaṃ 
iti 
ananyathā'rthena tathateti avikārārthenetyarthaḥ 
tadeva pradarśanārtham āha nityaṃ tathaiveti kṛtvā 
nityaṃ sarvadā'saṃskṛtatvān na vikriyata ityarthaḥ 
aviparyāsārthena bhūtakoṭiḥ 
bhūtaṃ satyam aviparītam ityarthaḥ 
koṭiḥ paryanto yataḥ pareṇānyajjñeyaṃ nāstītyato bhūtakoṭir bhūtaparyanta ucyate 
kathaṃ tathatā jñeyam ucyate  jñeyāvaraṇaviśodhanajñānagocaratvāt 
aviparyāsārthentyanadhyāropānapavādārthena 
atraiva kāraṇam āha  viparyāsā'vastutvād iti 
viparyāso hi vikalpaḥ 
vikalpā'nālambanatvān na viparyāsavastu 
nimittanirodhārthenā'nimittam iti 
atrā'nimittatvaṃ nimittanirodha ucyate 
etad eva pradarśanārtham āha  sarvanimittābhāvād iti 
sarvair eva saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtanimittaiḥ śūnyatā śūnyety animittam ucyate 
sarvanimittā'bhāvād animittaḥ 
animittam evā'nimittaḥ 
āryajñānagocaratvāt paramārtha iti paramaṃ hi lokottarajñānaṃ 
tad arthaḥ paramārthaḥ 
etad eva pradarśayann āha  paramajñānagocaratvād iti 
āryadharmahetutvād dharmadhātuḥ 
dharmaśabdenātrāryadharmāḥ samyag dṛṣṭyādayaḥ samyag vimuktijñānaparyantāśceti 
taddhetutvād dhātuḥ 
tadeva vibhāvayann āha  āryadharmāṇāṃ tad ālambanaprabhatvād iti 
svalakṣaṇopādāyarūpadhāraṇe'py ayaṃ dhātuśabdo vartata ity āha hetvartho hy atra dhātvarthaḥ 
tadyathā  suvarṇadhātus tāmradhātū raupyadhātuḥ 
sūtrāntareṣv anye paryāyā uktā apyanenaiva nyāyena svārthe nirdeṣṭavyāḥ 
 śūnyatāyā grāhyagrāhakābhāvarūpatvād bhedam asambhāvayan pṛcchati athavā paryāyārthānantaraṃ bhedo vijñeya ity uktam atas tannirdeśānantaraṃ pṛcchati  kathaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ prabhedo vijñeya iti 
abhūtaparikalpo hi saṃkleśaḥ tasya prahāṇaṃ viśuddhir ucyate 
sankleśaviśuddhikāle ca śūnyatāvyatiriktam anyan nāsti yat sankliśyate viśuddhyate vā 
tasmāt saṃkleśaviśuddhikālayoḥ śūnyataiva sankliśyate viśuddhyate ceti pradarśanārtham āha  sankliṣṭā ca viśuddhā ca ity asyāḥ prabhedaḥ 
kadā sankliṣṭā kadā nirmaletyanavabodhāt pṛcchati  kasyām avasthāyāṃ saṃkliṣṭā kasyāṃ ca viśuddheti  samalā nirmalā ca sā 
iti vistaraḥ 
āśrayā'parāvṛttiparāvṛttyapekṣayā samalā ca prahīṇamalā ca vyavasthāpyate 
yeṣām aviduṣāṃ grāhyagrāhakā'bhiniveśarāgādikleśamalinānāṃ cittasantānānām apratipattivipratipattidoṣācchūnyatā na prakhyāti tān prati samalā  vyavasthāpyate 
yeṣām āryāṇāṃ tattvajñānād aviparītacetasāṃ śūnyatā nirantaram ākāśavad virajaskā prakhyāti tān prati prahīṇamaletyucyate 
evaṃ śūnyatāyā āpekṣikā saṃkleśaviśuddhir draṣṭavyā na malinasvarūpatvena prakṛtyā prabhāsvaratvāt 
yadi samalā bhūtveti vistaraḥ 
na hy avasthābhedo vikāram antareṇa dṛṣṭaḥ 
vikāraścotpādavināśābhyām anusyūta iti 
ata āha  kathaṃ vikāradharmiṇītvādanityā na bhavatīti 
na hi sankliṣṭāvasthātaḥ śūnyatāviśuddhā'vasthāyām anyo vikāraḥ 
tattvastititā tu svabhāvāntaram anāpadyamānāyā āgantukamalāpagamāt 
yasmād  abdhātukanakākāśaśuddhivac chuddhir iṣyate 
tasmād anityā na bhavatīti 
yathaiva hy abdhātukanakākāśānām atatsvabhāvatvān malasvabhāvatā'bhāve'pyāgantukamalavattvaṃ 
āgantukamalā'pagame ca te viśuddhā eva svabhāvāntarapratipattimantareṇāpi 
evaṃ śūnyatāpy āgantukamalaiḥ sankliśyate avikṛtasvarūpāpi tad vigamāc ca viśuddhyatīti 
yo hi tameva bhāvaṃ pūrvaṃ sankleśalakṣaṇaṃ paścād viśuddhisvabhāvaṃ vyavasthāpayati tasya vikāradharmanivṛttir na bhavati vikārasvabhāvatvāt na tu yatrāpy āgantukaṃ tad ubhayaṃ 
tasmān nāsau vikāradharmatāṃ spṛśatīti 
  prabhedanirdeśādhikāre sarve śūnyatāprabhedā vaktavyā ityata āha ayam aparaḥ prabheda iti 
ṣoḍaśavidhā śūnyateti vastubhedena ṣoḍaśavidhā bhavati 
dvayābhāvasvarūpe tu bhedo nāsti 
sā ṣoḍaśavidhā śūnyatā prajñāpāramitāyāṃ paṭhyate  adhyātmaśūnyatā yāvad abhāvasvabhāvaśūnyateti 
saiṣā samāsato veditavyā  bhoktṛbhojanatad dehapratiṣṭhāvastuśūnyatā 
ityevam ādi 
sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ sarvadharmasyā'dvayasvarūpatvaṃ 
nānyathā tan nānātvaṃ śakyate darśayitum ityato vastunānātvena tan nānātvaṃ darśayati 
pūrvaṃ tāvad bhoktā vibhāvayitavyaḥ tat snehābhiniveśatyājanārthaṃ 
tat snehābhiniveśo hi buddhatvavimokṣaprāptipratibandhako bhavati 
tad anantaraṃ tad bhojanaṃ 
tad anantaraṃ tayor adhiṣṭhānaṃ śarīraṃ 
tad anantaraṃ tad adhiṣṭhānasya śarīrasya pratiṣṭhābhājanaloko vibhāvayitavyaḥ bhoktur upakārakatvād ātmīyasnehagrāhavyāvartanārthaṃ 
etac catur vidhaṃ vastu tac chūnyatā vastuśūnyatety ucyate 
tatra bhoktṛśūnyatā ādhyātmikānyāyatanāny ārabhyeti 
tāni ca cakṣūrādīni yāvan manaḥ paryantāni 
tad anyasya bhoktur abhāvāt 
cakṣūrādīnāñca viṣayopabhogapravṛttidarśanāl lokasya cakṣurādiṣt eva bhoktṛbhimāna ity ataścakṣūrādyāyatanaśūnyatā bhoktṛśūnyatety ucyate 
bhojanaśūnyatā bāhyānīti rūpādīni yāvat dharmaparyantāni 
tāni viṣayābhāvena bhujyanta iti bhojanam ato bāhyāyatanaśūnyatā bhojanaśūnyatety ucyate 
  tayor bhoktṛbhojanayoḥ śarīre parasparā'vinibhāgenā'vasthānāt tad dehaḥ śarīram ityatas tacchūnyatā'dhyātmabahirdhāśūnyatety ucyate 
pratiṣṭhāvastu bhājanalokaḥ sarvatra sattvānāṃ pratiṣṭhāvastutvena prajānāt 
ata evāha  tasya vistīrṇatvāt tacchūnyatā mahāśūnyatocyate iti 
vastuśabdaḥ pratyekam abhisambadhyate 
tasyaivaṃ yogino bodhisattvasya caturvidhajñeyavastuśūnyatāyāṃ savitarkeṇa yoniśomanaskāreṇa manaskriyamāṇāyām ayamanyo nimittagrāha upatiṣṭhate yenedaṃ śūnyatājñānenādhyātmikabāhyāyatanādi śūnyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tatra yo grāhyagrāhakābhiniśeśo'yam eva cātra paramārthākāro yathā tac chrutājñānena dṛṣṭam iti vikalpaḥ 
tasya dviprakārasya yogibhūmibhrāntinimittasya vikalpasya vibhāvanārthaṃ śūnyta śūnyata paramārtha śūnyatā ca yathākramaṃ jñanakāralopaṃ kṛutvā nirdiṣṭā 
śūnyathāviṣayatvād vā taj jñānaṃ śūnyatety uktaṃ 
tasya grāhyagrāhakabhāvena śūnyatā śūnyatāśūnyatā 
ādhyātmikāayatanādikaṃ ca tena śūnyatājñānena yathā dṛṣṭaṃ so'tra paramārtha iti paramārthākāreṇa tasya śūnyatā paramārthaśūnyatā 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  paramārtho hi śūnyaḥ parikalpitena svabhāveneti 
ayam anyo'pi nimittagrāhaḥ śūnyatābhāvanopaplavabhūtaḥ yadarthaṃ bodhisattvaḥ śūnyatāṃ pratipadyate tasya bhāvasvarūpatvaṃ samāropayati tad vibhāvanārthaṃ saṃskṛtaśūnyatādayaḥ sarvadharmaśūnyatāparyantāḥ śūnyatā nirdiṣṭāḥ 
  kim arthañca pratipadyate  śubhadvayasya prāptyarthaṃ yāvad buddhadharmāṇāṃ viśūddhyarthaṃ śūnyatāṃ pratipadyate śūnyatāṃ prabhāvayatītyarthaḥ 
śubhadvayaṃ hi saṃskṛtam asaṃskṛtañca mārgo nirvāṇañca 
tābhyāṃ sambadhyate yathākramaṃ saṃskṛtaśūnyatā'saṃskṛtaśūnyatā ca 
sadāsattvahitāya ca 
iti sarvākāraṃ sarvakālañca mayā sattvahitaṃ kartavyam iti tac chūnyatā'tyantaśūnyatā 
saṃsārā'tyajanārthañca iti sattvārthaṃ mayā saṃsāro na parityajyaḥ 
saṃsāre hi parityakte'labdhvā bodhisattvabodhi śrāvakabodhau vyavatiṣṭhate 
tasya śūnyatā anavarāgraśūnyatā 
kim arthaṃ punas tasya śūnyatā deśyata ity ata āha  anavarāgrasya hi saṃsārasya śūnyatām apaśYan khinnaḥ saṃsāraṃ parityajeteti 
kuśalasyā'kṣayāya ca 
iti 
mayā kuśalamūlāni na kṣīyante nirupādhiśeṣe nirvāṇe'pīti nāvakiratītyetad evācaṣṭe notsṛjatīti 
yadyevaṃ kathaṃ tarhi nirupadhiśeṣo nirvāṇadhātuḥ siddhyati  sāsravadharmavipākakāyābhāvāt 
anāsravabhūtadharmakāyasya tu buddhasya bhagavato nirupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātāv api na vyuparamād iti siddhāntaḥ 
atas tac chūnyatā anavakāraśunyatety ucyate 
  gotrasya ca viśuddhyarthaṃ tasya śūnyatā prakṛtiśūnyatā 
atraiva kāraṇamāha  gotraṃ hi prakṛtir iti 
kuta etat 
ata āha  svābhāvikatvād iti 
svabhāvikam anādikālikam anāgantukam ityarthaḥ 
yathā'nādau saṃsāre kiṇcic cetanaṃ kiñcid acetanam evam ihāpi kiñcit ṣaḍāyatanaṃ buddhagotraṃ kiñcic chrāvakādigotram iti 
na cākasmikatvaṃ gotrasya anādiparamparāgatatvāt cetanācetanaviśeṣavad iti 
sarvasattvasya tathāgatagotratvād atra gotram iti tathātvaṃ jñeyam ity anye 
lakṣaṇavyañjanāptaye 
ity ataḥ sānuvyañjanānāṃ mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇānāṃ śūnyatā lakṣaṇaśūnyatety ucyate 
kiñca  śuddhaye buddhadharmāṇāṃ bodhisattvaḥ prapadyate 
ante prapadyata ity abhidhānāt sarvatra śubhadvayasya prāptyarthaṃ bodhisattvaḥ prapadyate 
sadā sattvahitāya ca bodhisattvaḥ prapadyata iti yojyaṃ 
katareṣāṃ buddhadharmāṇām ity ato bravīti balavaiśāradyāveṇikādīnām iti 
saṃkṣepataḥ sarvabuddhadharmāṇāṃ prāptaye mayā prayatitavyam iti pratipadyate 
tasmā chūnyatāvibhāvanayā sarvadharmaśūnyatocyate 
kīdṛśī vibhāvaneti  jñeye jñānasyāvyāvahitapravṛttiḥ 
evaṃ tāvac caturdaśānānām adhyātmaśūnyatādīnāṃ sarvadharmaśūnyatāparyantānāṃ vyavasthānaṃ veditavyaṃ 
  kā punar atra bhoktrādau śūnyatā katamat svarūpam ityata āha  pudgalasyā'tha dharmāṇām abhāvaḥ śūnyatā'tra hi 
tad abhāvasya sadbhāvastasmin sā śūnyatā'aparā 
iti 
tatra yathoktānāṃ bhoktrādīnāṃ pudgaladharmā'bhāvaś ca śūnyatā 
tad abhāvasya ca sadbhāvaḥ śūnyatā 
tatra pudgaladharmayor asadbhāvo'bhāvaśūnyatā 
tad abhāvasya sadbhāvo'bhāvasvabhāvaśūnyatā 
kim arthaṃ punar eṣā dvividhā śūnyatā'nte vyavasthāpyate  ata āha  śūnyatālakṣaṇakhyāpanārtham iti 
kim arthaṃ punaḥ śūnyatākhyāpanamata āha  pudgaladharmasamāropasya tac chūnyatā'pavādasya ca parihārārthaṃ yathākramaṃ 
pudgaladharmasamāropasya parihārārtham abhāvaśūnyatāṃ vyavasthāpayati 
tac chūnyatā'pavādaparihārārthañcā'bhāvasvabhāvaśūnyatāṃ 
yady abhāvaśūnyatā nocyeta parikalpitasvarūpayor dharmapudgalayor astitvam eva prasajyeta 
yady abhāvasvabhāvaśūnyatā nocyeta śūnyatāyā abhāva eva prasajyeta 
tad abhāvāc ca pudgaladharmayoḥ pūrvavad bhāvaḥ syāt 
tatrādhyātmikeṣvāyataneṣu vipākavijñānasvabhāveṣu bālānāṃ bhoktṛsammateṣu bhoktṛpudgalasya kalpitalakṣaṇānāṃ ca cakṣurādīnām abhāvas tad abhāvasya ca sadbhāvo'dhyātmaśūnyatā 
bāhyeṣv āyataneṣu rūpādivijñapty ābhāsasvabhāveṣu bālānāṃ bhogyasammateṣu bhojanasyātmīyasya parikalpitalakṣaṇānāṃ ca rūpādīnām abhāvas tad abhāvasya ca sadbhāvo bahirdhāśūnyatā 
tad dehe śarīre bhoktṛpudgalasya bālajanaparikalpitānāṃ rūpādīnāṃ dehasya cā'bhāvas tad abhāvasya ca bhāvo'dhyātmabahirdhā śūnyatā 
bhājanaloke sattvalokā'bhāvas tat parikalpitasvarūpābhāvas tad abhāvas tad abhāvasadbhāvaś ca mahāśūnyatā 
śūnyatājñāne paramārthakāre ca jñātur ākāragrahītṛpudgalasya parikalpitalakṣaṇaśunyatā paramārthākārasya cā'bhāvas tad abhāvas tad abhāvasya ca sadbhāvo yathākramaṃ śūnyatāśūnyatā paramārthaśūnyatā ca 
yad arthaṃ bodhisattvaḥ pratipadyate teṣu saṃskṛtādiṣu sarvabuddhadharmaparyanteṣu  bodhisattvapratipattavyeṣu pudgalasya parikalpitalakṣaṇānāṃ ca dharmāṇām abhāvas tad abhāvasya ca sadbhāvo yathākramaṃ saṃskṛtaśūnyatā yāvat sarvadharmaśūnyateti 
tathāhi nāsti saṃskṛtasya svāmī vā prayoktā vā pudgalo nāpi saṃskṛtaṃ bālajanaparikalpitenātmanā 
saṃkṣepataḥ sarvavikalpagrāhapratipakṣārthaṃ sarvasūtrāntābhisandhivyākaraṇārthaṃ caitā bodhisattvānāṃ śrāvakair asādhāraṇāḥ ṣoḍaśaśūnyatā nirdiṣṭāḥ 
atra ca bhagavatā śūnyatāviṣayaḥ śūnyatāsvabhāvaḥ śūnyatābhāvanāprayojanañca darśitaṃ 
tatra śūnyatāviṣayo bhoktrādyartho yāvat buddhadharmaparyantaḥ 
tat pradarśanaṃ punaḥ śūnyatāyāḥ sarvadharmavyāpakatvajñāpanārthaṃ 
śūnyatāsvabhāvo'bhāvasvabhāvo'bhāvabhāvasvabhāvaś ca 
śūnyatāsvabhāvapradarśanaṃ punar adhyāropāpavādapartipakṣeṇa sarvadṛṣṭiniḥsaraṇātmakatvajñāpanārthaṃ 
śūnyatābhāvanāprayojanaṃ śubhadvayasya paraptyartham ityārabhya buddhadharmāṇāṃ prāptaya iti paryantaṃ 
tat pradarśanaṃ punaḥ svaparātmano rūpadharmakāyasampat prakarṣaḥ śūnyatābhāvanād eva prāpya iti pradarśanārtham iti 
evaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ prabhedo vijñeya iti samalāvasthāyāṃ saṃkliṣṭā nirmalāvasthāyāṃ viśuddhety adhyātmaśūnyatādiṣoḍaśaprakārabhedo'nantarokto veditavyaḥ 
 bhedoddeśānantaraṃ tat sādhanam uddiṣṭam ityatas tannirdeśānantaraṃ pṛcchati  kathaṃ sādhanaṃ vijñeyam iti 
atra kiṃ sādhyate  āgantukopakleśasaṃkliṣṭatā svabhāvaviśuddhatā ca 
tatra saṃkliṣṭāsādham adhikṛtyāha  saṃkliṣṭā ced bhaven nā'sau muktāssyuḥ sarvadehinaḥ 
  iti 
muktiḥ saṃkleśaprahāṇaṃ 
tat saṃkleśaprahāṇāñca mārgabhāvanātaḥ 
tatra yadi dharmāṇāṃ śūnyatā āgantukair upakleśair anutpanne'pi pratipakṣe apiśabdād utpanna iva na saṃkliṣṭā bhaved evaṃ sati saṃkleśābhāvād ayatnata eva muktāḥ sarvasattvā bhaveyuḥ 
atyatnata eveti pratipakṣam antareṇaiva 
na tu pratipakṣam antareṇa prāṇinām asti mokṣa ity avaśyaṃ pṛthag janāvasthāyāṃ tathātāyām āgantukair malaiḥ saṃkliṣṭatā'bhyupagantavyeti 
evaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ saṃkliṣṭaḥ prabhedaḥ sādhito bhavati 
idānīṃ viśuddhiprabhedaṃ sādhayann āha  viśuddhā ced bhavennā'sau vyāyāmo niṣphalo bhavet 
iti 
dehinām iti sambadhyate 
athotpanne'pi pratipakṣe apiśabdhād anutpanna iva na viśuddhā bhaved evaṃ sati mokṣārtha ārambho niṣphalo bhavet pratipakṣabhāvanayāpi tanmalasyā'vigamāt samalasya vimokṣānupapatteś ca 
na tu mokṣārtha ārambho niṣpahal iṣyate 
tasmād avaśyaṃ pratipakṣābhyāsād āgantukopakleśavigamāc chūnyatāyā viśuddhirabhyupagantavyeti 
evaṃ śūnyatāyā viśūddhiprabhedaḥ sādhito bhavati 
atra saṃkleśadharmopādānāt saṃkleśo viśuddhi dharmagrahaṇād viśuddhiḥ 
na tu śūnyatāyā sākṣāt saṃkleśo viśuddhir veṣyate dharmaparatantratvādharmatāyāḥ 
ata evāḥ muktāḥ syuḥ sarvadehinaḥ 
iti 
ata hi dehina iti tadupādānamevoktaṃ 
anyathā vā yadi śūnyatāyāḥ sākṣāt samkleṣo viṣuddadirvā bhavet tataḥ kaḥ sambandho dehibhir bhavedyena śūnyatāviśuddhiś ca dehināṃ viśuddhiḥ śūnyatāsaṃkleśaś ca saṃkleśa ucyate  
  yadā ca śūnyatā ca kliṣṭā pṛthagjanāvasthāyāṃ śuddhā cāryāvasthāyāṃ bhavati ata evedaṃ siddhaṃ bhavati  na kliṣṭā nāpi cā'kliṣṭā śuddhā'śuddhā na caiva sā 
iti 
kathaṃ na kliṣṭā nā'pi cā'śuddhā 
śuddhaiva dvayaśuddhyā prakṛtagamakatvāt 
atraivāgamam āha prakṛtyaiva  prabhāvasvaratvāc cittasya iti 
atra ca cittadharmataiva cittaśabdenoktā cittasyaivaṃ lakṣaṇatvāt 
kathaṃ nā'kliṣṭā na viśuddhā kiṃ tarhi kliṣṭaiveti pratiṣedhadvayātpratipādayati 
sā  kleśasyāgantukatvataḥ 
kliṣṭā na tu prakṛtyeti darśayati 
sā cāgantukair upakleśair upakliśyata ity atrāpy āgamaḥ 
sankliṣṭaviśuddhatayā dvidhā bheda ukte kimarthaṃ punarścaturdhā bheda ucyate  laukikāl lokottarāc ca mārgād viśeṣārtham ityekaḥ 
laukiko hi mārgaḥ svabhūmikair malaiḥ kliṣṭo na tv adharaiḥ tat pratipakṣatvāt 
lokottaras tu mārgo mṛdumadhyādibhedād aśuddho 'nāsravatvāt śuddhaḥ 
naivaṃ śūnyateti 
na kliṣṭety uktvā punaścakṣurādibhyo viśeṣārtham ucyate nāśuddhetyanye cakṣurādayo hy anivṛttā'vyākṛtatvān na kliṣṭā na ca teṣāṃ sāravatvāt prakṛtiviśuddhir ity aśuddheti 
evaṃ na'pi sā kliṣṭeti cheduchyate  na ṣuddheti kuśalasāsravāt viśeṣaṇārthamāḥ 
kuśalasāsravaṃ hi saṃsāraparyāpannatvān nā'kliṣṭaṃ 
iṣtavipākatvāc ca śuddhaṃ naiva dharmatā 
sā hi kliṣṭā'vasthāyām aśuddhaiveti 
evaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ sankleśaviśuddhyoddiṣṭaḥ prabhedaḥ sādhito bhavati 
  śūnyatāpiṇḍdārthaḥ  śūnyatāpiṇḍdārtho lakṣaṇatāṃ vyavasthānataśceti veditavyaḥ 
tatra lakṣaṇato 'bhāvalakṣaṇato bhāvalakṣaṇataś ceti dvayābhāvo hītivacanād abhāvalakṣaṇataḥ abhāvasya ca bhāva iti vacanād bhāvalakṣaṇataḥ 
bhāvalakṣaṇataś ca na bhāvo nā'pi cā'bhāva iti vacanāt 
bhāvābhāvavinirmuktalakṣaṇatas tattvānyatva vinirmuktalakṣaṇaś ceti 
etac ca śūnyatāyā lakṣaṇaṃ 
tasmād abhūtaparikalpān na pṛthaktvaikalakṣaṇam iti vacanāt 
evaṃ lakṣaṇataḥ piṇḍārthaḥ 
kathaṃ vyavasthānataḥ piṇḍdārtho veditavya ityta āha  vyavasthānaṃ punaḥ paryāyādivyavasthānato veditavyaṃ 
paryāyatas tadarthas tadabhedas tat sādhanañcetyarthaḥ 
etayā catuḥprakāradeśanayā caturvidhopakleśapratipakṣeṇa svalakṣaṇaṃ karmalakṣaṇaṃ sankleśavyavadānalakṣaṇaṃ yuktilakṣaṇañcodbhāvitaṃ bhavati 
tatra svalakṣaṇaṃ vikalpasya pratipakṣeṇa tasya hi bhāvā'bhāvobhayapṛthaktvaikatvagrāhātmakatvatvāt 
karmalakṣaṇam anadhimuktānāṃ śūnyatālakṣaṇāśratyātrāsasya pratipakṣeṇa 
abhrāntitathatā karmā'viparyāsakarma sarvanimittaprahāṇakarma sarvalokottarajñānaviṣayatvā'vasthānakarma pratilabdhāryadharmahetubhāvakarma ca 
evaṃ śūnyatāsvarūpakarmaśravaṇena prāptagrahāṇāṃ kusīdināṃ kausīdyāpananārthaṃ prabhedalakṣaṇaṃ 
kathaṃ sā sankleśo bhavati vyavadānaṃ ceti saṃśayināṃ saṃśayāpanayanārthaṃ yukti lakṣaṇaṃ 
madhyāntavibhāgaśāstre lakṣaṇaparicchedasya prathamasya ṭīkā 
  āvaraṇaparicchedo dvitīyaḥ   tatra vyāpi kleśajñeyā''varaṇaṃ bodhisattvagotrakāṇāṃ sākalyāt 
prādeśikaṃ kleśā''varaṇaṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇāṃ 
udriktaṃ teṣām eva rāgādicaritānāṃ 
samaṃ samabhāgacaritānāṃ 
saṃsārā''dānatyāgā''varaṇaṃ bodhisattvagotrakāraṇaṃ apratiṣṭhitanirvāṇā''varaṇāt 
ity etad yathāyogam ubhayeṣām āvaraṇam ākhyātaṃ  bodhisattvagotrakāṇāṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇāñca 
lakṣaṇanirdeśānantaram nāvaraṇanirdeśā'vasaraḥ tadanantaramuddiṣṭatvādityāha  āvaraṇamadhikṛtyāha 
vyāpi prādeśikodriktasamādānavivarjanam 
dvayāvaranamākhyātam dvayāvaraṇam bodhisattvagotrakāṇāṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇāñcāvaraṇam 
āvaraṇīyārthabhedenāvaraṇasya bhinnatvaṃ pradarśayitum ayaṃ śloka ārabdhaḥ 
tatra vyāpi kleśajñeyāvaraṇaṃ bodhisattvagotrakāṇām iti 
vyāpnotīti vyāpi sakalārthāvaraṇāt 
sakalārtho hi svārthaḥ parārthaś ca 
athavā dvividhaṃ kleśaṃ jñeyaṃ cāvaraṇaṃ bodhisattvasya vyāpnotītyupacārād vyāpyucyate 
kleśa evāvaraṇamityāvaraṇasya kleśadharmatvena sārūpyādihopakleśo'pi kleśaśabdena gṛhyate 
anyathā navadhā kleśalakṣaṇaṃ 
  ityatrerṣyāmātsarye na gṛhyetām tayorupakleśatvāt 
jñeya evāvaraṇam iti jñeyāvaraṇam 
tena jñeyaprāvṛtatvāj jñānasya viṣaya eva nāsti 
jñāne vā jñeyāvaraṇaṃ jñeyasya jñānotpattipratibandhakatvād iti jñeyāvaraṇamityatra madhyamapadalopo draṣṭavyaḥ 
tailapātram iva 
tatpunarakliṣṭamajñātam 
bodhisattvagotrakāṇāṃ asvaparārthasampatprakarṣalābhāya buddhatvaprāptaye puṇyajñānasambhāraṃ sarvathā sarvatrā'nutiṣṭhatāṃ tad dvayam api pratibandhakabhūtam 
ityatastadāvaraṇaṃ vyavasthāpyate bodhisattvagotrakāṇām 
tatra vyāpi sarvaviṣayaṃ sakalaṃ sarvathā vyāpnoti 
kathaṃ sakalaṃ vyāpnotīti jñāyata iti cet  sākalyādāvaraṇaṃ vyāpītyucyate iti hetunirdeśāt 
atha vā vyāpiśabdo niravaśeṣārtha iti pradarśanāya sākalyādivacanam 
prādeśikaṃ kleśāvaraṇaṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇām iti svārthamātrāvaraṇādupacārādavyāpitvāc ca prādeśikākhyā 
kiṃ śrāvakapratyekabuddhānām akliṣṭamajñānaṃ nāsti yasmāt teṣāṃ kleśāvaraṇam eva vyavasthāpyata iti bhavatu na tu tadāvaraṇaṃ teṣām tasmin vidyamāne śrāvakapratyekabuddhabodhiprāpteḥ 
nanvajñānaṃ duḥkhādisatyaviṣaye jñānotpattipratibaṃdhakatvam eva śrāvakādīnām 
tatas teṣām api dvayāvaraṇaṃ bhavet 
tasmān na vaktavyaṃ kleśāvaraṇaṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇām iti 
naitadevam ajñānaṃ hi kleṣṭaṃ jñānapratipakṣabhūtaṃ saṃsāramūlaṃ ca kleśṣāvaraṇameveti vyavasthāpyate na tu jñeyāvaraṇaṃ saṃśaya iva 
yathā vimatir hi duḥkhādisatyaviṣaye vicikitsā kleśaścocyate na tu viṣayāntare 
viṣayāntare hi saṃśaya eva na kleśo na vicikitsā 
evavṃ duḥkhasatyādiviṣaye evā'jñānamavidyā kleśaścocyate na tu viṣayāntare 
viṣayāntare tvajñānam eva na cā'vidyā naiva kleśaḥ 
tasmāt tasya jñeyajñānamātrapravṛttāvāvaraṇatvāt tajñeyāvaraṇam ucyate na hi kleśakarmajanmanāmapi tāni cotpadyanta evāvidyāyā eva 
yadyevaṃ bodhisattvānām āvaraṇaṃ na vyavasthāpyate 
naitadevam bodhisattvānāṃ hi śrutasambhāraprabhāvitatvāt teṣāmāvaraṇaṃ jñeyāvaraṇam 
taduktam  āryho'pyagyūḥ pañca vidyāpadāni nārabhya syāt kadāpi sarvajñaḥ 
tato'nyeṣāṃ nigrahā'nugrahārthaṃ svajñānārthaṃ vā'rabhet tatra yatnam 
iti 
udṛktaṃ tu mṛdvapi rāgādivastu teṣām eva bodhisattvagotrakāṇāṃ rāvakādigotrakāṇañcā'dhimātramabhīkṣṇaṃ ca pravartitaṃ rāgādicaritānām āvaranam iti 
yeṣāṃ  mṛdāvapi viṣaye rāgādīnām anyatamat adhimātramabhīkṣṇyaṃ ca pravartate te rāgādicaritāḥ 
samaṃ punasteṣām eva bodhisattvagotrakāraṇaṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇāñcāvaraṇam 
samaṃ hi prakāradvittvābhāvāt 
samabhāgacaritānām āvaraṇam iti yeṣāṃ viṣayasādṛśye sāmīpye kleśa utpadyate na tvabhīkṣṇaṃ te samabhāgacaritāḥ 
saṃsārādānatyāgāvaranamityādi 
bhodisattvo hi kāruṇyādhipattyāt saṃsāramupādatte prajñādhipattyāc ca saṃsāradoṣaṃ yathābhūtaṃ dṛṣṭvā tyajati 
tataḥ kleśābhāve'pi sattvākicanāj janmaparigraho'pratiṣṭhataṃ nirvāṇam saṃsāranirvāṇayor dvayorapratiṣṭhitatvāt 
tadāvaraṇantu kleśābhibhūtena yathā saṃsāramupādāya yathābhūtadoṣādarśanāccā'kṛpayā parityajanam 
ajñānamihāvaraṇamucyate kṛpāprajñayoḥ pratibandhakatvādityanye 
athavā yathoktaṃ mahāratnakūṭe  sa āśayena nirvāṇe tiṣṭhati saṃsāre ca prayogeṇa tiṣṭhatīti 
etaddhi bodhisattvānām apratiṣṭhitaṃ nirvāṇam 
tatra nirvāṇapṛṣṭhībhāvād āśayaprayogābhyāṃ saṃsāramupādatte agotrasthasattva iva
