tathā ca saṃsārapṛṣṭhībhāvānnirvāṇagatābhyāmāśayaprayogābhyāṃ saṃsāraṃ tyajati śrāvakādigotrakā iva 
evaṃ saṃsārādānaṃ tatparityajanaṃ ca bodhisattvagotrakāṇāmapratiṣṭhitanirvāṇāvaraṇam saṃsāranirvāṇayorekāntapatitatvāt 
bodhisattvās tu tathāgatatvaprāptikāle kleśajñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇāt saṃsāre na tiṣṭhanti nirupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇe ca dharmakāyaprabandhān na tiṣṭhanti nirvāṇe śrāvakādivat 
tataḥ saṃsāranirvāṇayor ubhayhatrāpi na pratiṣṭhantīti 
atra bodhisattvasya śrāvakādīnāñca mārge teṣāṃ prayoge phale apratiṣṭhitanirvāṇaṃ ca pratibandhakatvādetāni pañcavidhānyāvaraṇānyākhyātāni 
ityetad yathāyogamiti yathāsambhavam 
tatra prathamamantyaṃ ca bodhisattvagotrakāṇām āvaraṇam 
prathamādavaraṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇām āvaraṇam 
itarad dvayaṃ punarubhayeṣām āvaraṇamākhyātam 
tatra ca jñeyāvaraṇaṃ bodhisattvānām āvaraṇam uktam 
taccā'kliṣṭamajñānam iti 
 nava saṃyojanāni kleśāvaraṇaṃ 
kasyaitāny āvaraṇaṃ 
anunayasaṃyojanaṃ saṃvegasyāvaraṇaṃ 
pratighasaṃyojanam upekṣāyāḥ tena hi  pratikūlam api pratighavastu upekṣituṃ na śaknoti 
śeṣāṇi tattvadarśanasyāvaraṇaṃ 
kathaṃ kṛtvā 
tāni hi yathākramaṃ 
saṃkleśasya parijñāne saṃyojanānyāvaraṇaṃ bhavanti 
mānaṃ saṃyojanaṃ hi satkāyadṛṣṭiparijñāne bahvaty āvaraṇaṃ abhisamayakāle sāntaravyantarā'smimānasamudācāravaśena tad aprahāṇāt 
avidyāsaṃyojanaṃ satkāyadṛṣṭivastuparijñāne tenopādānaskandhā'parijñānāt 
dṛṣṭisaṃyojanaṃ nirodhasatyaparijñāne satkāyā'ntagrāhadṛṣṭibhyāntad uttrāsāt mithyādṛṣṭyā cāpavādāt 
parāmarśasaṃyojanaṃ mārgasatyaparijñāne anyathā'praśuddhiparāmarśanāt 
vicikitsāsaṃyojanaṃ ratnatrayaparijñāne tad guṇā'nabhiśraddhānāt 
īrṣyāsaṃyojanaṃ lābhasatkāraparijñāne tad doṣā'darśanāt 
mātsaryasaṃyojanaṃ saṃlekhaparijñāne pariṣkārā'dhyavasānāt   mānādi bhedena 
ātmātmīyagrāhyagrāhakatvavivekena bālajanaparikalpitadharmasvabhāvavivekena ca yat satkāyadrṣṭir darśanaṃ tat satkāyadṛṣṭiparijñānaṃ 
tasya mānasaṃyojanaṃ bhavaty āvaraṇaṃ tad utpattivibandhāt 
kutra katham ityāha  abhisamyakāle sāntaravyantarā'smimānasamudācāravaśena tad aprahāṇād iti 
satyābhisamayakāle nirvedhabhāgīyāvasthāyāṃ 
tatra sāntaraḥ pratipakṣavyavahitaḥ vyantaraḥ pratipakṣā'vyavahitaḥ 
sa cādhimātre mṛdau ca pratipakṣe veditavyaḥ 
yāvat sāntareṇa vyantareṇa cāsmimānena samudācarati na tāvat satkāyadṛṣṭEḥ prahāṇam asti 
satkāyadṛṣṭibalenaivāsmimānapravṛttitaḥ 
avidyāsaṃyojanaṃ satkāyadṛṣṭivastuparijñāne āvaraṇam iti sambadhyate 
satkāya dṛṣṭer vastu pañcopādānaskandhāḥ tad ālambanataḥ 
yathoktaṃ sūtre  ye kecicchramaṇā brāhmaṇā vā ātmā ātmeti samanupaśyantaḥ samanupaśYanti abhiniviśamānā abhiniviśante ta imān eva pañcopādānaskandhānupādāyeti 
kim punas tat parijñānaṃ 
  ātmanyātma śūnyatāyāḥ skandheṣu bālajanaparikalpitadharmasvabhāvaśūnyatāyāś ca yad darśanam anityato duḥkhataḥ śūnyato'nātmataḥ samudāyādito vā yad darśanaṃ tat teṣāṃ parijñānaṃ 
atraiva kāraṇam āha  tenopādānaskandhā'parijñānād iti 
avidyayā hi nityādiprakārāvṛteṣu skandheṣu tat parijñānā'bhāvād avidyā skandhaparijñānāvaraṇaṃ 
dṛṣṭisaṃyojanaṃ nirodhasatyaparijñāne āvaraṇam iti vartate 
dṛṣṭisaṃyojanaṃ hi tisro dṛṣṭayaḥ satkāyāntagrāhamithyādṛṣṭayaḥ 
tatra satkāyadṛṣṭiḥ pañcasūpādānaskandheṣvātmata ātmīyato veti darśanaṃ 
antagrāhadṛṣṭir hi tasminnevātmābhikalpitabhāve śāśvatadarśanam ucchedadarśanaṃ vā 
yena darśanena hetuṃ vā phalaṃ vā kriyā vā sad vā vastu apavadate mithyā vā parikalpayati tan mithyādṛṣṭiḥ 
nirodhasatyaparijñānaṃ śāntādibhir ākaraiḥ 
katham punas tat tasyāvaraṇam ityata āha  satkāyāntagrāhadṛṣṭibhyāntaduttrāsāt mithyādṛṣṭyā cā'pavādād iti 
tatra satkāyāntagrāhadṛṣṭibhyām ahaṃ tatra na bhaviṣyāmīti nirodhād uttrasyati mithyādṛṣṭyā cā'pavadate nāstyeva nirodha iti 
tatra satkāyāntagrāhadṛṣṭibhyāṃ śāntataḥ praṇītato nissaraṇataś ca na parijānāti mithyādṛṣṭyā nirodhato na parijānāti 
evaṃ dṛṣṭisaṃyojanaṃ nirodhaparijñāna āvaraṇaṃ 
parāmarśasaṃyojanaṃ mārgasatyaparijñāne 
tatra parāmarśasaṃyojanaṃ dṛṣṭiparāmarśaḥ śīlavrataparāmarśaśca 
tatra dṛṣṭiparāmarśo dṛṣṭau dṛṣṭyāśrayeṣu ca pañcasūpādānaskandheṣu yad utkarṣādito darśanaṃ 
śīlavrataparāmarśaḥ śīlaṃ vrataṃ tad ubhayaṃ tadāśrayān vā pañcopādānaskandhān śuddhito muktito nairyāṇikato vā samanupaśyato yad darśanaṃ tacchīlavrataparāmarśaḥ 
mārgasya parijñānam punar nairyāṇikādibhir ākāraiḥ 
katham punaḥ parāmarśasaṃyojanaṃ mārgaparijñāna āvaraṇam ityata āha  anyathā 'praśuddhiparāmarśanād iti 
śīlavratamātrakeṇa vā kāmasukhālayena vā duṣkaracaryayā vā sāṃkhyādijñānena vā śuddhiparāmarśanāt 
dṛṣṭiparāmarśena tu yenaiva śuddhiṃ pratyeti tadevā'grataḥ parāmṛśati 
evaṃparāmarśasaṃyojanena mārgaṃ tyajati anyathā ca śuddhimparāmṛśatīti 
vicikitsāsaṃyojanaṃ ratnatrayaparijñāne āvaraṇam iti vartate 
katham ityato bravīti  tad guṇā'nabhiśraddhānād iti 
vicikitsāsaṃyojanaṃ saty aratneṣu vimatiḥ 
prakarṣeṇā'panītasarvaguṇadoṣasya paryantāśrayatvena buddharatne parijñānaṃ 
  saṃsārasāgarottarakatvena sarvasahetukaduḥkhā'tyantaviyogātmakatvena tat pratipādakatvena ca dharmaratne parijñānaṃ 
śrāmaṇyapahalasthatvenānuttaradakṣiṇīyakṣetratvena cāsangharatne parijñānaṃ 
satyadarśanāt prahīṇavicikitsaścā'vetya prasādalābhena ratnatrayaguṇe'bhiśraddatte nā'prahīṇavicikitsa iti 
ato vicikitsāsaṃyojanaṃ ratnatrayaparijñāna āvaraṇam uktaṃ 
īrṣyāsaṃyojanaṃ lābhasatkāraparijñāna āvaraṇaṃ 
atraiva kāraṇam āha  tad doṣā'darśanād iti 
īrṣyāsaṃYojanaṃ hi lābhasatkārarakto'nyasampatpratighāṃśikaścetaso vyāroṣaḥ 
sarvānarthāśrayatvā'vabodho lābhasatkāraparijñānaṃ 
īrṣyayā tu lābhasatkāraṃ sarvaguṇavipakṣabhūtatvena vividhā'narthamūlatvena ca na parijānātītyato lābhasatkāra parijñāna āvaraṇam irṣyāsaṃyojanaṃ 
mātsaryasaṃyojanaṃ saṃlekhaparijñāna āvaraṇam iti 
katham ityata āha  pariṣkārā'dhyavasānād iti 
mātsaryaṃ pariṣkāre'ṣv avyavasito rāgāṃśikaścetasa upakaraṇeṣv āgrahaḥ 
saṃlekhaḥ pariṣkārair vivekaḥ 
tasya sarvaguṇāśrayavastutvenā'vabodhaḥ parijñānaṃ 
na tu mātsaryeṇa pariṣkārā'dhyavāsānāt sarvaguṇāśrayetvena parijānātītyataḥ saṃlekhaparijñāne mātsaryāvaraṇatvam uktaṃ 
tatrā'nunayapratighasaṃyojane tattvādhigamaprayogāvaraṇe 
śeṣāṇi tu prayuktasya tattvadarśanasyāvaraṇāni tasmād eva teṣām anukramaḥ 
tadyathā'vaśyaṃ prathamam eva mumukṣūṇāṃ saṃsārāc citttam udvejayitavyaṃ 
tataḥ sarvata upekṣeṇa bhavitavyaṃ 
tataḥ sarvā'narthamūlatvāt satkāyadṛṣṭiḥ parijñeyā 
tad anantaraṃ dukḥ samudayātmakatvena tadvastu parijñeaṃ
tatastannirodho vijñeyaḥ
tad anantaraṃ lābhamārgo vijñeyaḥ 
tataḥ satyadarśanād ratnatraye tad guṇā'vabodhād avetya prasādalābhaḥ 
satyadarśanabalenaiva ca lābhasatkārasaṃlekhayor doṣaguṇadarśī bhavatītyevam āvaraṇīyadharmakramahetunā tadāvaraṇakramo veditavyaḥ 
nanu sarvasyāpi sarvatrāvaraṇatvena saṃbhavād vastupratiniyamenāvaraṇanirdeśo na yuktaḥ 
naivā'tra vastupratiniyamaḥ kriyate kintarhi pratyāsattitaḥ prādhānyaiṣa nirdeśaḥ 
  bodhisattvāvaraṇaṃ   kim etad evāvaraṇaṃ 
etat tu sāmānyaṃ bodhisattvaśrāvakādīnāṃ 
bodhisattvānāntvāvaraṇaṃ 
śubhādau daśadhā'paraṃ 
āvaraṇaṃ 
ke ca śubhādaya iti na jñāyate 
ata āha  aprayogo'nāyatane 'yogavihitaś ca yaḥ 
ityevamādyāvaraṇaṃ 
śubhādayaḥ punaḥ 
śubhaṃ bodhiḥ samādānaṃ ityādi daśārthāḥ 
tatra śubhaṃ hi bodhihetubhūtaṃ sarvakuśalamūlaṃ 
bodhis tu tat phalaṃ 
tatra śubhaṃ sāmānyata uddiṣṭaṃ prabhedataḥ svabhāvataś ca na vijñāyata ity atas tat pratipādanārtham ārabhyate  samādānaṃ dhīmattā'bhrāntyanāvṛtī 
nānyatrāso'matsaritvaṃ vaśitvaṃ ca ityetac chubham iti 
bodhir api vacanamātreṇa svabhāvato na vijñāyata ityasyā vibhutvaṃ darśayati 
śubhasya bodheś ca samādānādīnām iva svātantryeṇāvaraṇanirdeśāt svātantryam evā'tra vijñāyate na tad deśanirdeśabhāva ityeke 
utpattyāvaraṇaṃ hi śūbhe vyavasthāpyate tac ca bodhicittādīnāṃ sāmānyaṃ tasyāḥ śubhotpādyatvāt 
dhṛtyādyāvaraṇantu samādānādyāvaraṇaṃ samādānādiṣu vṛttyādyarthabhedāt bodhirapyekopyā prāptavyā cetyatas tasyāḥ sthityāvaraṇaṃ prāptyāvaraṇaṃ ca vyavasthāpyate 
tasmān nāsty atra svātantryaprasanga iti 
kramaś ca teṣāṃ samāsataḥ  kuśalamūlaṃ niravaśeṣaṃ niṣpādya bodhiḥ prāptavyā 
vyāsataḥ punaḥ prathamata eva bodhicittam utpādayitavyaṃ svaparārthasampadādhārabhūtatvāt 
tataścittotpādanā'nurūpā dānādiṣu pratipattiḥ yayā bodhisattva ityākhyāṃ labhate 
tato'saṃkhyeyakalpenābhyasyataḥ puṇyajñānasambhārasañcayād āśayaviśodhanārthaṃ pudgaladharmabhrāntipratipakṣeṇā'bhrāntyātmako darśanamārga utpādayitavyaḥ 
tataścāvaraṇavigamaprabhāvito bhāvanāmārgaḥ prakarṣaṃ netavyo viśuddhiviśeṣayogārthaṃ 
  tataḥ śrāvakādyatikramaṇaprayogeṇa yathopacitāni sarvāṇyetāni laukikakalokottarāṇi kuśalamūlāni bodhau pariṇāmayitavyāni 
tataś ca nāmavasthāmāgato mahābodhyāśayatvād buddhabodhisattvānāṃ gambhīrodāreṣu nirdeśeṣu na trasyati 
tato bahuśrutapratipattiyukta udāraṃ dharmaṃ nirdiśati sattvaparipācanārthaṃ 
tataḥ paripakvavineyeṣu tadvimocanārthaṃ vaśitvaṃ buddhatvam avāpnotīti 
atra hi triṃśadāvaraṇāny uktāni āvaraṇīyārthāḥ śubhādayo daśa cetyataḥ pṛcchati  eṣāṃ tu śubhādīnāṃ kasya katyāvaraṇāni vijñeyānīti 
ata āha  trīṇi trīṇi ca eteṣāṃ jñeyānyavaraṇāni hi 
iti 
kuśalasya trīṇyāvaraṇānīti 
aprayogo'nārambhaḥ 
kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  yena kleśena na prayujyate pramādena kausīdyena vā yasminn avasthāviśeṣe kleśabījānugate'vyākṛte kliṣṭe vā na prayujyate 
na prayujyate nityaṃ gauravād vā alapatvād vetyapratyoga ucyate na tu prayogābhāvāt tasminn āvaraṇā'nupapatteḥ 
anāyatanaprayogo bodher bodhyāvāhakānāñca kuśalamūlānāṃ yat pravacanam utpattidvāraṃ tadāyatanaṃ tasmād anyad anāyatanaṃ 
tasmin prayogo'nāyatane prayoga etasmād bāhyeṣvartheṣu 
tatra kimāvaraṇaṃ  yenā'jñānena dṛṣṭikleśena vā'nāyatane prayujyate sa eva ca prayoga āvaraṇaṃ 
ayoniśaḥ prayoga iti 
yonir upāyaḥ 
yasya ya upāyas tasmād anyathā prayogo'yoniśaḥ prayogaḥ 
ihaiva śāsane paṭhyate yad uta rāgacaraṇabhāvānāṃ hi na rāgaprahāṇopāyaḥ pratighacaraṇasyā'śubhabhāvaneti 
atrā'pyayoniśo manaskāras tannimitto vā prayoga āvaraṇaṃ 
bodhes trīṇi 
yathārtham avabodho bodhiḥ 
kuśalasyā'nutpattir iti pūrvoktam eva 
katham anutpattirāvaraṇaṃ  kuśale'sati bodhir na bhavet tataḥ kuśalasyā'nutpattir bodher āvaraṇaṃ 
yo vā kleśo 'vasthāviśeṣo vā kuśalotpatter āvaraṇaṃ sa eva bodher api 
yo hi yat sambhārasyāvaraṇaṃ niyatam asau tat phalasyāpīti 
utpannasyāpy amanasikaraṇaṃ abhāvanā'napekṣetyarthaḥ 
yena kausīdyādikleśena yasminn avasthāviśeṣa utpannam api kuśalaṃ paunaḥ punyena na manasi karoti tad atrāvaraṇaṃ 
aparipūrṇasaṃbhāratā ceti 
yāvatā sambhāreṇa bodhiḥ prāpyate tāvān  puṇyajñānasambhāro'pūrṇaḥ pūrvavad avasthākleśo'lpasambhāro vā 
anyaḥ punar āha  aviśeṣavacane'pi nirvedhabhāgīnānām evātrā'nutpattir abhipretā nānyeṣāṃ 
utpanānām api teṣām evā'manasikaraṇaṃ manasikurvato'py asaṃbhṛtasambhāra āvaraṇam ucyata iti 
samādānaṃ bodhicittotpāda iti 
niravaśeṣāḥ puṇyajñānasambhārās tat phalañca buddhatvaṃ sarvasattvāś ca niruttare nirupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau pratiṣṭhāpayitavyenā'nena iti samādānaṃ bodhicittotpādaḥ 
sa punaḥ svaparahitakriyāśayaścetanācchandasahitaḥ 
tasyāvaraṇeṣu triṣu gotravaidhuryaṃ 
agotrakaḥ śrāvakādigotrako vā 
kalyāṇamitravaidhuryaṃ 
satyapi gotre ye taṃ bodhicittotpāde samādāpayanti tair asamavadhānaṃ yān vāgamya bodhir vyāvartate kuśalair vā dharmair na vardhate 
satyapi kalyāṇamitrasamavadhāne saṃsāraduḥkhena parikhedacittatā vipratipannasattvānām udvagacittasyāśu parinirvāṇābhiprāyaḥ 
kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  hetuvaikalyaṃ pratyayavaikalyaṃ sattveṣu cā'kāruṇyaṃ kausīdyaṃ vā 
akāruṇiko hi sattvārthena khidyate kusīdo vā 
dhīmattvaṃ bodhisattvateti 
svabhāvena śrāvakādigotrakebhyamtīkṣṇendriyatvāt sarvathā sarvajñeyopaparīkṣādhikāritvāt gambhīrodāradharmā'dhimukteś ca bodhisattva eva dhīmān nā'nyaḥ 
bodhisattvatā'viparyastā parārthaparā pratipattiḥ 
pratipatter vaidhuryaṃ pāramitādiṣv apravṛttiḥ 
bodhisattvo hi pratipattivṛtto jñeyaḥ 
kujano mūrkhajana iti aparīkṣakajana ityarthaḥ 
kujano hi pratipattiyuktam api bodhisattvopamitaṃ na jānīte 
duṣṭajanaḥ pratihata iti bodhisattvadveṣiṇaḥ 
te hi randhrā'nvayitvād bodhisattvasya bhūtān guṇān na paśyanti 
asaddoṣadarśanāt pratigharaudracittād vā bhūtān guṇān pracchādyā'dhyāropyā'bhūtān doṣān prakāśayanti 
kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  dānapāramitādivipakṣo 'jñānam pradveṣaśceti 
abhrāntes trīṇi 
adhyāropāpavādād bhrāntiḥ tat pratipakṣas tu bhrātyabhāvo darśanamārgaḥ 
viparyāsadauṣṭhulyaṃ grāhyagrāhakā'bhiniveśavāsanā paripuṣṭir iti kecit 
sarveṣāṃ darśanaheyānām anuśayānāṃ sarvatragadharmadhātubodhapratibuddhasya  vā'kliṣṭasyā'jñānasyālayavijñānasanniviṣṭabījaparipoṣa ity anye 
ātmādyabhāva ātmādivikalpo hi viparyāsa ity apare 
kleśādyāvaraṇatrayād anyatamā'vaśiṣtateti 
tatra kleśāvaraṇaṃ yastīvrāyatakālasamudācārikleśo rāgādikas tat pratipakṣaprayogā'navakāśād abhrānter āvaraṇaṃ 
karmāvaraṇamānantaryādikarma yadapāyaniyamanaṃ 
vipākāvaraṇam apāyādayaḥ tatrotpannasyāryadharmotpattibhāgo nāsti 
teṣāṃ kleśakarmajanmanām anyatamam apy aviśīṣṭam āvaraṇaṃ na punaḥ kṛtsnaṃ 
vimuktiparipācinyāḥ prajñāyā aparipakvatā ceti 
vimuktyāvāhikāyāḥ prajñāyā akarmaṇyatā 
nirvedhabhāgīyāvasthāyā aprāptyatvād iti kecit 
anyetvāhuḥ nirvikalpā'tra prajñā vimuktiparipācinī tat prayogikā ca dvitīyā 
tayor aparipakvatā tattvādhigamā'yogyatā tad upaniṣadbhāvā'yogyatā cā'paripūrṇaṃbhāratvād yathākramam iti 
kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  darśanaheyakleśasya puṣṭavāsanākleśāvaraṇādīnām anyatamā'vaśiṣṭatā prajñāparipākavibandhabhūtam ajñānaṃ sambhārā'paripūrṇatā ca 
āvaraṇaprahāṇam anāvaraṇam iti 
āvaraṇaṃ prahīyate 'nenety āvaraṇāprahāṇam āvaraṇapratipakṣād anāvaraṇaṃ bhāvanāmārgaḥ 
tasya trīṇi 
sahajaṃ dauṣṭhulyaṃ bhāvanāheyakleśā'nuśayaḥ 
sahajaṃ vātmadṛṣṭyādīnāṃ dharmadhātusparśārthādiprativedhavibandhakasyā'kliṣṭasyā'jñānasyālayavijñānasanniviṣṭaṃ paripuṣṭabījaṃ 
kausīdyaṃ mohāṃśikādālasyāc cittā'nabhyutsāhaḥ 
pramādaś ca viṣayavyāsangaḥ kuśale cā'navadhānaṃ 
samādher āsvādinā'tra pramāda ity eke 
tatra dauṣṭhulyāc ca mārgaṃ na bhāvayati 
pramādād akuśalāc cittāṃ na rakṣati 
kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  etad eva trayaṃ 
pariṇātes trīṇi yair anyatra cittaṃ pariṇāmayatīti 
tatra pariṇatirutpannānāṃ kuśalamūlānāṃ buddhatvaṃ eva cittena niyamanaṃ 
tasyāstrīṇyāvaraṇāni 
katamāni trīṇi yair anyatra buddhatvāt saṃsāre śrāvakādibodho vā cittaṃ pariṇāmayati nā'nuttarāyāṃ samyaksambandhau 
tāni punar bhavasaktirbhogasaktilīnacittatā ca 
bhavaḥ pañcopādānaskandhāḥ 
bhujyanta iti bhogā rūpādayo viṣayāḥ 
tayor abhiṣvangaḥ saktiḥ 
līnacittatā'nudāracittatā kva buddhatvaṃ kva ca madvidha ityātmanyasambhāvanā 
tatra ca bhavasaktyā bhogasaktyā ca sugatau cittaṃ pariṇāmayati līnacittatatyā śrāvakādiyāne pariṇāmayati kimatrāvaraṇaṃ  bhavabhogatṛṣṇā kausīdyam akāruṇyañca 
  atrāsasya trīṇi 
ko'yam atrāsaḥ  śūnyatāyāṃ gambhīrodāreṣu ca buddhabodhisattvadharmeṣv adhimuktir abhīrutā 
asambhāvanā pudgale mahāyānanayābhidhyāyinaḥ pudgalasya bhrāntyā'vagamo vacanañca śīlasamādhiprajñādiguṇasya vā'sampratyayaḥ 
anadhimuktir dharme gambhīrodāranayapratipādake buddhavacanatvenā'viparītā'rthena cā'sampratyayaḥ 
yathārutavicāraṇā'rthe 
anutpannā'niruddhādiśāntādyartha yathāśabdam eva pratipadyate na cābhiprāyikārthatattvam avagacchati 
tasmād anutpannādyarthā'nadhimuktiḥ 
kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  vicikitsāprajñāsamādhivipakṣabhūtajñānamābhiprāyikārthamitirūtavicāraṇā vipakṣabhūtañceti 
amātsaryasya trīṇi 
amātsaryaṃ yataḥ saddharmasthitaye'nyānugrahārthaṃ vā dharmadeśanā 
saddharme'gauravaṃ acitrīkāraḥ 
tenā'nyasantānā'prāpaṇāc cirasthitikaṃ saddharmaṃ na karoti 
lābhasatkārapūjāyāṃ gauravaṃ citrīkāraḥ saddharmagaurave mā'nyo'pi mattulyo'dhiko vā bhaviṣyatītyāśankā 
tasmāl lābhādivyavadhānaṃ bhaviṣyatīti bhītyā dharmaṃ na deśayati 
lābhasatkārādhyavasāne'vidyamāne'pi sattveṣvakāruñañceti sattveṣu karuṇābhāvān na deśayati 
na hyakāruṇikaḥ sattvaduḥkhenā'pakriyate 
kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  agauravaṃ lābhasakārasaktir akāruñañceti 
vaśitvasya trīṇi āvaraṇānītyarthaḥ 
vaśitvaṃ hi sarveṣāṃ cittavaśitvānāmprāptir buddhatvaṃ 
tasya trīṇyāvaṇāni punar na jñāyanta ityata āha  yair vibhutvaṃ na labhate iti 
cittavaśitvapratibandhād vaśitvasya yair vaśitvaṃ na labhate tānyeva vaśītvasyāvaraṇānītyāha 
vibhutvam punar jñānaprahāṇaprabhāvasampannatā 
atha vā vaśitvaparyāye nirdiṣṭatvādyair vaśitvaṃ na labhata iti vṛddhatvaṃ na labhata ityarthaḥ 
śrutavyasanaṃ saddharmaśravaṇenā'tyantaviyogaḥ 
bandhubhir atyantaviyogo bandhuvyasanaṃ 
tat punaḥ śrutavyasanaṃ saddharmavyasanasamvartanīyakarmaprabhavanād bhavati 
svadarśanaparāmarśasthitatvād akalyāṇamitrāśritatvād vā yair avipratisārair mahāyānasūtrāntaḥ pratikṣipto mārabhāṣito'yam apāyahetuśca nā'pyambuddhabhāṣita iti anyān api tasmād vicchindayanti  likhitaṃ conmṛṣanti dāhayanti pāvayantītyādiprakāraiḥ saddharmavyasanasamvartanīyakarmotpadyate saddharmaśravaṇavidhurātmabhāvaparipuṣṭitaḥ 
asati śrutavyasane'lpaśrutatvaṃ jñānasambhārasyā'paripūritā āvaraṇam iti prakṛtaṃ 
alpaśruto he na śaknoti dharmān pravivektum 
bahuśrutasyāpi samādher aparikarmtvañcāvaraṇam iti sambandhaḥ 
chandādīnām anyatamā'bhāvāt aparipūrṇatvād bhāvanāyāṃ vā'ṣṭānāṃ prahāṇasaṃskārāṇām anyatamābhāvāt samādher aparikarmitatvaṃ 
vajropamādīnāṃ vā buddhasamādhīnām apariniṣpannatvam aparikarmitatvaṃ 
kimatrāvaraṇaṃ  dharmavyasanasamvartanīyakarma alpaśrutatvaṃ duṣprajñatā samādhipratyanīkaścopakleśo layauddhatyādika iti 
  daśakāraṇāni   tat punaretad āvaraṇam aprayogādikaṃ 
śubhādau vaśitvaparyantadaśavidhe vastuni 
yatrā'rthe daśa kāraṇāni bhavantīti  utpattyādau prāptiparyante yasminn arthe tadāvaraṇaviparyayeṇa prayogādīni samādhiparikarmitatvā'vasānāni daśakāraṇāni bhavanti 
atra cotpattyādikāraṇatvā'viśeṣād bhinnasyā'pi pratyekam apy abhedanirdeśaḥ 
tad arthādhikāreṇety utpattyyādyarthādhipatyenetyarthaḥ teṣāṃ hi śubhādīnām utpattyādikāraṇavibandhaṃ vartamānam utpattyādyāvaraṇam ucyate tadyathā kuḍyādikam ālokamāvṛnvat kāryasya cakṣur vijñānasyāvaraṇam ucyate 
evaṃ kṛtvaiṣāṃ daśānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ triṃśad āvaraṇaviparyayeṇa triṃśat kāraṇaṃ veditavyaṃ 
 tatra śubhotpattikāraṇaṃ trīṇi  prayoga āyatanaprayogo yoniśaḥ prayogaś ca 
tad yathā cakṣur ādaya ityatraiva dṛṣṭāntaḥ 
cakṣurādayo vijñānasyotpattikāraṇam eva sthityādikāraṇaṃ 
tatrā'prayogādayaḥ prayogādīnāṃ sākṣād vibandhe vartamānāḥ paramparayā śubhotpatter api pratibandhakāḥ 
evam utpattyāvaraṇaṃ śubhe draṣṭavyam ityāha tasyotpādanīyatvād iti śubhe sthityādyasambhavād utpattyāvaraṇam evaitad iti darśayati 
sthitikāraṇaṃ bodhau 
āśrayaparāvṛttir bodhiḥ āśrayo nirmalatathatā 
atra kāraṇam āha  akopyatvād iti 
yāval lokas tāvad avasthānād akopyatvaṃ nā'nyathā bhavati vinivartate vā 
śrāvakādīnān tu bodhiḥ svasantāna eva kṛtārthatvād vyāvartate 
bodhisattvā hi sarvasattvahitasukhādhyāśayena sambhāreṣu pravartamānā  āśrayaparāvṛttilakṣaṇatvād bodher yāvat sattvās tāvad avatiṣṭhantīty ucyate na tv anutpattimātratvāc chrāvakādivat 
utpattiṃ vinā bhāvitatvāt tu sthiter utpattir apyatra bhavati 
tasmād bodhisthitikāraṇam evocyate notpattikāraṇaṃ 
na cā'nyat tad vyatirekeṇa sthitikāraṇam astītyata etad evoktaṃ 
viśuddhatathatā vā bodhiḥ 
na tathātāyāḥ svabhāvavuśuddhātvād utpattir asti kintarhyāgantukamlā'pagamād anyantam ebhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ sthitirevocyate notpattiḥ 
sthitikāraṇāni punar bodheḥ kuśalotpādo manasikāraḥ paripūrṇasambhāraś ca 
atra ca śubhānutpattyādayaḥ kuśalotpatyādivibandhe vartamānā bodheḥ sthitiṃ kurvantīti sthityāvaraṇam uktāḥ 
tadyathā catvāra āhārāḥ sattvānām ityatraiva nidarśanaṃ 
na hi kavaḍākārādibhir āhārair apūrvāḥ sattvā utpadyante purvotpannās tu vyavasthāpyanta eva 
dhṛtikāraṇam iti 
dhṛtir bodhicittaṃ sarvakuśaladharmādhārabhūtatvāt 
atraiva nidarśanaṃ yadyasyādhārabhūtan tatra tasya dhṛtiḥ dhāryate'neneti kṛtvā 
tadyathā bhājanalokaḥ sattvalokasyeti 
tat kāraṇaṃ gotraṃ kalyāṇamitrasampannatā cittā'parikhedatā ca 
tatra dhṛtikāraṇaviruddhatvād gotravaidhuryādikandhṛter apyāvaraṇam uktaṃ 
etad evāha  dhṛtyāvaraṇaṃ samādāna āvaraṇaṃ bodhicittasyādhārabhūtatvād iti 
abhivyaktikāraṇaṃ dhīmattve bodhisattvasya prakāśanīyatvāt 
tacca pratipattisampat sujanavāso duṣṭajanā'vāsaś ca 
atra dhīmattve pratipattivaidhuryād ayo'bhivyaktyāvaraṇatvenocyante 
ata evāha  abhivyaktyāvaraṇaṃ dhīmattve tasya prakāśanīyatvād iti 
tad yathā  āloko rūpasyetyatraiva nidarśanaṃ 
āloko hi rūpamātrasyā'bhivyaktikāraṇam eva notpattyādikāraṇaṃ 
vikāraṇam abhrāntau 
samāropā'pavādabhrāntiparivṛttyātmakatvād abhrāntir darśanamārgo'bhrānter vikāra ucyate 
tadyathā bhasmādayaḥ kāṣṭhādīnāṃ 
tasya trīṇi kāraṇāni  viparyāsadauṣṭhulyopaghātaḥ kleśādyāvaraṇānāṃ trayāṇām abhāvo  vimuktiparipācinyāḥ prajñāyāḥ paripakvabhāvaḥ 
tadyathā agnyādayaḥ pākyādīnām iti 
pākyo hyodanādikas taṇḍulādivilakṣaṇas tat santānāntarbhūtaḥ 
tat kāraṇaṃ cāgnyādi 
viśleṣakāraṇam anāvaraṇe 
darśanamārgapraheyādāvaraṇāc cheṣam āvaraṇam anena prahīyata ityanāvaraṇaṃ bhāvanāmārgaḥ 
tasya trīṇi kāraṇāni  sahajadauṣṭhulyopaghāto vīryam apramādaś ca 
teṣāñca viśleṣakāraṇapratipakṣatvāt 
ata evāha  viśleṣāvaraṇam anāvaraṇe 
etad api viśleṣakāraṇapratipakṣabhāvenaivāvaraṇaṃ 
atraiva kāraṇam āha  tasyāvaraṇaviṣaṃyogatvād iti 
visaṃyujyate'neneti viśleṣaḥ 
pariṇatikāraṇaṃ natau 
tasya mahābodhau kuśalamūlaprayojakalakṣaṇatvāt 
tat punar bhavabhogavaimukhyaṃ līnacittatā'bhāvaś ca 
tataś ca pariṇatyāvaraṇaṃ pariṇatikāraṇavibandhena draṣṭavyaṃ 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  nater mahābodhau cittapariṇatilakṣaṇatvād iti 
sampratyayakāraṇam atrāse 
tac ca pudgalasambhāvanā dharmā'dhimuktir ābhiprāyikārthā'dhigamaś ca 
ebhir dharmaiḥ sampratyayo bhavatītyataś ca sampratyayakāraṇavibandhena sampratyayāvaraṇamatrāse 
atraiva kāraṇam āha  asampratyayena trasanād iti 
asampratyayena hi dharmasya trasyati 
sampratyāyanakaraṇamamatsaritve 
tat punaḥ saddharme gauravaṃ lābhasatkārapūjādinirapekṣatāa sattveṣu ca kāruṇyaṃ 
sampratyayāyanakāraṇaviruddhatvāc ca sampratyāyanāvaraṇam amatsaritve 'vasthāpyate 
atraiva kāraṇam āha  dharmā'matsaritvena parasampratyāyanāditi 
saddharme'gauravādito dharme mātsarye karoti 
dharmamātsaryeṇa ca pareṣāṃ dharmaṃ na deśayati 
ataḥ sampratyāyanāvaraṇam amatsaritva iti 
vaśitvasya trīṇi kāraṇāni  dharmavyasanasaṃvartanīyakarmā'bhāvo bahuśrutatvaṃ samādhiparikarmitatvañca 
tadviruddhatvāc cu tavyasanādikaṃ vaśitva āvaraṇaṃ vyavasthāpyate 
atraiva kāraṇam āha  tasya vaśitvasya vibhutvaprāptilakṣaṇatvād iti 
kecit tu śubhādīnām evam anukrame kāraṇam āhuḥ 
kuśaladharmopaṣṭabdhasatatir bodhiḥ prāptavyā 
tata āditaḥ śubham uktaṃ 
tad anantaraṃ bodhir uktā 
bodhicittañcāgamyaitad ubhayasampādane samartho bhavati ā bodher bodhicittasya sarvakuśaladharmādhārabhūtatvād atas tad anantaraṃ bodhicittam uktaṃ 
utpāditabodhicittasya ṣaṭpāramitāsu prayogaḥ kujanaduṣṭajanābhyāñca parihāraḥ 
evam asya bodhisattvabhāvaḥ prakāśībhavati 
  ataḥ samādānānantaraṃ dhīmatvam uktaṃ 
evañca prayujyamāno viparyāsaṃ prajahāti aviparyastaṃ ca jñānam utpādayati 
ato dhīmatvānantaram abhrāntir uktā sa punar darśanamārgaḥ 
tad abhyasanenāvaraṇaṃ vijahātītyatas tad anantaram āvaraṇaprahāṇam anāvaraṇam uktaṃ 
nirāvaraṇasya bhavabhogasaktyabhavād buddhatva eva mānasaṃ pariṇāmayati nānyatreti 
atas tad anantaraṃ natiruktā 
evam bhūtasya ca sugambhīreṣv api buddhadharmeṣu prāmodyotpatīratrāsa ityatas tad anantaramatrāsa uktaḥ 
evaṃ dharmapratyakṣeṇa yena yenopāyena sattvavinayaṃ paśyati tantamevopāyambhajata iti tasya kuto mātsaryambhaved ityatrāsānantaram amātsaryam uktaṃ 
evam prahīṇāvaraṇaḥ paripūrṇaśukladharmā ca bodhisattvaścittavaśitve pravartata ityatas tad anantaraṃ vaśitvam uktaṃ 
eṣo'nukrama iti 
asmin paricchede āvaraṇaprasanga ityataḥ śubhādīnām utpatīkāraṇāny āvaraṇavat sūtritāni 
prasangāgatānām antaraślokena sangrahaḥ kriyate 
kāraṇaṃ daśadhotpattau sthitau dhṛtyāṃ prakāśane 
vikāraviśleṣanatipratyayaprāyaṇāptiṣu 
eṣa dvitīyo'ntaraśloka udāharaṇasangrahārthaṃ  cakṣurāhārabhūdīpa vahnyādis tad udāhṛtiḥ 
dātraśilpajñatādhūmahetumārgādayo'pare 
iti 
   bodhipakṣyapāramitābhūmiṣv āvaraṇāni  pūrvaṃ hyaviśeṣeṇa śubhaṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ tadāvaraṇañca 
idānīntu pakṣyetyādibhedena sādhāraṇā'sādhāraṇabhedena ca śubhaṃ nirdiśati 
vastvakauśalakausīdyaṃ ityādibhedena ca pakṣādīnām āvaraṇaṃ 
tatra sādhāraṇaṃ bodhipakṣāḥ śrāvakabodhisattvayor aviśeṣeṇa tatrā'vikārāt 
asādhāraṇantu pāramitābhūmayo bodhisattvānāṃ karaṇaṃ bodhisattvānām eva tadādhipatyāt 
pūrvañca śubhādihetvāvaraṇadvāreṇa phalāvaraṇam uktaṃ iha tu sākṣāt phalāvaraṇam eveti pūrvasmād anyad ucyate 
atha vā'prayogādibhyo vastvakauśalādikam anyadeveti tad anyad ucyate 
athavā śubhaṃ bodhiścetyatra bodhisattvasyaivopāyasahitayoścaryāphalayor aprayogādikam āvaraṇam uktaṃ iha tu śubhasyaiva sādhāraṇasyā'sādhāraṇasya ca bodhipakṣādivibhāgena vastvakauśalādikam aprayogādikād anyad āvaraṇaṃ veditavyaṃ 
tatra śrāvakādibhedena bodhitrayaṃ tadanurūpeṇa smṛtypasthānādayo mārgaparyantā bodhipakṣā ity ucyate daśa pāramitā daśa ca bhūmayo yathāsūtraṃ 
smṛty upasthāneṣu vastvakauśalam āvaraṇam iti 
tāni punaḥ  kāyavedanācittadharmasmṛtyupasthānāni catvāri 
teṣām punar vastu kāyavedanācittadharmāḥ tad viṣayatvāt 
tatrāśrayam abhiniveśavastu kāyaḥ 
ātmaparibhogābhiniveśavastu vedanā 
ātmābhiniveśavastu cittaṃ 
ātmasankleśavyavadānābhiniveśavastu dharma iti 
kāyādiṣu yaḥ svasāmānyalakṣaṇā'navabodhaḥ sa tatrā'kauśalaṃ 
tatra svalakṣaṇam anekāśucidravyeṇa sangṛhītātmakatvaṃ kāyasya 
sukhādisvabhāvo vedanāyāḥ 
viṣayaprativijñaptir vijñānasya
dharmāṇāṃ yathāsambhavaṃ 
sāmānyalakṣanampunarnityadukhaśūnya'nātmādyākārāḥ
athavā kāyādiṣv aśuciduḥKhā'nityā'nātmākāreṇā pratipattiḥ śucisukhanityātmākāreṇa vā vikalpo vastv akauśalam yasmād ajñānaṃ darśaṇaṃ vā smṛtyupasthāneṣvāvaraṇaṃ 
prajñāsmṛtisvābhāvye sati smṛtyupasthānānāṃ kasmād vastvakauśalam evāvaraṇam ucyate na tu vastvasmaraṇam apīti  prajñādhīnapravṛttitvāt 
tathā hi darśanātmakatvāt prajñāyāḥ prajñāpṛṣṭhalabdha ālambane smṛtyādayaḥ pravartante na tu svātantryeṇa prajñāvat 
tasmān nā'smaraṇamatrāvaraṇam uktam iti 
sampyakprahāṇeṣu kauṣīidyaṃ 
kiṃ  āvaraṇam iti prakṛtaṃ 
vīryaṃ hy atrotpannā'nutpannavipakṣaprahāṇā'nutpātaye utpannapratipakṣasya bhūyobhāvotpādāya ca pravartamānaṃ samyakprahāṇākhyāṃ pratilabhate 
tat punar bhedābhāve'pi phalabhedāc caturdhā vyavasthāpyata iti smṛtiḥ 
ataḥ samyak prahāṇānāṃ vīryātmakatvād ālasyam āvaraṇam uktaṃ 
ṛddhipādeṣu samādher dvayahīnatāvaraṇam iti 
anenaddharyata ity ṛddhiḥ 
sā ca cchandavīryacittamīmāmsāsamādhiḥ 
saivardhhipādaḥ ākāśagamananirmāṇādikāyā ṛddheḥ pratiṣṭhābhūtatvāt 
gamanaṃ vā ṛddhiḥ ākāśagamanādikā samṛddhir ityarthaḥ 
tasyāḥ pādā ṛddhipādāḥ tadādhāratvāt 
saiva cchandasamādhyādicaturvidhā samādhiḥ 
tatracchandasamādhau chandaprādhānyaṃ tad dvāreṇa samādhilābhāt 
na tu vīryādayas tatra na santi chandasahāyatvād apradhānās tu te tatreti na te prakāśitāḥ 
evaṃ vīryacittamīmāṃsā samādhiṣu vācyaṃ 
samādher dvayahīnatāvaraṇam uktaṃ 
na taj jñāyate ata āha  aparipūryā ca cchandavīryacittamīmāṃsānām anyatamavaikalyād bhāvanayā ca prahāṇasaṃskāravaikalyād iti 
tatra paripūrihīnatā tāsāṃ chandavīryacittamīmāṃsānām anyatamavaikalyāt tadādhipatyasya samādher abhāvād bhāvanā hīyata ity aṣṭaprahāṇasaṃskārāṇām anyatamavaikalyaṃ 
te punaḥ śraddhācchandavīryapraśrabdhismṛtisamprajanyacetanopekṣātmakāḥ 
eṣāṃ hi prahāṇasaṃskārāṇāṃ bhāvanayā samādhau vaśitvam avāpyate nānyathetyata eṣāṃ vaikalyād bhāvanāhīnateti na samādhau vaśitvam avāpyate 
kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  chandādipratipakṣāṇāṃ prahāṇasaṃskārāṇāñca vipakṣopakleśaḥ yaduta kausīdyatṃ ālambanasampramoṣaḥ layauddatye'saṃskāraḥ saṃskāraśceti 
indriyeṣu mokṣabhāgīyānām aropaṇam iti 
saṃsārād uttrasto mokṣam adhikṛtya  kuśalamūlam abhisaṃskaroti tena mokṣalābhaniścayāt mokṣabhāgīyam ucyate tasmiścāropite śraddhādaya indriyākhyāṃ pratilabhante nānyathetyato mokṣabhāgīyānām aropaṇam indriyeṣv āvaraṇam uktaṃ 
kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  yenopakleśena mokṣabhāgīyaṃ na rocyate 
sā punar bhavasaktir nirvāṇabhītiś ca 
baleṣu teṣām evendriyāṇāndaurbalayaṃ 
āvaraṇam iti prakṛtaṃ 
katham punar indriyāṇān daurbalyam ityata āha  vipakṣavyavakiraṇād iti 
āśraddyakausīdyam uṣitasmṛtivikṣepaduṣprajñātmakena vipakṣeṇābhibhūtatvād ityarthaḥ 
indriyāṇi hy uṣmagata mūrdhānābhyāṃ prabhāvitāni 
etac ca dvividham api nirvedhabhāgīyān durbalam aśraddhyādivipakṣābhibhavāt 
ata eva tasmāt parihāṇisambhavaḥ 
nirjitavipakṣatvāt tu śraddhādīni kṣāntyagradharmāvasthāyāṃ balākhyāmpratilabhante 
tasmād yat teṣām eva śraddhādīnām uṣmagatamūrdhānāvasthāyāṃ vipakṣā'bhibhavād daurbalyantad balānām āvaraṇaṃ 
tasmin sati balā'vasthā'sambhavād iti 
kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  sa evāśraddhyādiko vipakṣaḥ 
bodhyangeṣu dṛṣṭidoṣaḥ 
āvaraṇam iti prakṛtaṃ 
bodhir hyatra darśanamārgo'bhipretaḥ 
tasyāstāni smṛtidharmapravicayavīryaprītypraśrabdhisamādhyupekṣātmakāni sapta bodhyangāni darśanaheyakleśaprahāṇakāla utpadyanta ityangānīty ucyate 
yadi tu bodheranukūlatvād angāni syur evaṃ smṛtyupasthānādīnām api bodhyangatvamprasajyeta 
katham idaṃ bodhyangeṣu dṛṣṭidoṣa āvaraṇam ityata āha  teṣān darśanamārgaprabhāvitatvād iti darśanamārgavyavasthāpitatvād ity arthaḥ 
kaḥ punar anyadṛṣṭidoṣaḥ  parikalpitāḥ pañca dṛṣṭayo vicikitsā'vidayā tadālambanāṣca rāgādayaḥ sasamprayogāḥ kleṣopakleṣāḥ 
nanu vicikitsā'dayopya attrāvaraṇaṃ 
āvaraṇambhavatu 
iha tu pradhānavivakṣayā dṛṣṭidoṣopadeśa iti na teṣām anupadeśo virudhyate 
teṣāñca dṛṣṭyādīnām ālayavijñānasanniviṣṭaṃ bījam eva darśanamārgapraheyatvāt tad āvaraṇam ucyate 
mārgāngeṣu samyag dṛṣṭisaṃkalpakarmāntājīvavyāyāmasmṛtisamādhyākhyeṣū dauṣṭhulyadoṣa āvaraṇam iti prastutaṃ 
atraiva kāraṇaṃ āha  teṣām mārgāngānāṃ bhāvanāmārgaprabhāvitatvād iti bhāvanāmārgavyavasthāpitatvād 
kaḥ sa dauṣṭhulyadoṣaḥ  vyāsataḥ satkāyāntagrāhadṛṣṭī sahaje sasamprayoge tadālambanā viṣayālambanāś ca rāgādayaḥ kleśopakleśāḥ sasamprayogāḥ 
teṣām ālayavijñānasanniviṣṭaṃ yad bījantad dauṣṭhulyaṃ 
sankṣepatas tu darśanaprahātavyād anyā sāsravā tacchaktir ālayavijñānasanniviṣṭā dauṣṭhulyaṃ 
tac ca bhāvanāmārgapraheyatvān mārgāngeṣv āvaraṇatvena vyavasthāpyate 
uktaṃ bodhipakṣeṣvāvaraṇaṃ 
   pāramitāsvāvaraṇāni  tad anantaramparāramitāsu vaktavyam ityata āha  pāramitāsvāvaraṇaṃ 
aiśvaryasyā'tha sugateḥ sattvā'tyāgasya cāvṛtiḥ 
iti vistaraḥ 
atra daśānāṃ pāramitānāṃ yasyāḥ pāramitāyā yat phalaṃ tadāvaraṇena tasyā āvaraṇam udbhāvitaṃ 
kimatra kāraṇaṃ yan mātsaryādayo vastuto dānādivibandhe vartamānas tat phalāvaraṇatvenocyante na punaḥ pāramitāvaraṇatveneti  tat phalārthena dānādau sarvaḥ pravartate 
tasmān mātsaryādiprahāṇa ādarotpādanārthaṃ phalāvaraṇam uktaṃ na pāramitāvaraṇam iti 
athavā mātsaryādikam āvaraṇam aiśvaryādivipakṣabhūtaṃ dāridryādiphalaṃ janayadaiśvaryādiphalapratibandhāt tadāvaraṇam ucyate 
kintāsāmphalaṃ  tatra dānapāramitāyāḥ phalaṃ prādhānyenaiśvaryādhipatyaṃ 
śīlapāramitāyāḥ sugatiḥ 
kṣāntipāramitāyāḥ sattvā'parityāgaḥ 
vīryapāramitāyā doṣaguṇahānivṛddhī 
dhyānapāramitāyāḥ śāsane sattvāvatāraṇaṃ 
prajñāpāramitāyā guruvimocanaṃ 
upāyakauśalyapāramitāyāṃ bodhipariṇāmanayā kuśalā'kṣayatvaṃ 
prāṇidhānapāramitayāḥ śubhanairantaryaṃ 
balapāramitāyāḥ kuśaladharmaniyatīkaraṇaṃ 
jñānapāramitāyā dharmopabhogaḥ sattvaparipācanañca 
aiśvaryādhipatyāvaraṇam iti 
tatraiśvaryaṃ dhanopakaraṇabahulatā 
ādhipatyaṃ  tad upabhogavaśitvaṃ 
asyobhayasyāvaraṇam āvaraṇaṃ dānapāramitāyās tat phalatvāt 
kim punas tat  mātsaryaṃ 
sugatyāvaraṇam iti 
śobhanā gatiḥ sugatiḥ manuṣyo devaś ca 
tasyāvaraṇam āvaraṇaṃ śīlapāramitāyās tat phalatvāt 
tat punar dauśīlyaṃ kutsitaṃ kāyavākkarma 
sattvā'parityāga iti 
upakārivad apakārisattvopādānaṃ 
etac ca kṣānti phalaṃ tadāvaraṇaṃ krodhaḥ 
doṣaguṇahānibuddhī iti 
svaparā'pakāraprayuktānām utpannānāṃ prahāṇaṃ anutpannānāñcā'nutpādo doṣāṇāṃ hāniḥ 
svaparā'nugrahapravṛttānām utpannānāṃ bhūyobhāvo'nutpannānāñcotpādo vṛddhiḥ 
kiṃ punar atrāvaraṇaṃ  kausīdyaṃ 
vineyāvatāraṇāvaraṇam iti 
vineyānāṃ śāsane'vatāraṇaṃ svargā'pavargalābhakāraṇatvenā'bhyupagamāt 
upaśāntyā gaurava utpadyamāne sattvāḥ sañjalparddhyāpryatnena śāsanampratipadyante 
atra ca vikṣepa āvaraṇaṃ 
vimocanāvaraṇam iti 
vimocanaṃ kleśaprahāṇaṃ 
taccā'nuśāsanyā bhavati anuśāsanī ca prajñā nā'nyathetyataḥ prajñāpāramitāphalaṃ vimocanaṃ 
tadāvaraṇaṃ kliṣṭaprajñā moho duṣprajñā vā 
dānādyakṣayatvāvaraṇam iti 
dānaśīlādīnām akṣayatve yadāvaraṇam tad upāyapāramitāyā āvaraṇaṃ 
tat punar dānādyakṣayatvaṃ kathambhavatītyata āha  bodhipariṇāmanayā tad akṣayatvād iti 
mahābodhipariṇataṃ dānādi kuśalamūlaṃ na kṣīyate buddhatvam iva 
tadāvaraṇaṃ mahābodhipariṇāmanā lakṣaṇā'nupāyajñatetyeke 
anupāyakauśalyaṃ trimaṇḍalagrāhas tadāvaraṇam ity anye 
sarvajanmasu kuśalanairantarya pravṛttyāvaraṇam iti 
kuśalanairantaryaṃ pratidinaṃpratikṣaṇaṃ vā 
tac ca praṇidhānapāramitāyāḥ phalaṃ 
katham ityata āha  praṇidhānavaśena tad anukūlopapattiparigrahād iti 
praṇidhāvaśena hi dānādīnāṃ nairantaryapravṛttyā 'nuguṇām upapattiṃ parigṛhṇāti 
tasyāvaraṇaṃ dānādyanukūlopapattāv apraṇidhānaṃ 
tasyaiva kuśalasya niyatīkaraṇāvaraṇam iti 
pratidinaṃ pratikṣaṇaṃ vā niyatīkaraṇaṃ niścayaḥ 
atraiva kāraṇam āha  pratisaṃkhyānabhāvanābalābhyāṃ vipakṣā'nabhibhavād iti 
atra pratisaṃkhyānabalaṃ dhairyasahitā prajñā 
dhairyaṃ punaḥ prajñaptidharmaḥ 
sahaje vīryasamādhiprajñātraye pratisaṃkhyānatvāt 
bhāvanābalam abhyāsasahitenā'prayatnena  dānādiṣu pravartanaṃ tat pratipakṣeṇa mātsaryādinā'nabhibhavāt 
kimatrāvaraṇaṃ  apratisaṃkhyānabhāvanā daurbalyaṃ 
ātmaparayor dharmasambhogaparipācanāvaraṇam iti 
sambhogikāparṣanmaṇḍale vyavasthānaṃ gambhīrodāramahāyānadharmasya sambhogo vicitrākārair nirmāṇakarmābhidharmadeśanayā sattvaparipākaś ca phalaṃ 
tadāvaraṇam punar yathābhūtaśrutārthavicāraṇā mandaprajñatā cāvaraṇam iti 
atra ca dravyataḥ ṣaṭ pāramitāḥ nāmato daśa 
prajñāpāramitāprabhāvitatvāc catasṛṇām pāramitānāṃ 
tatra prajñāpāramitā lokottaranirvikalpajñānaṃ 
tena jñānena krameṇa sarvāvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ 
upāyapraṇidhānabalajñānapāramitāḥ punar lokottaramārgapṛṣṭhalabdhajñānasangṛhītāḥ 
jñānapāramitā prakṛṣṭā satī kathaṃ na nirvikalpa iti  jñānapāramitā hi nirvikalpajñānapṛṣṭalabdhajñānaṃ 
taj jñānāvabuddhatvaṃ paricchidya svayaṃ ca dharmasambhogaṃ pratyanubhavati parāṃś ca pratipācayati 
tac caitan nirvikalpe dvayam api nāstītyato na nirvikalpā jñānapāramiteti 
uktaṃ pāramitānām āvaraṇaṃ 
  bhūmiṣvāvaraṇāni   daśavidham āvaraṇaṃ yathākramaṃ tad vipakṣatvād iti bhūmivipakṣatvāt 
bhūmayo hi lokottarasamādhiprajñādyavakāśaviśeṣātmakāḥ 
tad utpattivibandhād akliṣṭam ajñānaṃ vipakṣaḥ 
na cā'trakliṣṭamevā'jñānam āvaraṇaṃ kintarhyanye'pi kleśopakleśāḥ 
tathā hi pramuditāyāḥ sarva eva darśanamārgapraheyā āvaraṇaṃ 
yasmāt sarvatrārthā'vabodhena darśanamārgeṇa satyeṣu sarve vipratipattyanuśayāḥ prahīyante bhāvanāpraheyāḥ punaḥ śeṣābhir bhūmibhiḥ 
te tv aprahīṇā api prahīṇavat bodhisattvānāṃ na saṃkleśakarā bhavantīti 
imam eva cā'rthamadhikṛtyoktā gāthā  kleśo bodhynga āpanno mohopāyaprayogataḥ 
saṃsāro'pyupaśāntātmā tato'cintyas tathāgataḥ 
daśasu ca bhūmiṣu daśa pāramitā yathākramam atiriktatarā bhavantīti vacanāt tad vipakṣasyāpi mātsaryādikasya yathākramaṃ prahāṇam iti gamyate 
yadyanyo'pi kleśa āvaraṇaṃ syāt kasmād uktaṃ bhūmiṣv akliṣṭam evājñānam āvaraṇam iti  asādhāraṇatvāt 
etaddhi bodhisattvānām eva nirvāṇādhigamavibandhair vartate na śrāvakādīnāṃ 
tathā hi  śrāvakāḥ pratyekabuddhāś ca tasmin satyeva mucyante na tu bodhisattvā ityato'sādhāraṇaṃ 
etad bhūmiṣv āvaraṇam uktaṃ na tvetad eva bhūmiṣvāvaraṇam iti kṛtvā 
kleśas tu śrāvakādibhir bodhisattvānāṃ samāna iti tasyāvaraṇatvena bodhisattvabhūmiṣu na vidhir na pratiṣedha iti tasyā'vacane'pyāvaraṇaṃ na nivartate 
anya āha  akliṣṭam ajñānaṃ śrāvakādibhir bodhisattvānāṃ samānam iti bhūmīnāṃ viśeṣeṇāvaraṇam ucyate 
kleśastvānuṣangika iti noktaṃ 
kleśo'pi śrāvakādibhir bodhisattvānāṃ samāna evetyasāvānuṣangiko na syād iti 
anye tvāhuḥ  yad bhūmīnām ajñānam āvaraṇaṃ tacchrāvakādīnām akliṣṭam ajñānaṃ sannāpi vimuktivibandhanaṃ 
yasmācchrāvakā bhūmiṣvajñāne satyeva vimucyante 
bodhisattvānān tu kliṣṭaṃ nirvāṇādhigame vibandhahetubhāvād iti 
naitadevam ityanye  akliṣṭaṃ daśadhāvṛtiḥ 
iti 
prathamayā hi bhūmyā dharmadhātoḥ sarvatragārthaṃ pratividhyatīti 
tatra prathamā lokottaraprajñā saparivārā darśanamārgasaṃgṛhītā 
dharmadhātuḥ śūnyatā 
sāmānyalakṣaṇenaikatra yathā sarvatrā'pi tatheti sarvatragatvāt sarvatragaḥ 
dharmadhātuvinirmukto yasmād dharmo na vidyate 
  iti vacanaṃ dharmadhātoḥ sarvatragatvajñāpakaṃ 
pratividhyatīti sākṣātkarotītyarthaḥ 
yena prativedhenātmaparasamatāṃ pratilabhate 
yo'haṃ sa paro yo vā paraḥ so'ham iti paratrātmani ca śūnyatāyā abhedadarśanāt svaparātmanor abhedaṃ manyate 
ata evāsyāṃ bhūmau dānapāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavati 
tato'tra bodhisattvo yathā svārthe tathā parārthe pravartate 
evaṃ hi prativedhaḥ pratipakṣaḥ pratipakṣaphalañcodbhāvitaṃ 
etac ca tritayam itarāsv api bhūmiṣu vijñeyaṃ 
dvitīyayā'grārthaṃ 
dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatīti sambadhyate 
prakṛtiprabhāsvaradarśanāt 
yenā'syaivaṃ bhavati  tasmāt tarhyasmābhis samāne'bhinirhāre sarvākārapariśodhanābhinirhāra eva yogaḥ karaṇīya ityāgamaṃ darśayati 
sūtre hy uktaṃ  yasmāditi daśakuśalāḥ karmapathāḥ prajñākāreṇa pratibhāvyamānā yāvac chrāvakayānaṃ saṃvartayanti 
tata uttaraṃ pariśodhitā yāvad pratyeka buddhyānaṃ saṃvartayanti
tata uttaraṃ pariśodhitā yāvad bodhisattvabhūmipariśuddhipāramitāpariśuddhicaryāvipulatvāya saṃvartante 
tata uttaraṃ pariśuddhitaratvād yāvad daśabalabalatvāya saṃvartante 
tasmāt tarhyasmābhis samāne'bhinirhāra iti vistaraḥ 
yasmād etad asyaiva bhavati dvitīyāyāṃ bhūmau tasmāt tarhītyādi 
tasmād dvitīyayā'grārthaṃ pratividhyatīti vijñāyate 
abhinirhāraḥ prayatnaḥ kṛtyaṃ vā 
sarvākārapariśodhanaṃ dharmadhātau kliṣṭā'kliṣṭamohanirākaraṇaṃ 
tasmāt tasyāṃ bhūmau śīlapāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavati viśiṣṭārthaprārthanayā sutarām ātmamātrīkaraṇāt 
tṛtīyayā tan niṣyandāgrārthaṃ 
pratividhyatīti prakṛtaṃ 
dharmadhātuprativedhaprabhāvitatvād buddhavacanasya 
yasmāt sarvākārapariśuddhadharmakāyasaṃjñakena dharmadhātuvaśena prabhāvito dharmadhātuniṣyandaḥ sūtrādiko deśanādharmaḥ 
dharmadhātvagratayā tanniṣYandadeśanādharmāgratayā dharmadhātupariśuddhinimittatvāc ca 
tena dharmadhātuniṣyandasya  śrutasyā'gratāṃ viditveti vistaraḥ 
teneti pratividhhadharmadhātunā 
śrutasyeti śrutasūtrādidharmasya tasyā'gratā viditveti nirvikalpena jñānena tathā pratyātmaṃ jñātvetyarthaḥ 
tad artham iti buddhavacanaśravaṇārthaṃ 
trisāhasramahāsāhasrapramāṇāyām apy agnikaṇḍāyām ātmānaṃ prakṣiped iti 
uktaṃ hi sūtre  sa ced idaṃ kaścidevaṃ brūyāt  evam ahaṃ tubhyam idaṃ dharmapadaṃ samyak sambuddhopanītaṃ bodhisattvacaryāpariśodhanaṃ saṃśrāvayeyaṃ sa cet tvaṃ mahatyām agnikhaḍāyāṃ samprajvalitāyām ekajvālībhūtāyām ātmānaṃ prapātayeḥ mahāntaṃ ca duḥkhavedanopakramaṃ svaśarīreṇopādadyāḥ 
tasyaivaṃ bhavati  utsahe'ham ekasyāpi dharmapadasya samyaksambuddhopanītasya bodhisattvacaryāpariśodhanasyārthāya trisāhasramahāsāhasralokadhātāv agniparipūrṇe brahmalokād ātmānam utsraṣṭuṃ 
kim punaḥ prākṛtāyām agnikhaḍāyāṃ 
api tu khalu punaḥ sarvair nirayāpāyaduḥkhasaṃvāsair apy asmābhis sarvabuddhadharmāḥ paryeṣitavyāḥ kiṃ punar manuṣyaduḥkhasaṃvāsair iti 
ata evāsyāmbhūmau kṣāntipāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavati śrutārthaṃ sarvakleśasahanādibhir apy abhedyatvāt 
caturthyā niṣparigrahārthaṃ dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatīti prakṛtaṃ 
caturthyam bhūmau samatvād anātmīyatvaṃ dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyati yasmān na dharmadhātoḥ kasyacit samatāstīti 
athavā sarvaviparyāsā'viṣayatvān na kasyacit parigrahaḥ 
svayam aviṣayatvān nā'tra kaścit parigrahaḥ 
yasmād dharmatṛṣṇā'pi vyāvartata ityāgamavacanaṃ 
evam arciṣmatyāṃ niṣprapañcena jñānena dharmadhātvadhigamād bodhipakṣadharmaprātpiḥ 
bodhisattvasya yā'pi sūtrādidharmatṛṣṇā pūrvam āsīt sā'pi vyāvartate 
dhyānasamādhisamāpattir dharmatṛṣṇetyanye 
tasmāt tasyābhūmau vīryapāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavati 
abhīkṣṇaṃ vānmanojalpasamatikrānte bodhipakṣair viharaṇāt 
pañcamyā santānābhedārthaṃ 
dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatīty adhikṛtaṃ 
atītā'nāgatavartamānānāṃ sarvabuddhānāṃ paramparato bodhisattvānāñca santānair ātmanaḥ  santānā'bhedaṃ paśyati 
daśabhiścittāśayaviśūddhisamatābhir ityāgamaṃ darśayati 
atītabuddhadharmaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca anāgatabuddhadharmaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca pratyutpannabuddhadharmaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca śīlaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca cittaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca dṛṣṭikānkṣāvimativilekhā'panayanaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca mārgā'mārgajñānaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca pratipatprahāṇajñānaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca sarvabodhipākṣika dharmottarottaravibhāvanaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca sarvasattvaparipācanaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca 
ābhiḥ samatābhiḥ sarvabuddhānāṃ santānā'bhedaṃ pratividhyati ālayavijñānaparāvṛttilakṣaṇadharmakāyasyā'bhinnatvāt 
tasmāt tasyāṃ bhūmau dhyānapāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavati paramārthataḥ satyākārabhāvanābahulatvāt 
ṣaṣṭhyā niṣsankleśaviśuddhyarthaṃ 
dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatīti sambadhyate 
pratītyasamutpādalakṣaṇaḥ sankleśaḥ tasminnāgantukāt prakṛtyā na sankliśyate 
prākṛtikaviśuddherna viśuddhyati 
evaṃ svasaṃvedyākāreṇa nirvikalpena jñānena dharmadhātuṃ pratividhyatītyatraivāgamaṃ darśayati 
pratītyasamutpāde nāsti sa kaścid dharmo yaḥ sankliśyate vā viśuddhyate veti prativedhāt 
ṣaṣṭhyāṃ bhūmau bodhisattvaḥ pratītyasamutpādaṃ vidhyati 
tatra na kasyacid dharmasya sankleśaṃ vyavadānaṃ vā pratividhyati dharmadhātoḥ prakṛtiprabhāsvaratvāt pratītyasamutpādāngañca sankleśamātratvāt na ca tad vyatirikto'nya ātmā'styātmīyo vā yasmin sankleśaḥ sankalpyate viśuddhir vā 
tasmād vā'syāṃ bhūmau prajñāpāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavati nissankleśa viśuddhyarthena pratītyasamutpādagāmbhīryā'vabodhād iti 
saptamyā'nānārthatvaṃ 
dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatītyadhikṛtaṃ 
tasyāṃ bhūmau bodhisattvo'bhibhavati sarvanimittasamudācārābhāvāt nimittasamudācāradvārakaṃśca nānātvasamudācāra iti 
ato nimittasamudācārā'bhāvāt saptamyā'nānātvārthaṃ dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatīty ucyate 
imam evārthaṃ pradarśayann āha  nirnimittatayā sūtrādidharmanimittanānātvā'samudācārād iti 
yaiḥ sūtrādidharmanimittair dharmadhātuṃ praviśati  tāni balān nānātvena tat praveśatat pṛṣṭalabdhayor abhimukhībhavanti yāvat ṣaṣṭhī bhūmiḥ 
saptamyāntu bhūmau sarvanimittaikarasākāreṇa jñanena dharmadhātor nimitttābhāvatvaṃ pratividhyatīti tāni tāni nimittāni na samudācaranti 
tasmāt tasyāṃ bhūmāv upāyaparamitā'tiriktatarā bhavati yataḥ sarvanimittāny animittatvena pratividhyati nimittakṛtaṃ ca vyavahāraṃ na virodhayati 
tat prativedhāc ca tasyām eva vaśitvaṃ pratilabhate 
aṣṭamyā'hīnadhikārthaṃ 
dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatīti sambadhyate 
dharmadhātoḥ prakṛtipariśuddhatvāt samalā'malā'vasthayor viśeṣā'bhāvāt 
ata evā'sau nityaṃ tathaiveti kṛtvā tathatetyucyate 
nimittā'bhāve kvacid api hīnatā nāsti 
sanimittatve kvacid apyadhikatvaṃ nāsti 
tathā hi nimittam evā'nimittam iti kiñcid anutpattikadharmakṣāntilābhād ityatraiva kāraṇaṃ 
aṣṭamyāṃ hi bhūmau bodhisattvo'nutpattikadharmakṣāntipratilambhād dharmadhātor abhyuccayā'bhāvatvam apacayā'bhāvatvaṃ caivaṃ pratividhyati 
sankleśe vyavadāne vā kasyacid dharmasya hānivṛddhyadarśanādityapūrvadharmā'nutpādāt 
caturthā vaśitā  nirvikalpavaśitā kṣetrapariśuddhivaśitā jñānavaśitā karmavaśitā ca 
tatra nirvikalpavaśitāśrayatvaṃ dharmadhātor veditavyaṃ anābhogenasarvanimittasamudācārā'bhāvāt 
saptamyām api nimittasamudācārābhāvaḥ sambhavaty abhisaṃskāreṇa 
iha tv anabhisaṃskāreṇeti viśeṣaḥ 
kṣetrapariśuddhivaśitāśrayatvaṃ cā'ṣṭamyāpratividhyatīti prakṛtaṃ 
kṣetrapariśuddhivaśitāśrayatvaṃ dharmadhātor yatheṣṭaṃ buddhakṣetraparṣanmaṇḍalasandarśanaśaktipratilambhāt 
tasmāt tasyāṃ bhūmau praṇidhānapāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavati nirvikalpakṣetravaśitālābhena kuśalanirantaraprayogāt 
jñānavaśitāśrayatvaṃ navamyā 
dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatīti prakṛutaṃ 
kathame tad vijñayate navamyā jñanavaṣitāśrayatvaṃ pratividhyatīti  ata āha  pratisaṃvil lābhāt 
asyāṃ hi bhūmau dharmārthaniruktipratibhānapratisaṃvido'nyair aparyāntāḥ pratilabhate 
ato'tra jñānavaśitāśrayatvaṃ dharmadhātoḥ pratividdham iti vijñāyate 
tasmāt tasyāṃ bhūmau balapāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavati prajñābalaviśeṣayogāt 
  karmavaśitāśrayatvaṃ daśamyā pratividhyatīti sambadhyate 
kartam etad gamyate  ata āha  yathecchaṃ nirmāṇaiḥ sattvārthakaraṇād iti 
niścayenā'nena daśamyām bhūmau dharmadhātoḥ karmavaśitāśrayatvaṃ pratividhyati tena tathāgatakarma svādhipatyaṃ pratilabhate 
tathā hi sugatatvād daśadiganantalokadhātusthitānāṃ sattvānāṃ nirmāṇakāyair yatheṣṭaṃ yasya yathā yasmin kāle yat kartavyaṃ tasya tathā tasmin kāle tat karoti 
tasmād asyām bhūmau jñānapāramitā'tiriktatarā bhavati 
dharmaparibhogasattvaparipākaviśeṣayogād iti 
evam āsāṃ yathoktānāṃ bodhisattvabhūmīnāṃ daśavidhadharmadhātuprativedhasarvākārapariṣodhanavibhandhabūtaṃ yad akliṣṭam ajñānam ekaikāyām api bhūmyām āvaraṇaṃ tat pratipakṣā bodhisattvānāṃ daśa bhūmayo vyavasthitāḥ navamyā daśamyāśca bhūmeḥ phalena viśeṣaḥ paridīpito nāvaraṇabheda prativedhaviśeṣeṇa tad vihārasya kāmapyanirūpyā'vasthāṃ gatatvāt 
sarvatragādyarthaprativedhaprayojanaṃ daśabhūmiṣu daśānām pāramitānāṃ viśeṣagatir yathākramaṃ 
tasmād etad evoktaṃ  bhūmyāvaraṇaṃ pāramitāviśeṣagatyāvaraṇam iti 
athavā sūtroktam eva samādhisamāpattyādikam uttarottarabhūmiviśiṣṭam sarvākāraṃ nānā'vasānaṃ phalaṃ sarvatragādyarthaprativedhaprayojanam iti 
  āvaraṇasamāsaḥ  prāg uktāni bahuvidhāni sarvāvaraṇāni dvayāvaraṇāntar gatānīti pradarśanārtham āha  samāsena punaḥ  kleśāvaraṇam ākhyātaṃ jñeyāvaraṇam eva ca 
katham etad gamyate  samāsato dvayam eva na punas tṛtīyam apy astīti 
ata āha  sarvāñ āvaraṇānīha iti 
atrāntargatānīti vākyaśeṣaḥ 
sarvāvaraṇāni dvayāvaraṇāntargatāni nānyat tṛtīyam astīti gamyate 
yataś ca sarvāvaraṇānyatraivāntargatānyatasyaiva sarvāvaraṇasangrāhakasya kleśajñeyāvaraṇadvayasya kṣayāt sarvāvaraṇebhyo mukhtiriṣyate sarvāvaraṇānā prahāṇa mityarthaḥ 
buddhabūmyā varaṇe'nākhyāte katham atraivāntar bhāvaḥ  na hy abhidhānād antarbhāvaḥ kin tarhi svabhāvāt 
api ca vyāpyāvaraṇavacanāt tad apy uktam eva 
anyathā ca pradeśāvaraṇam eva bhavatīti 
athavā buddhabhūmyāvaraṇasangrahārtham āha  sarvāṇyāvaraṇānīha yat kṣayān muktir iṣyate 
  buddhāvaraṇā'kṣaye na muktir astīti 
ataḥ śeṣāvaraṇavat tad apy āvaraṇam iti pratipāditam bhavati 
saukṣmyaprakarṣāvasthaṃ tv akliṣṭam ajñānam kleśavāsanāś ca buddhabhūmer āvaraṇam ucyate 
tasmāt saukṣmyaprakarṣād anyathā prekṣituṃ na śakyata ityevam ākhyānam bhavati 
  āvaraṇapiṇḍārthaḥ  mahāvaraṇaṃ yad vyāpi kleśajñeyāvaraṇaṃ bodhisattvagotrāṇāṃ 
pratanvāvaraṇaṃ prādeśikaṃ kleśāvaraṇam eva śrāvakādigotrāṇāṃ 
prayogāvaraṇaṃ yad udriktam iti teṣām eva rāgādicaritānāṃ taiḥ prayogā'prāpteḥ 
prāptyāvaraṇaṃ yat samam iti samabhāgacaritānāṃ taddhi prāptivibandhe vartate 
prāptiviśeṣāvaraṇaṃ yadādānavivarjane iti bodhisattvagotrāṇām adhigamaviśeṣāvaraṇatvāt 
apratiṣṭhitaṃ nirvāṇam adhigamaviśeṣaḥ 
eṣa caiva phalaviśeṣo veditavyāḥ 
samyak prayogāvaraṇaṃ yan navadhā kleśalakṣaṇam iti nava saṃyojanānyāvaraṇam iti vacanāt 
tāni samyak prayogasyāvaraṇaṃ bhavanti yathā tathoktaṃ 
hetvāvaraṇaṃ yac chubhādau daśavidhetvadhikārād iti 
taddhi śubhādihetuvibandhadvāreṇāvaraṇaṃ bhavantīti hetvāvaraṇam ucyate 
tattvapraveṣāvaraṇaṃ yad bodhipakṣyeṣv iti 
tair hi tattvam praviśati 
śubhānuttaryāvaraṇaṃ yat pāramitāsu tata uttari śubhābhāvāt 
tad viśeṣagatyāvaraṇaṃ yad bhūmiṣv iti pāramitā eva hi lokottaraviśeṣāśrayabhūtā bhūmaya ucyante 
sangrahāvaraṇaṃ yat samāsato dvividham iti kleśāvaraṇaṃ jñeyāvaraṇañca etena sarvāvaraṇasangrahāt 
piṇḍārthavacanaṃ sukhodgrahaṇadhāraṇārthaṃ 
piṇḍīkṛtaṃ hi sukham udgṛhyate dhāryate ceti 
āgamānusāriṇyāṃ mādhyantavibhāgaṭīkāyām ācāryabhadantasthi ramativyākhyātāyām āvaraṇaparicchedo dvitīyaḥ samāptaḥ 
   tattvaparicchedas tṛtīyaḥ   āvaraṇanirdeśānantaraṃ tattvanirdeśāvasaraḥ tad anantaram uddiṣṭatvād ityatas tattvam adhikṛtyāhetyāha 
tattvasya ca bahuvidhatvaṃ vidyate 
atas tadbhedā'navabodhe tattvasvarūpaṃ duravagamam ityatas tattvaprabhedam evādau pratipādayann āha  mūlalakṣaṇatattvaṃ iti vistareṇa daśavidhaṃ tattvaṃ 
tatra mūlatattve'nyatattvāntarbhāvasandarśanārthaṃ mūlatattvavacanaṃ 
mūlatattve parijñānaprahāṇasākṣātkaraṇasamprayuktasya doṣaprahāṇārthaṃ lakṣaṇatattvavacanaṃ 
saṃsārād udvegopāyapradarśanārtham aviparyāsatattvavacanaṃ 
udvignasya śrāvakayānaniryāṇasandarśanārthaṃ phalahetutattvavacanaṃ 
śrāvako hi catur āryasatyaprativedhabhāvanābhyāṃ niryāti 
sarvākārajñānapratipattyupāyasandarśanārtham audārika tattvavacanaṃ 
sarvāvaraṇaprahāṇopāyasandarśanārthaṃ sūkṣmatattvavacanaṃ 
suvyavasthitadharmanirdeśopāyasandarśanārthaṃ sarvaparapravādinigrahopāyasandarśanārthañca prasiddhatattvavacanaṃ 
same'pi dharmadhātau  kāraṇena svabhāvas trividho mūlatattvam ity ucyate tat pradarśayann āha  tatrā'nyatattvavyavasthāpanād iti 
tatrā'nyasya lakṣaṇāditattvasyā'ntargatatvam ityarthaḥ 
kim arthaṃ svabhāvas trividha upadhāryate  vyavahāraparamārthatad āśrayapradarśanārtham ity eke 
viparyāsatannimittatatpratipakṣālambanapradarśanārtham ityanye 
bodhisattvānām āvaraṇavisaṃyogārthaṃ prahāṇaparijñāsākṣāt kriyāvastupradarśanārtham ityanye 
prakṛtyā gambhīrasya prajñāpāramitārūpasya trisvabhāvadvāreṇā'bhrāntipratipattyartham ityanye 
evaṃ hy uktam abhidharmasutragrāthādvaye  māyādideśanāṃ bhūte kalpitān nāsti deśanā 
caturvidhaviśuddhes tu pariniṣpannadeśanā 
 śuddhiḥprakṛtivaimalyaṃ nārgatālambanan tathā 
viśuddhānāṃ hi dharmāṇāṃ caturdhā grahaṇam mataṃ 
iti 
laukikalokottaratatpṛṣṭhalabdhajñānaviṣayatvapradarśanārthaṃ yathāsambhavaṃ trayopādānaṃ svabhāvatam ity anye 
kim atra svabhāvatraye tattvam iṣyata iti 
aviparītārtho hi tattvārthaḥ 
kimatra svabhāvatraye'viparītatvam iti yasmāt svabhāvatraye tattvam iṣyata iti pṛcchābhiprāyaḥ 
svabhāvas trividho'sacca nityaṃ ityādi vistaraḥ 
parikalpitalakṣaṇaṃ nityam asad iti yatra hi bālānāṃ grāhyagrāhakavācyavācakābhiniveśaḥ svapna iva pravartate 
asacca sasvarūpābhāvāt kalpitasvabhāvaḥ 
tasmād asadātmakatvād abhrāntitvāc ca parikalpitalakṣaṇam asattvaṃ 
etat parikalpitasvabhāve'sattvam eva tattvam ucyate 
aviparītatvād iti aviparītārtho'tra tattvārthaṃ iti darśayati 
paratantralakṣaṇam sacca na ca tattvata iti 
grāhyagrāhakādikalpitavyavahārāśrayatvāt sattvaṃ 
grāhyagrāhakādyātmakatvenāsattvān na tathā tattvata iti 
etad eva pratipādayann āha bhrāntimātratvād iti 
etad uktaṃ bhavati  yat khyāti māyopādānavat tad asti 
yathā khyāti grāhyagrāhakākāreṇa naitad eva māyāpuruṣādivat 
ato bhrāntir iti 
ityetat paratantrasvabhāve tattvaṃ anyathā vidyamānasya svātmany avidyamānenākāreṇa prakhyānaṃ 
atrāpyaviparītatvād iti prakṛtatvāt sambadhyate 
  pariniṣpannalakṣaṇaṃ sadasat tattvataśceti 
sadasacca tattvaṃ pariniṣpannalakṣaṇaṃ 
dvayā'bhāvabhāvātmakatvāt sattvaṃ 
dvayā'bhāvātmakatvād asattvañca 
viśuddhyālambanatvāt tattvaṃ 
etat pariniṣpanne svabhāve tattvaṃ 
aviparītatvād iti sambadhyate 
  lakṣaṇatattvaṃ  svabhāvatrayasya tattvam uktaṃ na tu lakṣaṇam ityataḥ pṛcchati 
athavā mūlatattvā'nantaraṃ lakṣaṇatattvam uktaṃ taccā'prasiddham iti pṛcchati lakṣaṇatattvaṃ katamad iti 
ata āha  samāropā'pavādasya dharmapudgalayor iha 
iti vistaraḥ 
pudgaladharmayoḥ samāropā'pavādadarśanaṃ yasya jñānān na pravartate tat parikalpitasvabhāve tattvalakṣaṇam iti 
ātmarūpādayaś ca dharmās tat pratibhāsavijñānavyatiriktasya tadālambanabhūtāḥ paramārthataḥ santītyabhiniveśaḥ samāropadarśanaṃ 
vyavahārārtho'pi na santīty apavādadarśanaṃ 
anya āhuḥ 
pudgaladharmapratibhāsavijñānaparihāro'pavādadarśanam iti grāhā'pakṣepa iti cintyam etat 
pudgaladharmayoḥ samāropā'pavādadarśanaṃ yasya lakṣaṇasya paricchedān na pravartate tat parikalpitasvabhāve tattvalakṣaṇaṃ samāropāpavādavarjitaṃ veditavyaṃ 
tac ca vyavahāreṇa tattvaṃ na tu svabhāvena yasmāt parikalpitā'vabodhāddharmapudgalayoḥ samāropāpavādadarśanam na pravartate 
na jāyata ity arthaḥ 
grāhyagrāhakayoḥ samāropāpavādadarśanam iti vistaraḥ 
grāhyagrāhakapratibhāsabhrāntiryā dharmeṇa pudgalena ca gṛhyate sā yadi tattvenaivāstītyabhiniviśate evaṃ grāhyagrāhakasamāropaḥ 
atha grāhyasyeva grāhaksyāpyabhāvam abhiniviśate evaṃ grāhyagrāhakāpavādaḥ 
yasya lakṣaṇasya jñānād grāhyagrāhakayoḥ samāropā'pavādadarśanaṃ na pravartate tat paratantrasvabhāve tattvalakṣaṇaṃ samāropāpavādavarjitaṃ jñātavyaṃ 
tat punaḥ kalpitayā grāhyagrāhakātmatayā'sattvaṃ tad vyavahārāśrayatvena ca sattvaṃ 
evaṃ hi parijñānāt  paratantre samāropā'pavādadarśanaṃ na pravartate 
bhāvā'bhāva samāropāpavādadarśanam iti vistaraḥ 
kecidāhuḥ yadi śūnyatāṃ bhāva eveti samanupaśYati evaṃ bhāvasamāropadarśanaṃ bhavati 
athā'bhāva evetyevam abhāvadarśanaṃ 
etad ubhayam api bhāvābhāvadarśanaṃ 
yasya lakṣaṇasya jñānān na te bhāvābhāvadarśane pravartete tat pariniṣpannasvabhāve tattvalakṣaṇam iti 
tac ca bhāvā'bhāvāvimuktasvabhāvaṃ 
taj jñānāddhi pariniṣpanne svabhāve bhāvā'bhāvapradarśanaṃ na pravartata ityeke 
anye punar āhuḥ  dvayābhāvasvarūpaiva śūnyatetyabhāvasamāropāntaḥ bhāvā'bhāvavimuktātmakatve bhāvasvarūpasamāropaṇāt 
bhāvā'bhāvavimuktena dvayā'bhāvasvarūpeṇa nirvikalpajñānagocareṇā'sau nāstītyabhāvāpavādāntaḥ 
bhāvā'bhāvayoḥ pratyekaṃ samāropā'pavādadarśanasyābhisambandhāc cintyam etad vyākhyānādvayam ityaparaḥ 
bhāvo'tra dvayā'bhāvasya bhāvaḥ 
taṃ yadi bhāvam eva gṛhṇātyevaṃ bhāvaḥ samāropito bhavati 
yady abhāvam eva gṛhṇātyevam apodito bhavati 
bhāvo'pidvayābhāvasthaṃ yadi ucchedato gṛhṇātyevaṃ bhāvo'tyantābhāvatvena samāropito bhavati
atha dvayata eva gṛhṇātyevam apodito bhavati yasmādetad dvayābhāvena prabhāvitaṃ 
athavā taṃ bhāvā'bhāvasvarūpeṇa gṛhṇātyevaṃ samāropito bhavati 
athā'bhāvam eva gṛhṇātyevaṃ saṃkleśo vyavadānañcā'poditam bhavatīti 
etad antadvayavidhātanaṃ pariniṣpannatve tattvalakṣaṇaṃ 
nanu pūrvam api trisvabhāvalakṣaṇam uktaṃ  arthād abhūtakalpāc ca dvayābhāvāc ca deśitaḥ 
iti 
tatra svabhāvo lakṣaṇam iha tu cihnam iti nāsti punaruktatā 
yajjñānān na pravarteta taddhi tattvasya lakṣaṇaṃ 
iti pudgalādisamāropāpavādadarśanaṃ yaj jñānān na pravartate tan mūlatattvasya lakṣaṇaṃ 
  aviparyāsatattvaṃ   lakṣaṇatattvānantaram aviparyāsatattvaṃ vaktavyaṃ tad anantaram uddiṣṭatvād ityata āha  aviparyāsatattvam iti vistaraḥ 
anityaduḥkhaśūnyā'nātmato hi nityasukhaśuddhātmaviparyāsapratipakṣatvād aviparyāsatattvam ity ucyate 
mūlatattve tad anyatattvāntarbhāvaḥ pūrvaṃ pratijñāta ityataḥ pṛcchati  mūlatattve katham iti vistaraḥ 
anityāditeti 
anityādayo ye'nityaduḥkhaśūnyā'nātmaprakārās te'nityādayaḥ 
tad bhāvo'nityāditā 
mūlatattve'viparyāsatattvasyāntarbhāvapradarśanārtham āha  asadartho hy anityārtha iti vistaraḥ 
trividho hy anityārthaḥ  asadarthaḥ utpādavyārthaḥ samalāmalatārthaś ca 
yaḥ sarvadā tathāsti sa nityaḥ 
tad viparīto'nityaḥ 
teṣu yathākramam iti 
tatra sarvadā'sadarthā'nityārthena parikalpitasvabhāvo'nityaḥ 
asannityam anityam iti niruttinyāyena veditavyamityanye 
pratikṣaṇamutpādavyahalakṣaṇenā'nityārthenā'nityaḥ paratantrasvabhāvaḥ 
tasya pratyayotpādyatvād vināśe cā'hetukatvāt 
samalāmalatā'rthalakṣaṇenāgantukenā'nityārthenā'nityo'vikāradharmo'pi pariniṣpannasvabhāva iti 
duḥkhamādānalakṣmākhyaṃ iti vistaraḥ 
duḥkham api trividhaṃ  upādānaduḥkhaṃ lakṣaṇaduḥkhaṃ sambandhaduḥkhañca 
tatra kalpitasvabhāva upādānato duḥkhaṃ 
aparijñātenehā'mutra vā duḥkham upādīyata iti duḥkhaṃ 
yathā ca tenā'parijñātena duḥkham upādīyate tat pradarśayann āha   śaśaviṣāṇādisvarūpavad bhrāntyā na kenacit prakāreṇa yenāpi sattvaṃ grāhyaṃ nāsti ityabhāva evā'sya śūnyateti 
atadbhāvaśūnyatā paratantrasya 
etad eva pratipādayann āha  paratantralakṣaṇaṃ tathā nāsti yathā bālair dvayātmanā parikalpyate 
na tu sarvathā nāsti yathā cā'sti tathā śuddhalaukikajñānenādhigamyate 
tasyā'tadbhāvaḥ śūnyateti 
prakṛtiśūnyatā pariniṣpannasya 
ata evāha  pariniṣpannalakṣaṇaṃ dvayābhāvasvabhāvatvāc chūnyatāsvabhāvam eveti 
tasmāt prakṛtir eva svabhāva evā'sya śūnyatā 
alakṣaṇañca nairātmyaṃ iti vistaraḥ 
trividhaṃ nairātmyaṃ  alkṣaṇanairātmyaṃ vilakṣaṇanairātmyaṃ svalakṣaṇanairātmyañca 
tatra parikalpitasya svabhāvasya lakṣaṇā'bhāvād alakṣaṇam eva nairātmyaṃ 
ata evāha  parikalpitasya svabhāvasya lakṣaṇam eva nāstītyalakṣaṇam evāsya nairātmyaṃ nānyena prakāreṇeti darśayati 
paratantrasya vilakṣaṇanairātmyaṃ yasmāt paratantrasyāsti lakṣaṇaṃ vasturūpaṃ 
na tu tad yathā bālaiḥ parikalpyate dvayatvena 
tad vilakṣaṇam iti parikalpitalakṣaṇenā'sadṛśaṃ 
paratantralakṣaṇaṃ tan nairāmyaṃ 
evaṃ parikalpitenātmanā nairātmyam asya darśītaṃ bhavati 
svalakṣaṇaṃ nairātmyaṃ pariniṣpannasya 
yataḥ pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvo grāhyagrāhakābhāvarūpatvān nairātmyam eveti svalakṣaṇam asya nairātmyam iti pariniṣpannasya dharmasya nairātmyasvabhāvatāṃ darśayati 
kaḥ punar anayoḥ śūnyatā'nātmatayor viśeṣaḥ  yadyatra nāsti tat tena śūnyaṃ 
yat tu yasyātmā svabhāvo na bhavati tat tenā'nātmetyayam anayor viśeṣa ity eke 
arthataḥ ko'pi viśeṣo nāsti vyavasthānabhedena tu bhedaḥ 
yasmādyadyatra nāsti tena tasya niḥsvabhāvatām upādāya nairātmyam itarasya tu tatrā'niṣpannasvabhāvatām upādāya śūnyatvam iti 
  trividhe mūlatattve samāropāpavādāntayoḥ pratipakṣeṇāgantukamalapradarśanena ca yathākramaṃ trividhā'nityatā paridīpitā 
sā'sadartha'nityatā utpādabhangā'nityatā samalanirmalā'nityatā ca 
evaṃ yāvat trividhaṃ nairātmyam ityuktam aviparyāsatattvaṃ 
  phalahetutattvaṃ  tad anantaraṃ phalahetutattvaṃ vaktavyam ityata āha  phalahetumayantattvaṃ mūlatattvaṃ iti vistaraḥ 
tatra sankleśapakṣam adhikṛtya duḥkhasatyaṃ phalatattvaṃ 
samudayasatyaṃ hetutattvaṃ vyavadānapakṣe'pi nirodhasatyaṃ phalatattvaṃ mārgasatyaṃ hetutattvaṃ 
evaṃ duḥkhādīni catvāri satyāni phalahetutattvaṃ 
mūlatattve duḥkhasamudayanirodhamārgasatyam ityuktaṃ 
tac ca na vijñāyate kathaṃ mūlatattvaṃ duḥkhādisatyasvabhāvam ityataḥ pṛcchati  kathaṃ trividhaṃ mūlatattvaṃ duḥkhādisatyam iti  ata āha  yatas tad anityādilakṣaṇaṃ  duḥkhasatyaṃ tato mataṃ 
iti 
anityaduḥkhaśūnyānātmatāyā duḥkhasatyalakṣaṇatvāt tac ca samastaṃ pratyekaṃ kalpitādiṣv astīti vistareṇoktaṃ 
ataḥ kalpitādayaḥ pratyekaṃ duḥkhasatyatvenābhipretā iti 
trividhena samudayā'rthena mūlatattvaṃ samudayasatyaṃ yathākramaṃ 
sa eva samudayo na jñāyata ityata āha  trividhaḥ samudayārthaḥ 
vāsanā'tha samutthānam avisaṃyoga eva ca 
iti 
trividhaḥ samudayo vāsanāsamudayaḥ samutthānasamudayaḥ avisaṃyogasamudayaś ca 
tatra vāsanāsamudayaḥ parikalpitasvabhāvo veditavyaḥ 
ata āha  parikalpitasvabhāvābhiniveśavāsaneti 
asti hi parikalpite svabhāve'stītyabhiniveśam upādāya laukikā dharmā vikalpakleśavāsanāṃ vyavasthāpayanti na tu vigatābhiniveśā lokottarā 
tataḥ parikalpitasvabhāvo vāsanāsamudaya ucyate 
samutthānasamudayaḥ paratantraḥ 
samutthāna ātmalābhaḥ 
sa yato bhavati sa samutthānasamudayaḥ  samudetyasmād iti kṛtvā 
sa punaḥ kiṃsvarūpa ityata āha  karmakleśā iti 
te ca vastusvarūpatvāt paratantrasvabhāvaḥ 
avisaṃyogasamudayasthatāyā iti 
katham ityata āha  āvaraṇā'visaṃyoga iti 
etad uktaṃ bhavati  yāvadāvaraṇair na visaṃyuktā tathatā tāvat samudeti duḥkham iti 
āvaraṇair avisaṃyuktā vā tathatā samudayadharmateti samudayanāmmlābha iti 
 trividhena nirodhena mūlatattvaṃ nirodhasatyaṃ 
tac ca na vijñāyata ityata āha  trividho nirodhaḥ  svabhāvadvayanotpattir malaśāntidvayaṃ mataṃ 
iti 
tatra svabhāvā'nutpattiḥ parikalpitasya yasya hi niḥsvabhāvatvād ātyantikyanutpattir vandhyāputravat 
grāhyagrāhakayor anutpattiḥ paratantrasya 
tasyāpi grāhyagrāhakasvarūpābhyām atyantarahitatvād dvayabhrāntyātmanā'nutpattiḥ 
malaśāntidvayaṃ pariniṣpannaḥ 
ca śabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ 
tat punar na vijñāyata ityata āha  pratisaṃkhyānirodhatathatākhyam iti 
malaṃ dvividhaṃ rāgādyāvaraṇaṃ parikalpitaś ca 
tatrā'nāsveṇa jñānenāśrayād bīja uddhṛte rāgādimalānām atyantam anutpādātmikā śāntiḥ pratisaṃkhyānirodhaḥ 
tathatāgocareṇā'dvayajñānena parikalpitamalasyā'nutpādātmikā śāntis tathatā 
etaddhi dvayaṃ pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvaḥ 
eṣa trividho nirodhaḥ kalpitādau mūlatattve yathāsaṃkhyaṃ vijñeyaḥ 
  anye tu tathatāprativedhena kleśaparikalpitamaladvayaśāntir iti malaśāntistathatety ucyate dvayanirodhaḥ prakṛtinirodhaśceti vacanāt 
prakṛtir iti tathatā prakṛtiprabhāsvaratvāc cittasyeti 
atas tathatālambanādyo nirodhaḥ sa prakṛtinirodha ity ucyate 
niruddhamātraṃ pratisaṃkhyānirodhaḥ 
nirodhyate'syām iti nirodhastathatetyapare 
nirodhasya punar anutpādātmakatvāt sarve svabhāvānutpattyādikaṃ saṃkṣipya nirodhasatyam ity ucyate 
ukto nirodhasatyasya mūlatattve'ntarbhāvaḥ 
tad anantaraṃ tu mārgasatyam antarbhāvayitavyam ityataḥ pṛcchati  mārgasatyaṃ trividhamūlatattve kathaṃ vyavasthāpyata ityata  parijñāyāṃ prahāṇe ca ityādi 
parikalpitasya parijñāna iti 
parikalpitato'tyantam asanneveti tasya parijñānam eva na prahāṇaṃ 
na hyasataḥ prahāṇaṃ yujyate 
paratantrasya parijñāne prahāṇe ca 
paratantro hi yathā khyāti tathā'sattvaṃ vijñeyaṃ na tu sarvātmatvenāsattvaṃ kalpitavat 
karmakleśayor bhāvātmatvāt prahātavyaś ca 
pariniṣpannasya praijñāne prāptisākṣātkaraṇe ceti 
pariniṣpanno hi bhāvābhāvavinirmuktalakṣaṇam ataḥ parijñeyaḥ āśrayaparāvṛttitāyāś ca 
āśayaparāvṛttitā vinirmuktadharmakāyatvena sākṣātkartavyeti śūnyatā parijñeyā 
nirodhaḥ sākṣātkartavyaḥ prāptisākṣātkriyayā 
ubhayaṃ cobhathetyanye 
dvividhā hi parijñā  jñānaparijñā prahāṇaparijñā ca 
tatra jñānaparijñāyaparijñeyaṃ prathamaṃ tṛtīyañca 
dvitīyaṃ tūbhayaparijñeyaṃ 
sākṣātkriyāpi dvidhā  jñānasākṣātkriyā prāptisākṣātkriyā ceti 
tatra jñānasākṣātkriyayā trayam api sākṣātkartavyaṃ 
prāptisākṣātkriyayā tu tṛtīyam eva 
evam atra mūlatattve parijñā prahāṇasākṣātkriyāyāṃ mārgasatya vyavasthānaṃ veditavyaṃ na tu tatrāntarbhāvāt 
atra ca satyacatuṣṭayena yaḥ sankleśo yataś ca tayoś ca viśuddhir yā yataśca tat paridīpitaṃ 
anukramas tveṣāṃ yathā'bhisamayam iti 
 audārikasūkṣmatattvaṃ   audārikasūkṣmatattvañceti 
audārikatattvaṃ saṃvṛtisatyaṃ sūkṣmatattvaṃ tu paramārthasatyaṃ 
yata ādāvaudārikeṇa sattvān paripācayati paripakvāṃs tu sūkṣmeṇa vimocayati ataḥ pūrvam audārikaṃ paścāt sūkṣmaṃ 
kārikā'nuguṇyād viparyayoktiḥ 
tatrā'samāhitajñānaviṣayatvāt saṃvṛti satyam audārikatattvaṃ 
samāhitajñānaviṣayatvāt paramārthasatyaṃ sūkṣmatattvaṃ 
athavā vijñānaviṣayatvād audārikaṃ 
jñānaviṣayatvāt sūkṣmaṃ 
sarvatattvānāṃ mūlatattve'ntarbhāvaḥ pratijñāta ityataḥ pṛcchati  tan mūlatattve kathaṃ veditavyaṃ  ityata āha  prajñaptipratipattitaḥ 
tathodbhāvanayaudāraṃ iti 
prajñaptiḥ pratipatīr udbhāvanā caudārikatattvaṃ mūlatattve veditavyaṃ 
etad eva pratipādayann āha  trividhā hi saṃvṛtir iti vistaraḥ 
asato'rthasya rūpaṃ ghaṭaḥ paṭaśceti vyavasthānaṃ prajñaptisaṃvṛtiḥ 
rūpavedanāsaṃjñādisvabhāvaviśeṣeṇa nāmābhilāpaḥ prajñaptisaṃvṛtir ityanye 
abhilāpāpekṣayā yad vyavahriyate rūpaṃ vedaneti vā tat prajñaptisaṃvṛtir iti kecit 
taccaitad asattvāt parikalpitaḥ svabhāvaḥ 
pratipattisaṃvṛtir vikalpena yena rūpādayo ghaṭādayaś ca  vijñānanirbhāsād abahirbhūtam api bahirbhūtam iva vasturūpeṇa yathā vyavasthānam abhiniviśate sa vikalpaḥ pratipattisaṃvṛtiḥ 
udbhāvanāsaṃvṛtiśceti 
caśabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ 
vikalpā'bhilāpātikrāntasyāpi pariniṣpannasya śūnyatā tathatā samalā nirmaletyevam ādibhiḥ paryāyaiḥ sandarśanam udbhāvanāsaṃvṛtiḥ 
tayā trividhayā saṃvṛttyā saṃvṛtisatyatvaṃ mūlatattve yathākramaṃ veditavyaṃ 
saṃvṛtir vyavahāraḥ 
prajñaptir ityabhidhānaṃ 
arthābhāve'bhidhānamātreṇa vyavahāraḥ prajñaptisaṃvṛtiḥ 
ata evārthābhāvāt prajñaptisaṃvṛtyā parikalpitaḥ saṃvṛtisatyaṃ 
avidyamāne'rthe'rthābhiniveśaḥ pratipattis tayā vyavahāraḥ pratipattisaṃvṛtiḥ 
sā punar abhiniveśavikalpaḥ 
tasmāt pratipattisaṃvṛtyā saṃvṛttisatyaṃ paratantraḥ 
tathatādiśabdair nirabhilāpyasya dharmadhātor yā saṃsūcanā sodbhāvanā 
tayā dharmadhātor vyavahāra udbhāvanāsaṃvṛtiḥ 
ataścodbhāvanāsaṃvṛtyā pariniṣpannaḥ saṃvṛtisatyaṃ 
tatra prajñaptyudbhāvanāsaṃvṛtyor avasarasangrahavyavasthānaṃ veditavyaṃ na tu svabhāvata iti 
uktaṃ saṃvṛtisatyaṃ 
 idānīṃ paramārthasatyaṃ vaktavyam ityata āha  paramārthantu ekataḥ 
iti 
kalpitaparatantrayoḥ paramārthato'sambhavatvaṃ 
satyaṃ punar ekasmāt  pariniṣpannād eva svabhāvād veditavyaṃ 
sa punaḥ pariniṣpannaḥ kena kāraṇena paramārtha ucyate  ityata āha  arthaprāptipratyayā hi paramārthas tridhā mataḥ 
iti 
trividho hi paramārthaḥ  arthaparamārthaḥ prāptiparamārthaḥ prayatiparamārthaś ca 
tatrārthaparamārthas tathatā 
paramo hi lokottaraṃ jñānaṃ tasyārtho viṣaya iti kṛtvā tathatā paramārtha ity ucyate indriyārthavat 
tadeva pradarśayann āha  paramasya jñānasyārtha iti kṛtveti 
ālambanabhāvena vyavasthānād ityarthaḥ 
jñānā'pṛthaktvāt tasmin kāla ālambanaṃ na vartate vijñaptimātrapratibhāsavat 
tadyathā yeṣāṃ vijñaptimātraṃ kṣamate na teṣāṃ rūpādivijñaptimātraṃ muktvā rūpādipratibhāsā vidyante 
prāptiparamārtho nirvāṇaṃ ekāntanirmatathatāśrayaparāvṛttilakṣaṇam 
kathaṃ paramārtha ityata āha  paramo'rtha iti kṛtvā 
paramaścāsāvarthaśceti kṛtvā paramārthaḥ 
tatra saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtadharmāgratvāt paramaḥ mārgaprayojanatvād arthaḥ 
tathā hi mārgo nirvāṇaprāptiprayojanaḥ 
nirvāṇantvarthaḥ sarvāpakāradoṣarahitatvāt 
yasmād doṣasahito'nartha ity ucyate 
pratipattiparamārtho mārgaḥ 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  paramo'syārtha iti kṛtvā 
viṣayaḥ prayojanaṃ vārthaḥ 
viṣayas tathatā prayojanaṃ nirvāṇaṃ 
viṣayadvāreṇa parama ucyamāne katham anyo'nyasamarthanaṃ na syāt  anyo'nyasamarthanaṃ cet ko doṣa iti  niścayābhāvaḥ 
naivaṃ bhaviṣyaty anyonyasamarthanāt siṃhavanavat 
katham asaṃskṛtaṃ nirvāṇākhyaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ ca mārgākhyaṃ pariniṣpannasvabhāva ucyate  paramārthasatyaṃ hi pariniṣpannasvabhāvo nirdiṣṭaṃ 
mārgas tu pariniṣpannon na yujyate 
na pūrvāparabhāgābhāva iti kṛtvā 
tasmān na mārgaḥ paramārthasatyaṃ na cā'pariniṣpanne paramārthasatyasaṃgraha iti 
ata āha  nirvikārā'viparyāsapariniṣpattito dvayaṃ 
iti 
athavā katham asaṃkṛtaṃ nirvāṇākhyaṃ saṃskṛtañca mārgākhyaṃ pariniṣpannasvabhāva  ucyate 
pariniṣpanno hi tathatā 
eṣā ca dvayalakṣaṇarahitatvaṃ paratantrasyeti na nirvāṇamārgayoḥ pariniṣpannatā yujyate 
tadidam avācyaṃ yatas tatra dvayābhāvaḥ pariniṣpanna eva 
na tu dvayābhāva eva pariniṣpanna iti tad anyapratiṣedhaḥ 
atas tad anyac ca 
nirvikārā'viparyāsapariniṣpattito dvayam api pariniṣpanna iti sambaddhyate asaṃskṛtaṃ nirvāṇaṃ tathatā ca 
asaṃskṛtam ananyathābhāvād avikārapariniṣpattyā pariniṣpannaṃ 
saṃskṛtaṃ mārgasaṃgṛhītaṃ nānyatra 
aviparyāsapariniṣpattyā pariniṣpannam iti sambadhyate 
katham ityato 'bravīt  punar jñeyavastuviparyāsād iti 
yasmān na punar jñeye viparyāsam āpadyate tasmān na mārgo'pi pariniṣpanna ityataśca dvayor api saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtayoḥ pariniṣpannatvaṃ pṛthag abhiprāyād ityavirodhaḥ 
  prasiddhatattvaṃ  tatra  lokaprasiddham ekasmāt iti 
yathābhidhānam asambhavāt parikalpitād eva tat nānyasmāt tasya tu svarūpaṃ na jñāyata ityata āha  yasmin vastunīti vistaraḥ 
saṃketaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñitasambandhajñānaṃ 
saṃstavas tasya vāramvāramprayogadarśanaṃ 
tatrā'nupraviṣṭayā buddhyeti 
kaḥ punar buddheḥ saṃketasaṃstavānupraveśaḥ  tat smaraṇāt 
etad uktaṃ bhavati  saṃketasaṃstavānusmaraṇānugatatyā buddhyā sarveṣāṃ laukikānāṃ śāstravidāṃ tad avidāṃ ca vyāhṛtibhāve kvacit  pṛthyvyeveyam ityādivaṃśādidarśanatulyateti 
etal lokaprasiddhaṃ tattvaṃ 
lokaprasiddhyā tat tathaiveti kṛtvā 
trayādyuktiprasiddhakaṃ 
iti 
trividham api hi svabhāvam adhikṛtya yuktiḥ kriyata iti 
ataḥ svabhāvatrayeṇa yuktiprasiddhatvaṃ vyavasthāpyate 
tac ca na vijñāyata ityataḥ pradarśayann āha  yat satāṃ yuktārthapaṇḍitānām ityādi 
tatra santo ye yuktārthapaṇḍitāḥ 
tārkikā ye mīmāṃsakāḥ 
pūrvasya vyākhyānāśayasya paścān nirdeśoktiḥ 
athavā santo'nveṣakāḥ kiṃ kuśalam iti 
yuktā'rthapaṇḍitā apekṣākāryakāraṇopapattidharmatāyukticatuṣṭayā'viruddhārthakṛtakauśalāḥ 
tārkikās tuhapohasamarthās tathāgatapravacanasamāśrayeṇā viparītaśāstrapraṇetāraḥ 
mīmāṃsakāḥ svaparaśāstrapaṇḍitāḥ śreyodoṣaparīkṣakāḥ 
kecit mīmāṃsakā iti na paṭhanti 
ta evam āhuḥ  satām ityukte ke punaḥ santaḥ ityata āha  yuktārthapaṇḍitā iti 
te ca tarkabhūmau bhāvābhūmau ca vyavasthitatvād dvividhāḥ 
tasmāt tārkikā ity ucyanta iti 
teṣāṃ ca kaścil lokaprasiddhānusārītyata āha pramāṇatrayaṃ niśrityeti pramāṇatrayāvirodhena 
pramāṇatrayaṃ punaḥ pratyakṣam anumānam āgamaś ca 
tatra pratyakṣaṃ pañcendriyajaṃ mānasaṃ ca sukhaduḥkhādisamvedanaṃ 
trirūpalingenānumeuyārthajñānam anumānaṃ 
āptavāgāgamaḥ 
āptāḥ punar anṛtahetuvimuktāḥ 
athavā pratyakṣānumānāgamaprasiddhena hetunā dṛṣṭāntena ca tat prasiddhasyaiva sādhyasya paramprati sādhyatvāt pramāṇatrayaṃ niśrityeti 
upapattisādhanayuktyā prasiddhaṃ vastu iti 
upapattis trirūpaṃ lingaṃ sādhyapratipādanopāyatvāt 
upapatteḥ sādhanam upapattisādhanaṃ trirūpalingākhyānaṃ tena tat pratipādanāt 
yuktir upāyo yena prayoganiyamena lingasya trirūpyam ākhyāyate 
athavopapātir ananyathāsambhavaḥ 
sādhanyuktir avayavasambandhaḥ 
upapatteḥ sādhanayuktir iti vigrahaḥ 
athavopapattir eva sādhanayuktir iti vigrahaḥ 
anyasādhanayuktibhyo vyavacchedārtham upapattigrahaṇaṃ 
evaṃ pramāṇatrayaṃ niśrityopapattisādhana yuktyā yat prasiddhaṃ vastu trayāṇāṃ bhāvanām anyatamat tad yuktiprasiddham ucyate 
uktaṃ prasiddhatattvaṃ 
  viśuddhigocaratattvaṃ   tad anantaraṃ tu viśuddhiviṣayaṃ vaktavyam ityata āha  viśuddhigocaratattvaṃ dvividham iti 
tattu yathā dvividhaṃ tat pradarśayann āha  kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānagocaraṃ jñeyāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānagocarañceti 
kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhiḥ kleśāvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ 
kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhaye kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhau vā jñānaṃ kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānaṃ 
kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhiprayojanaṃ tan nimittaṃ vetyarthaḥ 
tasya kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānasya gocaram iti viṣaya ityarthaḥ 
evaṃ jñeyāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānasya gocaram api vaktavyaṃ 
tatra kleśāvaraṇaṃ sarve darśanabhāvanāmārgaprahātavyāḥ kleśopakleśā ityato darśanabhāvanātad upacārajñanaviṣayaṃ śrāvakapratyekabuddhānāṃ yat tattvaṃ duḥkhasamudayanirodhamārgasatyam ucyate tat kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānasya gocaraṃ 
jñātavyaṃ jñeyaṃ 
tac ca sarvātmanā pañca vidyāsthānāni 
tāni punar adhyātmavyākaraṇahetucikitsāsarvaśilpakarmasthānākhyāni 
tatra jñānavibandhabhūtam akliṣṭam ajñānaṃ jñeyāvaraṇaṃ 
tad viśodhanaṃ lokottarajñānānulomādhimukticaryābhūmisangṛhītaṃ tat pṛṣṭhalabdhañca jñānaṃ 
tat punar bodhisattvatathāgatasantānavartiṃ 
tasya ca tathatā sarvatragādyarthamukhenālambanam ityato jñeyāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānagocarasya tattvaṃ tathatā 
phalahetutattvoktyā sūkṣmatattvoktyā ca viśūddhigocaraṃ dvividham api nirdiṣṭam eveti punar asya vidhānaṃ vyarthaṃ 
na vyarthaṃ 
yatas tat phalahetutattvaṃ sūkṣmaṃ ca vastu vyavasthānata uktaṃ 
atra tvāvaraṇaṃ yathā viśuddhyate tathaitan nirdiṣṭaṃ 
idaṃ dvividhaṃ viśuddhigocaram ekasmāt pariniṣpannād eva svabhāvāt kīrtitaṃ 
atraiva kāraṇam āha  na hyanyaḥ svabhāvo viśuddhijñānagocaro bhavatīti 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  abhūtaparikalpasya dauṣṭhulyamaladvayena samalabhūtatvāt parikalpitasya cāsattvāt 
dvividhajñānaviṣayasya tu dharmatāyā viśuddhiviṣayatattvaṃ pariniṣpannād eva vyavasthāpyata iti 
uktaṃ viśuddhigocaratattvaṃ 
  sangrahatattvaṃ   tad anantaraṃ tu sangrahatattvaṃ vaktavyam ityataḥ pṛcchati  kathaṃ trividhe mūlatattve sangrahatattvaṃ veditavyam iti 
sangrahatattvaṃ trividhe mūlatattve saṃgṛhītaṃ pradarśayann āha  nimittasya vikalpasya nāmnaśca dvayasaṃgrahaḥ 
iti vistaraḥ 
dvaye paratantre parikalpite ca sangrahaḥ 
tatra sangrahatattvaṃ pañca vastūnītyata āha  yathāyogaṃ pañca vastūny ārabhyeti 
yathāyogaṃ mūlatattve pañca vastūni sangṛhītāni veditavyāni na tu yathākramaṃ 
pañca punar vastūni nimittaṃ nāma vikalpas tathatā samyag jñānaṃ ceti 
sarvasya jñeyasyāsmin pañcavidhe vastuni sangrahād etat pañcavidhaṃ vastu saṃgrahatattvam ity ucyate 
tatra nimittam ālayavijñānaṃ kliṣṭamanaḥpravṛttivijñānāni ca 
anyo'nyanimittabhāvān nimittaṃ 
nāma yat tasyaiva nimittasyā'nabhilāpyasyāpi sato'kṣinikocavad sūcakam abhidhānaṃ 
yathoktanimittasvabhāvaviśeṣavikalpakāstraidhātukapratisaṃyuktāścittacaittā vikalpaḥ 
śūnyatā tathatā 
samyag jñānaṃ lokottaraṃ tathatālambanaṃ 
kramaḥ punar eṣāṃ tatra sankleśaprajñaptivastutvān nimittam ādau 
sankleśaprajñaptitvād anantaraṃ nāma 
yathā nāma tathā sankleśaprajñaptivastuvikalpatvāt tad anantaraṃ vikalpaḥ 
sa ca sankleśas tathatāsamyag jñānena nirudhyata iti tad anantaraṃ tathatā samyag jñānañceti kecit 
bhrāntinimittaṃ bhrāntidauṣṭhulyaṃ tan nimittam iti 
tasmād bhrāntis tasya nimittaṃ prakṛtiśamas tatra jñānaṃ 
ity anayā gāthayā'sya pañcavidhasya vastuno'rtha ity anye 
tatrā'dhyātmikacakṣurādivijñānsaṃgṛhītāyā bhrānter nimittaṃ bāhyādhyātmikā rūpādicakṣurādisaṃgṛhītā bhrāntiḥ 
tasyā bāhyādhyātimikāyā bhrānter nimittaṃ dauṣṭhulyaṃ 
tat punar ālayavijñānavāsanā 
tasyā vāsanāyā nimittaṃ saiva bāhyādhyātmikabhrāntiḥ 
tasmāt tatrābhilāpapravṛttiḥ 
abhilāpavaśāc ca vāsanāyā avasthānam ālayavijñāne 
prakṛtiśama iti tathatā 
prakṛtyā kliṣṭatvād dharmadhātoḥ 
tatra ca jñānam iti tathatālambanaṃ mārgasaṃgṛhītaṃ yaj jñānaṃ 
tatra nimittavikalpayoḥ paratantreṇa sangrahaḥ hetupratyayotpāditatvāt 
  nāmnaḥ parikalpiteneti 
yathānāmārthābhāvān nāmnaḥ parikalpitena sangrahaḥ 
evam adhikārasangrahaḥ parikalpitena nāmno na svabhāvasangrahaḥ iti yad uktaṃ niṣsvabhāvasiddhatvāt parikalpitaḥ svabhāvo nimittādipañcavastubhir na sangṛhīta iti tan na virudhyate tatra svabhāvasangrahasya vivakṣitatvāt 
samyag jñānasatattvasya iti 
sadā śobhanaṃ vā tattvaṃ satattvaṃ tathatā śūnyatālambanādvayajñānaṃ tat pṛṣṭhalabdhaśuddhalaukikaṃ ca samyag jñānaṃ 
tathatāsamyag jñānayor avikārā'viparyāsapariniṣpattyā yathākramaṃ pariniṣpannatvād ekenaiva pariniṣpannena svabhāvena sangraha iti 
tad uktaṃ sangrahatattvaṃ 
  prabhedatattvaṃ  idānīṃ prabhedatattvaṃ katividhaṃ kathañca tanmūlatattve sangṛhītam iti na vijñāyata ityataḥ pṛcchati  prabhedatattvaṃ mūlatattve katham veditavyam iti 
ata āha  saptavidhaṃ prabhedatattvaṃ 
katham ityata āha  pravṛttitattvaṃ lakṣaṇatattvam iti vistaraḥ 
yaiva ca sandhinirmocaranasūtre saptavidhā tathatā nirdiṣṭā pravṛttitathatāyāvat samyag pratipattitathateti saivā'tra saptavidhaṃ prabhedatattvam ityuktā pravṛttitattvaṃ yāvat samyakpratipattitattvam iti 
tatra pravṛttitattvaṃ yā saṃsārā'navarāgratā saiva ca pravṛtti tathatā yasmān na jātu tasyāgratāyogo bhavati 
lakṣaṇatattvaṃ pudgaladharmanairātmyaṃ 
  ananyatvāc caturvidhalakṣaṇatathatā 
vijñaptitattvaṃ vijñaptimātratā dharmāṇāṃ 
nirvikalpaṃ jñānaṃ vijñaptyāśrayabhāvād vijñptitattvam ity apare 
ananyathābhāvatvād vijñaptitattvasya vijñaptitathatocyate 
sanniveśatattvaṃ duḥkhasatyaṃ saṃskārāṇāṃ duḥkhasanniviṣṭatvāt 
saiva ca tathatā nityaṃ tathaiveti kṛtvā 
mithyāpratipattitattvaṃ samudayasatyaṃ 
sā punar yā teṣu saṃskāreṣu guṇadarśanena pravṛttiḥ 
viśuddhitattvaṃ kleśajñeyāvaraṇaviśuddhiḥ 
sā punas tathā nirodhasatyañca 
āśrayaparāvṛttyātmatā nirodhātmatā nirodhasatyam evetyapare 
samyakpratipattitattvaṃ mārgasatyaṃ 
vijñaptitattvaṃ yoniśaḥ prayogaḥ 
samyakpratipattitattvaṃ vijñaptitattvaṃ ca mārgasatyam evetyanye 
etāny api trīṇi tattvāni nityaṃ tathaiveti tathatāvacanam bhavati 
tatra  pravṛttitattvaṃ dvividhaṃ mūlatattvaṃ veditavyaṃ parikalpitaparatantralakṣaṇaṃ 
tatra pravṛttir janmanāmanādimān prabandhaḥ 
sā cā'vidyamānatvāt parikalpitaḥ svabhāvaḥ 
yeṣāṃ tu sa prabandhaṣthe hetuprabhāvitatvāt paratantraḥ svabhāvaḥ 
evaṃ yeṣāṃ yā ca pravṛttis tat pravṛttitattvam iti nirdiṣṭaṃ bhavati 
athavā kleśakarmajanmanām anādimān utpādaḥ saṃsārapravṛttir ityucyate 
sā ca parikalpitasvabhāvābhiniveśaprabhāvetetyāha  pravṛttitattvaṃ dvividhaṃ mūlatattvam ity uktaṃ 
tathā  sanniveśakupannatā 
iti 
mithyāpratipattiḥ kupannatā 
tathaiva dvividhaṃ mūlatattvam iti duḥkhasamudayayor hetupratyayaprabhāvitatvāt parikalpitaviṣayatvāc ca sanniveśamithyāpratipattitattvaṃ dvividhe saṃgṛhītaṃ 
ekaṃ lakṣaṇavijñaptiśuddhisamyak prapannatā 
lakṣaṇatattvaṃ vijñaptitattvaṃ viśuddhitattvaṃ samyak pratipattitattvaṃ etāni catvāri tatvāny ekam eva mūlatattvaṃ yad uta pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvaḥ 
tatra lakṣaṇatattvaviśuddhitattvayor ananyathāpariniṣpannatvāt pariniṣpannaḥ 
vijñaptitattvaṃ samyak pratipattitattvaṃ cā'viparyāsapariniṣpattyā pariniṣpannaḥ 
  atra pravṛttisanniveśamithyāpratipattitattvais tribhiḥ sattvasāmyaṃ darśitaṃ 
lakṣaṇavijñaptitattvābhyāṃ dharmasāmyaṃ 
viśuddhitattvena bodhisāmyaṃ 
samyakpratipattitattvena prajñāsāmyaṃ pradarśitam iti 
āha ca  sattvasāmyaṃ tribhiḥ proktaṃ dharmasāmyaṃ dvayena tu 
bodhiprajñāsāmyam evam ekaikena pradarśitaṃ 
iti 
  kauśalyatattvaṃ  prabhedatattvānantaraṃ kauśalyatattvam uddiṣṭaṃ 
kuśalyatattvaṃ darśanapratipakṣeṇaety uktaṃ 
tatpunaḥ skandhādiṣu kathaṃ daśavidham ātmadarśanam iti na jñāyata ityataḥ pṛcchati  katham eṣu skandhādiṣu daśavidham ātmadarśanam iti  ata āha  ekahetutvabhoktṛtve kartṛtvavaśavartate 
ādhipatyārthanityatve kleśaśuddhyāśraye'pi ca 
yigotvā'muktamuktatve ātmadarśnam eṣu hi 
iti 
skandhādiṣv iti sambadhyate 
eṣa tu daśavidha ātmā'sadgrāha  ityātmano'sattvād asadgrāha ityāha 
yadyātmā nāsti kathaṃ grāhaparatantraḥ sannirviṣayo grāhaḥ pravartata iti natveṣa nirviṣayaḥ skandhādiṣu pravartate 
tasmāt teṣāṃ pratipakṣeṇa daśavidhaṃ skandhādikauśalyam uktaṃ 
kathaṃ punaḥ skandhādiṣv evāyam ātmagrāho natvāmā sanniścīyate  yataḥ skandhādivyatirikta ātmā yuktyā parīkṣyamāṇo nopalabhyate 
yadātmatvādīnām ātmakriyāsvarūpaṃ tat sarvam api pravartate skandhādiṣvevetyataḥ skandhādaya evātmagrāhanibandhanam iti pratīyate 
ebhir daśavidhair ātmābhiniveśo nāmātmagrāhaḥ pravartate nānyair ityataḥ skandhādikauśalyaṃ sarvātmagrāhasya pratipakṣatvena veditavyaṃ 
yad uta ekatvagrāha iti pañcopādānaskandheṣu piṇḍātmagrāhataḥ tat pratipakṣeṇa skandhakauśalyaṃ 
hetutvagrāha iti cakṣurādīnāṃ prayojakatvād ātmani hetutvagrāhaḥ tat pratipakṣeṇa dhātukauśalyaṃ 
evam anyeṣv api vipakṣapratipakṣaṃ vaktavyaṃ 
athavātmatvāt sarvaṃ pravartata ityayaṃ hetutvagrāhaḥ 
yasya veṣṭam aniṣṭañceha janmani phalaṃ tasya śubhāśubhasya karmaṇa ātmā hetur iti cetanā hetutvagrāhaḥ 
bhoktṛtvagrāha iti ātmā bhoktā cetanatvāt 
vyaktāvyaktaṃ tu bhojanam acetanatvāt 
athavā yasya śubham aśubhaṃ karmabhir utpadyate sa eva tat phalānāṃ bhokteti bhoktṛtvagrāhaḥ 
kartṛtvagrāha iti ātmaiva sukṛtaduṣkṛtānāṃ karmaṇāṃ karteti yo grāhaḥ yo vā karaṇādyupetas tās tāḥ kriyāḥ karoti sa ātmeti kartṛtvagrāhaḥ 
svatantragrāha iti yat svairaṃ vaśitvaṃ sa ātmā yo'dhikāraḥ sa ātmeti yo grāhaḥ 
hetvanurūpasyaiva vā phalasyotpattau vaśitvam asyeti svatantragrāhaḥ 
adhipatitvagrāha iti yo'dhipatiḥ prabhurīśvaraḥ sa ātmeti 
phalasyaiva vā'nurūpeṇācaraṇaṃ tad adhipatitvād ātmetyadhipatitvagrāhaḥ 
nityatvagrāha iti hetvādivastunā pañcavidhenā'viśuddho'pyātmā nitya eva anyathā  tv akṛtābhyāgamaḥ kṛtasya nāśaśca 
tathā smṛteḥ pratyabhijñānasya cābhāvaḥ prasajyate 
sankliṣṭvyavadānatvagrāha iti sankleśavyavadānāśrayatvāt 
yogitvagrāha iti ātmani manaso dhāraṇaṃ yogaḥ prāṇamanasor vā nigrahaḥ 
ātmano manasāṃ saṃyogaviśeṣo yogaḥ so'syāstīti yogī 
amuktamuktatvagrāhaśceti ātamno bandhād vimuktir iti yo vikalpaḥ 
 katham idaṃ daśavidhaṃ kauśalyatattvaṃ mūlatattve'ntarbhavatīti 
kauśalyaṃ hi skandhādiṣu vaicakṣaṇyaṃ 
tat kathaṃ triṣu svabhāveṣv antarbhavati  asambhāvayataḥ praśnaḥ 
yatas triṣu svabhāveṣu te skandhādayo'ntarbhūtā iti kauśalyaviṣayā ete kauśalyaśabdenodbhāvitāḥ 
na tu tasminn eva kauśalya iti 
ataḥ akuśalyatattvasyāpy adhikāratas tatrāntarbhāvo na tu svarūpata iti veditavyaṃ tadyathā phalahetutattvamārgasatyaṃ triṣvantarbhūtam uktam iti 
nanvevam api naiva vijñāyante yathā'ntarbhūtā iti pṛcchati katham antarbhūtā iti ataścāha  parikalpavikalpārthadharmatā'rthena teṣu te 
iti 
teṣu triṣu svabhāveṣu te skandhādayo'ntarbhūtā ityadhikṛtaṃ 
tatra dhātvādibhyaḥ pūrvaṃ skandhānām antarbhūtatvaṃ prakāśayitavyaṃ prathamaṃ nirdiṣṭatvāt tatrāpi rūpasyeti 
  ata āha  trividhaṃ rūpaṃ 
kathaṃ  parikalpitaṃ rūpaṃ vikalpitaṃ rūpaṃ dharmatārūpañca 
tatra kiṃ parikalpitaṃ rūpaṃ  yo rūpasya parikalpitaḥ svabhāva iti 
tac ca yā'nyatra nāmnopalabdhis tatra viṣayasvabhāvaḥ parikalpyate 
so'tyantam asattvāt parikalpita ity ucyate 
vikalpitaṃ rūpaṃ yo rūpasya paratantraḥ svabhāva iti hetupratyayapratibaddha ityarthaḥ 
kim arthaṃ punar idaṃ vikalpitaṃ rūpam ucyata ityata āha  tatra hi rūpavikalpaḥ kriyata iti 
yasmād rūpakhyātavijñāne'dṛṣṭatattvair aparijñātarūpasaṃjñatvād rūpābhiniveśaḥ kriyate yathā skandheṣv ātmagrāhaḥ 
tasmāt paratantre vikalpitaṃ rūpam ityucyate 
dharmatārūpaṃ yo rūpasya pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāva iti 
tad vikalparūpaparikalpitarūpavigatātmikā śūnyatā 
yathā rūpam iti 
yathā rūpam tridhā bhittvā triṣu svabhāveṣv antarbhāvitam evaṃ vedanādayaḥ skandhadhātvādayaś ca yojyā iti vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskāravijñānaskandhā dhātvāyatanāni pratītyasamutpādāngānyāyatanānāyatanāniindriyāṇi adhvatrayaṃ satyacatuṣṭayaṃ yānatrayaṃ saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtañcetyetad api vedanādikaṃ dhātvādikañca pratyekaṃ parikalpitavikalpitadharmatāsvabhāvabhedatas tridhā bhittvā triṣu svabhāveṣv antarbhāvayitavyaṃ 
tatra pratibhāseṣu vedanādiṣu yo'tyantam asadbhūto grāhyagrāhakabhāvo rūpapratibhāseṣu yathā grāhyabhāvaḥ parikalpyate sā parikalpitā vedanā yāvat parikalpitaṃ vijñānaṃ 
yasmin grāhyagrāheka vikalpaḥ kriyate sā vikalpitā vedanā yāvad vikalpitaṃ vijñānaṃ 
dharmatāvedanā yo vedanāyāḥ pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvaḥ 
evaṃ yāvad dharmatāvijñānaṃ veditavyaṃ 
evaṃ dhātvāyatanādiṣv api yathāsaṃbhavaṃ vistareṇa vaktavyaṃ 
rūpavedane yāvat saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtam iti yo nāmābhidheyo bhāvaḥ so'pi porikalpitaparatantrapariniṣpannasvabhāvo veditavyaḥ 
kathaṃ  tatra rūpādisvabhāvaprajñaptatvāt parikalpitaḥ prajñaptyadhiṣṭhānabhāvāt paratantraḥ pratyayaparatantratvāt tasyaiva rūpādibhāvātyantavigatatvaṃ pariniṣpannaḥ 
nanu paratantra eva manuṣyādibhāvena nāmnocyate na parikalpita ity anarthaka  eva parikalpitavikalpaḥ 
nānarthakaḥ 
tatra manuṣyādisvabhāvasyādhyāropitatvāt 
yathā hi nāmārthe pravartate tathā tathaiva nāsti 
bālas tu tat svabhāvam abhiniviśanti tac ca mithyā'dhyavasitaṃ na tu bhūtārtheneti 
kuta etat  nāmārthayoḥ sārūpye vairūpye ca vācyavācakabhāvavyāvṛttitaḥ 
yadi vṛkṣādiśabdānāṃ tad arthānāṃ cābhinnarūpatā evaṃ nāmnas tadarthaṃ rūpā'vyatirekād vācakatvaṃ vyāvartyate'rthavat 
arthasyāpi nāmasvarūpā'vyatirekād vācyatvaṃ vihīyate niyamahetvabhāvāt
