namno'pi vānyat vācakārthasya ca vācyaṃ prasajyata ityanavasthāprasangāth
ekasya cārthasya nāmabahutve nāmnaścārthabahutve'nekarūpatā prasajyate 
ekasya tu bahusvarūpatvaṃ na yujyate 
abhāvavācakānām arthavatām asattvaṃ tad arthasyābhāvarūpatvāt tad arthasyāpi vā sattvaṃ nāmno'stitvād iti 
vairūpye'pi śabdānurūpyeṇārthapratyayābhāvaḥ 
śabda eva hi tatra vṛkṣo nārthaḥ 
arthastu na vṛkṣo nāpyavṛkṣaḥ 
tasmād vṛkṣaśabdārthasya na vṛkṣajñānaviṣayatvaṃ tad arthasyā'vṛkṣātmakatvāt 
tad vidhañca śabdārthayor vācyavācakabhāvavyāvṛttiḥ 
vailakṣaṇye ca vācyavācakaniyamo na syāt niyamakāraṇābhāvāt 
nāma cārtham utpādayed abhivyañjayed vā 
tatra notpādayati utpanne'rthe nāmakaraṇāt 
utpanno'pi punaḥ punar utpādayitavya iti prasanga punaḥ panar nāmakaraṇāt 
nāpyabhivyañjayati yasmād arthaṃ gṛhītvā nāma kriyate na ca gṛhītasyābhivyañjakaṃ yuktaṃ 
tenaiva nāmnā tamevārtham anyo na gṛhṇāti yas tan na jānāti 
tadeva tasyaivārthasyābhivyañjakaṃ cānabhivyañjakañceti na yuktaṃ 
nābhivyañjakapradīpādayo vyangyam arthaṃ vyutpattyapekṣā vyañjayanti 
na ca vyangyeṣu ghaṭapaṭādiṣu vyañjakaniyamo dṛṣṭa iti sarvo'rthaḥ sarveṇa nāmnā'bhivyajyeta 
na ca gandhādiṣu niyamābhāvaḥ 
yatmāt kuthārajalādīnāṃ gandhādyutpādayitṛtvam iṣṭaṃ na tu vyañjakatvaṃ 
  tasmād vācyavācakābhiniveśo grāhyagrāhakābhiniveśavad asadarthaṃ eveti pratīyate 
evaṃ triṣu svabhāveṣu skandhādīnām anantarbhāvād daśavidhaṃ kauśalyatattvaṃ mūlatattva eva draṣṭavyaṃ 
skandhādikauśalyam idam idamātmadarśanapratipakṣatvenoktaṃ 
yasmistvarthe skandhādikauśalyaṃ vipakṣātmadṛṣṭapratipakṣaḥ skandhādyartho nokta ityataḥ sa idānīm ucyate 
  skandhārthaḥ  amekartvābhisankṣepaparicchedārtha āditaḥ 
ādita ityādāv ucyata iti sambadhyate 
āditas tāvat skandhā ucyante 
te ca trividhenārthena veditavyāḥ 
anekatvārthena yat kiñcid rūpam atītānāgatapratyutpannamādhyātmikaṃ vā bāhyaṃ vā audārikaṃ vā sūkṣmaṃ vā hīnaṃ vā praṇītaṃ vā yadvā dūre yadvā'ntike ityevam anekārthena bahūnām atītānāgatādīnāṃ dravyāṇāṃ skandhaśabdenoktatvāt 
abhisankṣipyetivacanād abhisaṃkṣepārthena skandha iti 
abhisaṃkṣiptetyekīkṛtya 
paricchedārthena ca skandha iti sambadhyate 
caśabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ anekārthābhisaṃkṣepārthadvayasyāpi 
atra kāraṇam āha  skandhānāṃ rūpādilakṣaṇasya vedanādilakṣaṇebhyaḥ pṛthag vyavasthāpanād iti 
pṛthakparicchinna iti paryāyaḥ 
kim atra kāraṇam ebhis tribhirangaiḥ skandhārtho vyavasthāpyate  rāśyartho hi skandhārtha ityata evaṃ vyavasthāpyate 
evañca loke rāśyartho dṛṣṭaḥ 
yo'neko'bhisaṃkṣītaḥ paricchinnaḥ sa rāśir ityucyate 
yathā rūpaskandha evaṃ vedanādayo'pi skandhā veditavyāḥ 
tatra yo'yam ekātmagrāho yathā puruṣa evedaṃ sarvaṃ yad bhūtaṃ yac ca bhāvyam ityādi tasya  pratipakṣeṇa yathā skandhārthe kauśalyaṃ kāryaṃ tathoktaṃ 
katham iti  atītādibhinnarūpādiṣvaikadhyam abhisaṃkṣipteṣu rūpādiskandhaprajñāpanāt 
etac ca trividhasammohapratipakṣeṇa trividhaskandhavyavasthāpanaṃ 
trividhaḥ sammoha ekatvasammohaḥ saṃvṛti sammoho lakṣaṇasankīrṇasammohaś ca 
  dhātvarthaḥ  skandhārthānantaraṃ dhātava uddiṣṭāḥ 
tasmāt skandhārthānanataraṃ dhātvartham āha  grāhakagrāhyatad grāhavījārthaścāparo mataḥ 
iti 
aparaśabdo'tra dhātāveva sambadhyate skandhānantaram uddiṣṭatvāt 
ata eva bhāṣyakāro'pyāha katamo'paraḥ 
dhātur iti 
bījārtho dhātvarthaḥ tadyathā svarṇo sati svarṇadhātur ucyate svarṇabījam iti gamyate 
sa ca phalabhedāt tridhā bhidyate  grāhakadhātuḥ grāhyadhātuḥ tad grāhadhātuṣca 
tatra grāhakabījārthaścakṣurdhātvādayaḥ 
cakṣurdhāturādir yeṣāṃ manaḥparyantās te cakṣur dhātvādayaḥ 
te ca rūpādiviṣayagrāhāśrayabhūtatvād grāhakāḥ 
sajātīyānāṃ cakṣurādīnāṃ hetutvād dhātava ucyante 
grāhyabījārtho rūpadhātvādayo dharmadhātuparyantāḥ 
cakṣurādivijñānaviṣayatvād grāhyāḥ 
te'pyevaṃ sabhāgānāṃ rūpādīnāṃ hetubhāvād dhātava ucyante 
tad grāhabījārthaścakṣurvijñānadhātvādayaḥ 
rūpādipratipattisvabhāvatvād rūpādigrāhāścakṣurivjñānādayo manovijñānaparyantāḥ 
te'pi sabhāgānām eva cakṣurādivijñānānāṃ hetubhūtatvād dhātava ucyante cakṣurvijñānadhātvādayo manovijñānadhātuparyantāḥ 
anye tvāhuḥ  cakṣurādyabhiniveśakarmavāsitam ālayavijñānaṃ yathākramaṃ cakṣurādīnāṃ bījaṃ 
tathā rūpādyabhiniveśakarmavāsitam ālayavijñānaṃ yathākramaṃ rūpādīnāṃ bījaṃ 
tathā cakṣurādivijñānābhiniveśakarmavāsitam ālayavijñānam eva cakṣurādivijñānānāṃ yathākramaṃ bījam iti 
evaṃ tvālayavijñānam eva dhātuśabdavācyaṃ na cakṣurādaya iti cintyam etat 
kartṛkriyākarmasammohavyāvartanārthaṃ trividhe bījārthe dhātur vyavasthāpitaḥ 
atra pūrvacakṣurādaya uttaracakṣurādīnām eva hetavo bhavanti na tatrānyaḥ kaścid ātmā'nyo vā hetuvidyata ityevaṃ dhātukauśalyād ātmani hetugrāhavyāvṛttiḥ 
   āyatanārthaḥ  dhātvarthānantaram āyatanānām artho vaktavyaḥ 
ata āha  veditārthaparicchedabhogāyadvārato'paraṃ 
iti 
dhātor aparāṇāṃ hyāyatanapratītyasamutpādādīnāṃ bahutvād aparaśabdasya ca sāmānyatvāt praśnaḥ kim aparam iti 
dhātubhyo'nantaram uddiṣṭatvād arthata āyataneṣvevāyam aparaśabdo'vatiṣṭhata iti jñāpanārtham āha  āyatanam iti 
tatra veditopabhogāyadvārārthena ṣaḍādhyātmikānyāyatanāni 
arthaparicchedopabhogāyadvārārthena ṣaḍ bāhyānīti 
āyadvārārthaṃ āyatanārthaḥ 
āya āgamaḥ 
taṃ veditārthaparicchedopabhogayos tanvantītyāyatanāni 
veditasaṃjñopabhogāyadvārebhedanādhyātmikabāhyaprabhedaḥ 
veditaṃ hi sukhaduḥkhā'duḥkhā'sukhaṃ 
tadevopabhujyata ity upabhogaḥ 
anubhūyata ityarthaḥ 
tasya vedanopabhogasyāyadvāram ādhyātimkānyevāyatanāny uktāni 
satyapi viṣayāṇāṃ tadāyadvārabhāve cakṣurādīnām āśrayāṇām anugrahopaghātatvena tat pravīṇatvena cāsādhāraṇatvenāśrayatvāt sati cakṣurādau taddvāreṇa vedanopabhogān nāstīti 
arthaparicchedaḥ saṃjñā arthanimittodgrahaṇātmakatvāt 
saivārthapratipattyatmakatvād viṣayam upabhunkte 
tadāyadvārabhāvena bāhyānyāyatanānyuktāni na tvādhyātmikāni satyapi tadāyadvārabhāve yasmād viṣayābhāve'rthaparicchedopabhogābhāvaḥ satyapy ādhyātmike cakṣurādyāyatane 
veditārthaparicchedayoḥ sasamprayogayor ayadvārabhāvatvād etānyāyatanāni veditavyāni 
pradhānaṃ hi dvayagrahaṇaṃ 
grahaṇaprādhānyaṃ punaḥ karmaphalopabhogād arthaparicchedātmakatvāc ca 
veditārthaparicchedopabhogamukhena bhoktṛvikalpaḥ pravartata ityato dvividhenārthenāyatane vyavasthānaṃ kṛtaṃ 
evam āyatanakauśalyaṃ bhoktā''dhyātmikānyāyatanāni bhojanam āyatanāni bāhyāni 
nānyo bhoktetyātmani bhoktṛtvagrāho vyāvartate 
yad uktaṃ cakṣuāradyāyatanānām anugrahopaghātāt tad adhiṣṭhāna eva bhoktṛtvavyavahāra iti tad ayuktaṃ 
rūpapratiṣedhena cakṣurādīnām āyatanānām apy asattvādātmavad iti naiṣa  upālambhaḥ 
yasmāt parikalpitarūpasyaivātra pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate na vikalpatārūpasya 
tatra cakṣurādiprapañcaparibhāvitakarmākṣiptatvenālayavijñānaṃ pariṇāmaviśeṣaprāptamādhyātmikam āyatanaṃ 
tan nimittasya pravṛttivijñānasya rūpādipratibhāsaṃ bāhyāyatanaṃ 
ya ālayavijñānasya sādhāraṇārthapratibhāso yaś ca sattvapratibhāsaḥ so'pi grāhyagrāhakapratibhāsasya pravṛttivijñānasyotpattāvadhipatipratyayatvād bāhyam āyatanam ucyate na tu tad viṣayatvād iti 
nanvevaṃ dvayam āśritya cakṣur vijñānādaya utpadyanta iti sūtravacanena virudhyate 
rūpādipratibhāso vijñānād bhinnaḥ  na ca tadeva tasyaivotpattipratyayo yuktaḥ 
utpannānutpannāvasthayor bhāvād abhāvāc ca svātmani vṛttivirodhāt 
tasmād avaśyaṃ vijñānanirbhāsād bhinnā rūpādayo'bhyupagantavyā iti 
naiṣo'pyupālambhaḥ 
yasmād pādinirbhāsavijñānṃ sabhāgavijñānotpattaye pratyayavijñāne vāsanām ādhatte 
vasanāpariṇāmāc ca rūpādyābhāsaṃ punar vijñānaṃ jāyate 
evaṃ vijñānanirbhāsātmakatvena vāsanāhito vijñānapratyaya ukta iti na sūtravirodhaḥ 
evaṃ rūpādinirbhāsasyālambanārtho'py upapannaḥ svanirbhāsākārasya vijñānasya pratyayatvāt 
athavā yathā bāhyārthavādibhir vijñānena sahaja ālambanapratyayo vyavasthāpyate janyajanakavad abhāve'pi tad bhāvābhāvābhyāṃ vijñānabhāvābhāvāvadhikṛtya evam ihāpi rūpādinirbhāsasya vijñānasya vā'satyapi janyajanakabhāve tad bhāvābhāvayor vijñānabhāvābhāvavyabhicārāt pratyayapratyayitvaṃ vyavasthāpyate 
rūpanirbhāsavijñānayor abhinnatvād dṛṣṭāntena mukhyato'sādṛśyam iti na bhedopacārāt 
tadyathā grāhyagrāhakavikalpādhiṣṭḥānatvāt svapnamāyāgandharvanagarādivijñānaṃ paramārthato'abhinnam api grāhyagrāhakākāreṇa bhinnam iva vyavasthāpyata ālambyālambakabhāvatvena tathā'nyatrāpi nāsti virodhaḥ 
api cālambyālambakabhāvaḥ sarvatropacaryata eva na mukhyo'sti 
nahi vijñānam utpannam anutpannaṃ vā viṣayam ālambate 
utpattyanantaravināśitvāt kriyākāle'navasthānād asattvāc ca 
viṣayaścotpanno'nutpanno vobhayathā'pyālambanatvenāyogyaḥ 
utpannasyā'navasthānād anutpannasya cāsattvāt 
nahi nirādhārālambanakriyā yujyate 
yasyāpi sattāmātreṇa kāryakāraṇabhāva evālambyālambakabhāvas tasyāpi vartamānasya vijñānasyālambanaṃ nirarthakaṃ  bhavati tadātmatvena siddheḥ 
utpadyamānasyāpi nirarthakam asattvāt 
notpadyamānasya nirarthakaṃ yasmād viṣayasadbhāve vijñānaṃ tan nirbhāsam ātmānaṃ pratilabhate 
yadi viṣayanirbhāso vijñānasya bāhyārthanimittaḥ evam atītānāgatasvapnādivijñānasya nirākāratvaṃ vartate 
tad arthābhāvād vā sattvaṃ 
na vikalaiḥ pratyayaiḥ kāryam utpadyate atiprasangāt 
na cāsataḥ pratyayatvaṃ yujyate 
na ca bāhyārtha ālambanapratyayo vijñānasya tena vināpi bhāvāt 
tasmāt sarvam eva vijñānaṃ taimirikādīnām iva bāhyārthālambananirapekṣam evābhyupagantavyaṃ 
  pratītyasamutpādārthaḥ  āyatanā'rthānantaraṃ pratītyasamutpādārtho vaktavya ityata āha  pratītyasamutpādārthaḥ 
punar hetuphalāyāsā'nāropā'napavādataḥ 
nirīhānityasamarthapratyayotpādanārthaḥ 
yathoktaṃ sūtre'pi  etad asmin satīdambhavati 
asyotpādādidam utpadyate yad utāvidyāpratyayāḥ saṃskārā iti vistaraḥ 
ayaṃ ca pratītyasamutpādo hetupahalakriyāṇāṃ samāropāpavādapratiṣedheneṣyata iti pratipādayann āha  hetuphalakriyāṇām asamāropavādārthaḥ pratītyasamutpādārtha iti 
āyāsaśabdena tu kriyoktā 
tatra hetusamāropaḥ avidyādīn hitvā puruṣeśvarāṇupradhāṇādīnāṃ hetutvakalpanāt 
etad eva pratipādayann āha  saṃskārādīnāṃ jarāmaraṇaparyantānāṃ viṣamahetukalpnād iti 
saṃskārādīnāṃ hy anityānāṃ nityaḥ puruṣādiko hetur viṣamo visadṛśa ityarthaḥ 
athavā hetuḥ svarūpavikriyā'pekṣo bījādiko'nkurādīnāṃ dṛṣṭaḥ 
na ca nityasya svarūpavikriyā'stīti viṣamahetau hetutvakalpanād hetusamāropaḥ 
  hetvapavādo nirhetukatvakalpanād iti saṃskārādīnāṃ nirhetukotpādābhyupagamād avidyādīnāṃ saṃskārādihetutvam apoḍhaṃ bhavati 
phalasamāropaḥ sātmakānāṃ saṃskārādīnām avidyādipratyayapravṛttikalpanād iti 
satyātmani saṃskārādīnām avidyādipratyayapravṛttitvaṃ na tv astīti saṃskārādiphaleṣv ātmasamāropa ityeke 
ātmadravyasamavāyitvena tad anugrahopaghātakartṛtvena vā sātmakānāṃ saṃskārādīnām avidyādipratyayapravṛttikalpanāt phalasamāropa ityapare 
phalāpavādo na santy avidyādipratyayāḥ saṃskāradaya iti kalpanād iti 
tad yathā  sucaritaduścaritaparalokāpavādināṃ nāsti sucaritaṃ nāsti duścaritaṃ nāsti paraloka iti 
kriyāsamāropo'vidyādīnāṃ saṃskārādyutpattau vyāpārakalpanād iti 
yadi vasturūpam arthāntarabhūtaṃ saṃskārādyutpattāv avidyādayaḥ kurvantīti kalpyeta evaṃ kriyāsamāropaḥ 
kriyāpavādo nissāmarthyakalapanād iti 
avidyādīnāṃ sattāmātreṇa saṃskārāṇāṃ hy utpādanasamarthānām api niḥsāmarthyakalpanāt kriyāpavādaḥ 
tad abhāvād asamāropānapavādo veditavya iti 
tasya hetuphalakriyāṇāṃ samāropāpavādasyābhāvād asamāropānapavādo veditavyaḥ 
evam idaṃ pratītyasamutpādakauśalyam avidyādivyatirekeṇātmanyanyasmin vā yaḥ kartṛtvagrāhas tasyaṃ pratipakṣeṇa veditavyaṃ 
na hy atrātmānyo vā'vidyāvyatirekeṇa śubhāśubhānāṃ karmaṇāṃ kartā 
anyaḥ saṃskāravyatirekeṇa vijñānasya kartā nāsti 
evaṃ sarvatrāpi yathāyogaṃ vaktavyaṃ nirīhebhyo'nityebhyaḥ samarthebhyaścāvidyādibhyaḥ saṃskārādyutpattitaḥ 
  sthānā'sthānārthaḥ   pratītyasamutpādānantaraṃ sthānā'sthānārtho vaktavya ityata āha  aniṣṭeṣṭaviśuddhīnāṃ iti vistaraḥ 
sthānāsthānaṃ saptavidhapāratantryārthena veditam iti 
tatra sthānaṃ hetuḥ asthānamahetuḥ 
yathoktaṃ gāthāyāṃ  satyaṃ vaden na ca kruddhed dadyād alpoo'pi yācitaḥ 
ebhis tribhir iha shtānair devānāṃ samitiṃ vrajet 
hetubhir iti gamyate 
athavā sthānaṃ sambhavaḥ asthānaṃ punar asambhavaḥ 
tat kauśalyaṃ sthānāsthānakauśalyaṃ 
paratantrasya bhāvaḥ pāratantryaṃ 
parāyattatetyarthaḥ 
tac ca saptavidham api triṣvantarbhavati karmakleśajanmapāratantryeṣu 
tatrāniṣṭe pāratantryam iti 
aniṣṭā duargatayaḥ 
tatra gamanaṃ duścaritāyatattvaṃ pāratantryañceti pradarśayann āha  duśaritena prāṇātipātādinā kāyavānmanaḥkarmasaṇggṛhītena saprayogapṛṣṭhenā'nicchato'pi durgatigamād iti 
durgatayo narakāḥ pretāstiryañcaś ca 
teṣām ekāntena duḥkhatvān na kasyacit tatra gamanecchā bhavati 
karmaṇāṃ balavattvād durgatigetutvāc ca duścaritasyānicchato'pi tatra karmavaśād eva gamanaṃ bhavati 
iṣṭe pāratantryaṃ sucaritena sugatigamanād iti 
iṣṭaṃ sugatigamanaṃ 
sugatir devā manuśyāś ca 
sucaritaṃ saprayogapṛṣṭhebhyaḥ prāṇātipātādibhyo viratiḥ dānamānasatkārādikriyā śāstṛguruṇānvitādiṣu maitrīkaruṇādayaś ca guṇaviśeṣāḥ 
pāratantryaṃ sucaritamantareṇānyathā prārthayatām api sugatigamanābhāvāt 
sucaritapratibaddhataiva sugatyutpatteḥ 
viśūddhau pāratantryam iti vistaraḥ 
viśuddhiḥ kleśaprahāṇaṃ 
pañca nivaraṇāni kāmacchando vyāpādaḥ styānamiddhamauddhatyakaukṛtyaṃ vicikitsā ca 
styānamiddhamekīkṛtya auddhatyakaukṛtyañca pañca bhavati 
abhedena kuśalapakṣaṃ nivṛṇvantīti nivaraṇāni bhedena punar yathākramaṃ pravrajatyābhiratiṃ tad anurūpe kāyavākkarmāṇi sabrahmacāribhiḥ samyak coditasya samyak pratipattiṃ śamathakāle'līnatāṃ pragrahakāle'vikṣepaṃ śamathavipaśyanākāle svarasavāditāṃ chādayantīti nivaraṇāni 
tānyaprahāyātyaktvā yāvat sapta bodhyangānyabhāvayitveti 
yāvad iti paryantopadeśāt smṛtyupasthānasamyak prahāṇarddhipādendriyabalānām api grahaṇaṃ 
duḥkhasyāntā'karaṇād iti 
duḥkhasyānto  yatra duḥkhaṃ nāsti tac ca nirvāṇaṃ tasyākaraṇam aprāptir nirvāṇaṃ na prāpnotītyarthaḥ 
athavā duḥkhasyānto yasmād duḥkhādanyaduḥkhaṃ na sandhīyate tat tādṛśaṃ duḥkhaṃ na karotītyapratisandhikaṃ duḥkham na karotītyarthaḥ 
pañca nivaraṇaprahāṇapratibaddhatā viśuddhau pāratantryaṃ 
samotpattau pāratantryaṃ dvayor apūrvācaramayor iti sahitayor ityarthaḥ 
tathāgatayoścakravartinoścaikasmil lokadhātāvanutpādād iti 
tathāgatayos trisāhasramahāsāhasro lokadhātur abhipretaḥ 
cakravartinos tu cātur dvīpaka iti kecit 
tathāgatayor api cātur dvīpaka evetyapare 
buddhā hi bhagavanto dharmakāyādhipatyāt trisāhasramahāsāhasre lokadhātau pratyekaṃ cātur dvīpakeṣu nirmāṇakāyenābhisambodhiṃ parinirvāṇaṃ ca darśayanti 
tathā hi yadekasmiñcāturmahādvīpake tuṣiteṣu manuṣyeṣu ca cyutijanmaparigraho bodhisattvānām prayojanaṃ 
taditareṣv api cātur dvīpakeṣu samānaṃ 
tasmād akaniṣṭhabhavana evābhisambuddho bhagavān nirmāṇakāyena trisāhasramahāsāhasre vantargateṣu sarvacāturdvīpakeṣu tuṣiteṣūpapattiṃ manuṣyeṣu ca janmaparigrahādikaṃ sarvaṃ darśayatīti manyante 
tatra ca samasaṃvartanīyakarmāyattatā buddhacarkravartyutpatteḥ sahabhāve pāratantryaṃ 
ādhipatye pāratantryaṃ striyā cakravartitvādyakaraṇād iti cakravartisaṃvartanīyasya karmaṇaḥ pumātmabhāva eva vipākadānasāmarthyāt 
na hi strīḥ stryādiratnopabhogasamarthā 
ādiśabdena śakratvādr gṛhyate 
samprāptau pāratantryaṃ stryāpratyekānuttarabodhyanabhisambodhāt 
prāptir buddhapratyekabuddhatvādhigamaḥ 
tatra pāratantryaṃ puruṣasya prāptir na tu striyaḥ 
tasyā hi saṃsargābhāvāt khaḍgavat tribhūmiśāstrītvāsambhavādyathākramaṃ 
sā punaḥ sarvadhūrtajanagamyā alpaprajñatvād anācāryakābhisambodhāyogyā ceti 
samudācāre pāratantryaṃ dṛṣṭisampannasya vadhādyasamudācārāt pṛthagjanasya ca samudācārād iti 
dṛṣṭisampanno dṛṣṭasatyaḥ 
vadhaḥ prāṇātipātaḥ 
  ādiśabdenādattādānādayaḥ saṃgṛhyante 
te vadhādayaḥ kāyavākkriyāsvabhāvā dṛṣṭisampannasya na samudācaranti darśanamārgeṇa vadhādiduścaritasamutthāpakakleśaprahāṇāt pṛthagjanasya samudācaranti tad aprahāṇāt 
tad aprahāṇaṃ punas tat pratipakṣeṇa mārgānutpannatvāt 
evam aniṣṭādipāratantryānugatam asthānakauśalyaṃ puruṣeśvarādau svātantryāgrāhapratipakṣaḥ 
yadi hi svatantraḥ kaścit syān na duścaritena durgatiṃ gacchet 
evam anyatrāpi vācyaṃ 
  indriyārthaḥ  sthānāsthānārthanirdeśānantaram indriyārtho vaktavya ityata āha  indriyaṃ dvāviṃśatividham iti cakṣurindriyaṃ yāvad ājñātāvindriyāvasānaṃ 
atra punar ādhipātyarthaṃ indriyārthaḥ 
kasya punaḥ kvādhipatyam ityata āha  grahaṇasthānasandhānabhogaśuddhidvayārthataḥ 
iti 
atra ca dvayādhipattyārthata iti yuktau kārikānukūlārtham ādhipatyaśabdo lupto draṣṭavyaḥ 
tasmād bhāṣyakāra āha  teṣu tadādhipatyād iti 
grahaṇārtheneti 
arthaśabdo'tra prayojanavācī 
grahaṇaprayojanaṃ nimittaṃ tatrendriyam iti darśayati 
evam anyatrāpi yathāyogaṃ vaktavyaṃ 
teṣvityarthagrahaṇādiṣu ādhipatyam ityadhikaprabhutvam ityādhipatyaṃ hetutvam ityarthaḥ 
rūpādayo dharmaparyantā rūpādiviṣayāḥ 
teṣāṃ grahaṇaṃ cakṣurādivijñānaṃ 
tatra cakṣurādīnāṃ ṣaṇṇām ādhipatyaṃ 
cakṣuṣo niravaśeṣarūpaprabhedavijñānāśrayatvād rūpādīnām adhikaprabhutvam itīndriyam ucyate 
na tu nīlarūpaṃ pītarūpādivijñānasyālambanaṃ bhavati 
evaṃ śrotrādiṣv api yathāsambhavaṃ vistareṇa vācyaṃ 
sthāne jīvitendriyasyeti 
jīvitendriyaṃ punaḥ karmavāsanāvidhaṃ vipākasantāne'sati vicchittipratyaye pūrvpūrvakṣāṇasarūpeṣūttarottarakṣaṇeṣu pratisandhisāmarthyaṃ 
sthāne jīvitendriyasyādhipatyam ityatraiva kāraṇam āha  tad ādhipatyenā'maraṇād iti 
amaraṇaṃ pūrvakarmākṣiptanikāyasabhāgānuvṛttiḥ 
satyapi sattvasthitikāraṇatve nāhārādīnām indriyatvaṃ 
tat sadbhāve'pyāyuṣaḥ kṣaye'vasthānā'sadbhāvāt 
  rūpārūpyadhātāv asatyapi kavaḍīkārāhāre jīvitendriyādevā'vasthānasadbhāvāt 
na ca tatra sparśādīnām avasthāna ādhipatyaṃ yujyate 
nirodhā'saṃjñisamāpattyavasthāyām āsaṃjñike ca sparśādyabhāve'pi sattvānāṃ sthitisambhavād iti 
kulasandhāne strīpuruṣendriyayor ādhipatyam iti 
putrotpattau kulāvyuparatatā vartata iti putrotpattiḥ kulasandhānaṃ 
etad eva darśayann āha  prasavādhipatyād iti 
kāyendriyapradeśa eva kaścid ādhipatyaviśeṣāt strīpuruṣendriyākhyaṃ pratilabhate 
yatra stīndriyaṃ puruṣendriyañcas tastatra kulavyavasthānam asti 
tad vaśena kulo na vyuparamate 
kāmāvacareṣv api ca deveṣu strīndriye puruṣendriye ca sati kulavyavasthānaṃ nā'satīti 
nahi gandharvādīnāṃ tatrādhipatyaṃ satyapi gandharvādau paṇḍakādiṣu strīpuruṣendriyayor asadbhāve putraprasavasāmārthyābhāvāt 
āhārādīnāṃ punaḥ sattve'saṃkhyātatvāt satyapyādhipatye nendriyatvaṃ 
upabhoge vedanendriyāṇāṃ 
ādhipatyam ityadhikṛtaṃ 
katham ityata āha  kuśalākuśalakarmaphalopabhogād iti 
vedanendriyāṇi pañca  sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ saumanasyaṃ daurmanasyam upekṣā ca 
tarhi kuśalākuśalakarmaphala upabhujyate anubhavātmakatvāt 
na nāmarūpasya tadādhipatyaṃ vedanāsambhārabhāvāt 
tat sambhārabhāvaś ca vedanāpradhānatvād vipākasyeti 
laukikaviśuddhiḥ prahāṇaṃ laukikakleśānāṃ 
tatra śraddhādīnām iti śraddhāvīryasmṛtisamādhiprajñāpañcendriyāṇāṃ 
ādhipatyam iti vartate 
teṣām aśraddhādipratipakṣetvena laukikamārgaprabhāvitatvāt 
mokṣabhāgīyaprabhāvitatvād ity apare 
lokottaraviśuddhāvanājñānamājñāsyāmīndriyādīnām ityādhipatyam iti vartate 
lokottaramārgeṇa kleśānāṃ prahāṇaṃ lokottaraviśuddhiḥ 
tatrānājñātam ājñāsyāmīndriyājñendriyājñātāvīndriyāṇāṃ trayāṇām ādhipatyaṃ 
teṣāṃ darśanabhāvanā'śaikṣamārgeṣu yathākramaṃ saṃgṛhītatvāt 
tatra śraddhādīnāṃ pañca manaḥsukhasaumanasyopekṣāṇi cānāgamyādyāśritaviśeṣeṇa sambhavam adhikṛtyaitāni navendriyāṇi darśanamārge'nājñātam ājñāsyāmīndriyaṃ 
bhāvanāmārga ājñendriyaṃ 
aśaikṣaṃārga ajñātāvīndriyam ity ucyate 
yogācārāṇāṃ tv anyathā vyavasthānaṃ 
  anājñātam ājñāsyāmīndriyājñendriye dvaye daśendriyāṇi 
pūrvokteṣu navasu daurmanasyam adhikaṃ prakṣipya daśa bhavanti 
ājñātāvendriyan tu navaiva 
tatra prayogamārge nirvedhabhāgīyātmake pañcadaśasu ca darśanamārgakṣaṇeṣu manaindriyaṃ pañca śraddhādīnyanāgamyādyāśritaviśeṣeṇa yathāsaṃbhavaṃ sukhasaumanasyadaurmanasyopekṣendriyāṇāṃ cānyatamād daurmanasyendriyaṃ punaḥ prayogakāle nirvedhabhāgīyapṛṣṭhenottaravimokṣaspṛhāsangṛhītaṃ veditavyaṃ 
tadetat saṃbhavato daśavidham indriyaṃ 
anājñātam evājñātuṃ pravṛttatvād anājñātam ājñāsyāmīndriyam ucyate 
tadeva daśavidham indriyaṃ ṣoḍaśadarśanamārgakṣaṇādyāvad vajropamaḥ samādhir ityetasmin śaikṣamārgam ājñendriyam ity ucyate apūrvājñātājñeyābhāvāt 
aśaikṣamārge daurmanasyendriyavyatiriktāni śiṣṭānyājñātāvīndriyākhyāṃ pratilabhante 
ājñātāvīndriyam iti ājñātāvīndriyam ucyate 
evam indriyakauśalasya yaḥ puruṣanārāyaṇeśvarādiṣv adhipatigrāhaḥ sa vyāvartate 
  adhyārthaḥ  indriyārthānantaram adhvatrayo vaktavya ityata āha  phalahetūpayogārthanopayogāt tathā'paraṃ 
iti 
tatra janmakāraṇaṃ hetuḥ 
phalaṃ janamasaṃgṛhītaṃ 
phaladānaṃ hetor upayogaḥ 
phalasyopāyogo'nubhūtasya parikṣayaḥ 
evam prakāraścātīto hetus tatphalaṃ cetyataḥ phalasya taddhetoścopayogārthenānīto'dhvā 
tenaiva prakāreṇa phalasya hetoścā'nupayogārthenā'nāgato'dhvā 
vartamānaḥ punar adhvā vartamānaṃ janma 
hetordattaphalatvād hetūpayogārthena tatphalañca vartamānaṃ janmā'nuvartata eveti phalā'nuyogārthena ca veditavyaḥ 
bhāvānāñca pratikṣaṇaṃ hetuphalabhāvatvena kṣaṇatvam adhikṛtyā'dhvavyavasthānaṃ veditavyaṃ 
tatra hetūpayogaḥ svaphalasyotpādānāt 
phalopayogaḥ phalasya janmānantaravināśāt 
evaṃ phalahetūpayogārthenātīto'dhvā phalahetvor anupayogārthenānāgato'rdhveti prakṛtaṃ 
kāryānutpādād anutpannasya ca vināśābhāvāt phalahetvor anupayogo veditavyaḥ 
  hetūpayogaphalānupayogārtheneti kāryotpādanād hetūpayogaḥ 
kāryā'vināśātphalā'nupayogaḥ 
evam adhvakuśalasya nityātmeti grāho vyāvartate 
adhavyatiriktasyānyasyā'nupalabdhatvāt 
  catussatyārthaḥ  adhvatrayārthānantaraṃ catuḥsatyārtho vaktavya ityata āha  vedanāsanimittārthatan nimittaprapattitaḥ 
iti vistaraḥ 
vedanā duḥkhārtha iti loke rūḍhaṃ 
śāstre ca yat kiñcid veditam idam atra duḥkhasyeti vacanāt 
satyavyavasthāyāṃ sarvā sāsravā sanimittā sukhā duḥkhā sukhāduḥkhā ca vedanā duḥkhasatyārtha iti pradarśayan bhāṣyakāra āha  tatra duḥkhasatyaṃ vedanāsanimittārtheneti 
sarvā vedanā duḥkham iti kuta etat  ata āha  yatkiñcid veditam idam atra duḥkhasyeti kṛtveti 
sā ca vedanā duḥkha duḥkhatāvipariṇāmaduḥkhatāsaṃskāraduḥkhatābhir yathāsambhavaṃ duḥkhā 
saṃskāraduḥkhatayaiva vā duḥkhā 
vedanānimittaṃ panar vedanāsthānīyā dharmā veditavyā iti 
sukhaduḥkhā'duḥkhāsukhavedanīyā dharmā vedanāsthānāni 
evaṃ pañcaskandhā duḥkhasatyaṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ 
tan nimitta pratipattitaḥ samudayasatyam iti 
tac chabdena duḥkhasatyam abhisambadhyate 
duḥkhaṃ yayā pratipattyā janyate sā pratipattiḥ samudayasatyaṃ 
sā punar vedanāyāṃ vedanāsthāniyeṣu ca dharmeṣu tṛṣṇāhetupūrvikā kāyavānmanaḥ pracalasvarūpā 
saṃkṣepataś ca bhavasamudbhavikaṃ karmasamudaya satyam ity uktam bhavati 
tayoḥ śamārthena nirodhasatyam iti 
tayor iti duḥkhasamudayasatyayoḥ 
śamārthenety utpādanārthena 
evañca sahetukaduḥKhānutpādalakṣaṇatvān nirodho dvividha uktaḥ samudayaśamārthena sopadhiśeṣaḥ duḥkhopaśamārthena nirupādhiśeṣa iti tayor evādhikṛtayor duḥkhasamudayayoḥ pratipakṣārthena duḥkhasamudayanirodhagāminī pratipan mārgasatyaṃ 
tadevaṃ satyakuśalasya sankleśavyavadānamātrāvagatatvāt tadanyaḥ sankleśavyavadānagraho vyāvartate tasyābhāvād iti 
  yānatrayā'rthaḥ   satyārthānantaraṃ yānatrayārthaṃ pratipādyata ityata āha  guṇadoṣā'vikalpena jñānena iti vistaraḥ 
jñānaśabda ubhayatra sambadhyate 
guṇadoṣajñānenā'vikalpajñānena ceti 
athavā'ntare vikalpaśabdo lupto draṣṭavyaḥ 
tatra guṇadoṣajñānena parataḥ svayañceti ata evāha  vṛttau yathāyogam iti 
tatra nirvāṇasaṃsārayor guṇadoṣajñāneneti 
nirvāṇaśabdenātra mārganirodhau sangṛhītau yathā praśāntaśabdaḥ 
tatra nirodhe śāntādyākāraiḥ mārge nairyāṇikādyākārair jñānaṃ nirvāṇe guṇajñānaṃ 
saṃsāro'pi duḥkhasamudayātmakaḥ 
tatrā'py anityaduḥkhādyākāraiḥ samudayapratyayādyākāraiś ca jñānaṃ saṃsāre doṣajñānaṃ 
parataḥ śrutveti buddhabodhisattvādibhyo nirvāṇasaṃsārayor guṇānyathokān doṣāṃś ca śrutveti 
niryāṇārtheneti saṃsāranirgamārthena 
śrāvakayānam iti paradghoṣasaṃniśrayeṇa niryāṇāt śrāvakāyanm iti pratyekabuddhayānād viśeṣaṃ darśayati 
tenaiveti nirvāṇasaṃsārayor guṇadoṣajñānena svayam aśrutvā parato buddhabodhasattvebhyo niryāṇārthena pratyekabuddhayānaṃ 
svayam aśrutveti śrāvakayānād viśeṣaṇaṃ 
avikalpena jñāneneti saṃsāranirvāṇayor anabhilāpyadharmatāprativedhād avikalpaṃ jñānaṃ 
svayam eva parato'śrutvā niryāṇārthena mahāyānaṃ 
atra hi jñāneneti pratyekabuddhayānād viśeṣaḥ 
anye tvāhuḥ  pudgalanairātmyaviṣayeṇa guṇadoṣā'vikalpena jñānena parataḥ śrutvā niryāṇaṃ śrāvakayānaṃ 
śravaṇanirapekṣasya svayaṃ niryāṇaṃ pratyekabuddhayānaṃ 
dharmanairātmyaviṣayeṇā'pratiṣṭhitanirvāṇaprāpakenā'vikalpena jñānena svayaṃ niryāṇaṃ mahāyānam ucyate 
etad vyākhyānaṃ bhāṣyeṇa virudhyate 
evaṃ yānatrayakuśalasya yogamātradarśanād ātmā yogīti grāho vyāvartate 
   bhogasangṛhītatamedevottaram uktaṃ 
tad dvayaṃ śeṣāṇi vijñānānyadhipativastutvena bhuñjata iti bhogaḥ 
athavā annapānādiko'rtho bhujyata iti bhogaḥ 
tan nirbhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ bhogasangṛhītaṃ 
etat saprajñapti sahetukaṃ nimittaṃ sasamprayogaṃ paratantrasvabhāvasangṛhītatvāt saṃskṛtaṃ veditavyaṃ 
samprayogaścaittāḥ 
tat saṃskṛtaṃ na kevalaṃ tadeveti darśayati 
kasya punas tannimittaṃ  nāmakāyādīnāṃ 
teṣāṃ tat svabhāvaviśeṣasaṃsūcakatvāt tadanusāreṇa ca svabhāvaviśeṣābhiniveśināṃ cittacaittānāṃ manaudgrahavikalpākhyānāṃ nimittaṃ 
manaudgrahavikalpaścālayavijñānasya nimittaṃ 
tasmin vāsanapoṣaṇatvād ityeke 
anye tu manyante  svabhāvaviśeṣaprajñāpanāt prajñapter nimittaṃ saṃjñāṃ nimittodgrahaṇātmiketi vacanāt 
pratiṣṭhādehabhogasaṃgṛhītam ālayavijñānaṃ nidānanimittaṃ vāsanāpoṣaṇatvāt 
ālambananimittañca mana udgrahavikalpā ālambananimittīkaraṇārthena 
ālambanālambana nimittaṃ cobhayathā nimittīkaraṇād iti 
tatra mano yan nityaṃ manyanākāram iti 
ahaṃ mameti yan nityaṃ manyate tanmata ucyate 
tac ca samprayuktam ātmamohātmadṛṣṭyātmasnehātmamānaiḥ pañcabhiś ca sarvatragair vedanāsaṃjñācetanāsparśamanaskārair iti 
udgrahaḥ pañca vijñānakāyā iti viṣayasvarūpagrahaṇalakṣaṇatvāt svasaṃvedyā ityākhyātum aśakyatvād udgraha ucyate 
vikalpo manovijñānaṃ 
tasya dharmasvasāmānyalakṣaṇavikalpakatvād iti 
etatsarvaṃ saprajñaptisahetukaṃ nimittaṃ karmakleśābhyām abhisaṃskṛtatvāt saṃskṛtaṃ 
asaṃskṛtaṃ punaḥ praśamaś ca nirodhaḥ praśamārthaś ca tathateti yuktaṃ nirodhasya praśamasvarūpatvaṃ sannimittaduḥkhapraśamalakṣaṇāt 
kathaṃ tathatā praśamārtham ucyata iti  praśamasyārtha iti kṛtvā 
nanu ca nirodhena tathatayā na kaścit sambandho'sti kathaṃ praśamārthatvaṃ  tathatāyā mārgālambanatvāt 
mārgasya punaḥ kathaṃ praśamatvaṃ  tena praśamanāt 
nirvāṇaṃ praśamaḥ praśamanāt 
anena ca praśamanāt praśamo mārgaḥ 
evaṃ vigrahabhedād ekābhidhānena nirvāṇamārgayor grahaṇaṃ praśama iti 
mārgasatyaṃ punaḥ kiṃ saṃskṛtam asaṃskṛtaṃ  saṃskṛtaṃ utpādyatvāt 
yadi karmakleśābhyām anabhisaṃskṛtād asaṃskṛtena ca prabhāvitād asaṃskṛtam iti brūyān na doṣaḥ syād iti 
ityetenārthena skandhādiṣu jñānaṃ skandhādikauśalyaṃ veditavyam iti 
  anekatvābhisaṃkṣepaparicchedārtha āditaḥ 
iti vistareṇa sarvatra vācyaṃ 
  tattvapiṇḍārthaḥ  tattvasya piṇḍārthaḥ 
samāsato dvividhaṃ tattvaṃ 
vistareṇa daśavidham uktaṃ 
ataḥ samāsato dvividham ityāha  ādarśatattvaṃ dṛśyatattvañca 
tatra mūlatattvam ādarśatattvaṃ 
tat punas trayaḥ svabhāvāḥ 
kim arthaṃ punas tad ādarśatattvam ityucyate  śeṣāṇāṃ lakṣaṇatattvādīnāṃ tatra darśanāt 
dṛśyatattvaṃ yat lakṣaṇatattvādikaṃ pūrvanirdiṣṭaṃ navavidhaṃ 
kimarthaṃ tad dṛṣyatattvam ity ucyate  tasya mūlatattve darśanāt nirabhimānadṛśyatattvaṃ lakṣaṇatattvaṃ 
tena hi nirabhimāno bhavati 
pudgaladharmayor grāhyagrāhakayor bhāvābhāvayoś cā'samāropānapavādaviparyāsa dṛśyatattvam aviparyāsalakṣaṇaṃ 
taddhi nityādiviparyāsapratipakṣabhūtaṃ 
śrāvakayānaniryāṇadṛśyatattvaṃ phalahetumayaṃ tattvaṃ 
caturāryasatya prativedhabhāvanayā śrāvakaniryāṇaṃ 
mahāyānaniryāṇadrśyatattvaṃ sūkṣmaudārikatattvaṃ 
audārikena saṃvṛtisatyena sattvaparipācanāt sūkṣmeṇa paramārthasatyena vimocanāt mahāyānena niryāti 
paravādinigrahadṛśyatattvaṃ prasiddhatattvaṃ 
katham ityata āha  dṛṣṭānasanniśrayeṇa yuktyā nigrahād iti 
nigrahe lokaprasiddho dṛṣṭāntaḥ 
yuktiprasiddhaśabdāśrayād yuktiḥ 
mahāyānābhidyotanadṛśyatattvaṃ viśuddhijñānagocaratattvaṃ 
  taddhi kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānagocarād anyasyābhidyotaka āgamaḥ 
tat punar mahāyānaṃ 
sarvākārajñeyapraveśadṛśyatattvaṃ saṃgrahatattvaṃ 
tac ca pañca vastūni tatra sarvajñeyānupraveśāt 
avitathatā'bhidyotanadṛśyatattvaṃ prabhedatattvaṃ 
tena hi bhāvānāmavitathatathatā'nanyatathatayor abhidyotanāt 
ātmagrāhavastusarvābhisandhipraveśadṛśyatattvañceti kauśalayatattvaṃ 
tena hy ātmagrāhavastu sarvābhiprāyamukhena praviśatīti yathā pūrvam uktaṃ daśabhir abhiprāyaiḥ skandhādiṣv ātmagrāhapravṛttitvaṃ 
tattvapiṇḍārthavacanaṃ sukhadhāraṇārtham arthād grantham ākarṣatīti 
asammohāparikhedārthañca paridṛṣṭādhikāraparyantasya hi na parikheda upajñāyate nāpi sammoho yathoddeśanirdeśādhigamād utapdyate 
uktaṃ tattvaṃ 
āgamānusāriṇyāṃ madhyāntavibhāgaṭīkāyām ācāryabhadantasthi ramatyuparacitāyāṃ tattvaparicchedastṛtīyaḥ samāptaḥ 
  pratipakṣabhāvanā'vasthāphalaparicchedaścaturthaḥ   pratipakṣabhāvanā   tattvapratipādanānantaraṃ pratipakṣabhāvanā vaktavyā tatrā'vasthā phalaprāptiś ca 
atas tatpratipādanārthaṃ caturthaparicchedārambhaḥ 
tattvānantaram uddiṣṭatvāt pratipakṣabhāvanāpratibaddhatvāc ca tad avasthāphalaprāptyor uddeśaḥ 
sūtre pratipakaṣatvena bodhipakṣo'numata iti pradarśanārtham āha  pratipakṣabhāvanā bodhipakṣyabhāveneti 
te hi yathoktāvaraṇavipakṣaprahāṇāya bhāvyamānaḥ prabhavantīti pratipakṣā ucyante 
te punaḥ saptatriṃśat  catvāri smṛtypasthānāni yāvadāryāṣṭānga mārgāḥ 
tad bhāvanā bṛṃhaṇāropaṇā abhyāso bahulā kriyeti paryāyāḥ 
sedānīṃ vaktavyā tattvānantaram uddiṣṭatvāt 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ smṛtyupasthānabhāvanaiva pūrvam ucyate nānyā bodhipakṣabhāvanā  āha  tatra tāvadādau  dauṣṭhulyāt tarṣahetutvāt iti vistaraḥ 
tatreti bodhipakṣabhāvanāyāṃ 
tāvacchabdārthaḥ kramārthaḥ 
ādau tāvat smṛtyupasthānabhāvanocyate 
paścād anyeṣām apīti 
nirvāṇasaṃsāryor guṇadoṣā'navabodhāt 
saṃskāreṣu sukhaśucinityātmābhiniveśena bālānāṃ bhavabhoge'bhivacanaṃ  nirvāṇārthaṃ trāsaḥ 
sa ca guṇadoṣānavabodhaḥ sukhādyabhiniveśaś ca satyadarśanād vinivartata ityataḥ saṃsārād udvajanārthaṃ nirvāṇe cābhimukhīkaraṇārthaṃ catuḥsatyāvatārāya smṛtyupasthānabhāvanaivādāv uktā 
kāyena hi dauṣṭhulyaṃ prabhāvyata iti 
dauṣṭhulyaṃ duḥsthitatā 
tathā hi pratidinam abhisaṃskriyamāṇo vikriyata eva kāya iti kāyena dauṣṭhulyaṃ prabhāvyate 
tataś ca kāyaparīkṣayā duḥkhasatyam avatarati 
kim artham etad ityāha  tasya sadauṣṭhulyasaṃskāralakṣaṇatvād iti 
yasmād duḥkhasatyasya sadauṣṭhulyāḥ saṃskārāḥ lakṣaṇaṃ svabhāvaḥ kāyena ca dauṣṭhulyaṃ prabhāvyate tasmāt kāyaparīkṣayā duḥkhasatyam avatarati 
dauṣṭhulyaṃ na vijñāyata ityata āha  dauṣṭhulyaṃ hi saṃskāraduḥkhateti 
saṃskāro bhāvanām utpattiḥ 
sa ca sarvaviplavastv iti dauṣṭhulyamāryāṇāṃ pratikūlatvāc ca duḥkhatā 
yathoktaṃ  anartho janmedaṃ sati hi janane santi ripavo jarāmṛtyuvyādhivyasanabandhaprabhṛtayaḥ 
anarthās te na syur yadi na bhavato nāśavibhavā vajāte vṛkṣe syān na hi dahanadavavāyucyutir api 
tayeti saṃskāraduḥkhatayā na vipariṇāmaduḥkhatāduḥkhaduḥkhatābhyāṃ tayor āvyāpitvāt saṃskāraduḥKhatānimittatvāc ca 
sarvaṃ sāsravaṃ vastvāryā duḥkhatā paśyanti nā'nāsavaṃ mārgasatyasya janmotpattipratipakṣatvāt na tu pṛthagjanā viparyāsasthānāśrayatvāt 
sūtre'py uktaṃ  samāsataḥ pañcopādānaskandhā duḥkham iti 
saṃskāraduḥkhatā'karmaṇyatetyanye 
na dauṣṭhulyam akarmaṇyātetyapare 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  akarmaṇyātāyāḥ sāsravatvād avaśyaṃ sāsravatāṃ bījakāraṇotpannā'bhyupagantavyā 
sā tv abījāpyarthasantāne kadācid āhārādyapacārād bhavati 
na cāsau dauṣṭhulyaṃ bhavitum arhatya nāsravatvād iti 
ataś ca sāsravadharmabījam ālayavijñānasanniviṣṭaṃ dauṣṭhulyenātreṣyate 
ayaṃ sukhaduḥkhā'sukhā'duḥkhasahitaḥ kāyastat phalaṃ 
tasmāt sukhādyavakāśasahitena kāyena pratikṣaṇabhāvinā tad dauṣṭhulyaṃ prabhāvyate pratīyata ityarthaḥ 
tadyathā khalavilāntargataṃ bījam ankureṇeti 
tasmāt kāyaparīkṣayā duḥkhasatyam avatarati 
atra kāraṇam āha   tasya sadauṣṭhulyasaṃskāralakṣaṇatvād iti sabījasaṃskārātmakatvād ityarthaḥ 
saṃskāraduḥkhatā hi vipariṇāmaduḥkhatāduḥkhaduḥkhatādauṣṭhulyābhyām anugatatvāt kāraṇatvāc ca dauṣṭhulyam ityktā 
ata eva saṃskāraduḥkhatayā sarvasāsravaṃ vastvāryaiḥ duḥkhatvenālokita 
evaṃ kāyasmṛtyupasthānena duḥkhasatyam avataratīti 
tṛṣṇāhetur vedanā  avidyāsaṃsparśajetyabhiprāyāt anāsravāyā atad hetutvāt 
tatra sukhā vedanā tat saṃyogāviyogatṛṣṇāyā hetuḥ 
duḥkhā tad asaṃyogaviyogatṛṣṇāyā hetuḥ 
aduḥkhasukhā tad avasthābhir atitṛṣṇāyās tat saṃyogāviyogatṛṣṇāyāś ca kasyāṃcit samāptau hetur iti 
sa duḥkhavedanayā spṛṣṭaḥ kāmasukham abhinandatīti vacanāt duḥkhāpi vedanā sukhāyāḥ tṛṣṇayā hetur bhavati 
tat parīkṣayā samudayasatyam avatarati 
sa hi vedanāṃ svarūpataḥ kāraṇataḥ kāryato'nityato duḥkhataścopaparīkṣamāṇaḥ samudayasatyam avatarati tṛṣṇāṃ tat kāryatvenāvagacchatītyarthaḥ 
tṛṣṇā hi sūtre samudayasatyam ityuktā 
ko duḥkhasamudayaḥ  paṭhyate  tṛṣṇā paunarbhavikānandā rāgasahagateti vistaraḥ 
evaṃ vedanāsmṛtyupasthānena samudayasatyam avatarati 
ātmābhiniveśavastu cittam iti 
anyasya nityādiguṇaviśiṣṭasyātmano'bhāvād ātmābhiniveśālambanaṃ cittam eva 
tasmāt tat parīkṣayā nirodhasatyam avatarati śāntatvena 
atraiva kāraṇam āha  ātmocchedabhayāpagamād iti 
citte hy anityatvādiparīkṣayā'tmābhiniveśo vyāvartate duḥkhasaṃjñā pravartate 
ataścātmocchedabhayāpagamād duḥkhamātrasyocchedān nirodhasatyaṃ śāntatvenāvataratīti 
evaṃ cittasmṛtyupasthānena nirodhasatyam avataratīti 
 dharmaparīkṣayā sānkleśikavyāvadānikadharmāsaṃmohān mārgasatyam avataratīti 
tatra sānkleśikā dharmāḥ kleśopakleśāḥ 
vyāvadānikās tu kleśopakleśapratipakṣabhūtāḥ premamaitryādayaḥ 
teṣāṃ sānkleśikānāṃ vyāvadānikānāñca vipakṣapratipakṣabhāvaṃ buddhvā sarvopadravātyantaprahāṇopāye mārgasatye'bhimukhībhavati 
evaṃ dharmasmṛtyupasthānena mārgasatyam avataratīti 
avatāro'tra pratyekaṃ satye satyalakṣaṇāvabodhaḥ 
tatra kāyasmṛtyupasthānabhāvanā anityato duḥkhataḥ śūnyato'nātmato'pi anekā'śucidravyasvabhāvato'pi aśucibījato'pi aśuciniṣyandato'pi aśucisthitihetuto'pi aśucivikārato'pi phenabhanga ivāsārato'pi gatito'pi yonito'pi 
vedanācittadharmasmṛtyupasthānabhāvanā punar anityaduḥkhaśūnyānātmato'pi svalakṣaṇato'pi hetuto'pi phalato'pi dhātubhūmigatito'pi kuśalākuśalāvyākṛtato'pi vipakṣapratipakṣato'pi 
bodhisattvānāṃ punaḥ smṛtyupasthānabhāvanā evañcānupalambhākāreṇa ca vikalpaprahāṇārthaṃ 
smṛtyupasthānānāṃ tu prajñāsvābhāvye'pi smṛtyupasthānavacanaṃ smṛtibalenopasthānād etāsāṃ prajñānāṃ smṛtyupasthānam ucyate 
   catvāri samyakprahāṇāni  smṛtyupasthānabhāvanānantaraṃ samyakprahāṇabhāvanoktā 
kiṃ kāraṇam ata āha yasmāt  parijñāte vipakṣe ca iti vistaraḥ 
smṛtyupasthānabhāvanayeti 
aviśeṣābhidhāne'pi dharmasmṛtyupasthānabhāvanayaiveti veditavyaṃ 
dhātubhūmyavakāśaiḥ sāmānyalakṣaṇādyākārais tathā sāsravānāsravanadhātubhūmiśaikṣāśaikṣādyākārais tathā sāsravānāsravadhātubhūmiśaikṣāśaikṣādibhedena ca vipakṣe pratipakṣe ca sarvaprakāra parijñāte 
vipakṣāgamāyeti 
vipakṣāpagamamo'trotpannānāṃ prabandhacchedo'nutpannānāṃ cānutpādaḥ 
pratipakṣopagamāya ceti 
pratipakṣāgama utpannānāṃ prabandhānuvṛttir anutpannānāñcotpādaḥ 
vīryaṃ caturdhā pravartata iti vipakṣapratipakṣayor utpanānutpannabhedena caturdhā vīryasya pravṛttiḥ 
utpannānāṃ pāpakānām akuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ prahāṇāyeti vistara itīdam āgamena vīryasyaiva caturdhā pravṛttiṃ darśayati 
vistaravacanena śeṣagranthābhisambandhaḥ 
tatrāyāṃ śeṣo granghaḥ  prahāṇāya chandaṃ janayati vyāyacchate vīryam ārabhate cittaṃ pragṛhṇāti samyakpradadhātīti 
evam anutpannānāṃ pāpakānām akuśalānāṃ dharmāṇām anutpādāya chandañjanayatīti vistaraḥ 
evam anutpannānāṃ kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇām utpādaya chandañjanayatīti vistaraḥ 
utpannānāṃ kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ sthitaye bhūyobhāvatāyai asampramoṣāya paripūraṇāya chandañjanayati vyāyacchate vīryam ārabhate cittaṃ pragṛhṇāti 
samyak pradadhāti 
utpannānāṃ sthitir aparihāṇiḥ 
bhūyobhāvaḥ prabandhenotpādaḥ 
paripūriḥ prakarṣagamanaṃ 
chandañjanayatīti sagauravodyaktavīryasamṛddhiṃ darśayati 
vyāyacchata iti kausīdyaprahāṇāya kāyacitte'bhimukhīkarotītyarthaḥ 
vīryam ārabhata iti layauddhatyāpakarṣaṇārthaṃ 
katham ārabheta  līnaṃ cittaṃ pragṛhṇāti samvejanīyapramodānīyadharmamanaskāraiḥ 
uddhataṃ cittaṃ tasminnevālambane samyak pradadhāti samvejanīyapramodanīyadharmamanaskārair dhārayatītyarthaḥ 
evañca  samyakpradhānāni vīryātmakānīti jñāpitam bhavati 
samyag ebhiḥ kāyavānmanāṃsi dhārayantīti samyakpradhānāni 
  catvāraḥ ṛddhipādāḥ  karmañatā sthites tatra iti vistaraḥ 
tatreti tasyāṃ vipakṣapratipakṣāyāpagamavīryabhāvanāyāṃ 
karmaṇyatā cittasthiteḥ sarvārthasamṛddhiyogyatā 
sā ca karmaṇyatā chandavīryacittamīmāṃsādhipatyaprabhavetyata āha  karmaṇyatā catvāra ṛddhipādā iti 
sarvasyābhijñādikasyārthasya samṛddhi ṛddhiḥ 
tasyāḥ pratiṣṭhārthena ṛddhipādā ṛddhihetava ityarthaḥ 
ata evāha  sarvārthasamṛddhihetutvād iti 
te punaścandasamādhiḥ prahāṇasaṃskārasamanvāgata ṛddhipādaḥ vīryasamādhiḥ prahāṇasaṃskārasamanvāgata ṛddhipādā cittasamādhiḥ prahāṇasaṃskārasamanavāgata ṛddhipādaḥ mīmāṃsāsamādhiḥ prahāṇasaṃskārasamanvāgata ṛddhipāda iti 
tatra cchandsamādhir yadā chandādhipatyād vīryabhāvanāyāṃ sagauravaṃ pravartamānaḥ spṛśati cittasyakāgratāṃ 
vīryasamādhir yadā vīryam ārabhamāṇaḥ sātatyaprayogāt spṛśati cittasyaikāgratāṃ 
cittasamādhir yadā pūrvasamādhibījam āgamya citta eva cittaṃ dhārayan spṛśati cittasyaikāgratāṃ 
mīmāmsāsamādhir yadālambanapravicito'nuspṛśati cittasyaikāgratām iti 
sthitiratra cittasthitiḥ samādhir veditavya iti samādhigrahaṇaṃ saṃskṛtalakṣaṇād vyavacchedārthaṃ 
yata ārabdhavīryasya cittakarmaṇyatā catvāra ṛddhipādā bhavanti ataḥ samyak prahāṇānantaraṃ ṛddhipādā nirdiṣṭāḥ 
sā punaḥ karmaṇyatā  kim prayojanā kiṃ hetukā cetyata āha  pañcadoṣaprahāṇāyāṣṭaprahāṇasaṃskārabhāvanānvayā videtavyeti 
anvayo hetuḥ 
  pañca doṣāḥ  te ca pañcadoṣā na vijñāyanta ityataḥ pṛcchati katame pañca doṣā iti 
tat pradarśayann āha  kausīdyam avavādasya sammoṣo laya udbhavaḥ 
iti vistaraḥ 
ete hi ṣaḍdoṣā ityata āha  tatra layauddhatyam eko doṣaḥ kriyata iti pañca bhavanti 
tatra kausīdyaṃ prayogakāle doṣas tenāprayogāt 
udyuktasyāvavādasammoṣo doṣas tena cittasamādhānabhāvāt 
samāhitasya layauddhatyaṃ doṣastena cittakarmaṇyatā'bhāvāt 
anabhisaṃskāro layauddhatyapraśamanakāle doṣaḥ 
anabhisaṃskāra upekṣā tayā tad dvayāśamanāt 
abhisaṃskāraḥ praśāntau doṣa iti 
abhisaṃskāraścetanā 
layauddhatyavigamāddhi samatāprāptatvāt praśāntam ity ucyate 
  aṣṭau prahāṇasaṃskārāḥ   prahāṇasaṃskārāḥ prahāṇāya saṃskārāḥ 
kasya prahāṇāya  anantaroktānāṃ pañcānāṃ doṣāṇāṃ prahāṇāya 
yadyevaṃ tena vaktavyam eṣāṃ prahāṇāya katham aṣṭau prahāṇasaṃskārā vyavasthāpyanta iti 
tatra kausīdyaprahāṇāya catvāraś chandavyāyāmaśraddhāprasrabdhayaḥ 
tatra cchando'bhilāṣaḥ 
vyāyāmo vīryaṃ 
śraddhā'bhisampratyayaḥ 
prasrabdhiḥ karmaṇyatā 
kathaṃ punar ete kausīdyaprahāṇāya vyavasthāpyanta ityata āha  te punar yathākramaṃ veditavyāḥ 
āśrayo'rthāśritas tasya nimittaṃ phalam eva ca 
iti 
ato'nyonyaprabhāvitatvād ete kausīdyaprahāṇāya samvartanta iti darśayati  āśrayaśchando vyāyāmasya āśrito vyāyāmaḥ 
abhilāṣasya vyāyāmapūrvakatvāt 
tasyāśrayasya chandasya nimittaṃ śraddhā 
katham ityato bravīti  sampratyaye saty abhilāṣād iti 
śraddadhānasya hi hetuphale kriyābhilāṣo bhavati 
tasyāśritasya vyāyāmasya phalaṃ prasrabdhiḥ 
katham ityata āha  prārabdhavīryasya samādhiviśeṣā'dhigamād iti 
samādhiviśeṣagamanaṃ hi prasrabdhinimittaṃ 
ata ārabdhavīryasya samādhiviśeṣagamanāt prasrabdhir vyāyāmaphalam ityuktaṃ 
tathā hy ārabdhavīryasya dauṣṭhulyavitarkādyapakṣālavigamāt pramoda utpadyate 
manaḥpramodāt kāyacittayoḥ prasrabdhiḥ karmaṇyatālakṣaṇatā 
tataḥ samādhiviśeṣagamanam iti 
atra ca vīryaṃ sahetukaṃ saphalaṃ ca kausīdyapratipakṣeṇoktaṃ 
caturṇāṃ doṣāṇāṃ yathāsaṃkhyaṃ pratipakṣa iti 
tatra smṛtir avavādasammoṣasya pratipakṣaḥ 
samprayojanyaṃ layauddhatyasya 
cetanā'nabhisaṃskārasya 
abhisaṃskārasyopekṣeti saṃskāropekṣā'tra veditavyā 
smṛtyādīnāṃ punar lakṣaṇavivakṣayedam āha  te punaḥ smṛtyādayo veditavyā yathākramam iti 
smṛtir ālambane'sammoṣa iti 
  vistarīkṛtamālambanam iti cittasthāpanīyam avavādavastv abhilapanam ityartaḥ 
samprajanyaṃ smṛtyasampramoṣe sati layauddhatyāvabodha iti 
upasthitasmṛtir hi samprajanyavān bhavatyevetyata āha  smṛtyasampramoṣe satīti 
anubuddhyā layauddhatyaṃ śamathavipaśyane yuganaddhādaprayatnena pravartetetyarthaḥ 
upekṣeti viṣayāntarānabhisaṃskāra ityarthaḥ 
etad uktaṃ bhavati  sūpasthitasmṛtiravavāde līnaṃ cittam uddhtaṃ vā yathābhūtaṃ prajānāti 
layauddhatyavigamāya ca tad abhisaṃskaroti layauddhatyavigamāc copekṣāṃ karotīti 
evaṃ tasya cittapraśaṭhatā karmaṇyatā 
atra ca karmaṇyatāsthitir iti svārthe bhāvapratyayaḥ svapeṭatvādivat 
  pañcendriyāṇi  ṛddhipādānantaraṃ pañcendriyāṇi śraddhādīnyuktānīti sambadhyate 
teṣāṃ kathaṃ vyavasthānam iti kenārthenetyabhiprāyaḥ 
ata āha  ropite mokṣabhāgīye chandayogādhipatyataḥ 
iti vistaraḥ 
ādhipatyata iti vartata ityanena cchandayogādhipatyata ityatrādhipatyaśabdaḥ prayukta uttaratrāpyanuvartata iti darśayati 
ṛddhipādaiḥ karmaṇyacittasyāropite mokṣabhāgīye kuśalamūle iti 
karmaṇyacittasya vimokṣabhāgīyaṃ kuśalamūlaṃ cittasandhāne pratiṣṭhāṃ pratilabhate chandādhipatyato yāvat pravicayādhipatyataḥ na tv akarmaṇyacittasya 
sā ca cittakarmaṇyatā ṛddhipādair bhavati 
tasmād ṛddhipādānantaraṃ vimokṣabhāgīyakuśalamūlaropaṇādhipatyataḥ pañca śraddhādīnīndriyāṇīti vyavasthāpyante 
chandādhipatyata iti kāraṇe kāryopacārāśchraddhaivātra chandaśabdenoktā tadyathā dadhatrapuṣaṃ sadyojvara iti 
athavāstitvaguṇaśaktiṣu yathākramam abhisampratyayaprasādābhilāṣāḥ śraddhāyā lakṣaṇaṃ 
ataścandagrahaṇenātrābhilāṣalakṣaṇā śraddhaiva gṛhyate na tu cchanda iti 
prayogādhipatyata iti prayujyate 'neneti prayogaḥ 
prayogaśabdena vīryam abhipretaṃ 
ālambanāsampramoṣādhipatyata iti smṛtīndriyādhipatyataḥ 
ālmbanābhilapanalakṣaṇaṃ smṛtīndriyaṃ 
avisārādhipatyata iti samādhīndriyādhipatyataḥ 
avisāro hi samādhīndriyaṃ cittaikāgratālakṣaṇatvāt 
pravicayādhipatyataśceti prajñendriyādhipatyataḥ 
prajñendriyasya dharmapravicayātmakatvāt 
ca śabdo vimokṣabhāgīyakuśalamūlaropaṇādhipattyāt 
  yathākramaṃ pañca śraddhādīnīndriyāṇi veditavyānīti darśayati 
śraddhadhāno hi saṃsāracārakān niḥsaraṇārthaṃ vīryam ārabhate 
ārabdhavīryasya triśikṣāniṣpattiḥ smṛtisamādhiprajñendriyāṇi yathākramaṃ 
evaṃ darśanamārgaprayogabhūmāv indriyāṇāṃ prādhānyam iṣyate 
anye tvāhuḥ  na mokṣabhāgīyakuśalamūlaropaṇādhipatyataḥ śraddhādīnām indriyatvaṃ 
kiṃ tarhi ropite mokṣabhāgīyakuśalamūle chandādīnām ādhipatyata etānīndriyāṇy ucyante 
etad eva pradarśayann āha  chandādhipatyataḥ śraddhāyā indriyatvam iti sambadhyate 
prayogo vyāpāraḥ 
asammoṣa ālambanavipraṇāśaḥ 
avisaraṇam avisāraḥ 
pravicayanaṃ pravicayaḥ 
teṣāṃ prayogasammoṣāvisārapravicayānām ādhipatyād vīryasmṛtisamādhiprajñākhyaścaittā indriyākhyaṃ bhavantīti 
atra tvetad vaktavyaṃ  ropite mokṣabhāgīye kuśalamūle ropitāvasthātaś candādyādhipatyasya śraddhādīnāñca kaścid viśiṣṭasvabhāvo nāsti yasmāt tadavasthāyāṃ tad ādhipatyāt teṣām indriyatvam avasthāpyata iti 
  pañca balāni  tānyeva śraddhādīni balavanti balānyucyante indriyānantaram uktānīti 
teṣāṃ punar balavattvaṃ kuta ityata āha  vipakṣasya hi saṃlikhāt iti 
vipakṣasya saṃlikhitatvāt 
etad eva pradarśayann āha  yadā tānīti śraddhādīndriyāṇi 
āśraddhyādibhir vipakṣair iti 
āśraddhyakausīdyavismṛtivikṣepāsamprajanyaiḥ śraddhādivipakṣair na vyavakīryante atyarthaṃ tanutvād antarāntarā samudācārābhāvān na vyāmiśryanta ityarthaḥ tadā balānyucyante 
tānīndriyāṇi vipakṣair avakīryante tadā tad vipakṣasyānirlikhitatvāt 
  yadyanirjitavipakṣāṇīndriyāṇi tat kathaṃ kauśalyatattve laukikaviśuddhyādhipatyena śraddhādīnām indriyatvam uktaṃ 
tatra hy abhedenendriyāṇy abhipretāni atra tu nirvedhabhāgīyasya kuśalamūlasya bhedapradarśanārthaṃ 
tasmān nāsti virodhaḥ 
atra evātrāha etānyevendriyāṇi balāny ucyanta iti 
śraddadhāno hi hetuphale vīryam ārabhate 
ayaṃ heturasyaiva phalasya idañca phalam asyaiva hetor ityevaṃ śraddadhānaḥ phalaśraddhayā taddhetau vīryam ārabhate 
ārabhdavīryasya tat paratvāt smṛtir upatiṣṭhate 
upasthitasmṛter vipakṣepābhāvāc cittaṃ samādhīyate ekāgraṃ bhavati 
samāhitacitto yathābhūtaṃ prajānātīti samādhyanugṛhītā prajñā sphuṭā bhavati 
avaropitamokṣa bhāgīyasyendriyāṇy uktāni 
mokṣabhāgīyānantaraṃ nirvedhabhāgīyānīti indriyānantarañca balānyato vaktavyaṃ nirvedhabhāgīyāni kim indriyāvasthāyāṃ veditavyānyāhosvid balāvasthāyāṃ  tathā kiṃ nirvedhabhāgīyānīnidriyāṇi balasvabhāvānyāhosvit tad vyatiriktasvabhāvānītyata āha  dvau dvau nirvedhabhāgīyāvīndriyāṇi balāni ca 
iti 
athavā yathā moksabhāgīyāni pratipakṣabhāvanāprabhāvitāni śraddhādiprabhāvitāni vā bhavanti tathā nirvedhabhāgīyāny api 
ata āha  ropitamokṣabhāgīyasyendriyāṇy uktānīti vistaraḥ 
ata āha  dvau dvau nirvedhabhāgīyau iti sarvaṃ 
uṣmagatāni mūrdhāścendriyāṇīti 
mṛdutvād ayuktatvād eṣāṃ kuśalānām eṣu balānām indriyāṇyeva 
kṣāntayo laukikāścāgradharmā balānīti 
adhimātratvād eṣām indiryāṇām asambhavāt kṣāntayo'gradharmāś ca balānyeva 
mṛdumadhyādhimātrabhedena hi trividhāni śraddhādīni 
tatra mṛdūni madhyāni cendriyāṇi 
adhimātrāṇi balāni 
yāni mṛdūni tānyuṣmagatāni 
madhyāni mūrdhānaḥ 
adhimātrāṇi punaścaturdhā kriyante 
tatra mṛdumadhyādhimātrāṇi yathākramaṃ mṛdumadhyādhimātrāḥ kṣāntayaḥ 
adhimātrādhimātrāṇi laukikā agradharmā iti 
etāni ca nirvedhabhāgīyāni sarvāṇi  samādhiprajñāsvabhāvāni sasaṃprayogāṇi 
tatroṣmaprakāra uṣmagataṃ 
yathā'raṇinirmathanāt tad dahanasamarthasyāgner utpatīcihnaṃ pūrvam ūṣmotpadyate evaṃ sarvakleśendhanadahanasamarthasyāryamārgāgneḥ pūrvarūpatvāt tad uṣmagatam ity ucyate 
calakuśalamūlebhyo mūrdhopagamanatvān mūrdhā 
kṣāntiḥ satyārthe kṣamāvattvāt 
tad anyasāsravadharmaśreṣṭhatvāc ca laukikā agradharmā ity ucyante 
teṣāṃ tv agratā tad anantaraṃ darśanamārgotpatteḥ 
te ca kṣaṇikāḥ śeṣāṇi nirvedhabhāgīyāni santānavanti 
tatra mokṣabhāgīyaṃ kuśalamūlaṃ saṃsāraprabhāvanaśaktighātayogena veditavyaṃ 
nirvedhabhāgīyam anāsravadharmotpattiśaktyādhānayogeneti 
  sapta bodhyangāni  agradharmānantaraṃ darśanamārgotpattes tasya bodhyangaprabhāvitatvād āha  balānantaraṃ bodhyangānīti 
teṣāṃ kathaṃ vyavasthānam iti 
kim arthaṃ vyavasthānam ityabhiprāyaḥ 
ata āha  āśrayāngaṃ svabhāvāngaṃ iti vistaraḥ 
darśanamārge bodhāvangāni bodhyangānīti 
adṛṣṭapūrvasya tattvasya tat prathamata ālocanād darśanaṃ āryabhūmiprāpakatvān mārga ityato darśanamārga ity ucyate 
nirvedhabhāgīyāvasthāyāṃ hi pelavavastrāntaritānīvopalakṣyante satyāni 
darśanamārgāvasthāyāṃ tadapanīta iveti 
tatra tattvābhisambodho bodhinirvikalpaṃ jñānaṃ tatra ṣaṭ smṛṭyādīni bodhyanukūlāt tadangāni 
dharmapravicayastv avabodhātmakatvād bodhiḥ itareṣāṃ ca sahāyabhāvād angatvaṃ 
anyaḥ punar āha  ānantaryamārgagṛhīto dharmapravicayo bodhyangaṃ vimuktimārgasangṛhītas tu bodhir iti 
tatra bodher āśrāngaṃ smṛtiḥ smṛtbalena tasminnālambane'vikṣepaṇāt 
svabhāvāngaṃ dharmapravicayaḥ jñānasvabhāvatvād bodheḥ 
niryāṇāngaṃ vīryaṃ vīryeṇa  pṛthagjanabhūmisamatikramāt 
anuśaṃsāngaṃ prītiḥ tathā kāyacittānugrahāt 
asankleśāngaṃ tridhā  prasrabdhisamādhyupekṣāḥ tāsāṃ sankleśapratipakṣabhūtatvāt 
athavā'sankleśanidānāśrayasvabhāvabhedāt 
kim arthaṃ punar asankleśāngaṃ tridhā deśitam iti 
kenārthena tridhā deśaitam ityabhiprāyaḥ 
ata āha  nidānenāśrayeṇeha svabhāvena ca deśitaṃ 
iti 
asaṃkleśasya nidānaṃ prasrabdhiḥ 
asankleśo viśuddhaḥ 
nidānaṃ kāraṇaṃ 
kathaṃ nidānam ityato bravīti  dauṣṭhulyahetukatvāt sankleśasya tasyāś ca tat pratipakṣatvād iti 
etad uktaṃ bhavati  sankleśanidānapratipakṣabhūtatvād asankleśanidānam iti 
kāyacittākarmaṇyatā dauṣṭhulyaṃ 
tasmin sati cittaikāgratā'sambhavāc cittavikṣepaḥ 
vikṣiptacittasya ca rāgādisankleśaḥ pravartate 
evaṃ dauṣṭhulyaṃ sankleśasya hetuḥ 
tasya dauṣṭhulyasya pratipakṣaḥ prasrabdhiḥ 
katham iti  prasrabdhyā kāyacittayoḥ karmaṇyatāpādanāt 
evaṃ prasrabdhirasankleśanidānaṃ vyavasthāpyate 
āśrayaḥ samādhiḥ prasrabdhyanugṛhītakāyacittasya cittaṃ samādhīyate 
samāhite citte yathābhūtaṃ prajānāti 
yathābhūtadarśanāt kleśaḥ prahīyante 
evam asankleśasya samādhirāśrayaḥ 
svabhāva upekṣeti sankliṣṭavihārānukūlāyāścittasamatāyāścittāpraśaṭhatāyāścittābhogāvasthitatāyāś ca pratipakṣatvāt 
evam upekṣā'sankleśasvabhāvaḥ 
anye tv āhuḥ  prahāṇair mārgair darśanaheye saṃkleśe prahīṇe tat sankleśānubandhavimuktā svabhāvaviśuddhā vimuktimārgasaṃgṛhītā jñeye suniścitā yā prajñā sātra prajñopekṣety ucyate kṛtakṛtyatvāt kṣaye kṣaya ity upekṣākaraṇād iti 
  aṣṭau mārgāngāni   bodhyangānantaraṃ mārgāngāni 
teṣāṃ kathaṃ vyavasthānam iti 
darśanamārgānantaraṃ bhāvanāmārgas tatra ca mārgāngānītyato bodhyangānantaraṃ mārgāngānīty ucyante 
teṣāṃ kenārthena vyavasthānam ato bravīti  paricchedo'tha samprāptiḥ iti vistaraḥ 
mithyādṛṣṭivipakṣeṇa yāvan mithyāsamādhivipakṣeṇa samyag dṛṣṭyādīnām aṣṭānāṃ mārgāngānāṃ yathākramaṃ vyavasthānaṃ 
kramaḥ punar eṣāṃ kāritrā'nukrameṇa bhāvanāmārga iti vistaraḥ 
niṣevaṇabhāvanayā bhāvyata iti bhāvanāmārgaḥ 
tasmin bhāvanāmārge darśanamārgasya prāptibhāvanābhāvitasya paricchedāngaṃ samyag dṛṣṭiḥ 
laukikīti savikalpatvāl laukikī tad utpattisāmarthyalābhān mārgasamāpannasyāpi sā vyavasthāpyate 
lokottarāt tu nirvikalpāt nirvikalpasya sato'pi samyag dṛṣṭyāśrayabhūtatvāt samyagdṛṣṣṭir ucyate 
ata evāha  lokottarapṛṣṭhalabdheti 
lokottarasya darśanamārgasya pṛṣṭhena balena labdhotpannetyarthaḥ 
sā punaḥ kiṃviṣayetyata āha  yayā svādhigamam iti 
darśanamārgādhigamaṃ paricchinattyevaṃ mayādhigatam iti 
darśanamārgasya viṣayatvāt samyag dṛṣṭir ityucyate 
parasamprāpaṇāngam iti vistaraḥ 
tayā samyag dṛṣṭyā paricchinnasya tattvasya samyag vācā samyak sankalpena ca paratra prāpaṇāt samyaksankalpaḥ samyagvāk ca parasamprāpaṇāngaṃ 
ata evāha  samutthānayā vācā tat prāpaṇād iti 
samyak saṃkalpo hi vācaḥ samutthānaṃ nāvitarkya nāvicārya vācaṃ bhāṣata iti sūtre vacanāt 
samāhito'pi tābhyāṃ samanvāgato veditavyas tad utpattilābhāt na tu samāhitaḥ sankalpayati bhāṣate vā 
parasambhāvanāngaṃ tridhā  samyagvākkarmāntājīvāḥ 
katham ityata āha  tair hi samyag vākkarmāntājīvair yathākramaṃ  dṛṣṭau śīle'tha saṃlekhe parivijñaptir iṣyate 
  iti 
tasya samyag vāceti vistaraḥ 
katheti dharmadeśanā 
sāṃkathyaviniścayaḥ paraiḥ sahābhisamayam ārabhya codyaparihārakriyā 
anena kathāsānkathyaviniścayena prajñāyāṃ sambhāvanā bhavati pareṣāṃ niyogādanena tattvam adhigataṃ tathā hy upaśamasaṃsaktaṃ suviniścatā'viruddhārthaṃ sphuṭārthaṃ vacanam idam iti 
samyakkarmāntena śīlasya iti 
sambhavanā bhavatīti vartate 
katham ityata āha  akṛtyākaraṇād iti 
samyakkarmānto hi duścaritavirodhītyatas tena sambandhāgato jīvitahetor apy akṛtyaṃ na karotītyata āryakāntaśīlavānayam iti sambhāvanā bhavati 
samyagājīvena saṃlekha sambhāvanā bhavatīti sambadhyate 
katham ityata āha  dharmeṇa mātrayā ca cīvarādyeṣaṇād iti kuhanādidoṣarahito jīvitopakaraṇārthaḥ kāyavāksamācāraḥ samyagājīvaḥ 
tena saṃlekhe sambhāvanā bhavati niścayenāsyopakaraṇatṛṣṇā prahīṇā tathā hyasau kevalam āśrayasthityartham eva nyāyena mātrayā ca cīvarādīna paryeṣate 
tatra samyag dṛṣṭyā ābhimāniko na bhavati yathābhūtaṃ svādhigamaparijñānāt 
samyaksankalpena samutthāpitavācā siṃhanādaṃ nadati samyag vāk karmāntājīvaiḥ svāṃ pratijñāṃ samudbhavayati 
tatra vipakṣapratipakṣāngaṃ tridhaiva 
tattu na jñāyata ityāha  samyagvyāyāmsmṛtisamādhaya iti 
te ca kasya vipakṣasya pratipakṣā ityata āha  eṣāṃ punar yathākramaṃ  kleśopakleśabhutvavipakṣapratipakṣatā 
iti 
tatra prathamasya samyag vyāyāma iti 
bhāvanāheyo hi kleśaḥ prathamo vipakṣaḥ 
tasya samyagvyāyāmaḥ pratipakṣaḥ 
katham ityata āha  teneti samyag vyāyāmena mārgabhāvanāt 
samyag dṛṣṭiparigṛhītaṃ layauddhatyaviagataṃ samādhyavasthāyāṃ vīryaṃ samyag vyāyāmaḥ 
tena bhāvanāprahātavyānāṃ kleśānāṃ prahāṇāya tat pratipakṣaṃ mārgaṃ bhāvayatīti samyaksamādhipratipādanāt samyagvyāyāmaḥ prathamasya pratipakṣa ucyate 
tasyām eva mārgabhāvanāyāṃ layauddhatyalakṣaṇasya dvitīyasyopakleśasya samyaksmṛtir iti 
pratipakṣa iti prakṛtaṃ 
katham ityato bravīti  śamathādinimitteṣu sūpasthitasmṛter layauddhatyābhāvād iti 
ādiśabdena pragrahanimittam upekṣānimittañca veditavyaṃ 
tatra vikṣepanimittopaśamanāc chamathaḥ 
śamathādinimittaṃ śamathādikāraṇaṃ 
taroddhate citta auddhatyābhiśankini vā samvejanīyavastumanaskāraḥ śamathanimittaṃ 
līne citte layābhiśankini vābhinandanīyavastumanaskāraḥ pragrahanimittaṃ śamathaikāntike vipaśya  naikāntike vā mārge yuganaddavāhini vā tad ubhayopakleśānupakliṣṭe'nābhogamanaskāra upekṣānimittaṃ 
abhijñādiguṇasvabhāvasya vibhutvasya yad vipakṣaḥ samāpattyāvaraṇātmakam akliṣṭam ajñānaṃ tasya tṛtīyasya samyak samādhiḥ pratipakṣa iti prakṛtaṃ 
katham ityata āha  dhyānasanniśrayeṇābhijñādiguṇābhinirhārād iti 
dhyānaṃ hi sarvaviśiṣṭaguṇābhinirhārāśraya ityabhijñādiguṇābhinirhāravipakṣabhūtasya samādhyāvaraṇasya pratipakṣaḥ 
tadevaṃ samyagvyāyāmena kleśāvaraṇavisaṃyogaṃ khyāpayati samyaksmṛtyā samādhipariśuddhiṃ samyak samādhinā samāpattyāvaraṇena viṣamam iti 
  pratipakṣabhāvanāprabhedaḥ  saiṣā pratipakṣabhāvanā samāsena trividhā veditavyā  ārambhapratilambhaniṣpattibhedena 
vyāsatastvenekavidhā 
kathaṃ  anukūlā viparyastā iti vistaraḥ 
tatrā'viparyāsānukūlā viparyastā 
aviparyāso darśanamārgaḥ tattvaviṣayatvāt 
tad anukūlatvād aviparyāsānukūlā 
iyañca pṛthagjanabhāvanetyatattvaviṣayatvād viparyastā pṛthagjanasya niravaśeṣā prahīṇakleśatvāt 
kathaṃ viparyastā satī aviparyāsānukūlā bhavati  suviśuddhadharmadhātuniṣyandāyāḥ 
śrutavāsanāyā utpādāt 
sā ca smṛtyupasthānabhāvanām ārabhya yāvad balabhāvaneti 
aviparyastā viparyāsānubandheti 
iyaṃ hi śaikṣāṇāṃ bodhyangabhāvanā mārgabhāvanā ca 
tattvaviṣayatvād aviparyastā bhāvanāprahātavyakleśasadbhāvāc ca viparyāsānubandhā 
aviparyastā viparyāsaniranubandheti 
iyam aśaikṣamārgabhāvanā tattvaviṣayatvād aviparyastā niravaśeṣamalaprahāṇād arhatāṃ viparyāsaniranubandhā 
  idānīṃ śrāvakādibhyo bodhisatvānāṃ pratipakṣabhāvanāyā viśeṣapradarśanārtham āha  bodhisattvānāṃ tu  ālambanamanaskāraprāptitas tad viśiṣṭatā 
iti 
tatrālambanato viśiṣṭatā śrāvakapratyekabuddhānāṃ hi svāsāntānikāḥ kāyādayaḥ 
kāyavedanācittadharmā ālambanaṃ 
bodhisattvānāṃ punaḥ svaparasāntānikāḥ kāyavedanācittadharmā ālambanaṃ 
kim artham ālambanaṃ bhinnaṃ  yasmāc chrāvakādīnāṃ svārtham evādhikṛtya pratipakṣabhāvanāpravṛttiḥ bodhisattvānāṃ punaḥ svapārtham adhikṛtyeti 
anityādibhir ākārair iti anityaduḥkhaśūnyātmākāraiḥ 
kasmāc chrāvakapratyekabuddhānām anityādibhir eva manaskāraḥ  tebhya udvegārthaṃ 
na hy anudvignastair visaṃyujyate 
bodhisattvā anupalambhayogeneti kalpitasvabhāvānupalambhaprakāreṇetyarthaḥ kim arhtam evaṃ manasi kurvanti  sarvavikalpaprahāṇārthaṃ 
eṣa hi teṣu viśeṣa ucyate na kevalam anupalambhayogenaiva manasi kurvanti kiṃ tarhy anityādibhirapyākāraiḥ 
evaṃ manasikāraviśeṣād viśiṣṭatā 
yāvad eva kāyādīnāṃ visaṃyogāyeti 
kāyādīnāṃ visaṃyogo nirupadhiśeṣanirvāṇaṃ tadālambanakleśaprahāṇañca 
bodhisattvā na visaṃyogāya nā'visaṃyogāya 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  ekāntena hi kāyādibhir visaṃyuktāś cā'visaṃyuktāśca sattvārthakaraṇasamarthā na syuḥ kṣīṇakleśetarasattvavat 
yadi na visaṃyogāya kimarthaṃ tarhi pratipakṣaṃ bhāvayatītyata āha  yāvadevā'pratiṣṭhitanirvāṇāya bhāvayatīti 
kiṃ tad apratiṣṭhitaṃ nirvāṇaṃ  bodhisattvāvasthāyāṃ tāvat karmopapattivaśitāsanniśrayeṇa kāruṇikatvāt saṃsāropapattiḥ prajñābalena tatrāsankleśaḥ 
tadidaṃ bodhisattvānām apratiṣṭhitaṃ nirvāṇaṃ vidhīyate 
saṃsārāvasthito'pi pṛthagjanavat saṃkliṣṭo na vartate 
na śrāvakādivan nirupādāno nirvāṇa iti 
tathāgatāvasthāyām api kleśajñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇān na saṃsāre pratiṣṭhitaḥ nirupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇe naiva pratiṣṭhito dharmakāyasyānucchedāt sāmbhogikanairmāṇikakāyay yorval lokas tāvat parārthakaraṇāt 
evam eṣā pratipakṣabhāvanā bodhisattvānāṃ śrāvakādibhya ālambanamanaskāraphalaviśeṣair viśiṣṭeti uktā pratipakṣabhāvanā 
  tatrā'vasthā   pratipakṣabhāvanānantaraṃ tatrāvasthoktetyataḥ pṛcchati  tatrā'vasthā katameti 
tatreti tasyāṃ pratipakṣabhāvanāyāṃ 
ata āha  hetvavasthāvatārākhyā iti vistaraḥ 
tatra hetvavasthā gotrasthasya pudgalasyeti 
gotraṃ hetur bījam ityarthaḥ 
tatra yo gotra eva vartate na cittotpādādiṣu sa gotrastha ihābhipretaḥ 
sa punar uttarāvasthāsv anuvartate na nivartate 
kecit tacca gotraṃ kuśalamūlasvabhāvam iti varṇayanti 
kuśalamūlānyeva hi kānicic chrāvakagotram ity ucyante 
evaṃ yāvat kānicid bodhisattvagotram iti 
pṛthagjanāvasthām ārabhyendriyabhedo gotram ucyate 
cittabījaśaktir gotram ityetad apyeka āhuḥ 
tasmin sati pṛthagjanāvasthāyāṃ śaikṣāvasthāyāñca śrāvakagotra ityucyate yāvad bodhisattvagotra iti 
aśaikṣāvasthāyāṃ tu śrāvaka ity ucyate pratyekabuddha iti vā 
na tad gotraṃ tasya  prakarṣāvasthānāt 
tac ca śrāvakādibhedena tridhābhidyate 
niyatāniyataprabhedena ṣaḍvidhaṃ bhavati 
avatārāvasthā utpāditabodhicittasyeti 
sā ca śrāvakapratyekabuddhatathāgatagotrāṇāṃ yathākramaṃ śrāvakapratyekabuddhasamyaksambuddhabodhiṣu cittotpādāt trividhā bhavati 
tasya prayogamūlabhūtatvāt tasminn utpanne prayogāvatāra iti tad utpādaḥ prayogāvatārāvasthety ucyate 
prayogāvasthā cittotpādādūrdhvam aprāpte phala iti 
utpāditabodhicittasya dānaśīlādiko balabhāvanāparyavasānakuśalasamārambhaḥ prathamaphalaprāpaka upāya iti sa prayoga ucyate 
kathaṃ hetvavatārāvasthā bodhipakṣabhāvanāvasthety ucyate  taddhetutvāt 
ata evoktaṃ  uttarottaraphalaṃ gotrāc cittotpāda ityevam ādi 
phalāvasthā prāpte prathamaphale 
phalārthaṃ hi prayujyate 
ataḥ prayogānantaraṃ phalāvasthā 
sakaraṇīyāvasthā hi śaikṣasya 
tasya phalānām aparisamāptatvātphalānantaraprāptipratikaraṇīyasadbhāvāt 
akaraṇīyāvasthā'śaikṣasyeti 
aśaikṣo hi tridhātukavītarāgāt 
tasya phalānāṃ parisamāptatvāt phalāntaraprāptikaraṇīyāsadbhāvād akaraṇīyāvasthā 
viśeṣāvasthā'bhijñādiguṇaviśeṣasamanvāgatasyeti 
samāne'rthattve'bhijñādibhir guṇaviśeṣaiḥ samanvāgata itarasmād viśiṣṭā'bhijñādiguṇaviśeṣaniṣpannāvasthā viśeṣāvasthetyucyate 
uttarāvasthā śrāvakapratyekabuddhebhyo bhūmipraviṣṭasya bodhisattvasya 
svaparārthakārikasya lokottarasya mārgasyobhayanairātmyaprativedhasya lābhena tadanyayānottarabhūtāt tadvasthottarāvasthetyucyate 
anuttarāvasthā buddhasya 
kim arthaṃ  ata āha  tata ūrdhvam avasthā'bhāvād iti 
sarvaguṇadoṣaprakarṣaniṣṭhādhiṣṭhānatvād buddhasya tata ūrdhvamanyā viśiṣṭāvasthā na vidyata iti saivānuttaretyucyate 
iyaduktaṃ parisamāptāpi niravaśeṣāvasthā bodhisattvānām ekādaśabhūmiprabhedasandarśanārtham adhimukticartyādyavasthābhiṣekādhya vastāvasānāḥ punar uktā 
buddhānāṃ tu kāyatrayaprabhedapradarśanārthaṃ prāptyavasthādikāḥ punas tisro nirdiṣṭāḥ 
tatra hetvavatārāvasthā bodhisattvetarasādhāraṇā veditavyā 
tatrā'dhimuktyavasthā bodhisattvānāṃ sarvasyām adhimukticaryābhūmāv iti 
cittotpādād ūrdhvaṃ yāvan na bhūmipraveśo'trāntare'dṛṣṭatattvo'pi dṛṣṭatattvaṃ iva  buddhabodhisattveṣvadhimuktyā svabhāvatrayamukhena dharmān pratipadyate 
tadanyasattvānāṃ duṣkaradānaśīlādiṣu buddhatvaniṣpādasambhāreṣu pravartata ityata iyam avasthādhimuktiprabhāvitattvād adhimukticaryetyucyate 
sā ca kalpāsaṃkhyeyam adhikaṃ vā 
praveśāvasthā prathamāyāṃ bhūmāv iti 
svabhāvatrayasyāvikalpena jñānena tatprathamata eva tattvasvasamvedanaprativedha iti praveśāvasthocyate 
eṣaiva bodhisattvasya darśanamārgaḥ niryāṇāvasthā tad uttarāsu ṣaṭsu bhūmiṣu iti 
bhāvanāprahātavyasya nimittanānātvābhiniveśasya prahāṇaniṣṭāgamanāt sābhogaprayoganiṣṭhāgamanāc caitā bhūmayo niryāṇāvasthety ucyate 
vyākaraṇāvasthā'ṣṭamyāṃ bhūmāv iti 
sarvathā sarvanimittābhogasaṃjñāvigamād aṣṭamyāṃ bhūmau niyatipatito bhavati buddhatva iti buddhair bhagavadbhiḥ sammukhavyākaraṇena vyākriyate 
kathakatvāvasthā navamyām iti 
navamyāṃ bhūmau śrāvakapratyekabuddhebhyaḥ prativiśiṣṭāścatasraḥ pratisamvidaḥ pratilabhata ity anuttaro mahādhārmakathiko bhavati 
abhiṣekāvasthā daśamyāṃ bhūmāv iti 
daśamyāṃ hi bhūmau bodhisatto mārganiṣṭhāgato daśadiglokadhātuvyavasthitānāṃ buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ raśmīṇām abhiṣekeṇābhiṣicyate 
prāptyavasthā buddhānāṃ dharmakāya iti 
sarvāvaraṇaprahāṇāt tat pratipakṣānāsravadharmabījapracayāc cāśrayaparāvṛttyātmakaḥ sarvadharmavartyānālaya iti buddhānāṃ dharmakāyāḥ 
tena dharmaprativedhaniṣṭhādhigamanāt prāptyavasthety ucyate 
anye tu niḥśeṣāgantukamalāpagamāt suviśuddho dharmadhātur eva dharmatākāyo dharmakāya iti varṇayanti 
sarvasminn api jñeye'saktāpratihatapravṛttiviśiṣṭaṃ jñānaṃ dharmakāya ityapare 
anuśaṃsā'vasthā sāmbhogikaḥ kāya iti 
svābhāviko yasmin kāye vyavasthite'bhisambudhyate yena kāyena niṣṭhāgatair bodhisattvaiḥ saha parṣanmaṇḍalena dharmasaṃgītim anubhavati sa sāmbhogikaḥ kāyaḥ 
kṛtyanuṣṭhānāvasthā nirmāṇakāya iti 
svābhāvikakāyāśritaḥ sattvāśayālocano vineyārthaṃ prakriyāpravṛttāvanantaprabhedo nairmāṇikaḥ kāyaḥ 
sarvāpyeṣā bahuvidhā'vasthā'bhisamasya veditavyā  dharmadhātau tridhā punaḥ 
iti 
katham ityata āha  aśuddhaśuddhaśuddhā ca viśuddhā ca yathārhataḥ 
iti 
tatrāśuddhāvasthā hetvavasthām upādāya yāvat prayogād iti  hetvavatāraprayogādhimuktyavasthā gṛhyante 
āsvavasthāsu dharmadhātor aprahīṇaniravaśeṣamalatvād aśuddhāvasthety ucyate 
aśuddhaśuddhāvasthā śaikṣāṇām iti 
atra ca phalasakaraṇīyaviśeṣottarapraveśaniryāṇavyākaraṇakathikābhiṣekāvasthā gṛhyante 
 etāsvapyavasthāsu dharmādhātoḥ prahīṇāprahīṇakleśatām upādāyāśuddhaśuddhāvasthety ucyate 
viśuddhāvasthā'śaikṣāṇām ityakaraṇīyaviśeṣānuttaraprāptyanuśaṃsākṛtyānuṣṭhānāvasthā viśuddhāvasthetyucyate aśaikṣāṇāṃ niravaśeṣakleśaprahāṇāt 
etāścāvasthāḥ pṛthagjanaśaikṣāṇāṃ vyavasthāpyante 
teṣāṃ ca bahudhā vyavasthānaṃ kathaṃ vijñāpanīyam ityata āha  pudgalāṇāṃ vyavasthānaṃ yathāyogamato mataṃ 
iti 
yathāyogam iti yathāsambhavaṃ 
ata ityato'vasthāprabhedād ityarthaḥ 
ayaṃ gotrastho'yam avatīrṇa ityevam ādi 
āditagrahaṇād ayaṃ prayuktaḥ  srotāapannaḥ sakṛdāgāmī anāgāmī arhan sālankāraḥ bodhisattvaḥ tathāgataḥ adhimukticārī śuddhyādhyāśayacārī niryāyī vyākṛtaḥ dhārmikathikaḥ abhiṣiktaḥ bodhiprāptaḥ bhogī parārthakṛd iti 
uktā avasthāḥ 
  phalaprāptiḥ   avasthāyāḥ phalapūrvakatvād avasthānantaraṃ phalabhāṣaṇārthaṃ pṛcchati phalaprāptiḥ katametyata āha  bhājanatvaṃ vipākākhyaṃ iti vistaraḥ 
tadidaṃ samāsena pañcavidhaṃ phalaṃ  bhājanatvaṃ balaṃ rucir vṛddhir viśuddhiśceti 
tatra bhājanatvaṃ yaḥ kuśalānukūlo vipāka iti 
sa punar aṣṭākṣaṇaprahāṇaḥ sāsravaviśiṣṭaṣaḍāyatano bodhipakṣadharmavipākaḥ sarvakuśaladharmotpattyāśrayatvād bhājanam ucyate 
balaṃ yā bhājanatvādhipatyād iti 
āśrayakleśopapattimandhatām upādāya kuśalamūlasyādhimātratā pṛṣṭatetyarthaḥ 
idam ucyate balaṃ 
ruciryā pūrvābhyāsāt kuśale rucir ityatīteṣu janmasu kuśaladharmābhyāsād vartamāne janmani kuśaladharmābhiprāyo nadīsrotonyāyena sā ruciḥ 
vṛddhiryā pratyutpannakuśalamūla dharmābhyāsād apūrvaviśiṣṭakuśaladharmotpattiḥ kuśalamūlaparipuṣṭir ityabhiprāyaḥ 
trayaṃ balavṛddhyor viśeṣaḥ balaṃ hi mandakuśalavipākāpekṣyaṃ dārḍhyaṃ vṛddhiḥ punaḥ kuśalasyottarottaraviśeṣaḥ 
anye punaḥ kuśalamūlapuṣṭir iti viśiṣṭakuśaladharmavāsanāpuṣṭir ihābhipreteti manyante 
viśūddhir yadāvaraṇaprahāṇam iti 
tatra śrāvakabuddhagotrāṇāṃ kleśāvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ viśuddhiḥ 
sambuddhagotrāṇāṃ kleśajñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ viśuddhiḥ 
etad yathārkamaṃ pañcavidhaṃ phalam iti 
vipākaphalaṃ yaḥ kuśaladharmānukūlo vipākaḥ 
adhipatiphalaṃ yā bhājanatvādhipatyāt kuśalasyādhimātratā 
niṣyandaphalaṃ yā pūrvābhyāsāt kuśale ruciḥ 
puruṣakāraphalaṃ yā pratyutpannakuśaladharmābhyāsāt kuśalamūlapuṣṭiḥ 
visaṃyogaphalaṃ yadāvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ 
asyaiva pañcavidhasya phalasya samāsoktasya prabhedaḥ samāsena nirdiṣṭaḥ  uttarottaram ādyañca iti vistaraḥ 
uttarottaraphalaṃ gotrāc cittotpādaścittotpādāt prayoga ityevamādi yathoktayā'vasthāparamparayā veditavyaṃ 
ādiphalaṃ prathamato lokottaradharmapratilambha  iti darśanamārgaprāptiḥ 
abhyāsaphalaṃ pareṇa śaikṣāvasthāyām iti 
darśanamārgāt pareṇa śikṣāvasthāyāṃ pañcapudgalaprabhāvitāyāṃ sakṛdāgāmiphalam anāgāmiphalañca saprayogapṛṣṭhabhāvanāmārgātmakatvād abhyāsaphalaṃ 
samāptipahlam aśaikṣā dharmā iti 
te punaḥ samyag dṛṣṭisankalpavākkarmāntājīvavyāyāmasmṛtisamādhivimuktivimuktijñānadarśanākhyāḥ sarvaphalaparyantāvasthitatvāt samāptiphalam ity ucyate 
ānukṛtyaphalam upaniṣadbhāvenottarottaraphalam eva veditavyam iti 
upaniṣad bhāvo hetuḥ 
tatra cittotpādo gotrānukūlatvāc cittotpādaḥ phalam iti 
uttarottaraphalādīnām ānukūlyaphalādīnāñca pṛthag upadeśo yathākramam uddeśanirdeśato veditavya iti 
vipakṣaphalaṃ prahāṇamārgaḥ yadevādiphalaṃ 
vipakṣa eva phalam iti vipakṣaphalaṃ prahāṇamārgo yena kleśebhyo visaṃyujyate 
ādiphalaṃ yat pūrvam uktaṃ prathamato lokottaradharmapratilambha iti 
vipakṣaśabdo yadyapi pratipakṣavibandhanārthenāvaraṇam ucyate atra tu vipakṣaḥ pratipakṣo'bhipreta iti āvaraṇanirvāsapakṣo vipakṣa iti vigrahāt 
visaṃyogaphalam abhyāsaphalaṃ samāptiphalaṃ ca kleśavisaṃyogaḥ śaikṣāśaikṣāṇāṃ yathākramam iti 
abhyāsaphalaṃ visaṃyogaḥ sakṛdāgāmiphalapratipannādīnāṃ pañcānāṃ śaikṣāṇāṃ śiṣṭakleśatvāt 
samāptiphalaṃ visaṃyogaḥ 
aśaikṣāṇāṃ parihāṇidharmādīnāṃ ṣaṇṇām api traidhātukāśeṣakleśaprahīṇatvāt 
pūrvaṃ bhedenoktam idānīm abhedeneti viśeṣaḥ 
viśeṣaphalam abhijñādiko guṇaviśeṣa iti 
etad apyabhyāsasamāptiphalaviśeṣa eva veditavyaṃ 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  anāgāminām arhatāṃ pratyekabuddhānāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ tathāgatānāñca vaiśeṣikaguṇalābhasya vivakṣitatvāt 
uttaraphalaṃ bodhisattvabhūmayaḥ 
atra kāraṇam āha  tad anyayā nottaratvād iti 
bodhisattvabhūmayo hi yadyapi darśanabhāvanāmārgātmakatvād ādiphalam abhyāsaphalañca tathāpi śrāvakapratyekabuddhayānāpekṣayā bodhisattvabhūmīnām uttaraphalatvaṃ nirvikalpatvād buddhagotrakatvān mahābodhiphalatvāc ca veditavyaṃ 
anuttaraphalaṃ buddhabhūmir iti 
etad api samāptiphalam eva yataḥ sarvasavāsanākleśopakleśaprahāṇād akliṣṭājñānaprahāṇāc ca tad uttarabhūmyantarābhāvād anuttaraphalam ity ucyate 
etad anyat phalaṃ samāsanirdeśataḥ vyāsatastvaparimāṇam iti 
vyāsataḥ śrāvakapratyekabuddhabodhisattvasambuddhaphalāni pratipādyamānānyaparimāṇāni bhavantīti 
  pratipakṣabhāvanāpiṇḍārthaḥ   pratipakṣabhāvanāyāḥ piṇḍārthaḥ 
vyutpattibhāvanā smṛtyupasthānabhāvanā caturāryasatyavyutpattitvāt 
nirlekhabhāvanā samyakprahāṇabhāvanā akuśaladharmāṇāṃ nirlekhāt 
parikarmabhāvanā ṛddhipādabhāvanā tatra samādhiparikarmakaraṇāt pañcadoṣaprahāṇāyāṣṭaprahāṇasaṃskārāsevanāt 
uttarasamārambhabhāvanā indriyabhāvanā tasya vimokṣabhāgīyakuśalamūlotpādakatvāt 
śliṣṭabhāvanā balā'balabhāvanā darśanamārgaśleṣāt 
praviṣṭabhāvanā bodhyangabhāvanā tatra tattvapraveśāt lokottaradharmapraveśādāryabhūmipraveśād vā 
utkṛṣṭabhāvanā mārgabhāvanā darśanamārgād bhāvanāmārgasyotkṛṣṭatvāt ādibhāvanā pṛthagjanāvasthāyām anukūlāviparyastā vā 
madhyabhāvanā śaikṣyāvasthāyām aviparyastā viparyāsasānubandhā vā paryavasānabhāvanā'śaikṣāvasthāyām aviparyastā viparyāsaniranubandhā
sottarā bhāvanā śrāvakādīnāṃ 
niruttarā ca bhāvanā bodhisattvānāṃ yā ālambanamanaskāraprāptiviśiṣṭeti 
avasito bhāvanāyāḥ piṇḍārthaḥ 
  avasthānāṃ piṇḍārthaḥ  avasthānāṃ piṇḍārthaḥ 
bhavyatāvasthā hetvavasthā 
ārambhāvasthā saha cittotpādena prayogāt 
aśuddhaśuddhāvasthā dve avasthe phalāvasthā sakaraṇīyāvasthā ca 
  viśuddhāvasthā'karaṇīyāvasthā 
sālankārāvasthā viśeṣāvasthā 
vyāptyavasthā uttarāvasthā 
bodhisattvānāṃ daśabhūmivyāpanād vyāptyavasthety ucyate 
anuttarāvasthā ca buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ tad uttarāvasthāntarābhāvāt 
sā ca prāptyavasthā anuśaṃsāvasthā kṛtyānuṣṭhānāvasthā ca yāḥ pūrvam uktāḥ 
  phalānāṃ piṇḍārthaḥ  phalānāṃ piṇḍārthaḥ saṃgrahatas tadviśeṣataḥ pūrvābhyāsataḥ uttarottaranirhārata uddeśato nirdeśataśceti 
eṣāṃ bhāṣyakāra eva vyākhyāṃ karoti 
tatra saṃgrahato vipākaphalādīni pañca phalāni teṣu sarvaphalasaṃgṛhītatvāt 
tad viśeṣataḥ śeṣāṇīti 
teṣām eva pañcānāṃ prabhedaḥ śeṣāṇy uttarottaraphalāni veditavyāni 
pūrvābhyāsato vipākaphalam iti 
pūrvajanmopacitāt kuśalāt pratyutpannajanmani vipākaḥ kuśalānukūlotpattir ityata uktaṃ pūrvābhyāsata iti 
uttarottaranirhāratas tad anyāni catvārīti 
adhipatiphalaṃ niṣyandaphalaṃ puruṣakāraphalaṃ visaṃyogaphalañca 
tatra vipākanirhṛtaṃ balaṃ 
balanirhṛtā ruciḥ 
ruchinirhṛtā vṛddhiḥ 
vṛddhinirhṛtā viśuddhiḥ 
kecid āhuḥ  uttarottarākhyānaprabhāvitātvād uttarottaranirhṛtatvam ity ucyate 
uddeśata uttarottaraphalādīni catvārīti 
uttarottaraphalamādiphalamabhyāsaphalaṃsamāptiphalañceti 
nirdeśata ānukūlyaphlādīni ṣaṭ 
teṣām eva caturṇāṃ nirdeśād iti 
tatrānukūlyaphalam uttarottaraphalasya nirdeśaḥ vipakṣaphalam ādiphalasya nirdeśaḥ visaṃyogaphalam abhyāsaphalasya samāptiphalasya ca nirdeśaḥ viśeṣaphalam uttaraphalam anuttaraphalañca samāptiphalasyaiva nirdeśaḥ tatraiva sālankārasya vivakṣitatvāt 
anye tvāhuḥ  viśeṣaphalam abhyāsasamāptiphalayor eva nirdeśo'nāgāmino'pyabhijñādiguṇasaṃbhavāt 
anuttaraphalantu samāptiphalasya nirdeśa iti 
āgamānusāriṇyāṃ madhyāntavibhāgaṭīkāyām āryasthiramatyparac itāyāṃ phalanirdeśonāma caturthaḥ paricchedaḥ samāptaḥ 
  yānā''nuttaryaparicchedaḥ pañcamaḥ   trividhā''nuttaryaṃ   lakṣaṇāvaraṇādiṣaṭpadārthoddeśānantaraṃ yānānuttaryam uddiṣṭam atas tannirdeśāt paraṃ yānānuttaryanirdeśaḥ prakṛtaḥ 
ata āha  yānānuttaryam idānīṃ vaktavyaṃ 
tad ucyata iti 
idānīm iti lakṣaṇādiṣaṭkanirdeśānantaram ityarthaḥ tad anantaram uddiṣṭatvād ityabhiprāyaḥ 
atha vā pratipaksabhāvanāvasthāphalaprāptayaḥ śrāvakādīnāṃ bodhisattvaiḥ sādhāraṇā nirdiṣṭāḥ 
asādhāraṇaprasangena yānānuttaryantu bodhisattvānāṃ śrāvakādibhir asādhāraṇam iha ca prādhānyenocyata iti pradarśayann āha  yānānuttaryam idānīṃ vaktavyaṃ tad ucyata iti 
nāsmād uttaram astītyānuttaryaśabdo viśiṣṭatvaprayāyaḥ 
kiṃ punar etat  mahāyānaṃ 
tathāhi śrāvakapratyekabuddhayānābhyāṃ mahāyānaṃ viśiṣṭaṃ 
naiva mahāyānādanyad viśiṣṭataram asti 
tatra hetuphalayos taratamabhedāt 
anuttarasya bhāva ānuttaryaṃ 
kiṃ punas tad ityata āha  ānuttarya prapattau hi 
iti vistaraḥ 
trividham ānuttaryaṃ mahāyāna iti 
kiṃ punas tan mahāyānaṃ  etad eva tṛtayaṃ pratipattir ālambanaṃ samudāgamaś ca 
tatra pratipatter anuttarya daśapāramitāniṣpādakatvāt 
pāramitāniṣpādakatve bodhisattvapratipattir ānuttaryam ucyate 
ālambanasya punaḥ pāramitādayo dharmā dharmadhātuś ca 
anena hy ālambanena bodhisattvānām aśeṣaparārthakaraṇasamarthā bhavantītyataḥ parārthakaraṇasāmarthyahetutvam ālambanānuttaryaṃ 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  tadvattvāt tad ālambanaṃ bodhisattvānām anuttaryam ucyate 
samudāgamo gotrādhimukticittorpādādīnāṃ phalaṃ 
samudāgacchanti prāpnuvanti gotrādibhyas taditi  samudāgamaḥ 
sa ca tato'nyaviśiṣṭasamudāgamābhāvād anuttara ity ucyate 
tato'tra tasmāt samudāgamād anuyaviśiṣṭābhāvavastutvam ānuttaryaṃ 
atra punaḥ pratipattir bodhisattvānāṃ sādhāra saphalā ca mahāyānam ityuktaṃ bhavati 
etac ca trividhenānuttaryeṇānantarokte nānuttaryam ity ucyate 
atha vā mahāyānaṃ sarvavikalpaprapañcavigataṃ jñānaṃ sasamprayogaṃ sasambhāraṃ saprayogaṃ sapṛṣṭhalabdhajñānaṃ saviśiṣṭaguṇaṃ sāalambanaṃ saphalañca 
tatrālambanaṃ tathatā 
phalam apratiṣṭhitaṃ nirvāṇam iti 
asya ca mahāyānasyābhidhāyikā yā sūtrādideśanāpi mahāyānaṃ bhavantīti grantho'pyadhikāra ivopacaryate 
yathā kaṃsavadhā maṇiharaṇañca 
tac ca saptavidhamahattvayogān mahat 
yāntyanena prāpnuvantyapratiṣṭhitaṃ nirvāṇam iti yānaṃ 
saptavidhaṃ punar mahattvam ālambanapratipattijñānavīryopāyaprāptikarmamahattvaṃ 
tatrālambanamahattvaṃ śatasāhasrikādyanantasūtradharmālambanād bodhisattvamārgasya 
pratipattimahattvaṃ sakalasvaparārthapratipattitaḥ 
jñānamahattvaṃ pudgaladharmanairātmyajñānāt 
vīryamahattvaṃ triṣu kalpasaṃkhyeyeṣv anekaduṣkaraśatasahasraprayogāt 
upāyakauśalyamahattvaṃ saṃsāranirvāṇapratiṣṭhānāt 
prāptimahattvaṃ balavaiśāradyāveṇikauddhadharmādyprameyasaṃkhyeyaguṇādhigamāt 
karmamahattvaṃ yāvat saṃsārastāvad bodhyabhisandarśanena buddhakāryānuṣṭhānāt 
etad eva mahāyānam anuttaraṃ tad anyasya viśiṣṭayānasyābhāvāt 
tadabhāva ānuttaryaṃ 
tat punaḥ pratipattyālambanasamudāgamāḥ 
tathāhi tadyogān mahāyānam anuttaram ucyate 
pratipattirevānuttaryaṃ pratipattyānuttaryaṃ 
evam ālambanānuttaryaṃ samudāgamānuttaryañca veditavyaṃ 
etad ānuttaryaṃ yathākramaṃ bodhisattvamārgaṃ tad adhiṣṭhānaṃ tat phalañcādhikṛtya vyavasthāpyate 
etāvac ca buddhavacanenocyate  yaduta pratipattir ālambanaṃ tat phalañceti 
  pratipattyānuttaryaṃ  ālambanapūrvikā pratipattir ityālambanapūrvanirdeśanayena pratipattiḥ pūrvam uktā bodhisattvānāṃ pratipattisāratāsandarśanārthaṃ 
tatra kathaṃ pratipattyānuttaryam ityata āha  pratipattyānuttaryaṃ daśapāramitāpratipattito veditavyam iti 
pāramitāpratipattiḥ  pāramitānuṣṭhānaṃ 
sā ca pāramitāpratipattir mahāyāna eva nirdiṣṭā nānyatra yāna iti mahāyānam evānuttaram iti darśayati 
sā ca pratipattir yiaḥ prakāraiḥ pāramitāsu prayujyamānasyānuttarā bhavati tān prakārān darśayann āha  pratipattis tu ṣaḍvidhā iti 
  paramā pratipattiḥ  sā ca pāramitāpratipattir na vijñāyate kathaṃ paramā yāvat katham aviśiṣṭetyata āha  tatra paramā dvādaśātmikā 
iti 
dvādaśaprakārā paramā mahatī niruttaretyarthaḥ 
tat prakārapradarśanārtham āha  audāryam āyatattvañca  iti vistaraḥ 
audāryaparamatā yāvan niṣpattiparamatetyeṣā dvādaśavidhā paramatā 
tatraudāryaparamatā sarvalaukika sampattyanarthakatvenotkṛṣṭatayā ca veditavyā 
sampattir abhyudayaḥ sa ca dvidhākāraḥ  prāptaścāprāptaś ca 
tatra prāpte na sajjate aprāptaṃ na prārthayati svasukhanirapekṣaparaduḥkhāpanayaprayuktatvāt 
yathoktaṃ  puṇyaṃ hi yat puṇyaphalañca sādhoḥ sarva parārthaṃ tava nātmahetoḥ 
iti 
prahāṇajñānaprabhāvasampannabuddhatvapalatvāad utkṛṣṭatvaṃ 
athavā loke hi dvividhā evodāra ucyate  yaḥ sthūlalakṣaḥ pratyupakārāprārthanaś ca 
tasmād bodhisattvaḥ sarvalokasampattyaprārthako'pyadhimātrā'dhimātrāsu ca dānādipāramitāsu prayujyata iti tat pratipatter audāryam ucyate 
āyatattvaparamatā āyatatvenotkṛṣṭatā 
āyatattvaṃ punar dānapāramitādiṣv āyatābhyāsaḥ 
tac ca na jñāyate kiyañciram ityata āha  vikalpāsaṃkhyeyaparibhāvanād iti 
bodhisattvānāṃ hi dānapāramitādibhāvanā kalpāsaṃkhyeyatrayaparyavasānatvād atyantamāyatā 
adhikāraparamatā sarvasattvārthakriyādhikārād iti 
bodhisattvānāṃ svasukhanirapekṣāṇāṃ dānādiṣu pravṛttiḥ sarvasattvānāṃ hitasukhakriyām adhikṛtyetyato'dhikārataḥ parametyucyate 
akṣayatvaparamatā akṣayatvena paramatā 
akṣayatvaṃ punaḥ kuta ityata āha  mahābodhipariṇāmanayā'tyantam apryādānād iti 
mahābodhipariṇāmitā hi dānādayaḥ sarvopapattyāyataneṣu vipākaphalaṃ dattvāpi nātyantaṃ samucchidyante āśrayaparāvṛttilakṣaṇasya dharmakāyasya niṣpādanāt tasya cākṣayatvan nirupādhiśeṣe'pi nirvāṇe na paryādīyante śrāvakādibodhipariṇāmanayā tu nirupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau sarvathā''śrayasya samucchedāt samucchidyante 
mahābodhipariṇāmanayā vā dānādīnyakṣayāṇi bhavanti prabhūtavipākatvāt 
prabhūtam apyakṣayam ucyate vipākadānenā'tyantam aparyādānāt na tvevaṃ śrāvakādipariṇāmanāyām akṣayatvaṃ 
  athavā satvārthaṃ mahābodhipariṇāmitāni kuśalamūlāni bodhisattvānāṃ sattvadhātuvad akṣayāṇi bhavantītyataś ca sattvadhātuvan nātyantaṃ paryādīyanta iti 
nairantarya paramatā ātmaparasamatādhimokṣāt sarvasattvadānādibhiḥ pāramitā paripūraṇād iti 
pramuditāyāṃ hi bhūmau dharmadhātoḥ sarvatragārthāvabodhād bodhisattva ātmaparasamatām abhimucyate 
sa svaparasamatādhimokṣāt prahīṇasvaparavikalpaḥ svadānādibhir iva paradānādibhir api sumuditacittaṃ labhate 
tataḥ pratikṣaṇaṃ pratimuhūrtaṃ pratidivasaṃ ca nirantaraṃ dānādipāramitāḥ paripūryanta iti 
akṛcchratvaparamatā anumodanāmātreṇa paradānādīnāṃ pāramitāparipūraṇād iti 
tathā bodhisattvāḥ sattvānāṃ dānādikuśalamūlāni samuditena manasā'numodayanti yathaiṣām anumodanāmātreṇa dānādipāramitāḥ paripūryanta iti 
vittatvaparamatā gaganagañjasamādhyādibhir dānādiparipūraṇād iti 
bodhisattvā dharmadhātuprativedhabhāvanayā gaganagañjasaṃjñakaṃ samādhiṃ pratilabhante 
tasya pratilambhātsattvānāṃ sarvābhiprāyaparipūraṇād dānapāramitāṃ paripūrayanti 
tadādhipatyena hi gaganam eva gañjo bhavatīti samādhir gaganagañja ityabhidhīyate yasmāt tad ṛddhyā sarvopakaraṇāni gaganāj jāyante 
ādiśabdena prajñāpāramitādisūtrapaṭhitānāṃ grahaṇaṃ 
parigrahaṇaparamatā nirvikalpajñānaparigṛhītatvād iti 
bodhisattvānāṃ hi dāpakadeyapratigrāhakatrayānupalambhān nirvikalpaṃ jñānaṃ 
evaṃ yāvaj jñātṛjñeyajñānatrayānupalambhān nirvikalpaṃ jñānaṃ 
tena parameṇa nirvikalpena jñānena parigṛhītā dānādipratipattiḥ kathaṃ  tad anuparivartitatvāt tad ālambanatvāc cetyataḥ parametyucyate 
ārambhaparamatā adhimukticaryābhūmāvadhimātrāyāṃ kṣāntāv iti 
prathamakalpāsaṃkhye yānām adhimukticaryābhūmir ity ucyate 
gotramitrabalena cotpāditabodhicittasya svabhāvatrayamukhenātyarthaṃ sarvadharmanairātmyādhimokṣo'dhimātrā kṣāntirāśraddhyādivipakṣair aparājaya iti 
sā hi bodhisattvasyārambhāvasthā 
tato'dhimātrāyāṃ kṣāntāvārambhaparamatety ucyate 
pratilambhaparamatā prathamāyāṃ bhūmāv iti 
prathamāyāṃ hi bhūmau dharmadhātoḥ sarvatragatvāvabodhāl lokottarāḥ pāramitāḥ pratilabhate pūrvantu prathamabhūmiprayogasangṛhītā laukikā evetyataḥ prathamāyāṃ bhūmau pratilambhaparamatety ucyate 
niṣyandaparamatā tadanyāsvaṣṭāsv iti 
prathamabhūmipratilabdhānāṃ tad anyāsv aṣṭāsu bhūmiṣu uttarottaraviśiṣṭapratilambho niṣyanda iti niṣyandaparamatā 
athavā'dhimukticaryābhūmau pāramitābhāvanābalena prathamabhūmipratilambhaḥ pratilambhaparamatā 
prathamā hi bhūmir bodhisattvānāṃ darśanamārgasangṛhītā tat praveśāc ca jātau  tathāgatasyotpannaḥ tad anukūlatadātmakadharmapratilambhād iti sūtrapāṭhaḥ 
pāramitābhāvanābalena pratilabdhāyāḥ prathamāyā bhūmer avaśiṣṭā bhūmayo niṣyandatvān niṣyandaparamatā 
athavā prathamabhūmipratilabdhānāṃ pāramitānām aṣṭau bhūmayo niṣyandabhūtatvān niṣyandapramatā 
niṣpattiparamatā daśamyāṃ bhūmau tāthāgatyāñca bodhisattvaniṣpattyā buddhaniṣpattyā ca 
daśamyāṃ hi bhūmau bodhisattvaḥ sarvabodhisattvacaryāniryāta iti tatra tathāgatair yauvarājye'bhiṣicyate 
acintyapuṇyajñānasambhāraparipūrṇatvāt sarvadharmavikalpavigatatvāt sarvathā svaparārthasampādakatvāc ca bodhisattvānāṃ viṣpattiparamatā 
tāthāgatyāñca bhūmau prahāṇajñānaprabhāvātiśayalābhād bhagavān sarvasya jagataḥ śāstā bhavatītyato buddhapariniṣpattyā niṣpattiḥ 
kā punar iyaṃ niṣpattiḥ  bodhisattvadharmāṇāṃ buddhadharmāṇāñca sarvaprakārābhinirhāraḥ 
athavā pāramitānāṃ śaikṣabhūmisangṛhītānāṃ prakarṣo daśamī bhūmiḥ 
atas tasyāṃ bodhisattvapariniṣpattiḥ 
aśaikṣabhumisangṛhītānāṃ kāṣṭhā buddhabhūmiḥ 
tasyāṃ bhūmau pāramitānāṃ śaikṣābhāvād buddhapariniṣpattyā pariniṣpattir ityevaṃ bodhisattvapariniṣpattyā daśamyāṃ bhūmau tāthāgatyañca buddhapariniṣpattiparamatā veditavyā 
tataś ca paramārthena daśa pāramitā matāḥ 
iti 
yata eṣā dvādaśavidhā paramatā bodhisattvānāṃ dānādiṣu saṃvidyate na śrāvakādīnāṃ dānādiṣu tataḥ parametyanenārthena bodhisattvānām eva dānādayo jñānaparyantā daśa pāramitā matā iti niruktinyāyeneti 
daśapāramitānāṃ yā pratipattiḥ sā punaḥ paramatety ucyate 
  ekeṣām iti yeṣāṃ pāramitānāṃ nāmamātram api na vyutpannaṃ teṣāṃ tan nāmavyutpādanārtham ucyate  dānaṃ śīlaṃ kṣaṃā vīryaṃ dhyānaṃ prajñā upāyatā 
praṇidānaṃ balaṃ jñānam etāḥ pāramitā daśa 
iti 
adhikāraparamatā sarvatattvārthakriyoddeśādityuktam ato'yaṃ praśnaḥ  kimāsāṃ pratyekaṃ karmeti 
ata āha  anugraho'vidhātaś ca karma tasya ca marṣaṇaṃ 
iti vistaraḥ 
dānena hi bodhisattvaḥ sattvānanugṛhṇātīti 
tatra pūjānugrahakānkṣayā bāhyātmikavastuni avadyatvāt pratyupakāravipākādinirapekṣo yayā cetanayā parityajati kāyavākkarmāṇi ca pratipādayatīdaṃ bodhisattvasyāmiṣadānaṃ 
anena kṣutpipāsādiduḥkhāpanayanāt sattvānānugṛhṇāti 
sattvānupaghātakānām ājīvaśāstrakalānipuṇānāṃ karuṇāpūrvakam upadeśaḥ sugatimokṣamārgopadeśaś ca dharmadānaṃ 
anenā'pyajīvikādurgatisaṃsāraduḥkhāpanayanāt sattvānanugṛhṇāti 
rājacauradāyādavyālādibhir āghrātānāṃ tebhyo vimokṣaṇam abhayadānaṃ 
anenāpi jīvabhogaputradārādivipadbhayāpanayanāt sattvānanugṛhṇātīti 
śīlenopaghātam eṣāṃ na karoti 
sarvakāyavāgduścaritaviratir lokānuvṛttyā ca pratiṣiddhād vihitasya ca kāyavākkarmaṇo viratir anuṣṭhānañca śīlaṃ 
asmin śīle vyavasthānāt sattveṣvapakāraṃ duṣṭopasaṃhāraṃ jīvitahetor api svayaṃ na karoti nāpi kārayatīti 
kṣāntyā paraiḥ kṛtam upaghātaṃ marṣayatīti 
karuṇāpuraḥsareṇa cetasā sarvākāraduḥkhamarṣaṇādhivāsanātmikā kṣāntiḥ 
tenānvair hiṃsābandhanatāḍanādikṛtam upaghātaṃ marṣayati pratyapakārāsamīhanāt 
vīryeṇa guṇān vardhayati 
dānādīnadhikṛtyotsāho vīryaṃ 
tena dānādiguṇābhyāsād viśiṣṭaguṇaniṣpattir vṛddhiḥ 
dhyānena ṛddhyādibhir āvarjyāvatārayatīti 
ādiśabdena cittaparyāyajñānaṃ  parigṛhyate 
dhyānaṃ samādhiścittasyaikāgratā 
ṛddhirākāśagamanādikā 
avatāraṇaṃ śāsanadharmatāpratipādanaṃ 
dhyānaphalābhyāṃ hi ṛdhyādeśanāprātihāryābhyām āvarjitaḥ śakyante śāsana avatartuṃ 
prajñayā samyag avavādadānād vimocanād vimocayati 
sarvākāradharmapravicayalakṣaṇā prajñā 
tasyāś ca karma samyag avavādadānaṃ kleśaprahāṇaṃ cāviparītānuśāsanapratibaddhamataḥ prajñayā samyag avavādadānād vimocayati 
upāyakauśalyapāramitayā mahābodhipariṇāmanād dānādīnakṣayān karoti 
yasya dharmasya niṣpattaye vivṛddhaye prāptaye prahāṇāya vā yā yuktiḥ sa tatropāyas tatra kauśalyaṃ vaicakṣaṇyam upāyakauśalyaṃ 
tasya kṛutopacitānāṃ dānādīnāṃ mahabodhipariṇāmanayā'kṣayakāraṇāṃ
mahābodhipariṇāmanayā kuśalamūlāni mahābodhivad akṣayāni bhavantīti 
praṇidhānapāramitayā'nukūlopapattiparigrahāt sarvajanmasu buddhotpādārāgaṇato dānādiṣu sadā pravartate 
praṇidhānam anekavidhaṃ prārthanātmakatvāt 
kuśalānukūlopapattiprārthanam atra praṇidhānam abhipretaṃ tasya janmani janmani buddhotpādārāgaṇato dānādiṣu sadā pravartanaṃ karma 
balapāramitayā pratisaṃkhyānabhāvanābalābhyāṃ niyataṃ dānādiṣu pravartate vipakṣānabhibhavād iti 
pratisaṃkhyānaṃ prajñā 
bhāvanā tu kuśaladharmābhyāsaḥ 
tad dvayaṃ vipakṣeṇānabhibhūtaṃ balapāramitety ucyate 
tasyāḥ kṣaṇanaiyamyena dānādiṣu pravṛttiḥ karma 
niyataśabdasya satataparyāyatvāt 
na hi pratisaṃkhyānabhāvanābalād dānādikuśalaṃ vipakṣeṇābhibhūyate 
jñānapāramitayā yathārutadharmasammohāpagamād dānādyādhipateyadharmasambhogañca pratyanubhavati sattvāṃśca paripācayatīti 
sarvasmin mahāyānadeśanādharme yathārutasammohavigatajñānaṃ jñānapāramitā
