ayaṃ punar yathārutasammohaḥ kaḥ  yenābhiprāyikam arthaṃ tyaktvā yathārutam eva kalpayatyayaṃ yathārutasammohaḥ 
dānam adhikṛtya dānam ālambya yaḥ sūtrādiko dharmo deśitaḥ sa dānādhipateyaḥ 
evaṃ śīlakṣāntivīryādyādhipateyo draṣṭavyaḥ 
mahāyānam ārabhya buddhabodhisattvenāviparītasāṃkathyaviniścayakāraṇāt sattvānāṃ cāviparītayā dharmadeśanayā paripācanād dharmsambhogānubhavanaṃ sattvaparipācanañca jñānapāramitāyāḥ karma 
sūtrādidharmopadeśasya jñānapāramitāprabhāvitatvāt 
  manasikārapratipattiḥ   paramapratipattinirdeśānantaraṃ manasikārapratipattir vaktavyā tatḥ pṛcchati  manasikārapratipattiḥ katametyata āha  yathāprajñaptito dharma mahāyānamanaskriyā 
iti vistaraḥ 
dānādīnyadhikṛtyeti dānaśīlakṣāntivīryādīny uddiśya 
yathāprajñaptānāṃ sūtrādidharmāṇām iti 
atra sūtrageyavyākaraṇādidharmā yena prakāreṇa  dānādīnyadhikṛtya bhagavatā deśitās teṣāṃ tathaivārthato vyañjanataścādhyāropāpavādarahitānāṃ manasikaraṇaṃ manasikārapratipattir nānyatheti 
mahāyāna iti na śrāvakayāne 
tatra hi svārthā eva dānādayo deśitā na svaparārthā yathā mahāyāne 
tasmān mahāyāna eva dānādīnyadhikṛtya yathāprajñaptānāṃ sūtrādidharmāṇāṃ bodhisattvair manasikaraṇaṃ manasikāra pratipattiḥ 
śrāvakayāne dānādīnyadhikṛtya bhāṣitānāṃ sūtrādīnāṃ manasikaraṇam mithyāmanasikārapratipattiḥ svārthamātrāśrayatvād iti jñāpitam bhavati 
te ca prāyeṇa cittasamatām asaktim anunnatim anupalaṃbhañcādhikṛtya prajñaptā iti 
tatreya cittasamatā yā guṇyaguṇināṃ samam upakāraprārthanā 
tatreyam asaktir yo bhavabhogaprārthanāvigatasya parārtham eva dānādiṣu prayogaḥ 
tatreyam anunnatir yad dānādibhir nātmānaṃ manyate na parān paribhavati 
tatrāyam anupalambho yā trimaṇḍalapariśuddhir dānadāyakapratigrāhakānām anupalambhanyāyeneti 
abhīkṣṇam iti punaḥ punaḥ 
śrutacintābhāvanāmayyā prajñayeti tatrāptavacanaprāmāṇyajo niścayaḥ śrutamayī 
yuktinidhyānajaścintāmayī 
bhāvanājo bhāvanāmayīti 
sarvā hi pravṛttiḥ pralārtham ataḥ pṛcchati  sā triprākarayā prajñayā manasikriyā kaṃ guṇam āvahatīty ata āha  dhātupuṣṭyai praveśāya cārthasiddhai bhavatyasau 
dhātur gotraṃ bījaṃ 
tasya puṣṭir vṛddhiḥ 
dhātupuṣṭyā cāyatyāṃ viśadamahaprajño bhavati 
tasya śrutasyārthaṃ bhāvena praviśatīti 
tasya sūtrādikasya śrutadharmasyārthe yuktibalotpāditayā cintāmayyā prajñayā'rthasadbhāvam āśayataḥ praviśatīti 
bhāvanāmayyārthasiddhiṃ prāpnoti 
arthasiddhis tattvādhigamaḥ 
katham ityata āha  bhūmipraveśapariśodhanād iti 
smṛtyupasthānādipariśuddhyā hi bhūmiṃ praviśatītyataḥ smṛtyupasthānādibhir eva bhūmiṃ praviśatīti nirdiṣṭaṃ 
tataḥ smṛtyupasthānādīnāṃ bhūmipraveśabhūtānāṃ bhāvanāmayyā prajñayā pariśodhanād arthasiddhiṃ prāpnotīti bhūmiṃ praviśatītyarthaḥ 
sā punar iyaṃ manasikārapratipattiḥ saparivārā vijñeyā na kevalā 
kastat parivāraḥ  āha  saṃyuktā dharmacaritaiḥ sā jñeyā daśabhiḥ punaḥ 
iti 
parigṛhītā veditavyeti parivāritetyarthaḥ 
dharmātmakāni dharmādhikārikāṇi  vā caritāni dharmacaritāni 
tāni punar na jñāyanta ityata āha  katamad daśadhā dharmacaritam iti 
ata āha  lekhanā pūjanā dānaṃ iti vistaraḥ 
tatra mahāyānasya svayaṃ pareṇa vā lekhanaṃ cirasthityarthaṃ śravaṇāvācanārthaṃ vā 
pūjanaṃ puṣpadhūpagandhādibhiḥ 
mahāyānasyeti prakṛtaṃ 
mahāyānapraviṣṭasya likhitapustakādīnāṃ parebhyaḥ satkṛtya dānaṃ 
pareṇa vācyamānasya satkṛtya śravaṇaṃ 
mahatā gauraveṇa svayaṃ vācanaṃ 
udgrahaṇaṃ mahatā prasādenātmasātkaraṇaṃ 
mahatā yatnena yogyebhyo granthastyārthasya vā āviṣkaraṇaṃ prakāśanaṃ 
svādhyāyanam uddhatasya punaḥ punar abhyasanaṃ 
cintanaṃ yuktidvāreṇa tadarthanirūpaṇaṃ 
bhāvamam abhyasanaṃ samāhitayā prajñayā 
ca śabdaḥ samuccaryārthaḥ 
tatra lekhanā pūjanā dānaṃ śravaṇam ityebhiś caturbhiḥ padaiḥ kāyakarma pradarśitaṃ 
vācanam udgrahaṇaṃ prakāśanā svādhyāyanam ityebhiś caturbhiḥ padair vākkarma pradarśitaṃ 
cintanā bhāvanā cetyābhyām api manaḥ karma pradarśitaṃ 
ameyapuṇyaskandhaṃ hi caritaṃ tad daśātmakaṃ 
yadet daśaprakāraṃ dharmacaritam uktaṃ tata ekaikasmād dharmacaritādyaḥ puṇyaskandhodbhavo na sa punaḥ svayaṃ pareṇa vā pramātuṃ śakyate atibahutvād iti kasmāt punar dānaśīladhyānādidharmanirdeśe tulye mahāyāna eva dharmacaritam atyarthaṃ mahāphalaṃ deśyate sūtreṣu na punaḥ śrāvakayāne  sūtreṣu dharmacaritaṃ mahāphalaṃ deśyata iti sambadhyate 
dvābhyāṃ kāraṇābhyām iti mahāyāne dharmacaritam atyarthaṃ mahāpalaṃ deśyata iti sambadhyate 
katam ābhyām ityata āha  viśeṣād akṣayatvāc ca iti 
etad api na jñāyata ityataḥ pṛcchati  kathaṃ viśeṣāt kahtma akṣayatvād ityata āha  parānugrahato'śamāt 
iti 
mahāyāne hi bodhisattvānāṃ dānādipratipattiḥ sarvasattvārthakaraṇaikaṃ deśyate 
śrāvakayāne tvātmārthapradhānetyataḥ śrāvakāyānān mahāyānaṃ parānugrahapravṛttatvād viśiṣyate 
evaṃ tāvad hetusamākhyānataḥ śrāvakayānān mahāyānasya viśiṣṭatvaṃ 
acintyapuṇyajñānasambhāraphalasya trikāyasaṃgṛhītasya yāval lokas tāvat sattvahitakriyāpravṛttasya nirupadhiśeṣe'pi nirvāṇadhātāv anuparatasyāsravaparāvṛttilakṣaṇasya dyotanād akṣayatvaṃ 
na tvevaṃ śrāvakayāne 
śrāvakasambhāraphalaṃ hi kṣayatvam ākhyātaṃ nirupadhiśeṣanirvṛtānāṃ sarvātmanā samucchedāt 
evaṃ nirvāṇe'pyanuparataṃ phalaṃ dyotanāc chrāvakayānān mahāyānaṃ viśiṣyate 
  athavā mahāyānasyārtho dānādikaḥ sarvasattvānugrahapravṛttaḥ natvevaṃ śrāvakānārthaḥ 
śrāvakāṇāṃ svārthaparatvāt 
dānādayaś ca bodhisattvānāṃ dharmā anāsravakāyatvena parivṛttāḥ parinirvāṇe'pi na vicchidyante 
śrāvakāṇān tu mārgasya kaulopamatvāt parinirvāṇe samucchidyata iti na teṣām akṣayatvaṃ 
tasmādyuktaṃ mahāyānasaiva dharmacaritaṃ mahāphalaṃ na śrāvakayāna iti 
  anudharmapratipattiḥ  manasikārapratipattyanantaram anudharmapratipātir vaktavyā ityataḥ pṛcchataḥ  anudharmapratipattiḥ katametyata āha  avikṣiptā'viparyāsapraṇatāvānudhārmikī 
iti 
dhyātavyajñeyadharmānugatā anupraviṣṭaśamathavipaśyanābhāvātmikā pratipattir anudharmpratipattiḥ 
tatra śamathabhāvanātmikā'vikṣiptā 
vipaśyanābhāvanātmikā'viparyāsapariṇatā 
iyaṃ dvividhā'nudharmapratipattiḥ 
  avikṣepapariṇatā  ayam akāro bahuṣvartheṣu vartata iti kahtam avivikṣepteti na vijñāyata ityata āha  tatra ṣaḍvidhavikṣepābhāvād avikṣipteti 
vikṣepo'pi na jñāyāte kathaṃ ṣaḍvidha ityata āha  ṣaḍvidho vikṣepaḥ  prakṛtivikṣepaḥ bahirdhāvikṣepa iti vistaraḥ 
  evam api prabhedamātraṃ darśitaṃ na vikṣepasvarūpam iti pṛcchati  sa eṣa ṣaḍvidho vikṣepaḥ kiṃ lakṣaṇo veditavya ityata āha  vyutthānaṃ viṣaye sāraḥ 
iti vistaraḥ 
dhīmatā iti dhaīmān bodhisattvaḥ 
tatra vyutthānaṃ samādhitaḥ pañcabhir vijñānakāyair iti 
yadā hi samāhitasya punaḥ pañcānāṃ cakṣurādivijñānānām anyatamad ekam utpadyate tadā samādhito vyutthito bhavati 
ayañca prakṛtivikṣepaḥ bahirmukhapravṛttatvāt 
pañcānāṃ vijñānakāyānāṃ vikṣepātmakatvāt pañcabhir vijñānakāyaiḥ samādhito vyutthānaṃ prakṛtivikṣepa ucyate 
viṣaye visāro bahirdhāvikṣepa iti 
yadā samāhitasya samādhyālambanād akāmakasyālambanāntare manovijñānaṃ pravartate tadālambanāntarasañcārād bahirdhāvikṣepa ityeke 
samāhitasya samādhyālambanaṃ hitvā manovijñānasya viṣayāntarasañcāro bahirdhā vikṣepa ityapare 
samādher āsvānadāṃ layauddhatyaṃ cādhyātmavikṣepa iti 
yadi samāhitastameva samādhiṃ tṛṣṇādinā kleśenāsvādayati tataḥ śuddhakāt samādher vikṣepo bhavati kliṣṭasamādhipratyupasthānāt 
layauddhatyañca śamathavipaśyanāsamavāhinaḥ samādher vikṣepo bhavati 
asamāhitattvāc cāsvādānālayauddhatyānām āsvādanādayo'dhyātmavikṣepa ity ucyante 
sambhāvanābhisandhir nimittavikṣepaḥ 
dhyāyyayaṃ mahātmetyevaṃ sambhāvanātmanītyanena nimittena samādhau prayuktasyāśayavilayatvālabdhād alabdhād vā kuśalapakṣād vikṣepo nimittavikṣepa ityucyate 
atraiva kāraṇam āha  tan nimittaṃ kṛtvā prayogād iti 
jñātukāmatayā taṃ sambhāvanābhisandhiḥ nimittaṃ kṛtveti sambhāvanātmanīti 
samādhiprayuktatvād iti 
sāhankaramanaskāratā dauṣṭhulyavikṣepa iti 
āśayena samādhiguṇārthino'pi sāhankaramanaskāro'smimānasam prayukto'ham asmi dhyāyīti 
tataścātmotkarṣamanyatrāvajñāṃ karotīti 
kasmād eṣa dauṣṭhulyamanaskāraḥ  ityata āha  dauṣṭhulyavaśenāsmimānasamudācārād iti 
etad uktaṃ bhavati  dauṣṭhulyaprabhāvito vikṣepo dauṣṭhulyavikṣepa iti 
kiṃ punar dauṣṭhulyaṃ  asmimānavāsanāparipuṣṭistayā hyasmimānaḥ samudācaratīti tadvaśenāsmimānasamudācārāt 
satkāyadṛṣṭir dauṣṭhulyam ityanye 
hīnacittatvaṃ manasikāravikṣepa iti 
aniyataśrāvakādigotrasya  mahāyānamanasikāraprayuktasya samsaraduḥkhabhīrutayā sattvavipratipānatvenākalyāṇamitraniṣevaṇena ca tac chrāvakapratyekabuddhacittam utpadyate 
taccittaṃ hīnaṃ svārthamātraparāyaṇatvāt 
tacchrāvakapratyekabuddhacittaṃ mahāyānamanasikāravikṣepakatvān manasikāravikṣepaḥ kathyate 
atraiva kāraṇam āha  hīnayāna manasikārasamudācārād iti 
hīnayānaṃ śrāvakapratyekabuddhayānaṃ 
ātmaparinirvāṇādhikārapravṛttatvān manasikārasamudācāro mahāyānamanasikārebhyo vikṣipatīti hīnaṃ cittaṃ manasikāravikṣepa ity ucyate 
evam iyaṃ bodhisattvasya ṣaḍvidhavikṣepadoṣarahitā śamathābhāvanā veditavyā 
  aviparyāsapariṇatā  evam avikṣiptena yathā'viparyāsapariṇatā'nudharmapratipattir bhāvayitavyā tathocyate 
aviparyāsātmanā pravṛttā'viparyāsapariṇatā 
tatra yad yathā vyavasthitaṃ vastu tathā tatra jñānam aviparyāsaḥ 
tad vastuta punar na jñāyate katividhe vastunītyata āha  tatrāviparyāso daśavidhe vastuni veditavya iti 
aviparyāsavastu pradarśanārthaṃ bravīti  yaduta  vyañjanārthamanaskārāvisāre lakṣaṇadvaye 
iti vistaraḥ 
idānīṃ teṣu vastuṣu yathā viparyāso bhavati tat pradarśanārtham āha  tatra saṃyogāt saṃbhavāc caiva viyogād apyasambhavāt 
arthasattvam asattvañca vyañjane so'viparyayaḥ 
iti 
saṃyoge sati vyañjanānām iti 
saṃyogo hi parasparasaṃśleṣaḥ 
na cāsau vyañjanānāṃ vidyate yaugapadyābhāvāt 
vyañjanānāṃ yugapad uccāraṇaṃ na yujyate 
pūrvavikalpānām uttaravyañjanoccaraṇakāle'navasthānam uccāraṇānantaram eva vinaṣṭatvād ityāśankāvyudāsārtham āha  avicchinnoccāraṇatayeti 
etad uktaṃ bhavati  aviparyastāvilambitoccāraṇam atra vyañjanānāṃ saṃyoga iṣyate na tu vyañjanānāṃ parasparasaṃśleṣaṇam iti 
asya cedaṃ nāmeti sambhavād iti 
yadi cāsya vastuna idaṃ nāmeti sanketo'bhyasto bhavati evam anena prakāradvayena sārthakatvaṃ vyañjanānāṃ pratyāyakatvam ityarthaḥ 
viparyayān nirarthakatvam iti 
ubhayābhāvo'nyataravaikalyaṃ vā viparyayaḥ 
yadevaṃ darśanam iti jñānaṃ 
so'viparyāso vyañjane veditavya iti saṃvṛttyā na tu paramārthataḥ 
paramārthenāviparyāsasya nirvikalpakatvād ityanenāviparyāsena bodhisattvaḥ śabdārtharahitān sarvadharmān pratividhyati 
idānīṃ vyañjanaprajñaptinimitte'rthe'viparyāsapradarśanārtham āha  dvayena pratibhāsatvaṃ tathā cāvidyamānatā 
iti vistaraḥ 
dvayena grāhyagrāhakatvena pratibhāsate 
kaḥ  paratantrasvabhāvaḥ 
kasmāt  grāhyagrāhakabījayuktatvāt 
kah punar atra pratibhāsārtha ityata āha  tadākārotpattita iti 
grāhyagrāhakākārotpattito grāhyagrāhakatvena pratibhāsate na punaḥ sphāṭikavad upadhānoparāgād iti 
tathā ca na vidyate yathā pratibhāsate advayaprakṛtitvāt 
iti evaṃ bhrāntivijñānotpattinimittabhūte'rthe yad darśanaṃ sa tatrāviparyāsaḥ sadasattvavarjanādityabhiprāyaḥ 
arthasya sattvena varjita ityatraiva kāraṇam āha  grāhyagrāhakābhāvād iti 
arthasya sattvaṃ  grāhyagrāhakasadbhāvaḥ 
tena varjito grāhyagrāhakākāreṇa śūnyatvād iti 
asattvena varjitaḥ 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  tat pratibhāsabhrāntisadbhāvād iti grāhyagrāhakapratibhāsabhrāntisadbhāvād ityarthaḥ 
ayam api saṃvṛttā'viparyāsa ucyate na paramārthataḥ savikalpatvāt 
anenāviparyāsajñānena bodhisattvo grāhyagrāhakasvabhāvarahitān sarvadharmān pratividhyatīti 
idānīṃ grāhyagrāhakaprakhyānanimitte ālayavijñāne'viparyāsapradarśanārtham āha  tajjalpabhāvito jalpamanaskāras tadāśrayaḥ 
iti vistaraḥ 
grāhyagrāhakajalpaparibhāvito jalpamaskāra iti 
tasmin grāhyagrāhakaprakhyānalakṣaṇe'rthe'yaṃ grāhyo'yaṃ grāhaka iti vānmanobhyāṃ yad abhilapanaṃ sa jalpa ity ucyate 
anena jalpena paribhāvito'nāgatataj jātīyajalpotpādāya bījaparipoṣaṇam iti paribhāvita ity ucyate 
so'yaṃ jalpaparibhāvitatvāj jalpamanaskāra ityākhyāyate kārye kāraṇopacārāt 
jalpavāsanā stvatra jalpaḥ 
jalpo'trāstītyādhārādheyayor abhedaṃ kṛtvā ādhāraśabdasya vā grahaṇāj jalpamanaskāra ityucyate 
tasya grāhyagrāhakavikalpasya jalpākhyasya bījādhāratvāt 
punaś ca jalpasya tat sanniśrayeṇotpāter āśrayo bhavatītyayaṃ manaskāre'viparyāsa ityaviparītaṃ jñānam ityarthaḥ 
sa tu manaskāro na vijṇyāte yasminn aviparyāsa ityataḥ pṛcchati  katam asminmanaskāre'viparyāsa iti 
ato manaskāraviśeṣaṇārtham āha  grāhyagrāhakasamprakhyānakāraṇe ālayavijñānaviśeṣātmaka ityarthaḥ 
yathāsau grāhyagrāhakasamprakhyānakāraṇaṃ bhavati tat pradarśanārtham āha  sa hyasau jalpamanaskāro'bhilāpasaṃjñāparibhāvitatvād iti 
grāhyagrāhakaprakhyānakāraṇaṃ bhavatīti sambadhyate 
athavā jalpamanaskāra ityato'bhidhānapravṛttinimittam āha 
abhilāpasaṃjñāparibhāvitatvāj jalpamanaskāra ucyata iti 
abhilāpasamutthā abhilāpasamutthāpikā vā saṃjñā abhilāpasaṃjñā 
tayā sasamprayogayā jalpamanaskāre svabījaparipoṣaṇāj jalpamanasikāraḥ paribhāvita ucyate 
ayam api saṃvṛttyaivāviparyāso na paramārthataḥ 
anena cāviparyāsena bodhisattvo viparyāsanidānaṃ grāhyagrāhakābhiniveśalakṣaṇaṃ parivarjayati 
evaṃ tad dauṣṭhulyaṃ sukhena varjitaṃ bhavatīti 
  idānīm avisāre'viparyāsapradarśanārtham āha  māyādivad asattvañca sattvañcārthasya tan mataṃ 
iti vistaraḥ 
yat tadarthasyāsattvaṃ sattvañcānantaramuktam iti 
katham anantaram uktam iti  dvayena praibhāsatvaṃ tathā cāvidyamānatā 
arthe sa cā'viparyāsaḥ sadasattvena varjtiaḥ 
iti tanamāyādivan mataṃ 
māyādīnām iva māyādivat 
etad eva pradarśayann āha yathā māyā svātmanyavidyamānena hastyādyātmanā prakhyānān na hastyādibhāvenāstīti 
hastyādibhāvena nāstīti sarvathaiva nāsti 
kiṃ tarhi na ca naivāsti tad bhrāntimātrāstitvād iti 
tasya hastyādyākāreṇa prakhyāyamānasya bhrāntimātrasyāstitvān na sarvathā nāsti 
tathārtho'pi na cāsti yathā samprakhyāti grāhyagrāhakatvena tathā naivāsti 
  tasya traidhātukacittacaittasvarūpasya tathāprakhyāyamānasya bhrāntimātrāstitvān nāpi nāsti 
ādiśabdena marīcisvapnodakacandrādayo dṛṣṭāntā yathāyogaṃ veditavyā iti 
nahi marīcisvapnodakacandrādayo yathā strīpumātmanā prakhyāyante tathā santi na ca santyeva bhrāntimātrāstitvāt evam artho'pīti vistareṇa pratyekaṃ yojayitavyaṃ 
atra cādiśabdena gandharvanagarapratiśrutkādayo veditavyāḥ 
evaṃ yan māyādyupamārthadarśanāt sattvāsattvapakṣayor avisāraṃ cetasaḥ avikṣiptatvaṃ paśyati so'visāre'viparyāsaḥ 
kaḥ punar avisāraḥ  madhyamā pratipat samādhir ityanye 
yadyevaṃ katham avisāre'viparyāsa ityata āha  tena bhāvābhāvayościttasyāvisaraṇād iti 
anenāviparyāsena bodhisattvo bhāvābhāvavikalparahitāchūnyatā'lambane'vikṣepaḥ 
tasmād avisāre viparyāsa ucyate 
ayam api saṃvṛttyairvāviparyāso na paramārthataḥ tasya nirvikalpakatvāt 
idānīṃ svalakṣaṇe'viparyāsapradarśanārtham āha  sarvasya nāmamātratvaṃ sarvakalpāpravṛttaye 
iti vistaraḥ 
sarvam idaṃ nāmamātraṃ yadidaṃ cakṣūrūpaṃ yāvan manodharmā iti 
ato dvādaśāyatanātmakaṃ jñeyaṃ sarvaṃ nāmamātraṃ 
tatra nāmasvabhāvaviśeṣaprajñaptiḥ 
na ca prajñaptyasyārthasya prajñapter vā svabhāvo'sti 
tenātmanā parikalpitatvāt parikalpitasya cāsattvāt 
anyathā nāmanirapekṣayā cakṣurāditvena grahaṇaṃ syāt 
na cāstyavyutpannasanketasya grahaṇaṃ 
tasmāc cakṣūrupam ityādyasyātat svabhāvatvān nāmamātram eva cakṣūrūpaṃ yāvan manodharmā ityevaṃ yaj jñānaṃ sarvavikalpānāṃ pratipakṣeṇa ayaṃ svalakṣaṇe'viparyāsa iti parikalpitadharmamukhena sarvadharmeṣu sarvavikalpapravṛttiḥ 
ato nāmamātraprativedhajñānaṃ sarvavikalpapratipakṣaḥ svalakṣaṇe'viparyāsa ity uktaṃ 
tatra na jñāyate kiṃ paramārthe svalakṣaṇe āhosvit saṃvṛtāv ityataḥ pṛcchati  katam asmin svalakṣaṇa iti 
ata āha  paramārthe svalakṣaṇe 
ayam aviparyāsaḥ 
paramārthasya svalakṣaṇasyānabhilāpyatvān na saṃvṛteḥ 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  saṃvṛttyā yato nedaṃ nāmamātram iti gṛhyate abhilāpadvāreṇa dharmasvarūpe sankalpapravṛtteḥ ayam api saṃvṛtyaiva na paramārthato nāmamātram iti vikalpanāt 
anena cāviparyāsena bodhisattvaḥ saṃvṛtiparamārthakuśalo bhavati 
  idānīṃ sāmānyalakṣaṇe'viparyāsapradarśanāyāha  dharmadhātuvinirmukto yasmād dharmo na vidyate 
iti vistaraḥ 
na hi dharmanairātmyena vinā kaścid rūpyarūpī vā dharmo vidyate 
sarva dharmāṇām anabhilāpyādvayaprakṛtatvād grāhagrāhakabhāvena rahitatvāt 
tasmād dharmadhātuḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ sāmānyaṃ lakṣaṇam iti 
sarvadharmeṣv apṛthaktvena tat sat sāmānyalakṣaṇam ucyate 
yadevaṃ jñānamayaṃ sāmānyalakṣaṇo'viparyāsaḥ saṃvṛttyā na tu paramārthataḥ 
tasya nirvikalpatvāt 
tad anena cāviparyāsena bodhisattvo viśuddhyālambanakuśalo bhavati nirvikalpajñānaviṣayatvāt 
viśeṣaḥ sāmānyalakṣaṇasvalaksaṇayoḥ ko vidyate  abhilāpasvabhāvasamāropitatvasya pratipakṣeṇānabhilāpyasvabhāvatā paramārthalakṣaṇaṃ 
parikalpitasvabhāvanairātmyaṃ punaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ prakṛtir iti sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ 
evaṃ darśanabhedavaśād viśeṣo bhavati na tv arthād iti 
idānīṃ dharmadhātv aviśuddhiviśuddhāv aviparyāsapradarśanārtham āha  viparyasta manaskārāvihāniparihāṇitaḥ 
iti vistaraḥ 
viparyasta manaskāraprahāṇaṃ tasya dharmadhātor aviśuddhiḥ tat prahāṇaṃ viśuddhir iti 
tatra viparyasta manaskāra ālayavijñānahetur viparyayavikalpaḥ 
tasyāprahāṇaṃ dharmadhātor aviśuddhiḥ prahāṇaṃ viśuddhiḥ 
yadevaṃ jñānamayam aviśuddhau viśuddhau cāviparyāso yathākramam iti 
viparyasta manaskārāprahāṇaṃ tasya dharmadhātor aviśuddhir iti dharmadhātor aviśuddhāvaviparyāsaḥ 
tasya prahāṇaṃ viśuddhir iti viśuddhāv aviparyāsaḥ 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  dharmadhātor āgantukenopakleśenopakliṣṭatvāt 
ayam api saṃvṛttyaivāviparyāso na paramārthataḥ 
anena cāviparyāsena bodhisattvo'prahīṇāvaraṇaṃ dharmadhātoḥ prahāṇañca prajānāti 
idānīṃ dharmadhātor aviśuddher viśuddheścāgantukatve'viparyāsapradarśanārtham āha  dharmadhātor viśuddhatvāt prakṛtyā vyomavat punaḥ 
iti vistaraḥ 
dharmadhātoḥ punar ākāśavat prakṛtiviśuddhitatvād dvayam apyetadāgantukam aviśuddhir viśuddhiś ca paścād iti 
tatra dharmadhātorabhūtavikalpopakliṣṭatvād aśuddhir uktā 
paścāc ca pratipakṣodayena tat prahāṇād viśuddhiḥ 
etad dvayam api dharmadhātāv āgantukaṃ 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  ākāśavad dharmadhātoḥ prakṛtiviśuddhatvāt 
prakṛtiviśuddhasyāviśuddhir āgantukī bhaved viśuddhes tu nityaviśuddhitaḥ katham āgantukībhāva iti  yā malavigamatātmatayā viśuddhiḥ sātra vivakṣiteti nāyaṃ doṣaḥ 
ata evoktaṃ viśuddhiś ca paścād iti 
yadevaṃ dharmadhātor jñānam etad dharmadhātor viśuddhi viśuddhyor āgantukatve'viparyāsaḥ 
ayam api saṃvṛttyā na tu paramārthataḥ 
anena cāviparyāsena bodhisattvo dharmadhātoḥ sankleśavyavadānāvasthayoḥ kṛtrimatvaṃ prajānātīti 
  idānīmatrāse'nunnatau cāviparyāsapradarśanārtham āha  sankleśaś ca viśuddhiś ca dharmapudgalayor na hi 
iti vistaraḥ 
na hi pudgalasya sankleśo na viśuddhiḥ nāpi dharmasya 
sankleśo viśuddhirśceti vartate 
atraiva kāraṇam āha  yasmān na pudgalo'sti na dharmaḥ 
astītyanuvartate 
yaḥ sankleśavyavadānavyatirekeṇa vidyate yasya sankleśo vyavadānaṃ vā parikalpayituṃ yujyate yat pṛthaktvena ca saṃkleśaviśuddhī syātāṃ sa tādṛśaḥ pudgalo nāsti pratyakṣānumānāviṣayatvāt 
dharmo'pi parikalpitātmako naivāsti ekasminn vastuny ekaparikalpapravṛtteḥ 
na caikasyānekātmakatā yujyate ato'sattvāt pudgaladharmayordvayo bandhnyaputrādivanna sanleśo na vyavadānaṃ 
paratantrsyāpi ṣuddaloukikajñanagocarasya sankleśaviśuddhī naiveṣyate 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  tasya nirabhilāpyādvayaprakṛtitvāt 
yadi paratantrasyāpi neṣyate kasya te syātāṃ  tasminn asati sankleśaparihāre vyavadānaprāptiyatnavaiyarthyaṃ 
dharmadhātoḥ sankleśaviśuddhī bhavata ity ayam adoṣaḥ 
dharmadhātor apyatanmayasyaiva te vyavasthāpyete dharmadhātau tayor āgantukatvād dharmadhātoścākāśavad avikārāt 
tataḥ na saṃkleśapakṣe kasyacid hānir na vyavadānapakṣe vā kaścid viśeṣo yatas trāso vā syān mānovetyamatrāse'nunnatau cāviparyāsa iti 
anye tvāhuḥ  na sankleśapakṣe kasyacid hānir na vyavadānapakṣe viśeṣo'sti tad ubhayavataḥ kasyacid abhāvāt 
yataḥ punas ta evaṃ bhavatas tatra kim iti trāso bhavaty ayaṃ me nāstīti kim iti māno bhavaty ayaṃ me viśeṣa iti 
  apare tu manyate  pudgalas tāvan naivāsti 
dharmo'pi naivāsti 
avasthādvayaṃ yo'nubhavati yasyaitad dvayaṃ kalpyeta 
kiṃ tarhi pratītyasamutpādamātram etat sankleśavyavadānam iti 
ayam api saṃvṛttyā na tu paramārthataḥ tasya nirvikalpakatvāt 
anena cāviparyāsena kṣayavṛddhyasadbhāvād avikāritvaṃ dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatīti 
anena cāviparyāsena sarvam āvaraṇaṃ prahāya nirāvaraṇo niryātītyanye 
atha vānena saṃvṛtyātmakena daśaviparyāsena paramārthāviparyāso'tra sūcitaḥ tasyānyathā nirdeśānupapatteḥ 
anyaḥ punar āha  ya ete vyañjane'rthe manaskāre'visāre svalakṣaṇe sāmānyalakṣaṇe'śuddhau śuddhāvāgantuke'trāse'nunnatau cāviparyāsāḥ kalpitā āśrayās te svabhāvatrayam adhikṛtyeti 
tatra vyañjanārthāviparyāsāv atra parikalpitaṃ svabhāvam adhikṛtya 
saṃyogino dvayapatitasya cārthasya kalpitatvāt 
atattvaviṣayatve'pi satyevaṃ tad dvayam aviparyāsa eva 
aviparyāsas tathaiveti 
manaskāre'viparyāsaḥ paratantrasvabhāvam adhikṛtya 
jalpamanaskārasya prakṛtyā ālayavijñānātmakatvāt 
avisāre'viparyāsaḥ pariniṣpannasvabhāvam adhikṛtya 
kuta etan nirvikalpasya jñānasya bhāvābhāvayor vikṣepavigatatvād aviparyāsapariniṣpattyā ca pariniṣpannasvabhāvasaṃgṛhītatvāt 
svasāmānyalakṣaṇayor aviparyāso dharmadhātā meva tasya vikalpaviśayātikrāta svarūptvāt
aśuddau śuddau caviparyāso dharmaavasthāviśeṣe 
āgantuke'viparyāso dharmadhātāv eva tasya hy ākāśavat prakṛtiviśuddhasya cittasankleśāc cittaviśuddhyā cāgantukam etad ubhayaṃ vyavasthāpyate 
atrāsānunnabhāvāviparyāso dharmadhātāv eva tasyākāśavad akṛtrimatvād hāniviśeṣābhāvāt 
evam ete daśa viparyāsāḥ svabhāvatraye veditavyāḥ 
  daśa vajrapadāni   ete cānantaroktā daśaviparyāsāḥ sūtrokteṣu daśasu vajrapadeṣu yathākramaṃ yojayitavyāḥ 
daśa vajrapadāni katamāni  sadasattā'viparyāsaḥ āśrayaḥ māyopamatā avikalpanatā prakṛtiprabhāsvaratā sankleśo vyavadānaṃ ākāśopamatā ahīnatā aviśiṣṭatā ceti 
tatra vajramiva vajraṃ sarvaviparyāsabheditvāt taiścābhedyatvāt 
anantaroktam aviparyāsajñānaṃ tac ca vajram ebhiḥ pratīyate avagamyata iti vajrapadāni 
vajravyākhyānam ityarthaḥ 
atha punarvyañjanārthamanaskārādaya eva padaśabdhenocyante tato vajrasya padānyālambanānityarthaḥ 
athava durbhedatayā vajravadetānyeva padāni vajra padānītyuccayante 
atrāviparyāsānāṃ sūtrayojanārthaṃ vajrapadopanyāsaḥ 
vajrapadānāṃ va daśavidhāviparyāsamukhenedaṃ vyākhyānam iti pradarśanārthaṃ 
tatra vyañjanānām arthasattvam asattvañca sadasattetyato vyañjaneṣv aviparyāso vajrapadeṣu sadasattayā veditavyaḥ 
dvayaprabhāsaḥ parikalpitaḥ sa cātrārthaḥ 
sa ca tathā na vidyata ityayam atrāviparyāsa ityarthāviparyāso vajrapadeṣv aviparyāse yojayitavyaḥ 
jalpamanaskāra evātrāśraya ityato manaskāre'viparyāso vajrapadeṣvāśraye yojayitavyaḥ 
māyādyupamayā yaścetaso'visāre'viparyāsaḥ sa vajrapadeṣu māyopamatāyāṃ yojayitavyaḥ 
dharmadhātusvalakṣaṇam eva kalpanārahitatvād avikalpanatā 
tena svalakṣaṇāviparyāso nirvikalpatvena draṣṭavyaḥ 
dharmadhātusāmānyaṃ prakṛtiprabhāsvaratvaṃ 
tena sāmānyalakṣaṇāviparyāsaḥ prakṛtiprabhāsvaratayā sangṛhītaḥ 
dharmadhātor aviśuddhiviśeṣo viśuddhiviśeṣaśca sankleśo  vyavadānañcetyato'śuddhau viśuddhau cāviparyāsaḥ sankleśavyavadānāntare sangṛhyate 
dharmadhātoḥ sankleśavyavadānayor āgantukatve'viparyāso'sāvapyākāśopamatāyāṃ yojayitavyaḥ 
sankleśavyavadānāvasthayor dharmadhātoḥ kṣayavṛddhyabhāvād atrāse'nunnatau cāviparyāso vajrapadeṣv ahīnāviśiṣṭatāyāṃ yojayitavyaḥ 
evam ete daśāviparyāsā daśasu vajrapadeṣu yathākramaṃ yojayitavyāḥ 
vajrapadānāṃ śarīravyavasthānam iti yānārthānadhikṛtya vajrapadānāṃ pravṛttis te'rthās teṣāṃ śarīraṃ 
teṣāntu caturdhā vyavasthānaṃ svabhāvataḥ ālambanataḥ avikalpanataḥ codyaparihārataś ca 
tatra trayaḥ svabhāvāḥ pariniṣpannaparikalpitaparatantrākhyā ādyais tribhiḥ padair yathākramam iti 
tatrādau bhavānyādyāni tāni punaḥ sadasattā'viparyāsa āśrayaśceti 
tatra sadasattayā pariniṣpanna uktaḥ 
aviparyāsena parikalpita uktaḥ 
āśrayatvena paratantra uktaḥ 
katham iti  pariniṣpannasya sadasattāyā sadasattayā nirdeśa iti kecit 
kathaṃ sadasal lakṣaṇatvāt pariniṣpannasya sadasattayā'bhidhānam ityeke 
saṃyogāt saṃstavācākṣarāṇāṃ kalpitenārthena sārthakatvaṃ paśyan viparyayāc ca nirarthakatvaṃ pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvo'nabhilāpya iti avagamyate 
atas tat sadasattā pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāva ity uktam ityanye 
mahāyānadeśanādharmaḥ suviśuddhadharmadhātuniṣyandatvād viparyāsapratipakṣālambanatvāc ca pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāva ity ucyate 
so'rthaḥ kalpitasvabhāvasya bhavati na tu parikalpitaḥ 
ataḥ sadasattā pariniṣpanna ityuktam ityapare 
anye tv āhuḥ  sadasattā'viparyastatvāt pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāva ukta iti 
aviparyāsena parikalpitas tasyāvidyamānena dvayarūpeṇa prakhyāti lakṣaṇāt 
āśrayeṇa paratas tasyābhidhānaṃ 
hetutvād āśraya ity ucyate phalatvāt paratantra iti 
etad eva svabhāvatrayam ālambanato jñeyaṃ 
avikalpanata ityatra vigrahabhedād āha  yena ca vikalpayati nirvikalpena jñānena yac ca na vikalpayati prakṛtiprabhāsvaratāṃ 
tatrārya vigrahabhedaḥ  na vikalpayatyanenetyavikalpanaṃ na vikalpyate tadityavikalpanaṃ 
tad bhāvo'vikalpanatā 
evam avikalpanatā dvābhyāṃ vajrapadābhyāṃ paridīpiteti darśayati 
tad anena jñeyajñānavyavasthānaṃ yathākramaṃ veditavyaṃ yad uta tribhiḥ svabhāvair avikalpanatayā ceti 
tatra tribhiḥ svabhāvair jñeyavyavasthānaṃ grāhyatvāt 
avikalpanatayā jñānavyavasthānaṃ grāhakatvāt 
codyaparihārata upayuktebhyaḥ śiṣṭāni vajrapadāni 
atra kiñcid vajrapradaṃ codyasya parihāra eva 
tadyathā māyopamatā ākāśopamatā ahīnāviśiṣṭatā ceti 
  kiñcit punaścodyam eva 
tadyathā saṃkleśo vyavadānam iti 
tasmācodyaparihāraś ca codyasya parihāraś ca codyaparihārau asarūpaikaśeṣaṃ kṛtvā 
tatra codyaṃ yadyete parikalpitaparatantralakṣaṇā dharmā na saṃvidyante grāhyagrāhakatveneti vākyaśeṣaḥ 
katham upalabhyante grāhyagrāhakatvenetyabhiprāyaḥ 
ata saṃvidyante dharmāṇāṃ prakṛtiprabhāsvaratā na yujyate grāhyagrāhakatvātmanā vidyamānatvāt 
etac codyaṃ 
tanmāyopamatayā pariharati 
yathā māyākṛtaṃ na saṃvidyata upalabhyate ceti 
na hi māyopalabhyatayā saṃvidyate tato'pyevaṃ saṃvidyata iti jñātuṃ śakyate 
yadi parkṛtiprabhāsvaratā dharmāṇāṃ tat kathaṃ pūrvaṃ saṃkleśaḥ paścād vyavadānam iti codyaṃ 
nahi prakṛti viśuddhe kadācid saṃkliṣṭatopapadyate 
asya parihāraḥ sankleśavyavadānam ākāśopamatayā veditavyaṃ 
yathā ākāśaṃ prakṛtipariśuddham āgantukenopakleśenasaṃkliśyate tad apagamād vyavadīyate ceti 
evaṃ dharmadhātoḥ prakṛtiviśuddhatvepyāgantukair upakleśaiḥ saṃkleśaḥ 
tad apagamāc ca vyavadānam iti yadyaprameyabuddhotpāde satyaprameyāṇāṃ sattvānāṃ kleśapraśamastat kathamanādisaṃsāre pratyekasyāpi buddhotpādasyāprameyāṇāṃ satvānaṃ saṃsārāpagamān nirvāṇapraveśāc ca na saṃsārasamucchedo na nirvāṇavṛddhri veti codyaṃ 
asyāhīnāviśiṣtatayā parihāraḥ 
aprameyatvāt sattvadhātor vyavadānapakṣasya ceti 
parimāṇavato hi vastuno hāniḥ samucchedo vā prajñāyate aprameyaś ca sattvadhātuḥ 
tasya hānir api na prajñāte kuta eva samucchedaḥ prajñāsyeta ākāśavat 
vyavadānasyāpyaprameyatvād viśeṣa eva nāsti tasya kathaṃ vṛddhir bhaviṣyati ākāśavat 
tasyāvaraṇāpagād āvaraṇābhāvāc ceti 
dvitīyaṃ śarīravyavasthānam iti vajrapadānām ity adhikṛtaṃ 
yatra yā ca yato bhrāntir abhrāntir yā ca yatra ca 
bhrāntyabhrāntiphale caiva paryantaś ca tayor iti 
vajrapadair bhrāntiviṣayo bhrāntisvarūpatā bhrāntihetur bhrāntiphalaṃ bhrāntiparyantaśca nirdiṣṭaḥ 
tathā'bhrāntisvarūpam abhrāntiviṣayo'bhrāntiphalaṃ tatparyantaś ceti 
tatra yatra bhrāntir iti sadasattāyāṃ vyañjanānāṃ sārthakatvanirarthakatvalakṣaṇāyām abhidhānābhidheyayos tat sambandhasya ca bhāvasvarūpeṇa parikalpitatvāt 
yā ca bhrāntir iti viparyāso bhrāntiḥ 
svātmanyavidyamānena dvayākāreṇa prakhyānāt 
yato bhrāntir ityāśrayād bhrāntir āśrayaḥ punar jalpaparibhāvito manaskāra ālayavijñānātmakaḥ 
abhrāntir yā ceti māyādivad arthataḥ sadasattāvisāro'bhrāntiḥ 
bhāvābhāvābhiniveśabhrāntipratipakṣaś cābhrāntiḥ 
sā yathākramaṃ māyopamatayā'vikalpanatā ca nirdiṣṭā 
yatra ceti yatra ca  sā'bhrāntiḥ 
sā punaḥ prakṛtiprabhāsvaratāyāṃ pariniṣpannasvabhāvalakṣaṇāyāṃ 
bhrāntyabhrāntiphale caiveti tatra bhrāntiphalaṃ hi sankleśaḥ 
bhrāntiniṣyanda iti vākyaśeṣaḥ 
abhrāntiniṣyandānāyā bhrānter abhrāntiphalatvāt 
abhrāntiphalaṃ vyavadānaṃ sasamprayogam iti vākyaśeṣaḥ 
evakārakaraṇaṃ tat phale sankleśo vyavadānam ityanenaivokte ākāśopamatayā tu paśyati dharmadhātor yasya bhrāntyabhrāntiphalaṃ tat sankleśavyavadānātmakaṃ 
nedaṃ tat prakṛtikam iti pradarśanārthaṃ 
paryantaś ca tayor iti sankleśavyavadānayoḥ paryanto nirvāṇaṃ 
taccahīnānadhikatvena paryantam uktam ityeke 
anye tvāhuḥ  saṃsārasyāprameyatayā'pacayābhāvād ahīnatāyuktaḥ sankleśaparyantaḥ 
nirvāṇasyāprameyatayopacayābhāvād aviśiṣṭatāyukto vyavadānaparyanta iti 
etāni daśa vajrapadāny aviparyāsaprasangadvāreṇoktāni 
na tu sūtritānītyatas tānyantaraślokābhyāṃ sangṛhītāni  sadasattā'viparyāsa āśrayo māyayopamā 
akalpanā prakṛtyā ca bhāsvaratvaṃ sadaiva hi 
 saṃkleśo vyavadānañca ākāśopamatā tathā 
ahīnatvādhikatvañca daśa vajrapadāni hi 
atra ca pariniṣpannaśabdārthasambandhadarśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ 
yathā pratyavabhāsate tathā 'rthānāṃ svabhāvasattādarśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ 
tad arthapravṛttikāraṇadarśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ 
arthasamāropāpavādadarśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ 
yathānām arthasvabhāvadarśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ 
bhāvānāṃ svasāmānyalakṣaṇayor vastutvena darśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ 
svastyasvastisañcārād viśuddhir aviśuddhiśceti darśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ 
ekasyaivāśuddhiviśuddhidarśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ 
sankleśavyavadānaprahāṇapratilambhayor hāniviśeṣadarśanāt trāsamānapravṛttir viparyāsaḥ 
ityete daśa viparyāsāḥ 
bodhisattvasya tad abhāvādaviparyāsāvasthitasya yathokteṣvartheṣvariṇatā vidarśanā bhāvanā veditavyā 
uktā'nudharmapratipattiḥ 
  antadvayavarjane pratipattiḥ   anudharmapratipattyantaram antadvayavarjane pratipattir vaktavyetyataḥ pṛcchati  antadvayavarjane pratipattiḥ katametyata āha  yā ratnakūṭe nāmadharmaparyāyeṇa samyak pratipatteḥ svabhāvapratipādanārthaṃ madhyamā pratipadupadiṣṭā 
tadyathā  kāśyapa iha mahāratnakūṭe dharmaparyāye śikṣitukāmena bodhisattvena yoniśodharmaprayuktena bhavitavyaṃ 
katamaśca yoniśodharmaprayogaḥ  yaduta  sarvadharmāṇāṃ bhūtapratyavekṣā 
yā nātmapratyavekṣā na sattvanajīvanapoṣanapudgalanamanujanamānavapratyavekṣā 
iyam ucyate kāśyapa madhyamā  pratipaditi vistareṇa yāvad dvitīyapradīpodāharaṇaparyantaḥ paṭhyate 
kasyāntasya varjanādasau veditavyā  katam asyāntasya varjanān madhyamā pratipatter jñātavyetyarthaḥ 
ata āha  pṛthaktvaikatvam antaś ca tīrthyaśrāvakayor api 
iti vistaraḥ 
ayaṃ pañcadaśavidho'ntadvayabhedaḥ 
asya varjanāt sā veditavyā 
atra pṛthagādidarśanamantaḥ 
ekaikapakṣābhiniviṣṭatvāt kārye kāraṇopacāraṃ kṛtvā 
tatra rūpādibhyaḥ pṛthaktvam ātmana ityantaḥ ekatvam ityantaḥ 
tatra ye rūpādīn sknadhānāyatanāni dhātūṃś ca nityātmana upabhogavastutvena kalpayanti tad rūpādibhyaḥ pṛthaktvamātmana ityantaḥ 
ye punar ādhyātmikān saṃskārān rūpādīnām ātmatvena pratipannā yaḥ paśyati śṛṇoti jānāti sa ātmeti bāhyāṃścātmīyatvena kalpayanti tad rūpādibhya ekatvam ātmana ityantaḥ yat sūtryate  sa jīvas taccharīram anyo jīvo'nyaccharīram iti darśanaṃ tadevātrāntaśabdenoktaṃ 
tat parivarjanārtham iti rūpādibhyas tattvānyatvāntaparivarjanārtham ātmanaḥ 
madhyamā pratipad yad dharmātraṃ viṣayabhūtaṃ jñānaṃ 
etad eva pradarśayann āha  yā nātmapratyavekṣā yāvannamānapratyavekṣeti dharmamātradarśanāddhi vandhyāpurtravad ātmā nāstītyavagacchan nātmānaṃ pratyavekṣate nānusaratītyarthaḥ 
kuta eva tasya rūpādibhyas tattvam anyatvaṃ vā gṛhyata iti  ātmaśabdenaiva tadarthe'vagamyamāne kimarthaṃ sattvādiparyāyaviśeṣābhidhānaṃ  na sarvasya sarvaparyāyavyutpattir ityataḥ sarveṣāṃ tadarthāvabodhārthaṃ paryāyāntaranirdeśaḥ 
tat kālavikṣiptānāṃ vā paryāyāntareṇa tadarthaprāpaṇārthaḥ 
tenaivābhidhānenocyamāne'nyeṣāṃ prāpaṇāt 
nityaṃ rūpam iti tīrthikāntaḥ 
te hi parikalpitarūpān vastutvenābhiniveśya nityatvena kalpayanti nityaviparyāsopahatatvāt 
anityam iti śrāvakāntaḥ 
tair api kalpitasvabhāvānāṃ rūpādīnāṃ vasturūpeṇānityatvena samāropaṇādantatvaṃ 
atyantasaṃsārodvegakarān nirvāṇasya cāntapātanād anityadarśnasyāntatvaṃ tad ubhayaparivarjanārtham iti nityānityadarśanaparivarjanārthaṃ madhyamā pratipad yā rūpādīnāṃ nanityapratyavekṣā nānityapratyavekṣeti 
tat punaḥ kiṃ 
nirvikalpajñānaṃ 
yan na rūpādīn rūpādiṣv eva nityatvenānityatvena cānugacchati 
rūpādīnām ityādiśabdena vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskāravijñānaskandhānāṃ pṛthivyaptejovāyvākāśadhātūnāṃ cakṣuḥśrotraghrāṇajihvākāyamanaāyatanānāṃ ca grahaṇaṃ 
  ātmeti śabdena pudgalasamāropānta iti skandhadhātvāyatana vyatiriktam avyatiriktaṃ vā vandhyāputravad asantam ātmānaṃ dravyataḥ paśyataḥ pudgalasyātmano vasturūpasamāropaṇam antaḥ 
nairātmyam ityapavādāntaḥ 
apavādo hi sato'sattva parikalpa ityuktaḥ 
ātmanastv asattvāt kathaṃ nairātmyam ity apavādānta āpadyata ityata āha  prajñaptisato'pyapavādāt nairātmyam apavādānta iti sambadhyate 
sa punar dharmāṇāṃ santāno yasmin hetuphalasambandhaḥ prajñāyate 
samudayo vā yatra devamanuṣyaprajñaptiḥ 
tat parivarjanārthaṃ madhyamā pratipad ityātmanaḥ sadasattādarśanaparivarjanārthaṃ 
tasyāḥ punar yasyā madhyamāyāḥ pratipado nirūpaṇārtham āha  yadātmanairātmyayor madhyamam iti 
kiṃ punas tan madhyaṃ 
nirvikalpaṃ jñānaṃ 
grāhyārthavikalpasyāntatvaṃ darśayitvā grāhakārthavikalpasyāntatvapradarśanārtham āha  bhūtaṃ cittam ityādi 
athavā pudgalasya samāropāpavādāntatvaṃ darśayitvā dharmasya samāropāpavādāntadarśanārtham āha  bhūtaṃ cittam ityādi 
yathā pratibhāsate yathā vā'bhilapyate cittaṃ tathaiva bhūtaṃ vidyata iti ayaṃ dharmasamāropāntaḥ abhūtasya cittasvabhāvabhūtatvena samāropāt 
abhūtaṃ cittam ityapavādāntaḥ 
tasya hi grāhyagrāhakarahitātmanā nirabhilāpyena ca vidyamānam apyabhūtam iti paśyataḥ sarvātmanā dharmasvabhāvāpavādād apavādāntaḥ 
tat parivarjanārtham iti samāropāpavādarahitasya dharmanairātmyasya pravitedhārthaṃ madhyamā pratipad 
sā yatra nacittaṃ na cetanā na mano na vijñānam iti 
abhiniveśā na pravartanta iti vākyaśeṣaḥ 
yatra vā viṣaye na cittaṃ sāsravavāsanābhiścittātmakaṃ pravartate na cetanā'bhisaṃskāralakṣaṇā na mano manyanākāraṃ na vijñānañca vikalpanam iyaṃ madhyamā pratipad ityucyate 
tatra cittam ālayavijñānaṃ sarvasrāvadharmavāsanābhiścittatvāt 
cetanā manaskarma kuśalākuśalāvyākṛteṣu cittapreraṇakarmikā 
manaḥ kliṣṭaṃ manaḥ 
vijñānaṃ ṣaḍvijñānakāyāḥ 
akuśalādayo dharmāḥ saṃkleśa iti vipakṣāntaḥ 
kuśalādayo vyavadānam iti  pratipakṣāntaḥ 
ādiśabdena sāvadyaanavadyalaukikalokottarasāsravānāsravasaṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtādayo nirdeśāḥ sambadhyante 
tatra yathaivākuśalāḥ kuśalāś ca dharmāḥ pratibhāsante'bhilapyante ca tathaiva saṃkleśo vyavadānañceti darśanaṃ vipakṣāntaḥ pratipakṣāntaś ca 
tatrā'kuśalā akṣemārthatvāt 
sāvadyā duścaritasamutthāpakatvāt 
laukikā viparyastatvāt 
sāsravā āsravānuśayitatvāt 
saṃskṛtāḥ pratyayotpāditvāt 
tad viparītās tu kuśalādayo veditavyāḥ 
tat parivarjanārthaṃ madhyamā pratipad iti 
vipakṣapratipakṣayors tacchavdenābhisambandhaḥ 
na madhyamā'tra pratipaj jñāyata ityata āha  yo'syāntadvayasyā'nupagamo'nudāhāro'pravyāhāra iti 
tatrā'nupagamo vipakṣapratipakṣayor anabhiniveśaḥ 
anudāhāras tasmin vipakṣapratipakṣānte pareṣām asamādāpanāt 
apravyāhāro vipakṣapratipakṣāntayor asaṃvarṇanāt 
tīrthikaśrāvakāntapratipakṣeṇa madhyamāṃ pratipadaṃ deśayitvā bodhisattvāntapratipakṣeṇa madhyamāṃ pratipadaṃ pratipādayann āha  astīti śāśvatāntaḥ nāstītyucchedāntaḥ tayor eva pudgaladharmayoḥ 
sarvadā svalakṣaṇasamārupād astīti śāśvatāntaḥ 
sarvathā svarūpāpavādān nāstītyucchedāntaḥ 
tat parivarjanārthaṃ madhyamā pratipad yad anayor antayor madhyamiti
ubhayāntavigamo'tra madhyamabhipretamityeke 
ubhaya lakṣanamatra dvayorantayo madhyamityapare 
kathaṃ kṛtvā  yo'hyabhūtaparikalpavad dharmadhātuvadvā jñeyamn abhidheyaṃ ca vastu dravyataḥ paramārthataścāstītyabhiniveśaḥ sa śāśvatāntaḥ 
tasya tahā'sattvāt 
tadvā śaśaviṣāṇavan nāstyeveti darśanam ucchedāntaḥ 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  tasya prajñaptito'stitvāt 
atas tan nirākaraṇenocchedānta ucyate 
ataścāstitva nāstitvayor madhyaṃ dravyaḥ paramārthaś ca nasti prajñaptito'stītyubhayalakṣaṇaṃ bhavati 
vipakṣapratipakṣayoḥ samāropāntam adhikṛtyāha  avidyā grāhyā grāhakā cetyantaḥ 
evaṃ vidyā saṃskārā asaṃskṛtañca tat pratipakṣo grāhyaṃ grāhyakañcetyantaḥ 
atra ca yāvaj jarāmaraṇam iti paryantagrahāṇād vijñānanāmarūpādayo'dhyākṣipyante 
vijñānaṃ grāhyaṃ grāhakañcetyantaḥ 
evaṃ nāmarūpaṃ ṣaḍāyatanaṃ sparśo vedanā tṛṣṇā upādānaṃ bhavo jātijarāmaraṇaṃ grāhyaṃ grāhakañcetyantaḥ 
tatrā'vidyā satyaratnāsaṃprakyānātmikā 
punyā punyānijñjasvabhāva cetanā sa punarbhāvabhisaṃskaraṇāt saṃskārāḥ 
evaṃ saṃkleśalakṣaṇavyākhyānānusāreṇa vijñānādayo'pi vistareṇa vaktavyāḥ 
vidyā'nāsravaṃ jñānaṃ 
saṃskārāṇāṃ jñānamevā'saṃskṛtaṃ pratipakṣaḥ 
atha vā'nyasmād asaṃskṛtād  vyavacchedārtham āha  tat pratipakṣa iti 
anye tv anutpattimatvād asaṃskṛtam aṣṭavidham apyatra manyante 
pratipakṣastvanāsravā cetanā punar bhāvanabhisaṃskaraṇād iti 
tan nirodho grāhyo grāhako vetyantaḥ 
tac chabdena vijñānādayo jarāmaraṇaparyavasānāḥ sambadhyante 
nirodho na vijñāyate kiṃ bhāvaḥ kāraṇaṃ vetyāha  yena tan nāmarūpaṃ nirudhyata iti 
kena punas tan nāmarūpaṃ nirudhyate 
nāmarūpapratipakṣeṇā'nāsraveṇa mārgeṇa 
vidyā cā'vidyā cādvayam etad advaidhīkāram ityetad evātra jñānaṃ saparivāraṃ mārgaḥ 
ataś ca nirudhyate'neneti nirodhaḥ 
kaḥ punar atrāntaḥ 
ayam eva grāhyagrāhakābhiniveśaḥ 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  advayaprakṛtiṣv avidyādiṣv avidyamānadvayādhyāropapravṛttavāt 
evaṃ grāhyagrāhakānto dvidhā  kṛṣṇaśuklapakṣabhedeneti 
tatra kṛṣṇapakṣe dvādaśabhavāngāni avidyā yāvaj jarāmaraṇaṃ 
evaṃ śuklapakṣe'pyvidhyādinirodhabhedena dvādaśaprakāra evāvidhyānirodho yāvaj jarāmaraṇanirodha iti 
atra ca nirydhyante'enā'vidyādaya iti tat pratipakṣabhūto mārga eva nirodhaśabdenoktaḥ 
tat parivarjanārtham iti grāhyagrāhakāntaparivarjanārthaṃ madhyamāpratipad uktyabhisambadhyate 
sā ca na vijñāyata ityata āha  vidyā cā'vidyā cādvayam etad iti 
kathaṃ vidyā cāvidyā ca yāvaj jarāmaraṇaṃ tan nirodhaścā'dvayam ityata āha  vidyāvidyādīnāṃ grāhyagrāhakatvābhāvād iti 
tad abhāvastv avidyādīnām advayaprakṛtitvāt 
athavā vidyā'vidyeti parikalpitasvabhāvo'taś ca parikalpitasvabhāvayor vidyā'vidyayorabhāvasamatayā vidyā cā'vidyā cādvayam iti 
evaṃ saṃskārāṇām asaṃskṛtasya ca vijñānasya tan nirodhasya ca yāvaj jarāmaraṇasya tannirodhasya ceti vaktavyaḥ 
kā punar atra madhyamā pratipat 
etad eva jñānaṃ vidyā cāvidyā cādvayam etadavaidhīkāram iti na vidyotpādayitavyā nā'vidyā nirodhayitavyā 
na saṃskārādayaḥ praheyāḥ 
na tannirodhaḥ prāptavya iti yadevaṃ jñānam etadavaidhīkāraṃ 
  trividhaḥ sankleśa iti 
tatra kleśaḥ karmajanmasaṃkleśanimittatvāt svayañca kliṣṭatvāt svaparātmanor vyābādhahetutvād vā saṃkleśa ucyate 
karmāpi kleśādhipatyanirvṛttatvāj janmahetutvāt svayam api ca kasyacit kliṣṭatvāt saṃkleśa ucyate 
janmāpi karmakleśanimittatvāt sarvopadravāspadabhūtatvāc ca saṃkleśaḥ 
punaḥ kleśasankleśasya tridhā bhedapradarśanārtham āha  kleśasankleśastrividha iti vistaraḥ 
tatra dṛṣṭayaḥ pañca satkāyadṛṣṭyādikāḥ 
rāgadveṣamohā eva nimittaṃ śokādihetutvāt punar bhavahetutvāc ca 
anye tvāhuḥ  rāgādīnāṃ nimittaṃ tad anukūlā indriyārthāḥ ayoniśo manaskāraḥ rāgādivāsanā ālayavijñānasanniviṣṭā 
evantu varṇayanti  rāgādinimittaṃ tadābhāsa iti 
punar bhavapraṇidhānaṃ punar bhavaprārthanā 
yasya pratipakṣo jñānaśūnyateti vistaraḥ 
tatra dṛṣṭānāṃ jñānaśūnyatā pratipakṣaḥ 
śūnyatāviṣayaṃ jñānamātra jñānaśūnyatā 
rāgādinimittapratipakṣo jñānā'nimittaṃ sarvanimittavigamāt 
animittaviṣayaṃ vā jñānam jñānānimittaṃ 
parikalpitarāgādiśūnyatāviṣayatvāt punarbhavapraṇidhānapratipakṣo jñānāpraṇihitaṃ 
punarbhavapraṇidhānavigataṃ punarbhavaśūnyatāviṣayaṃ vā jñānaṃ jñānapraṇihitaṃ 
karmasankleśaḥ śubhāśubhakarmābhisaṃskāraḥ punarbhavākṣepakayoḥ śubhāśubhayoḥ karmaṇor upacayo'bhinirvṛttir abhisaṃskāraḥ 
yasya pratipakṣo jñānā'nabhisaṃskāraḥ 
yena jñānena karma punarbhavann asya nā'bhisaṃskaroti taj jñānaṃ jñānābhisaṃskāraḥ 
tat punasthathatāviṣayaṃ 
janmasankleśaḥ punarbhavajātiḥ pratisandhicittaṃ 
jātasya cittacaittānāṃ pratikṣaṇotpādaḥ pratisandhibandhād ūrdhvam āmaraṇāt 
punarbhavaprabandha iti kleśasahito maraṇabhavaḥ 
tasmād anantaram antarbhāvaḥ 
tataś ca punarpyupapattibhavaḥ 
ārūpyasamāpattilābhinantu maraṇabhavād evānantaram upapattibhāvaḥ 
yasya pratipakṣo jñānā'jātir jñānānutpādo jñānāsvabhāvatā ca 
tatrājātāḥ sarvadharmāḥ prikalpitātmktveneti yaj jñanaṃ śunyatāviṣayaṃ vā taj jñānajātiḥ 
parikalpitadharmaśūnyatāviṣayaṃ jñanaṃ jṇanutpādaḥ tena tadanutpādprativedāt 
vandhyāputravad asattvād asvabhāvo bhāvaprabandha iti yaj jñānaṃ taj jñānāsvabhāvatā 
etaj jñānaśūnyatādikaṃ saptavidhajñānaṃ yathoktasya saptavidhasya dṛṣṭyādivipakṣasya pratipakṣaḥ 
etasyaiva trividhasya kleśakarmajanmasankleśasya saptadhābhinnasyā'pagamo vyavadānaṃ 
apagamaḥ prahāṇaṃ 
anye tu manyante tathatā mārgo nirvāṇañca vyavadānaṃ 
apagacchatyasminn anevāpagatiścetyevaṃ vigrahabhedāt tathatādayo vyavadānam iti 
tatra jñānaśūnyatādibhir iti ādiśabdāj jñānaśūnyatā jñānānimittaṃ jñānāpraṇihitaṃ jñānābhisaṃskāro jñānājātir jñānānutpādo jñānāsvabhāvatā ca parigṛhyante 
jñeyaśūnyatādayo dharmā iti 
atrāpyādiśabdena jñeyaśūnyatā jñeyanimittaṃ jñeyānabhisaṃskāro jñeyājātir jñeyānutpādo jñeyāsvabhāvatā ca pariniṣpannalakṣaṇāḥ parigṛhyante 
etena trividhena sankleśena yathāyogaṃ yāvan na śūnyatādayaḥ kriyanta iti 
anantaroktena  kleśakarmajanmasaṃkleśena pṛthagbhūtajñeyaśūnyatādayo dharmā jñānaśūnyatādibhir na kriyante 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ na kriyante 
yasmāt te prakṛtyaiva śūnyatādaya iti 
prakṛtyaivā'dṛṣṭyādisvabhāvā ityarthaḥ 
kuta etat  ata āha  dharmadhātoḥ prakṛtyasaṃkliṣṭatvāt 
ato jñeyaśūnyatādayo dharmāḥ prakṛtyaiva śūnyatādaya iti jñānaśūnyatādibhir na kriyante 
yathāyogam ityayam atra yathāyogārthaḥ 
jñānaśūnyatayā jñeyaśūnyatā dṛṣṭisaṃkleśena vimuktā virahitā na kriyante dṛṣṭiśūnyatāyāḥ svayam evādṛṣṭisvabhāvatvāt 
evaṃ jñānānimittena jñeyānimittaṃ rāgādinimittair virahitaṃ na kriyate rāgādinimittaiḥ śūnyatāyāḥ svayam evānimittatvāt 
jñānāpraṇihitena jñeyāpraṇihitaṃ na kriyate praṇidhānaśūnyatāyāḥ prakṛtyaivāpraṇidhānalakṣaṇatvāt 
jñānānabhisaṃskāreṇa jñeyānabhisaṃskāro na kriyate abhisaṃskāraśūnyatāyāḥ prakṛtyaivānabhisaṃskāralakṣaṇatvāt 
jñānājāthyā jñeyajātirṇaṃ kriyate jātiśūnyatāyāḥ prakṛutyai vā jāti lakṣaṇatvāt 
jñānānutpādena kriyānutpādo na kriyate cittacaittapratikṣaṇotpādaśūnyatāyāḥ prakṛtyaivānutpādalakṣaṇatvāt 
jñānasvabhāvatayā jñeyāsvabhāvatā na kriyate punarbhavaśūnyatāyāḥ prakṛtyaivāsvabhāvatvāt 
athavā trividhena saṃkleśena yathāyogam iti vistaraḥ 
kleśakarmajanmasaṃkleśena saptadhābhinnena jñeyaśūnyatādīnāṃ dharmāṇāṃ yasya dharmasya yena saṃkleśabhedena yogaḥ sa dharmo na jñānaśūnyatādibhiḥ kriyate kiṃ tarhyadhigamyate 
tatra dṛṣṭisaṃkleśena jñānaśūnyatāyogaḥ evaṃ yāvat punarbhavaprabandhena jñānāsvabhāvatāyogaḥ 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ na kriyate  yasmāt te prakṛtyaiva śūnyatādayo dharmā dharmadhātoḥ prakṛtyaivāsaṃkliṣṭatvād iti 
tatra dṛṣṭayo na jñānaśūnyatayā śūnyāḥ kriyante tāsāṃ prakṛtyaiva śūnyatā lakṣaṇatvāt 
rāgādinimittaṃ jñānānimittena nānanimittaṃ kriyate dharmadhātoḥ prakṛtyaivānimittatvāt 
evaṃ yāvat punar bhavaprabandho jñānāsvabhāvatayā nāsvabhāvaḥ kriyate yato'nutpanne'pi pratipakṣe parikalpitaḥ svabhāvo'sanneva 
yataścaitad evam ato yadi dharmadhātuḥ saṃkliśyate vā viśuddhyate veti kalpayatyam antaḥ 
kiṃ kāraṇam ityato bravīti  prakṛtyasaṃkliṣṭasya saṃkleśaśuddhyabhāvād ākāśavad iti 
etasyāntasya parivarjanārthaṃ madhyamāpratipad yan na śūnyatāyā vidyātmikāyā dharmānajñeyaśūnyatādīn pariniṣpannasvabhāvātmakaṃ tad vipakṣeṇa paratantrasvabhāvena dṛṣṭyādikena śūnyān virahitān karoti 
api tv anutpannāyām api vidyāyāṃ parikalpitena svabhāvena dṛṣṭisvarūpeṇa dharmā eva śūnyāḥ 
evaṃ yannānimittena dharmānanimittān karoti dharmā evānimittāḥ yāvadyannāsvabhāvatayā dharmānasvabhāvān karoti dharmā evāsvabhāvā iti 
yaivaṃ pratyavekṣā iyam ucyate kāśyapa dharmāṇāṃ bhūtapratyavekṣeti 
evaṃ vidyāstitvaṃ tad vipakṣāstitvāṃ ca parikalpitasvabhāvavigataṃ paridīpayann adhyāropāpavādāntapratikṣepaḥ kṛto bhavati 
  yo'yam anukrānto vikalpaprabhedastasmād ayam aparaḥ saptavidho vikalpadvayāntaḥ 
vikalpaprabhedapradarśanārtham āha  tadyathā bhāve'pi vikalpo'ntaḥ abhāve'pi vikalpo'nta iti 
katham ityato bravīti  pudgalo'sti yasya vināśāya śūnyatā nairātmyam api vā nāstīti vikalpanāt 
yadi śūnyatayā dharmān prakṛtiśūnyatvān na śūnyān karoti tena tarhi pudgalo'sti yasya vināśāya śūnyatā 
nairātmyam api vā nāsti pudgalābhāvāt 
na hi pratipakṣo nirvipakṣo'sti 
tasmād avaśyaṃ pudgalāstitvaṃ vā nairātmyaṃ bhāvo vā pratipattavya iti 
tadbhāvābhāve vikalpo'ntaḥ 
etasya bhāvābhāvavikalpadvayāntasya parivarjanārtham iyaṃ madhyamā pratipat 
na khalu punaḥ kāśyapa pudgalavināśāya śūnyatā 
api tu śūnyataiva śūnyeti vistareṇa sūtrapāṭhaḥ 
tatra na sankliṣṭa pudugalavināśāya na oyavadānpudgalothpādāya śūnyatā senādivatprajñaptisatvāt pudgalasyotpādavināśābhāvād api tu śūnyataiva śūnyā na tu pudgalena satkāyadṛṣṭisamāropitena tasyātyantam asattvāt 
evañca kṛtvā pudgaladharmātmanā na bhāvaḥ śūunyatā tad rahitatvāt 
pariniṣpannena nābhāvaḥ tac ca śūnyatāyāḥ pariniṣpannātmakatvaṃ pratipādayann āha  pūrvāntaśūnyatā aparāntaśūnyatā pratyutpannaśūnyateti kālatraye'pi tathaivāstitvapratipādanāt 
athavā pṛthagjanāśaikṣaśaikṣāvasthāsu tathaivāstitvapratipādanāt 
tatra pṛthagjanāvasthā pūrvāntaḥ aśaikṣāvasthā'parāntaḥ śaikṣāvasthā pratyutpanna iti 
yasmāc caivaṃ bhāvābhāvasvabhāvaśūnyatā tasmād āha  śūnyatāṃ kāśyapa pratisarateti nirvikalpajñānaviṣayatvāt na pudgalam ityabhidhānamātratvād iti 
  śāmye'pi vikalpo'ntaḥ śamane'pi vikalpo'nta ityanuvartate 
katham ityata āha  praheyaprahāṇakalpanayā śūnyatāyās trasanāditi 
tatra śāmyaṃ praheyaṃ praśamanaṃ prahāṇaṃ 
dharmān praheyatvena śūunyatāñca prahāṇatvena kalpayitvā śūnyatāyāmuttrāso jāyate 
kathaṃ  trividho hi sankleśaḥ praheyaḥ 
sa yadi prakṛtiśūnyaḥ tataḥ pudgalavan na praheyaḥ syāt 
tataś ca praheyābhāvāt prahāṇābhāva iti śūnyatāyām uttrāso jāyate 
ayam apyanta eva 
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  rūpavedanādayo hi dharmā yathaiva vijñānātmani viparivartante tathaiva te dravyataḥ santītyabhiniviṣṭāḥ teṣāṃ kalpitarūpāṇāṃ rūpādīnām ātmavat prakṛtyaivāsattvam ajānānās tacchūnyatāyā bibhyati 
tasmād etasya vikalpadvayāntasya parivarjanārtham ākāśadṛṣṭāntaḥ 
tadyathā  kāśyapa kaścid eva puruṣa ākāśajo bhītaḥ sorastāḍaṃ krandedevañca vaded apanayatadākāśam iti 
takiṃ manyase kāśyapa śakyam ākāśam apanetuṃ  āha  no hīdaṃ bhagavan 
bhagavān āha  evam eva kāśyapa ete śramaṇabrāhmaṇāḥ śūnyatāyām utttrasanti tān ahaṃ mahāvikṣepaprāptānīti vadāmi 
tat kasmād hetoḥ  śūnyatāyām eva hi te kāśyapa vicaranti tasyā eva bibhyantīti 
etad uktaṃ bhavati  yathākāśaṃ sarvarūpānugatatvād apanetum aśakyam evaṃ sarvadharmeṣu sarvakālaṃ śūnyatā vyavasthitetyapanetuṃ na śakyate 
na ca dharmaprahāṇena śūnyatā vyavasthāpayitum ataścāyam asthānasaṃtrāsa iti darśayati 
trāsye'pi kalpo'ntaḥ tataś ca trāsyād bhaye'pi 
kiṃ  vikalpo'nta ityadhikṛtaṃ 
yatastrāsaḥ sambhavati tat trāsyam ucyate 
bhīyate'smād iti bhayaṃ 
tasmād yad aniṣṭaphalaṃ tasmin strāsye tasmiṃśca bhaye yo vikalpayati so'ntaḥ 
katham ityato bravīti  parikalpitarūpāditrasanāt duḥkhabhīrutayeti 
bālā hi parikalpitarūpādīn vastutaḥ kalpayitvā tebhyo bhayam aniṣṭaṃ phalaṃ ca kalpayanti 
tataśca duḥkhabhīrutayā tebhyo rūpādibhyas tan nimittebhyaś ca bhayāt trasantīti 
etasya vikalpadvayāntasya parivarjanārthaṃ  citrakaradṛṣṭāntaḥ 
tadyathā  kāśyapa citrakaraḥ svayam eva bhīṣaṇaṃ yakṣarūpaṃ kṛtvā tasmād eva bhītasrasto'dhomukho nipatya sammohaṃ nigacchet 
evam eva kāśyapa sarvabālapṛthagjanāḥ svayam eva rūpaśabdagandharasasparśān kṛtvā tebhyaḥ saṃsāre bhrāmyanti na ca tān dharmān yathābhūtaṃ prajānantīti 
yathā ca citrakaraḥ svayaṃkṛte bhīṣaṇake yakṣarūpe mithyāvikalpena bhūtayakṣabhāvam adhyāropya tasmād bhītaḥ sammoham āpadyate 
evaṃ sarva eva bālā mithyāvikalpaprasrutāḥ svayaṃ kṛtair iti vikalpitaiḥ saṃsāre bhrāmyante kṣaṇāvasthānikāyasabhāgānavasthitatvāt 
pūrvako dṛṣṭāntaḥ śrāvakānadhikṛtyāyantu bodhisattvān iti 
śrāvako hi śūnyatāyām akṛtaparicayatvāc chūnyatāyās trasyati 
bodhisattvas tu parikalpitadharmavikalpena saṃkliśyate vikalpakleśatvādityeke 
nānayor arthaviśeṣo'styapi tu vargadvayavaśād dvayābhidhānam ityanye 
śrāvakaḥ śūnyatātrāsādadhigantavyaṃ nādhigacchati bodhisattvaḥ punar vikalpitadharmatrāsād ityapare 
pūrvaka ātmagrāhapratipakṣeṇa ayaṃ punar dharmagrāhapratipakṣeṇeti kecit 
 grāhye'pi vikalpo'nto grāhake'pi 
vikalpo'ntaḥ ityadhikṛtaṃ 
katham ete grāhyarūpādayas tad grāhakāśca vijñānakāyāḥ svalakṣaṇataḥ kāryataś ca gṛhyamāṇā ātmādivad adhyāropitātmāno bhaviṣyantītyevaṃ grāhyagrāhakayor vastutaḥ parikalpo'nto'bhipretaḥ 
etasya  vikalpadvayāntasya parivarjanārthaṃ māyākāradṛṣṭāntaḥ t tadyathā kāśyapa māyākāraḥ puruṣo māyākṛtaṃ nirmimīti 
atha sa māyānirmitas tameva māyākāraṃ khādet 
evam eva kāśyapa yogācāro bhikṣur yadyadevārambaṇaṃ manaskaroti tat sarvam asya riktam eva khyātīti vistaraḥ 
katham anenaivaṃ vidhaṃ vikalpadvayāntaṃ parivarjayantīti  ata āha  vijñaptimātrajñānakṛtaṃ hy arthābhāvajñānaṃ 
tac cārthābhāvajñānaṃ tadeva vijñaptimātrajñānaṃ nivartayati 
arthābhāve vijñaptyasambhavād ityetad atra sādharmyam iti 
māyākārasthānīyaṃ vijñaptimātratājñānaṃ 
nirmitayakṣasthānīyam arthābhāvajñānaṃ 
vijñaptimātrajñānaprabhāvitatvād arthābhāvajñānasya 
yathā nirmito nirmātāraṃ bhakṣyedevam arthābhāvajñānaṃ tadeva vijñaptimātrajñānaṃ bhakṣyati 
asatyarthe vijñaptimātrasyāsaṃbhavād arthopalabdhir vijñaptir iti kṛtvā 
samyaktve'pi vikalpo'nto mithyātve'pi vikalpo'nta ityadhikṛtaṃ 
nirvedhabhāgīyāvasthāyāṃ bhūtapratyavekṣāṃ samyaktvena vā vikalpayato mithyātvena vā 'ntadvayaṃ 
kathaṃ  samyaktvamanāsravā dharmā mithyātvaṃ sāsravāḥ 
tatra yadi bhūtapratyavekṣāṃ samyaktvenaivādhyavastyatyevaṃ kuśalasāsravā na bhūtapratyavekṣā syāt 
atha punar asamyaktvalakṣaṇam eva evam api mithyātvam evopapadyate traidhātukapratisaṃyuktakuśalavad iti 
etasyāntadvayasya parivarjanārthaṃ kāṣṭhadvayāgnidṛṣṭāntaḥ 
tadyathā kāśYapa kāṣṭhadvayaṃ pratītyagnir jāyata iti jātaś ca samānastadeva kāṣṭhadvayaṃ dahati 
evam eva kāśyapa bhūtapratyavekṣāṃ pratītyāryaṃ prajñendriyaṃ jāyate jātaṃ ca tām eva bhūtapratyavekṣāṃ dahatīti 
amamātrārthaḥ  yathā kāṣṭhadvayād anagnilakṣaṇād agnir jāyate jātaśca kāṣṭhadvayaṃ dahatīti 
evam evāsamyaktvalakṣaṇāyā bhūtapratyavekṣāyāḥ samyaktvalakṣaṇam āryaṃ prajñendriyaṃ jāyate 
jātaś ca tām eva bhūtaparatyavekṣāṃ dahati 
vibhāvayatītyarthaḥ 
sā hi vibhāvanād eva dagdheva dagdhety ucyate vikṛtidarśanāt 
iyañca bhūtapratyavekṣā sāsravāpi satī samyaktvānukūlyād bhūtapratyavekṣety ucyata iti 
vyāpṛtāv api vikalpo'ntaḥ avyāpṛtāv api 
vikalpo'nta ity adhikṛtaṃ 
katham ityata āha  jñānasya buddhipūrvāṃ kriyāṃ niḥsāmarthyaṃ vā kalpayata iti 
yadi  jñānam idam ajñānaṃ prajahāmītyavadhārya tat prahāṇāya pravartata ityayaṃ vyāpṛtau vikalpo'ntaḥ 
jñānasya kṣaṇikatvān na prahāṇavyāpārakāle saṃbhavaḥ 
ato'jñānaprahāṇasya niḥsāmarthyam tiyayam avyāpṛtau vikalpo'ntaḥ 
etasya vikalpadvayāntasya parivarjanārthaṃ tailapradyota dṛṣṭāntaḥ 
tadyathā kāśyapa tailapradyote kṛte tamo'ndhakāraṃ vigacchati na khalu punaḥ kāśyapa tailapradyotasyaivaṃ bhavaty ahaṃ sarvam andhakāraṃ vidhamāmīti 
api tu khalu tailapradyotaṃ pratītya tamo'ndhakāraṃ vigacchatīti 
evam eva kāśyapa jñāna utpanne'jñānaṃ vigacchati na khalu punaḥ kāśyapa jñānasyaivaṃ bhavaty aham ajñānaṃ vidhamāmīti 
api tu khalu jñānaṃ pratītyājñānaṃ vigacchatīti 
etad uktaṃ bhavati  yathā pradīpo vyāpāraśūnyas tamo'ndhakāravyudāsābhiprāyarahitaś ca punar yasmin pradeśe kriyate tasmāt pradeśāt pradīpasattāmātreṇa sarvatamo'ndhakāraṃ vigacchatīti 
evam eva yasmin santāne nirvikalpaṃ jñānam utpadyate tat sattāmātrasadbhāvād eva tasmāt santānād ajñānaṃ vigacchati jñānasya nirvikalpatvāt kriyā'bhāvārtheti 
evaṃ jñānasya vyāpārābhāvāt sāmarthyābhāvāt sāmarrthyābhāvaḥ pradīpavat sattāmātreṇa pratipakṣanirākaraṇād iti 
ajanmatve'pi vikalpo'ntaḥ samakālatve'pi 
vikalpo'nta ityanuvartate 
katham ityata āha  yadi pratipakṣasyānutpattiṃ vā kalpayati yatheyatā kālena notpannapūrvaḥ pratipakṣas tathedānīm api notpatsyata iti ayam ajanmatve vikalpo'ntaḥ 
sankleśasya vā dīrghakālatvam iti 
na hy ajñāne jñānapratiyoginyavasthita eva jñānam utpattuṃ samarthaṃ 
athāpi kathañcid utpadyeta tathāpi cirakālaviruddhatvād ajñānasya na jñānena tat kṣaṇikena vyudāsaḥ śakyate kartuṃ 
tataśca sankleśavyavadānayoḥ samānakālatvam iti 
etasya vikalpadvayāntasya parivarjanārthaṃ dvitīyas tailapradyotadṛṣṭānta iti 
tadyathā kāśyapa gṛhe vā layane vā'vacarake vā varṣasahasrasyātyayān na kenacit tailapradyotaḥ kuto bhavati 
atha tatra kaścid eva puruṣas tailapradyotaṃ kuryāt 
tat kiṃ manyase kāśyapāpi tu tamo'ndhākārasyaivaṃ bhaved varṣasahasrasañcito'haṃ nāham ato vigamiṣyāmīti 
āha  no bhagavan na hi tamo'ndhakārasya śaktir asti tailapradyote kṛte na vigantum avaśyaṃ tena vigantavyaṃ 
bhagavān āha  evam eva kāśyapa kalpaśatasahasrasañcito'pi karmakleśa ekena yoniśomanaskāreṇa vigacchati 
tailapradyota iti kāśyapa  idānīm ālambanānuttaryaṃ nirdeśāvasara ityata āha  ālambanānuttaryaṃ katamad iti 
atas tannirdhāraṇārthaṃ bravīti  vyavasthānaṃ tathā dhātuḥ iti vistaraḥ 
ityetad dvādaśavidham ālambanaṃ vyavasthānālambanam ārabhya yāvat prakarṣālambanaṃ 
tadanyasarvālambanotkṛṣṭatvād ālambanānuttaryam ucyate 
tatra prathamaṃ ye pāramitādayo dharmāste'pi buddhair bodhisattvaiś ca sattvānugrahārthaṃ vyavasthāpyanta iti vyavasthānaṃ 
etad eva pradarśayan bhāṣyakāro'pyāha  dharmaprajñaptivyavasthānālambanam iti 
dharmāṇāṃ dānapāramitādibodhipakṣāryasatyādīnāṃ prajñaptir dharmaprajñaptiḥ 
tayā vyavatiṣṭhate sā vā'tra vyavasthānam iti dharmaprajñaptivyavasthānaṃ 
abhisamayānukūlyāc cātra vyavasthānālambanādīnām ānupūrvīṃ draṣṭavyeti 
dvitīyaṃ tathatā dharmadhātuparyāyatvāt 
tṛtīyacaturthe iti 
tatra tṛtītaṃ sādhyālambanaṃ caturthaṃ sādhanālambanaṃ 
te eveti prathamadvitīya eva 
yathākramam iti prathamaṃ sādhyālambanaṃ dvitīyaṃ sādhanālambanaṃ 
tatraiva kāraṇam āha  dharmadhātuprativedhena pāramitādidharmādhigamād iti 
dharmadhātuprativedhād anāsravāḥ pāramitā adhigacchatītyataḥ sādhyālambanaṃ prathamaṃ sādhanālambanaṃ dvitīyam iti 
pañcamaṃ dhāraṇālambanaṃ 
tac chrutamayasya jñānasya 
śrutamātreṇa pāramitādīn dharmān dharmadhātuñca dhārayatīti śrutamayaṃ jñānaṃ dhāraṇety ucyate 
dhāraṇāyā ālambanaṃ dhāraṇālambanaṃ 
tat punaḥ prathamam eva dvayaṃ vyavasthānālambanaṃ dharmādhātvālambanañca 
ṣaṣṭhaṃ cintāmayasyāvagamya dhāraṇād iti 
apekṣākāryakāraṇopapattisādhanadharmatāyuktibhir avagamya śrutārthadhāraṇād avadhāraṇā cintāmayaṃ jñānaṃ tasyālambanam avadhāraṇālambanaṃ 
saptamaṃ bhāvanāmayasyālambanam iti prakṛtaṃ 
pratyātmaṃ dhāraṇād iti pratyātmam arthasya  dhāraṇāt pradhāraṇā prathamabhūmipraveśaprāyogikaṃ bhāvanāmayaṃ jñānaṃ 
tat punaḥ smṛtyupasthānānyārabhya yāvad balāni 
tasyālambanaṃ pradhāraṇālambanaṃ 
aṣṭamaṃ prathamāyāṃ bhūmau darśanamārgasyeti 
pratyātmam advayasya dharmadhātoḥ sarvatragatvaprativedhaḥ 
athavā darśanaheyānāṃ kleśānām akliṣṭasya cājñānasya sarvatragārthaviṣayasya pratyanīko vedhaḥ prativedhaḥ 
sa punar darśanamārgaḥ 
tasyālambanaṃ prativedhālambanaṃ 
navamaṃ bhāvanāmārgasya yāvat saptamyāṃ bhūmāv iti 
tasyaiva dharmadhātuprativedhasyābhyāsād uttarottaraprakarṣaṃ gatiḥ pratānatā bhāvanāmārgo yāvat saptamyāṃ bhūmau 
tasya bhāvanāmārgasyālambanaṃ pratānatālambanaṃ 
daśamaṃ tatraiva laukikalokottarasya mārgasyālambanam iti prakṛtaṃ 
prakāraśo dharmādhigamād iti 
tasyām eva bhūmau sarvasūtrādidharmanimittaprakārādyabhiniveśavigamamukhena prakāreṇa dharmādhigamāt pragama iti 
sa eva bhāvanāmārga ucyate saptamyām eva bhūmau 
pragamasyālambanaṃ pragamālambanaṃ 
ekādaśamaṣṭamyāṃ bhūmau 
aṣṭamyāṃ hi bhūmau sarvanimittābhogamanasikāravigatasya svarasena praśaṭhabvahanāt sa eva bhāvanāmārgaḥ 
praśaṭhasyālambanaṃ praśaṭhālambanaṃ 
dvādaśaṃ navamyādibhūmitraye navamyāṃ pratisaṃvijjñānaprakarṣalābhāt 
daśamyāṃ karmavaśitāprakarṣalābhāt 
buddhabhūmāv aśeṣakleśajñayāvaraṇaviśuddhiprakarṣālābhāt 
evaṃ navamyādibhūmitraye jñānakarmaviśuddhiprakarṣagamanāt tad bhūmivyavasthitasya yadālambanaṃ tat prakarṣālambanam ucyate 
anyaḥ punar āha  mārgaprakarṣasyaiva mṛdumadhyādhimātrabhedaṃ kṛtvā prakarṣālambanaṃ tisṛṣu bhūmiṣūktam iti 
tadeva hi prathamadvayaṃ tasyāṃ tasyām avasthāyāṃ tat tadālambananāma pratilabhata iti 
etac cālambanaṃ yad uta dharmavyavasthānālambanaṃ dharmadhātvālambanañca 
taccaitad ālambanadvayaṃ tasyāṃ tasyāṃ jñānāvasthāyāṃ tat tan nāma labhate 
śrutamayajñānāvasthāyāṃ dhāraṇālambanaṃ dhāraṇājñānaviṣayatvāc chrutasya 
tena ca dhāraṇājñānaṃ dhāraṇety ucyate 
evaṃ yāvat prakarṣālambanaṃ vaktavyaṃ 
navamyāṃ daśamyāṃ buddhabhūmau ca prakarṣāprāptaṃ lokottaraṃ jñānaṃ tat pṛṣṭhalabdhaṃ ca laukikaṃ 
tasyālambanaṃ prakarṣālambanaṃ 
uktam ālambanānuttaryaṃ 
  samudāgamānuttaryaṃ   idānīṃ samudāgamānuttaryasyāvasaraprāptasyā'vadhāraṇārtham āha  samudāgamaḥ katama iti 
tayā tayā pratipattyā samudānīyata iti samudāgamaḥ 
tad anyebhyaḥ samudāgamebhyo viśiṣṭatvāt tataścānyasya samudāgamasya viśiṣṭābhāvād ānuttaryam ucyate 
tat pradarśanārtham āha  avaikalyāpratikṣepo vikṣepaś ca prapūraṇā 
iti vistaraḥ 
tatra pratyayāvaikalyam ārabhya yāvad bodhisandarśanam ityeṣa daśavidhaḥ samudāgamaḥ 
tatra pratyayāvaikalyaṃ gotrasamudāgama iti 
pratyayānām avaikalyaṃ samagrāṇāṃ sānnidhyaṃ 
teṣv āhṛteṣu gotraṃ samudāgaccyati sphītaṃ tad viśiṣṭataraṃ bhavatītyarthaḥ 
tat punaḥ satpuruṣasaṃsevā saddharmaśravaṇaṃ yoniśo manaskāra ityevam ādayaḥ 
teṣāṃ tad gotramitrādivaikalyād vaikalyaṃ 
mahāyānāpratikṣepo'dhimuktisamudāgama iti 
yadi gāmbhīryaudāryalakṣaṇamahāyānadharmaṃ na pratikṣipatyevam asya niścayasya dhāraṇātmikāyā adhimukteḥ puṣṭir bhavati 
hīnayānāvikṣepaścittorpādasamudāgama iti 
yadutpāditabodhicittasya satsvapi bodhicittavyāvṛttipratyayeṣu śrāvakayāne pratyekabuddhayāne vā cittam asya na krāmatyevam asya tad bodhicittaṃ puṣṭim āpadyate 
pāramitāparipūraṇā pratipattisamudāgama iti 
utpāditabodhicittānāṃ tadvaśād dānādipāramitānāṃ paripūryā sarvajñatā pratipattipuṣṭir bhavati 
āryamārgotpādo nyāmāvakrāntisamudāgama iti 
prathamata evāpūrvasyāryamārgasyotpādo nyāmāvakrāntir bhavati 
āma ucyate doṣaḥ kṣayo vā 
sa yatra nāsti sā nyāmā nivātavadanāsravā bhūmiḥ nyāmāyāmavakrāntir nyāmāvakrāntiḥ praveśa ityarthaḥ 
  niyamāvakrāntipāṭhe'pi niyama eva niyamaḥ 
tathā hy utpannadarśanamārgo niyato bhavati sugatau nirvāṇe ceti 
kuśalamūlanirūḍhir dīrghakālaparicayāt sattvaparipākasamudāgama iti 
labdhadarśanamārgāṇāṃ tat pṛṣṭhalabdhasya bhāvanāmārgasya dīrghakālaparicayād abhyāsāt kuśalamūlavṛddhiḥ kuśalamūlanirūḍhiḥ 
tayā sattvaparipācanasamartho bhavati 
ataḥ kuśalamūlanirūḍhiḥ sattvaparipākasamudāgamaḥ 
anye tvāhuḥ  evam asya sattvaparipākaḥ samudāgato bhavatiḥ yadyanena dīrghakālābhyāsamāgamya sattvasantāneṣu kuśalamūlaṃ dṛḍhīkṛtaṃ 
cittakarmañatā kṣetrapariśuddhisamudāgama iti 
evaṃ bhāvanayā vivṛddhakuśalamūlānām ekāyatanamārgavipakṣayor nimittābhogayor vigamāc cittasya karmañatā 
yat karmañatādhipatyena yathecchaṃ sphaṭikādimayaṃ buddhakṣetraṃ darśayatītyaścittakarmaṇyatā kṣetrapariśruddhisamudāgamaḥ 
  yānānuttaryapiṇḍārthaḥ   yānānuttaryasya piṇḍārtha iti pūrvaṃ piṇḍārthākhyānaprayojanam ucyate 
samāsatas trividham ānuttaryam iti vyāsato'nantam iti 
pratipattir yad uktaṃ  ānuttaryaṃ prapattau hi pratipattyādhāro yad uktaṃ  punar ālambane iti 
pratipattiphalaṃ yad uktaṃ  samudāgama uddiṣṭaṃ iti 
sā ca pratipattir yādṛśī parameti  paramā dvādaśātmikā 
ityuktaṃ 
yeneti  yathāprajñaptito dharmamahāyānamanaskriyā 
  ityevam ādineti 
bodhisattvasya satataṃ prajñayā triprakārayā 
iti vacanāt 
tathā ca  saṃyuktā dharmacaritaiḥ sā jñeyā daśabhiḥ punaḥ 
iti 
yathā yena prakāreṇā'vikṣepapariṇatā ca śamathabhāvanayeti ṣaḍvidhavikṣepābhāvāt 
aviparyāsapariṇatā ca vipaśyanābhāvanayeti vyañjanādiṣu daśasu viparyāsābhāvāt 
yad arthañca madhyamayā pratipadā niryāṇārtham ityantadvayavarjane pratipattiḥ 
yatra ceti yāsu  daśasu bhūmiṣu 
kim ityata āha  viśiṣṭā cāviśiṣtā ca iti 
aviparyāsānāṃ piṇḍārthaḥ 
punar vyañjanā'viparyāsena śamathānimittaṃ pratividhyatīti saṃyogasvabhāvavigataṃ sākṣātkaroti 
arthāviparyāsena vipaśyanānimittaṃ dvayam api bhrāntimātratvena pratividhyati 
manaskārāviparyāsena viparyāsanidānam ālayavijñānāhitaṃ dvayābhiniveśabījaṃ parivarjayati 
aviasārāviparyāsena viparyāsanimittaṃ māyādivad sadasattvānabhiniveśena saṃgṛhītaṃ karoti 
svalakṣaṇāviparyāsena tat pratipakṣeṇāvikalpam abhilāparahitaṃ dharmasvalakṣaṇaviṣayaṃ mārgaṃ bhāvayati 
sāmānyalakṣaṇāviparyāsena vyavadānaprakṛtiṃ sarvadharmasāmānyatayā pratividhyati 
aśuddhiśuddhimanaskārāviparyāsena tadāvaraṇaprahīṇāprahīṇatāṃ prajānāti prakṛtiprabhāsvarasya dharmadhātor āgantukopakleśakliṣṭatvāt 
tadāgantukatvāviparyāsena saṃkleśavyavadānaṃ prajānāti iti prakṛtiprabhāsvarasyānyathā saṃkleśasya vyavadānasya cāsambhavāt 
atrāsānunnatyaviparyāsena pudgaladharmānabhiniveśato nirāvaraṇo niryātīti 
samāptā ceyam āgamānusāriṇī madhyāntavibhāgaṭīkā ācāryasthiramatyuparacitā
